::centre
Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa
::

# Saṃyuttanikāyo

## Sagāthāvaggo

### 1. Devatāsaṃyuttaṃ

#### 1. Naḷavaggo

#### 1. Oghataraṇasuttaṃ

{para:1} 1\. Evaṃ {pb:T:1.0001}{pb:V:1.0001}{pb:P:1.0001}{pb:M:1.0001} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Atha kho aññatarā devatā abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇā kevalakappaṃ jetavanaṃ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṃ ṭhitā kho sā devatā bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘‘kathaṃ nu tvaṃ, mārisa, oghamatarī’ti? ‘Appatiṭṭhaṃ khvāhaṃ, āvuso, anāyūhaṃ {pb:V:1.0002} oghamatari’nti. ‘Yathā kathaṃ pana tvaṃ, mārisa, appatiṭṭhaṃ anāyūhaṃ oghamatarī’ti? ‘Yadākhvāhaṃ, āvuso, santiṭṭhāmi tadāssu saṃsīdāmi{pb:T:1.0002}; yadākhvāhaṃ, āvuso, āyūhāmi tadāssu nibbuyhāmi {note:nivuyhāmi (syā. kaṃ. ka.)}. Evaṃ khvāhaṃ, āvuso, appatiṭṭhaṃ anāyūhaṃ oghamatari’’’nti.

::gatha1
‘‘Cirassaṃ vata passāmi, brāhmaṇaṃ parinibbutaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Appatiṭṭhaṃ anāyūhaṃ, tiṇṇaṃ loke visattika’’nti. –
::

::unindented
Idamavoca {pb:M:1.0002} sā devatā. Samanuñño satthā ahosi. Atha kho sā devatā – ‘‘samanuñño me satthā’’ti bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaṃ katvā tatthevantaradhāyīti.
::

#### 2. Nimokkhasuttaṃ

{para:2} 2\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:P:1.0002}. Atha kho aññatarā devatā abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇā kevalakappaṃ jetavanaṃ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṃ ṭhitā kho sā devatā bhagavantaṃ etadavoca –

‘‘Jānāsi no tvaṃ, mārisa, sattānaṃ nimokkhaṃ pamokkhaṃ viveka’’nti?

‘‘Jānāmi khvāhaṃ, āvuso, sattānaṃ nimokkhaṃ pamokkhaṃ viveka’’nti.

‘‘Yathā kathaṃ pana tvaṃ, mārisa, jānāsi sattānaṃ nimokkhaṃ pamokkhaṃ viveka’’nti?

‘‘Nandībhavaparikkhayā {pb:T:1.0003} {note:nandibhavaparikkhayā (syā. kaṃ.)}, saññāviññāṇasaṅkhayā, vedanānaṃ nirodhā upasamā – evaṃ khvāhaṃ, āvuso, jānāmi sattānaṃ nimokkhaṃ pamokkhaṃ viveka’’nti.

#### 3. Upanīyasuttaṃ

{para:3} 3\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:V:1.0003}. Ekamantaṃ ṭhitā kho sā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Upanīyati jīvitamappamāyu,
::

::gatha2
Jarūpanītassa na santi tāṇā;
::

::gatha3
Etaṃ bhayaṃ maraṇe pekkhamāno,
::

::gathalast
Puññāni kayirātha sukhāvahānī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upanīyati jīvitamappamāyu,
::

::gatha2
Jarūpanītassa na santi tāṇā;
::

::gatha3
Etaṃ bhayaṃ maraṇe pekkhamāno,
::

::gathalast
Lokāmisaṃ pajahe santipekkho’’ti.
::

#### 4. Accentisuttaṃ

{para:4} 4\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:M:1.0003}. Ekamantaṃ {pb:T:1.0004}{pb:P:1.0003} ṭhitā kho sā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Accenti kālā tarayanti rattiyo,
::

::gatha2
Vayoguṇā anupubbaṃ jahanti;
::

::gatha3
Etaṃ bhayaṃ maraṇe pekkhamāno,
::

::gathalast
Puññāni kayirātha sukhāvahānī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Accenti kālā tarayanti rattiyo,
::

::gatha2
Vayoguṇā anupubbaṃ jahanti;
::

::gatha3
Etaṃ bhayaṃ maraṇe pekkhamāno,
::

::gathalast
Lokāmisaṃ pajahe santipekkho’’ti.
::

#### 5. Katichindasuttaṃ

{para:5} 5\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:V:1.0004}. Ekamantaṃ ṭhitā kho sā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kati chinde kati jahe, kati cuttari bhāvaye;
::

::gathalast
Kati saṅgātigo bhikkhu, oghatiṇṇoti vuccatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañca chinde pañca jahe, pañca cuttari bhāvaye;
::

::gathalast
Pañca saṅgātigo bhikkhu, oghatiṇṇoti vuccatī’’ti.
::

#### 6. Jāgarasuttaṃ

{para:6} 6\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Ekamantaṃ {pb:T:1.0005} ṭhitā kho sā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kati jāgarataṃ suttā, kati suttesu jāgarā;
::

::gathalast
Katibhi {note:katīhi (sī.)} rajamādeti, katibhi {note:katīhi (sī.)} parisujjhatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañca jāgarataṃ suttā, pañca suttesu jāgarā;
::

::gathalast
Pañcabhi {note:pañcahi (sī.)} rajamādeti, pañcabhi {note:pañcahi (sī.)} parisujjhatī’’ti.
::

#### 7. Appaṭividitasuttaṃ

{para:7} 7\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:M:1.0004}. Ekamantaṃ {pb:P:1.0004} ṭhitā kho sā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Yesaṃ dhammā appaṭividitā, paravādesu nīyare {note:niyyare (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Suttā te nappabujjhanti, kālo tesaṃ pabujjhitu’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yesaṃ dhammā suppaṭividitā, paravādesu na nīyare;
::

::gathalast
Te sambuddhā sammadaññā, caranti visame sama’’nti.
::

#### 8. Susammuṭṭhasuttaṃ

{para:8} 8\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Ekamantaṃ ṭhitā kho sā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Yesaṃ {pb:T:1.0006} dhammā susammuṭṭhā, paravādesu nīyare;
::

::gathalast
Suttā te nappabujjhanti, kālo tesaṃ pabujjhitu’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yesaṃ {pb:V:1.0005} dhammā asammuṭṭhā, paravādesu na nīyare;
::

::gathalast
Te sambuddhā sammadaññā, caranti visame sama’’nti.
::

#### 9. Mānakāmasuttaṃ

{para:9} 9\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Ekamantaṃ ṭhitā kho sā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Na mānakāmassa damo idhatthi,
::

::gatha2
Na monamatthi asamāhitassa;
::

::gatha3
Eko araññe viharaṃ pamatto,
::

::gathalast
Na maccudheyyassa tareyya pāra’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mānaṃ pahāya susamāhitatto,
::

::gatha2
Sucetaso sabbadhi vippamutto;
::

::gatha3
Eko araññe viharaṃ appamatto,
::

::gathalast
Sa maccudheyyassa tareyya pāra’’nti.
::

#### 10. Araññasuttaṃ

{para:10} 10\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:V:1.0006}{pb:M:1.0005}. Ekamantaṃ {pb:P:1.0005} ṭhitā kho sā devatā bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Araññe {pb:T:1.0007} viharantānaṃ, santānaṃ brahmacārinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ekabhattaṃ bhuñjamānānaṃ, kena vaṇṇo pasīdatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atītaṃ nānusocanti, nappajappanti nāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Paccuppannena yāpenti, tena vaṇṇo pasīdati’’.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anāgatappajappāya, atītassānusocanā;
::

::gathalast
Etena bālā sussanti, naḷova harito luto’’ti.
::

::centre
Naḷavaggo paṭhamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Oghaṃ nimokkhaṃ upaneyyaṃ, accenti katichindi ca;
::

::gatha2
Jāgaraṃ appaṭividitā, susammuṭṭhā mānakāminā;
::

::gathalast
Araññe dasamo vutto, vaggo tena pavuccati.
::

#### 2. Nandanavaggo

#### 1. Nandanasuttaṃ

{para:11} 11\. Evaṃ {pb:T:1.0008} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa {pb:V:1.0007} ārāme. Tatra kho bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi – ‘‘bhikkhavo’’ti. ‘‘Bhadante’’ti te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṃ. Bhagavā etadavoca –

‘‘Bhūtapubbaṃ, bhikkhave, aññatarā tāvatiṃsakāyikā devatā nandane vane accharāsaṅghaparivutā dibbehi pañcahi kāmaguṇehi samappitā samaṅgībhūtā paricāriyamānā {note:paricāriyamānā (syā. kaṃ. ka.)} tāyaṃ velāyaṃ imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:M:1.0006} te sukhaṃ pajānanti, ye na passanti nandanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Āvāsaṃ naradevānaṃ, tidasānaṃ yasassina’’nti.
::

‘‘Evaṃ {pb:P:1.0006} vutte, bhikkhave, aññatarā devatā taṃ devataṃ gāthāya paccabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Na tvaṃ bāle pajānāsi, yathā arahataṃ vaco;
::

::gatha2
Aniccā sabbasaṅkhārā {note:sabbe saṅkhārā (sī. syā. kaṃ.)}, uppādavayadhammino;
::

::gathalast
Uppajjitvā nirujjhanti, tesaṃ vūpasamo sukho’’ti.
::

#### 2. Nandatisuttaṃ

{para:12} 12\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Ekamantaṃ {pb:T:1.0009} ṭhitā kho sā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Nandati puttehi puttimā,
::

::gatha2
Gomā {note:gomiko (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} gohi tatheva nandati;
::

::gatha3
Upadhīhi {pb:V:1.0008} narassa nandanā,
::

::gathalast
Na hi so nandati yo nirūpadhī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Socati puttehi puttimā,
::

::gatha2
Gomā gohi tatheva socati;
::

::gatha3
Upadhīhi narassa socanā,
::

::gathalast
Na hi so socati yo nirūpadhī’’ti.
::

#### 3. Natthiputtasamasuttaṃ

{para:13} 13\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Ekamantaṃ ṭhitā kho sā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Natthi puttasamaṃ pemaṃ, natthi gosamitaṃ dhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Natthi sūriyasamā {note:suriyasamā (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} ābhā, samuddaparamā sarā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Natthi attasamaṃ pemaṃ, natthi dhaññasamaṃ dhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Natthi paññāsamā ābhā, vuṭṭhi ve paramā sarā’’ti.
::

#### 4. Khattiyasuttaṃ

{para:14} 14\. ‘‘Khattiyo {pb:T:1.0010}{pb:M:1.0007} dvipadaṃ seṭṭho, balībaddo {note:balivaddo (sī. pī.), balibaddo (syā. kaṃ. ka.)} catuppadaṃ.

::gathalast
Komārī seṭṭhā bhariyānaṃ, yo ca puttāna pubbajo’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sambuddho dvipadaṃ seṭṭho, ājānīyo catuppadaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sussūsā seṭṭhā bhariyānaṃ, yo ca puttānamassavo’’ti.
::

#### 5. Saṇamānasuttaṃ

{para:15} 15\. ‘‘Ṭhite {pb:P:1.0007} majjhanhike {note:majjhantike (sabbattha)} kāle, sannisīvesu pakkhisu.

::gathalast
Saṇateva brahāraññaṃ {note:mahāraññaṃ (ka. sī. syā. kaṃ. ka.)}, taṃ bhayaṃ paṭibhāti ma’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ṭhite majjhanhike kāle, sannisīvesu pakkhisu;
::

::gathalast
Saṇateva brahāraññaṃ, sā rati paṭibhāti ma’’nti.
::

#### 6. Niddātandīsuttaṃ

{para:16} 16\. ‘‘Niddā {pb:V:1.0009} tandī vijambhitā {note:tandi vijambhikā (sī. pī.)}, aratī bhattasammado.

::gathalast
Etena nappakāsati, ariyamaggo idha pāṇina’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Niddaṃ tandiṃ vijambhitaṃ, aratiṃ bhattasammadaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vīriyena {note:viriyena (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} naṃ paṇāmetvā, ariyamaggo visujjhatī’’ti.
::

#### 7. Dukkarasuttaṃ

{para:17} 17\. ‘‘Dukkaraṃ {pb:T:1.0011} duttitikkhañca, abyattena ca sāmaññaṃ.

::gathalast
Bahūhi tattha sambādhā, yattha bālo visīdatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Katihaṃ careyya sāmaññaṃ, cittaṃ ce na nivāraye;
::

::gathalast
Pade pade visīdeyya, saṅkappānaṃ vasānugo’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kummova aṅgāni sake kapāle,
::

::gatha2
Samodahaṃ bhikkhu manovitakke;
::

::gatha3
Anissito aññamaheṭhayāno,
::

::gathalast
Parinibbuto nūpavadeyya kañcī’’ti.
::

#### 8. Hirīsuttaṃ

{para:18} 18\. ‘‘Hirīnisedho {pb:M:1.0008} puriso, koci lokasmiṃ vijjati.

::gathalast
Yo nindaṃ apabodhati {note:apabodheti (syā. kaṃ. ka.)}, asso bhadro kasāmivā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hirīnisedhā tanuyā, ye caranti sadā satā;
::

::gathalast
Antaṃ dukkhassa pappuyya, caranti visame sama’’nti.
::

#### 9. Kuṭikāsuttaṃ

::hangnum
19\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kacci {pb:V:1.0010}{pb:P:1.0008} te kuṭikā natthi, kacci natthi kulāvakā;
::

::gathalast
Kacci santānakā natthi, kacci muttosi bandhanā’’ti.
::

::gatha2
‘‘Taggha me kuṭikā natthi, taggha natthi kulāvakā;
::

::gathalast
Taggha santānakā natthi, taggha muttomhi bandhanā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kintāhaṃ {pb:T:1.0012} kuṭikaṃ brūmi, kiṃ te brūmi kulāvakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ te santānakaṃ brūmi, kintāhaṃ brūmi bandhana’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mātaraṃ kuṭikaṃ brūsi, bhariyaṃ brūsi kulāvakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Putte santānake brūsi, taṇhaṃ me brūsi bandhana’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāhu te kuṭikā natthi, sāhu natthi kulāvakā;
::

::gathalast
Sāhu santānakā natthi, sāhu muttosi bandhanā’’ti.
::

#### 10. Samiddhisuttaṃ

{para:20} 20\. Evaṃ me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati tapodārāme. Atha kho āyasmā samiddhi rattiyā paccūsasamayaṃ paccuṭṭhāya yena tapodā tenupasaṅkami gattāni parisiñcituṃ. Tapode gattāni parisiñcitvā paccuttaritvā ekacīvaro aṭṭhāsi gattāni pubbāpayamāno. Atha kho aññatarā devatā abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇā kevalakappaṃ tapodaṃ obhāsetvā yena āyasmā samiddhi tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā vehāsaṃ ṭhitā āyasmantaṃ samiddhiṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Abhutvā {pb:M:1.0009} bhikkhasi bhikkhu, na hi bhutvāna bhikkhasi;
::

::gathalast
Bhutvāna bhikkhu bhikkhassu, mā taṃ kālo upaccagā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kālaṃ {pb:T:1.0013}{pb:V:1.0011}{pb:P:1.0009} vohaṃ na jānāmi, channo kālo na dissati;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā abhutvā bhikkhāmi, mā maṃ kālo upaccagā’’ti.
::

Atha kho sā devatā pathaviyaṃ {note:paṭhaviyaṃ (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} patiṭṭhahitvā āyasmantaṃ samiddhiṃ etadavoca – ‘‘daharo tvaṃ bhikkhu, pabbajito susu kāḷakeso, bhadrena yobbanena samannāgato, paṭhamena vayasā, anikkīḷitāvī kāmesu. Bhuñja, bhikkhu, mānusake kāme; mā sandiṭṭhikaṃ hitvā kālikaṃ anudhāvī’’ti.

‘‘Na khvāhaṃ, āvuso, sandiṭṭhikaṃ hitvā kālikaṃ anudhāvāmi. Kālikañca khvāhaṃ, āvuso, hitvā sandiṭṭhikaṃ anudhāvāmi. Kālikā hi, āvuso, kāmā vuttā bhagavatā bahudukkhā bahupāyāsā; ādīnavo ettha bhiyyo. Sandiṭṭhiko ayaṃ dhammo akāliko ehipassiko opaneyyiko paccattaṃ veditabbo viññūhī’’ti.

‘‘Kathañca, bhikkhu, kālikā kāmā vuttā bhagavatā bahudukkhā bahupāyāsā, ādīnavo ettha bhiyyo? Kathaṃ sandiṭṭhiko ayaṃ dhammo akāliko ehipassiko opaneyyiko paccattaṃ veditabbo viññūhī’’ti?

‘‘Ahaṃ kho, āvuso, navo acirapabbajito adhunāgato imaṃ dhammavinayaṃ. Na tāhaṃ {note:na khvāhaṃ (sī. pī.)} sakkomi vitthārena ācikkhituṃ. Ayaṃ so bhagavā arahaṃ sammāsambuddho rājagahe viharati tapodārāme. Taṃ bhagavantaṃ upasaṅkamitvā etamatthaṃ puccha. Yathā te bhagavā byākaroti tathā naṃ dhāreyyāsī’’ti.

‘‘Na kho, bhikkhu, sukaro so bhagavā amhehi upasaṅkamituṃ{pb:T:1.0014}, aññāhi mahesakkhāhi devatāhi parivuto. Sace kho tvaṃ, bhikkhu, taṃ bhagavantaṃ upasaṅkamitvā etamatthaṃ puccheyyāsi, mayampi āgaccheyyāma dhammassavanāyā’’ti. ‘‘Evamāvuso’’ti kho āyasmā samiddhi tassā devatāya paṭissutvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi. Ekamantaṃ {pb:P:1.0010} nisinno kho āyasmā samiddhi bhagavantaṃ etadavoca –

‘‘Idhāhaṃ{pb:V:1.0012}{pb:M:1.0010}, bhante, rattiyā paccūsasamayaṃ paccuṭṭhāya yena tapodā tenupasaṅkamiṃ gattāni parisiñcituṃ. Tapode gattāni parisiñcitvā paccuttaritvā ekacīvaro aṭṭhāsiṃ gattāni pubbāpayamāno. Atha kho, bhante, aññatarā devatā abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇā kevalakappaṃ tapodaṃ obhāsetvā yenāhaṃ tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā vehāsaṃ ṭhitā imāya gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Abhutvā bhikkhasi bhikkhu, na hi bhutvāna bhikkhasi;
::

::gathalast
Bhutvāna bhikkhu bhikkhassu, mā taṃ kālo upaccagā’’ti.
::

‘‘Evaṃ vutte ahaṃ, bhante, taṃ devataṃ gāthāya paccabhāsiṃ –

::gatha1
‘‘Kālaṃ vohaṃ na jānāmi, channo kālo na dissati;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā abhutvā bhikkhāmi, mā maṃ kālo upaccagā’’ti.
::

‘‘Atha kho, bhante, sā devatā pathaviyaṃ patiṭṭhahitvā maṃ etadavoca – ‘daharo {pb:T:1.0015} tvaṃ, bhikkhu, pabbajito susu kāḷakeso, bhadrena yobbanena samannāgato, paṭhamena vayasā, anikkīḷitāvī kāmesu. Bhuñja, bhikkhu, mānusake kāme; mā sandiṭṭhikaṃ hitvā kālikaṃ anudhāvī’’’ti.

‘‘Evaṃ vuttāhaṃ, bhante, taṃ devataṃ etadavocaṃ – ‘na khvāhaṃ, āvuso, sandiṭṭhikaṃ hitvā kālikaṃ anudhāvāmi; kālikañca khvāhaṃ, āvuso, hitvā sandiṭṭhikaṃ anudhāvāmi. Kālikā hi, āvuso, kāmā vuttā bhagavatā bahudukkhā bahupāyāsā; ādīnavo ettha bhiyyo. Sandiṭṭhiko ayaṃ dhammo akāliko ehipassiko opaneyyiko paccattaṃ veditabbo viññūhī’’’ti.

‘‘Evaṃ vutte, bhante, sā devatā maṃ etadavoca – ‘kathañca, bhikkhu, kālikā kāmā vuttā bhagavatā bahudukkhā bahupāyāsā; ādīnavo ettha bhiyyo? Kathaṃ sandiṭṭhiko {pb:P:1.0011} ayaṃ dhammo akāliko ehipassiko opaneyyiko paccattaṃ veditabbo viññūhī’ti? Evaṃ vuttāhaṃ, bhante{pb:V:1.0013}, taṃ devataṃ etadavocaṃ – ‘ahaṃ kho, āvuso, navo acirapabbajito adhunāgato imaṃ dhammavinayaṃ, na tāhaṃ sakkomi vitthārena ācikkhituṃ. Ayaṃ so bhagavā arahaṃ sammāsambuddho rājagahe viharati tapodārāme. Taṃ bhagavantaṃ upasaṅkamitvā etamatthaṃ puccha. Yathā te bhagavā byākaroti tathā naṃ dhāreyyāsī’’’ti.

‘‘Evaṃ {pb:M:1.0011} vutte, bhante, sā devatā maṃ etadavoca – ‘na kho, bhikkhu, sukaro so bhagavā amhehi upasaṅkamituṃ, aññāhi mahesakkhāhi devatāhi parivuto. Sace kho, tvaṃ bhikkhu, taṃ bhagavantaṃ upasaṅkamitvā etamatthaṃ puccheyyāsi, mayampi āgaccheyyāma {pb:T:1.0016} dhammassavanāyā’ti. Sace, bhante, tassā devatāya saccaṃ vacanaṃ, idheva sā devatā avidūre’’ti.

Evaṃ vutte, sā devatā āyasmantaṃ samiddhiṃ etadavoca – ‘‘puccha, bhikkhu, puccha, bhikkhu, yamahaṃ anuppattā’’ti.

Atha kho bhagavā taṃ devataṃ gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Akkheyyasaññino sattā, akkheyyasmiṃ patiṭṭhitā;
::

::gathalast
Akkheyyaṃ apariññāya, yogamāyanti maccuno.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akkheyyañca pariññāya, akkhātāraṃ na maññati;
::

::gatha2
Tañhi tassa na hotīti, yena naṃ vajjā na tassa atthi;
::

::gathalast
Sace vijānāsi vadehi yakkhā’’ti {note:yakkhīti (pī. ka.)}.
::

‘‘Na khvāhaṃ, bhante, imassa bhagavatā saṅkhittena bhāsitassa vitthārena atthaṃ ājānāmi. Sādhu me, bhante, bhagavā tathā bhāsatu yathāhaṃ imassa bhagavatā saṅkhittena bhāsitassa vitthārena atthaṃ jāneyya’’nti.

::gatha1
‘‘Samo {pb:P:1.0012} visesī uda vā {note:athavā (sī. pī.)} nihīno,
::

::gatha2
Yo maññatī so vivadetha {note:sopi vadetha (ka.)} tena;
::

::gatha3
Tīsu {pb:V:1.0014} vidhāsu avikampamāno,
::

::gatha2
Samo visesīti na tassa hoti;
::

::gathalast
Sace vijānāsi vadehi yakkhā’’ti.
::

‘‘Imassāpi {pb:T:1.0017} khvāhaṃ, bhante, bhagavatā saṅkhittena bhāsitassa na vitthārena atthaṃ ājānāmi. Sādhu me, bhante, bhagavā tathā bhāsatu yathāhaṃ imassa bhagavatā saṅkhittena bhāsitassa vitthārena atthaṃ jāneyya’’nti.

::gatha1
‘‘Pahāsi saṅkhaṃ na vimānamajjhagā, acchecchi {note:acchejji (syā. kaṃ. ka.)} taṇhaṃ idha nāmarūpe;
::

::gatha2
Taṃ chinnaganthaṃ anighaṃ nirāsaṃ, pariyesamānā nājjhagamuṃ;
::

::gatha3
Devā manussā idha vā huraṃ vā, saggesu vā sabbanivesanesu;
::

::gathalast
Sace vijānāsi vadehi yakkhā’’ti.
::

‘‘Imassa {pb:M:1.0012} khvāhaṃ, bhante, bhagavatā saṅkhittena bhāsitassa evaṃ vitthārena atthaṃ ājānāmi –

::gatha1
‘‘Pāpaṃ na kayirā vacasā manasā,
::

::gatha2
Kāyena vā kiñcana sabbaloke;
::

::gatha3
Kāme pahāya satimā sampajāno,
::

::gathalast
Dukkhaṃ na sevetha anatthasaṃhita’’nti.
::

::centre
Nandanavaggo dutiyo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Nandanā {pb:T:1.0018} nandati ceva, natthiputtasamena ca;
::

::gatha2
Khattiyo saṇamāno ca, niddātandī ca dukkaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Hirī kuṭikā navamo, dasamo vutto samiddhināti.
::

#### 3. Sattivaggo

#### 1. Sattisuttaṃ

{para:21} 21\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:V:1.0015}{pb:P:1.0013}. Ekamantaṃ {pb:T:1.0019} ṭhitā kho sā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sattiyā viya omaṭṭho, ḍayhamānova {note:ḍayhamāneva (sabbattha)} matthake;
::

::gathalast
Kāmarāgappahānāya, sato bhikkhu paribbaje’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sattiyā viya omaṭṭho, ḍayhamānova matthake;
::

::gathalast
Sakkāyadiṭṭhippahānāya, sato bhikkhu paribbaje’’ti.
::

#### 2. Phusatisuttaṃ

::hangnum
22\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāphusantaṃ phusati ca, phusantañca tato phuse;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā phusantaṃ phusati, appaduṭṭhapadosina’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo {pb:M:1.0013} appaduṭṭhassa narassa dussati,
::

::gatha2
Suddhassa posassa anaṅgaṇassa;
::

::gatha3
Tameva bālaṃ pacceti pāpaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Sukhumo rajo paṭivātaṃva khitto’’ti.
::

#### 3. Jaṭāsuttaṃ

::hangnum
23\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anto {pb:T:1.0020} jaṭā bahi jaṭā, jaṭāya jaṭitā pajā;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ taṃ gotama pucchāmi, ko imaṃ vijaṭaye jaṭa’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sīle {pb:V:1.0016} patiṭṭhāya naro sapañño, cittaṃ paññañca bhāvayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ātāpī nipako bhikkhu, so imaṃ vijaṭaye jaṭaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yesaṃ rāgo ca doso ca, avijjā ca virājitā;
::

::gathalast
Khīṇāsavā arahanto, tesaṃ vijaṭitā jaṭā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yattha nāmañca rūpañca, asesaṃ uparujjhati;
::

::gathalast
Paṭighaṃ rūpasaññā ca, etthesā chijjate {note:vijaṭe (ka.)} jaṭā’’ti.
::

#### 4. Manonivāraṇasuttaṃ

{para:24} 24\. ‘‘Yato {pb:P:1.0014} yato mano nivāraye,

::gatha2
Na dukkhameti naṃ tato tato;
::

::gatha3
Sa sabbato mano nivāraye,
::

::gathalast
Sa sabbato dukkhā pamuccati’’.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na sabbato mano nivāraye,
::

::gatha2
Na mano saṃyatattamāgataṃ;
::

::gatha3
Yato yato ca pāpakaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Tato tato mano nivāraye’’ti.
::

#### 5. Arahantasuttaṃ

::hangnum
25\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo hoti bhikkhu arahaṃ katāvī,
::

::gatha2
Khīṇāsavo antimadehadhārī;
::

::gatha3
Ahaṃ {pb:T:1.0021} vadāmītipi so vadeyya,
::

::gathalast
Mamaṃ vadantītipi so vadeyyā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo {pb:V:1.0017}{pb:M:1.0014} hoti bhikkhu arahaṃ katāvī,
::

::gatha2
Khīṇāsavo antimadehadhārī;
::

::gatha3
Ahaṃ vadāmītipi so vadeyya,
::

::gatha2
Mamaṃ vadantītipi so vadeyya;
::

::gatha3
Loke samaññaṃ kusalo viditvā,
::

::gathalast
Vohāramattena so {note:sa (?)} vohareyyā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo hoti bhikkhu arahaṃ katāvī,
::

::gatha2
Khīṇāsavo antimadehadhārī;
::

::gatha3
Mānaṃ nu kho so upagamma bhikkhu,
::

::gatha2
Ahaṃ vadāmītipi so vadeyya;
::

::gathalast
Mamaṃ vadantītipi so vadeyyā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pahīnamānassa na santi ganthā,
::

::gatha2
Vidhūpitā mānaganthassa sabbe;
::

::gatha3
Sa vītivatto maññataṃ {note:mānanaṃ (sī.), maññītaṃ (?)} sumedho,
::

::gathalast
Ahaṃ {pb:P:1.0015} vadāmītipi so vadeyya.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mamaṃ vadantītipi so vadeyya;
::

::gatha2
Loke samaññaṃ kusalo viditvā;
::

::gathalast
Vohāramattena so vohareyyā’’ti.
::

#### 6. Pajjotasuttaṃ

::hangnum
26\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kati {pb:T:1.0022} lokasmiṃ pajjotā, yehi loko pakāsati {note:pabhāsati (ka. sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Bhagavantaṃ {note:bhavantaṃ (ka.)} puṭṭhumāgamma, kathaṃ jānemu taṃ maya’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cattāro {pb:V:1.0018} loke pajjotā, pañcamettha na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Divā tapati ādicco, rattimābhāti candimā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atha aggi divārattiṃ, tattha tattha pakāsati;
::

::gathalast
Sambuddho tapataṃ seṭṭho, esā ābhā anuttarā’’ti.
::

#### 7. Sarasuttaṃ

::hangnum
27\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kuto {pb:M:1.0015} sarā nivattanti, kattha vaṭṭaṃ na vattati;
::

::gathalast
Kattha nāmañca rūpañca, asesaṃ uparujjhatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yattha āpo ca pathavī, tejo vāyo na gādhati;
::

::gatha2
Ato sarā nivattanti, ettha vaṭṭaṃ na vattati;
::

::gathalast
Ettha nāmañca rūpañca, asesaṃ uparujjhatī’’ti.
::

#### 8. Mahaddhanasuttaṃ

::hangnum
28\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahaddhanā mahābhogā, raṭṭhavantopi khattiyā;
::

::gathalast
Aññamaññābhigijjhanti, kāmesu analaṅkatā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tesu ussukkajātesu, bhavasotānusārisu;
::

::gathalast
Kedha taṇhaṃ {note:rodhataṇhaṃ (syā. kaṃ.), gedhataṇhaṃ (ka.)} pajahiṃsu {note:pavāhiṃsu (syā. kaṃ. ka.)}, ke lokasmiṃ anussukā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hitvā {pb:T:1.0023} agāraṃ pabbajitā, hitvā puttaṃ pasuṃ viyaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Hitvā rāgañca dosañca, avijjañca virājiya;
::

::gathalast
Khīṇāsavā arahanto, te lokasmiṃ anussukā’’ti.
::

#### 9. Catucakkasuttaṃ

::hangnum
29\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Catucakkaṃ {pb:V:1.0019}{pb:P:1.0016} navadvāraṃ, puṇṇaṃ lobhena saṃyutaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Paṅkajātaṃ mahāvīra, kathaṃ yātrā bhavissatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Chetvā naddhiṃ varattañca, icchā lobhañca pāpakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Samūlaṃ taṇhamabbuyha, evaṃ yātrā bhavissatī’’ti.
::

#### 10. Eṇijaṅghasuttaṃ

::hangnum
30\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Eṇijaṅghaṃ kisaṃ vīraṃ, appāhāraṃ alolupaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Sīhaṃ vekacaraṃ nāgaṃ, kāmesu anapekkhinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Upasaṅkamma pucchāma, kathaṃ dukkhā pamuccatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pañca {pb:M:1.0016} kāmaguṇā loke, manochaṭṭhā paveditā;
::

::gathalast
Ettha chandaṃ virājetvā, evaṃ dukkhā pamuccatī’’ti.
::

::centre
Sattivaggo tatiyo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Sattiyā phusati ceva, jaṭā manonivāraṇā;
::

::gatha2
Arahantena pajjoto, sarā mahaddhanena ca;
::

::gatha1
Catucakkena navamaṃ, eṇijaṅghena te dasāti.
::

#### 4. Satullapakāyikavaggo

#### 1. Sabbhisuttaṃ

{para:31} 31\. Evaṃ {pb:T:1.0024}{pb:V:1.0020} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Atha kho sambahulā satullapakāyikā devatāyo abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇā kevalakappaṃ jetavanaṃ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhaṃsu. Ekamantaṃ {pb:P:1.0017} ṭhitā kho ekā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbhireva samāsetha, sabbhi kubbetha {note:krubbetha (ka.)} santhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sataṃ saddhammamaññāya, seyyo hoti na pāpiyo’’ti.
::

Atha kho aparā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbhireva samāsetha, sabbhi kubbetha santhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sataṃ saddhammamaññāya, paññā labbhati {note:paññaṃ labhati (syā. kaṃ.)} nāññato’’ti.
::

Atha kho aparā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbhireva samāsetha, sabbhi kubbetha santhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sataṃ saddhammamaññāya, sokamajjhe na socatī’’ti.
::

Atha {pb:M:1.0017} kho aparā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbhireva {pb:T:1.0025} samāsetha, sabbhi kubbetha santhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sataṃ saddhammamaññāya, ñātimajjhe virocatī’’ti.
::

Atha {pb:V:1.0021} kho aparā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbhireva samāsetha, sabbhi kubbetha santhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sataṃ saddhammamaññāya, sattā gacchanti suggati’’nti.
::

Atha kho aparā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbhireva samāsetha, sabbhi kubbetha santhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sataṃ saddhammamaññāya, sattā tiṭṭhanti sātata’’nti.
::

Atha kho aparā devatā bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘kassa nu kho, bhagavā, subhāsita’’nti? Sabbāsaṃ vo subhāsitaṃ pariyāyena, api ca mamapi suṇātha –

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbhireva {pb:P:1.0018} samāsetha, sabbhi kubbetha santhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sataṃ saddhammamaññāya, sabbadukkhā pamuccatī’’ti.
::

Idamavoca bhagavā. Attamanā tā devatāyo bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaṃ katvā tatthevantaradhāyiṃsūti.

#### 2. Maccharisuttaṃ

{para:32} 32\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Atha kho sambahulā satullapakāyikā devatāyo abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇā kevalakappaṃ jetavanaṃ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhaṃsu. Ekamantaṃ ṭhitā kho ekā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ {pb:T:1.0026} gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Maccherā {pb:V:1.0022} ca pamādā ca, evaṃ dānaṃ na dīyati {note:diyyati (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Puññaṃ ākaṅkhamānena, deyyaṃ hoti vijānatā’’ti.
::

Atha {pb:M:1.0018} kho aparā devatā bhagavato santike imā gāthāyo abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Yasseva bhīto na dadāti maccharī, tadevādadato bhayaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Jighacchā ca pipāsā ca, yassa bhāyati maccharī;
::

::gathalast
Tameva bālaṃ phusati, asmiṃ loke paramhi ca.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasmā vineyya maccheraṃ, dajjā dānaṃ malābhibhū;
::

::gathalast
Puññāni paralokasmiṃ, patiṭṭhā honti pāṇina’’nti.
::

Atha kho aparā devatā bhagavato santike imā gāthāyo abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Te matesu na mīyanti, panthānaṃva sahabbajaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Appasmiṃ ye pavecchanti, esa dhammo sanantano.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Appasmeke pavecchanti, bahuneke na dicchare;
::

::gathalast
Appasmā dakkhiṇā dinnā, sahassena samaṃ mitā’’ti.
::

Atha {pb:P:1.0019} kho aparā devatā bhagavato santike imā gāthāyo abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Duddadaṃ dadamānānaṃ, dukkaraṃ kamma kubbataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Asanto nānukubbanti, sataṃ dhammo duranvayo {note:durannayo (sī.)}.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasmā {pb:T:1.0027} satañca asataṃ {note:asatañca (sī. syā. kaṃ.)}, nānā hoti ito gati;
::

::gathalast
Asanto nirayaṃ yanti, santo saggaparāyanā’’ti.
::

Atha {pb:V:1.0023} kho aparā devatā bhagavato santike etadavoca – ‘‘kassa nu kho, bhagavā, subhāsita’’nti?

‘‘Sabbāsaṃ vo subhāsitaṃ pariyāyena; api ca mamapi suṇātha –

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammaṃ care yopi samuñjakaṃ care,
::

::gatha2
Dārañca posaṃ dadamappakasmiṃ;
::

::gatha3
Sataṃ sahassānaṃ sahassayāginaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Kalampi nāgghanti tathāvidhassa te’’ti.
::

Atha {pb:M:1.0019} kho aparā devatā bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kenesa yañño vipulo mahaggato,
::

::gatha2
Samena dinnassa na agghameti;
::

::gatha3
Kathaṃ {note:idaṃ padaṃ katthaci sīhaḷapotthake natthi} sataṃ sahassānaṃ sahassayāginaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Kalampi nāgghanti tathāvidhassa te’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dadanti heke visame niviṭṭhā,
::

::gatha2
Chetvā vadhitvā atha socayitvā;
::

::gatha3
Sā {pb:T:1.0028} dakkhiṇā assumukhā sadaṇḍā,
::

::gathalast
Samena dinnassa na agghameti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ sataṃ sahassānaṃ sahassayāginaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kalampi nāgghanti tathāvidhassa te’’ti.
::

#### 3. Sādhusuttaṃ

{para:33} 33\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:P:1.0020}. Atha kho sambahulā satullapakāyikā devatāyo abhikkantāya rattiyā {pb:V:1.0024} abhikkantavaṇṇā kevalakappaṃ jetavanaṃ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhaṃsu. Ekamantaṃ ṭhitā kho ekā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ udānaṃ udānesi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sādhu kho, mārisa, dānaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Maccherā ca pamādā ca, evaṃ dānaṃ na dīyati;
::

::gathalast
Puññaṃ ākaṅkhamānena, deyyaṃ hoti vijānatā’’ti.
::

Atha kho aparā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ udānaṃ udānesi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sādhu kho, mārisa, dānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Api ca appakasmimpi sāhu dānaṃ’’.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Appasmeke pavecchanti, bahuneke na dicchare;
::

::gathalast
Appasmā dakkhiṇā dinnā, sahassena samaṃ mitā’’ti.
::

Atha {pb:M:1.0020} kho aparā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ udānaṃ udānesi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sādhu kho, mārisa, dānaṃ; appakasmimpi sāhu dānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Api ca saddhāyapi sāhu dānaṃ’’.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dānañca yuddhañca samānamāhu,
::

::gatha2
Appāpi santā bahuke jinanti;
::

::gatha3
Appampi ce saddahāno dadāti,
::

::gathalast
Teneva so hoti sukhī paratthā’’ti.
::

Atha {pb:T:1.0029} kho aparā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ udānaṃ udānesi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sādhu {pb:V:1.0025} kho, mārisa, dānaṃ; appakasmimpi sāhu dānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saddhāyapi {pb:P:1.0021} sāhu dānaṃ; api ca dhammaladdhassāpi sāhu dānaṃ’’.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo dhammaladdhassa dadāti dānaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Uṭṭhānavīriyādhigatassa jantu;
::

::gatha3
Atikkamma so vetaraṇiṃ yamassa,
::

::gathalast
Dibbāni ṭhānāni upeti macco’’ti.
::

Atha kho aparā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ udānaṃ udānesi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sādhu kho, mārisa, dānaṃ; appakasmimpi sāhu dānaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Saddhāyapi sāhu dānaṃ; dhammaladdhassāpi sāhu dānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Api {pb:T:1.0030} ca viceyya dānampi sāhu dānaṃ’’.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Viceyya dānaṃ sugatappasatthaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Ye dakkhiṇeyyā idha jīvaloke;
::

::gatha3
Etesu dinnāni mahapphalāni,
::

::gathalast
Bījāni vuttāni yathā sukhette’’ti.
::

Atha kho aparā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ udānaṃ udānesi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sādhu kho, mārisa, dānaṃ; appakasmimpi sāhu dānaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Saddhāyapi sāhu dānaṃ; dhammaladdhassāpi sāhu dānaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Viceyya dānampi sāhu dānaṃ; api ca pāṇesupi sādhu saṃyamo’’.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo {pb:M:1.0021} pāṇabhūtāni {note:pāṇabhūtesu (sī. pī.)} aheṭhayaṃ caraṃ,
::

::gatha2
Parūpavādā na karonti pāpaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Bhīruṃ {pb:V:1.0026} pasaṃsanti na hi tattha sūraṃ,
::

::gathalast
Bhayā hi santo na karonti pāpa’’nti.
::

Atha kho aparā devatā bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘kassa {pb:P:1.0022} nu kho, bhagavā, subhāsita’’nti?

‘‘Sabbāsaṃ vo subhāsitaṃ pariyāyena, api ca mamapi suṇātha –

::gatha1
‘‘Saddhā hi dānaṃ bahudhā pasatthaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Dānā ca kho dhammapadaṃva seyyo;
::

::gatha3
Pubbe {pb:T:1.0031} ca hi pubbatare ca santo,
::

::gathalast
Nibbānamevajjhagamuṃ sapaññā’’ti.
::

#### 4. Nasantisuttaṃ

{para:34} 34\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Atha kho sambahulā satullapakāyikā devatāyo abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇā kevalakappaṃ jetavanaṃ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhaṃsu. Ekamantaṃ ṭhitā kho ekā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Na santi kāmā manujesu niccā,
::

::gatha2
Santīdha kamanīyāni yesu {note:kāmesu (ka.)} baddho;
::

::gatha3
Yesu pamatto apunāgamanaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Anāgantā puriso maccudheyyā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Chandajaṃ aghaṃ chandajaṃ dukkhaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Chandavinayā aghavinayo;
::

::gathalast
Aghavinayā dukkhavinayo’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:V:1.0027} te kāmā yāni citrāni loke,
::

::gatha2
Saṅkapparāgo {pb:T:1.0032} purisassa kāmo;
::

::gatha3
Tiṭṭhanti citrāni tatheva loke,
::

::gathalast
Athettha dhīrā vinayanti chandaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kodhaṃ {pb:M:1.0022}{pb:P:1.0023} jahe vippajaheyya mānaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Saṃyojanaṃ sabbamatikkameyya;
::

::gatha3
Taṃ nāmarūpasmimasajjamānaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Akiñcanaṃ nānupatanti dukkhā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pahāsi saṅkhaṃ na vimānamajjhagā {note:na ca mānamajjhagā (ka. sī.), na vimānamāgā (syā. kaṃ.)},
::

::gatha2
Acchecchi taṇhaṃ idha nāmarūpe;
::

::gatha3
Taṃ chinnaganthaṃ anighaṃ nirāsaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Pariyesamānā nājjhagamuṃ;
::

::gatha3
Devā manussā idha vā huraṃ vā,
::

::gathalast
Saggesu vā sabbanivesanesū’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ ce hi nāddakkhuṃ tathāvimuttaṃ (iccāyasmā mogharājā),
::

::gatha2
Devā manussā idha vā huraṃ vā;
::

::gatha3
Naruttamaṃ atthacaraṃ narānaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Ye taṃ namassanti pasaṃsiyā te’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pasaṃsiyā tepi bhavanti bhikkhū (mogharājāti bhagavā),
::

::gatha2
Ye taṃ namassanti tathāvimuttaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Aññāya {pb:T:1.0033} dhammaṃ vicikicchaṃ pahāya,
::

::gathalast
Saṅgātigā tepi bhavanti bhikkhū’’ti.
::

#### 5. Ujjhānasaññisuttaṃ

{para:35} 35\. Ekaṃ {pb:V:1.0028} samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Atha kho sambahulā ujjhānasaññikā devatāyo abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇā kevalakappaṃ jetavanaṃ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā vehāsaṃ aṭṭhaṃsu. Vehāsaṃ {pb:P:1.0024} ṭhitā kho ekā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Aññathā santamattānaṃ, aññathā yo pavedaye;
::

::gathalast
Nikacca kitavasseva, bhuttaṃ theyyena tassa taṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yañhi kayirā tañhi vade, yaṃ na kayirā na taṃ vade;
::

::gathalast
Akarontaṃ bhāsamānānaṃ, parijānanti paṇḍitā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na yidaṃ bhāsitamattena, ekantasavanena vā;
::

::gatha2
Anukkamitave sakkā, yāyaṃ paṭipadā daḷhā;
::

::gathalast
Yāya dhīrā pamuccanti, jhāyino mārabandhanā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:M:1.0023} ve dhīrā pakubbanti, viditvā lokapariyāyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Aññāya nibbutā dhīrā, tiṇṇā loke visattika’’nti.
::

Atha {pb:T:1.0034} kho tā devatāyo pathaviyaṃ patiṭṭhahitvā bhagavato pādesu sirasā nipatitvā bhagavantaṃ etadavocuṃ – ‘‘accayo no, bhante, accagamā yathābālaṃ yathāmūḷhaṃ yathāakusalaṃ {note:yathābālā yathāmūḷhā yathāakusalā (sabbattha)}, yā mayaṃ bhagavantaṃ āsādetabbaṃ amaññimhā. Tāsaṃ no, bhante, bhagavā accayaṃ accayato paṭiggaṇhātu āyatiṃ saṃvarāyā’’ti. Atha kho bhagavā sitaṃ pātvākāsi. Atha kho tā devatāyo bhiyyosomattāya ujjhāyantiyo vehāsaṃ abbhuggañchuṃ. Ekā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Accayaṃ {pb:V:1.0029} desayantīnaṃ, yo ce na paṭigaṇhati;
::

::gathalast
Kopantaro dosagaru, sa veraṃ paṭimuñcatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Accayo ce na vijjetha, nocidhāpagataṃ {note:nocīdha apahataṃ (syā. kaṃ.), nocidhāpakataṃ (?)} siyā;
::

::gathalast
Verāni na ca sammeyyuṃ, kenīdha {note:verāni ca sammeyyuṃ, tenidha (sī.)} kusalo siyā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kassaccayā na vijjanti, kassa natthi apāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ko na sammohamāpādi, ko ca dhīro {note:kodha dhīro (syā. kaṃ.)} sadā sato’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tathāgatassa {pb:P:1.0025} buddhassa, sabbabhūtānukampino;
::

::gatha2
Tassaccayā na vijjanti, tassa natthi apāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
So na sammohamāpādi, sova {note:sodha (syā. kaṃ.)} dhīro sadā sato’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Accayaṃ desayantīnaṃ, yo ce na paṭigaṇhati;
::

::gatha2
Kopantaro {pb:T:1.0035} dosagaru, sa veraṃ paṭimuñcati;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ veraṃ nābhinandāmi, paṭiggaṇhāmi voccaya’’nti.
::

#### 6. Saddhāsuttaṃ

{para:36} 36\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Atha kho sambahulā satullapakāyikā devatāyo abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇā kevalakappaṃ jetavanaṃ {pb:M:1.0024} obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhaṃsu. Ekamantaṃ ṭhitā kho ekā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Saddhā dutiyā purisassa hoti,
::

::gatha2
No ce assaddhiyaṃ avatiṭṭhati;
::

::gatha3
Yaso {pb:V:1.0030} ca kittī ca tatvassa hoti,
::

::gathalast
Saggañca so gacchati sarīraṃ vihāyā’’ti.
::

Atha kho aparā devatā bhagavato santike imā gāthāyo abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kodhaṃ jahe vippajaheyya mānaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Saṃyojanaṃ sabbamatikkameyya;
::

::gatha3
Taṃ nāmarūpasmimasajjamānaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Akiñcanaṃ nānupatanti saṅgā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pamādamanuyuñjanti{pb:T:1.0036}, bālā dummedhino janā;
::

::gathalast
Appamādañca medhāvī, dhanaṃ seṭṭhaṃva rakkhati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mā pamādamanuyuñjetha, mā kāmarati santhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Appamatto hi jhāyanto, pappoti paramaṃ sukha’’nti.
::

#### 7. Samayasuttaṃ

{para:37} 37\. Evaṃ {pb:P:1.0026} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sakkesu viharati kapilavatthusmiṃ mahāvane mahatā bhikkhusaṅghena saddhiṃ pañcamattehi bhikkhusatehi sabbeheva arahantehi; dasahi ca lokadhātūhi devatā yebhuyyena sannipatitā honti bhagavantaṃ dassanāya bhikkhusaṅghañca. Atha kho catunnaṃ suddhāvāsakāyikānaṃ devatānaṃ etadahosi – ‘‘ayaṃ kho bhagavā sakkesu viharati kapilavatthusmiṃ mahāvane mahatā bhikkhusaṅghena saddhiṃ pañcamattehi bhikkhusatehi sabbeheva arahantehi; dasahi ca lokadhātūhi devatā yebhuyyena sannipatitā honti bhagavantaṃ dassanāya bhikkhusaṅghañca. Yaṃnūna mayampi yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkameyyāma; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavato santike paccekaṃ gāthaṃ {note:paccekagāthaṃ (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} bhāseyyāmā’’ti.

Atha {pb:M:1.0025} kho tā devatā – seyyathāpi nāma balavā puriso samiñjitaṃ vā bāhaṃ pasāreyya pasāritaṃ {pb:V:1.0031} vā bāhaṃ samiñjeyya. Evameva – suddhāvāsesu devesu antarahitā bhagavato purato pāturahesuṃ. Atha kho tā devatā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhaṃsu. Ekamantaṃ ṭhitā kho ekā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ {pb:T:1.0037} gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Mahāsamayo pavanasmiṃ, devakāyā samāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Āgatamha imaṃ dhammasamayaṃ, dakkhitāye aparājitasaṅgha’’nti.
::

Atha kho aparā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Tatra bhikkhavo samādahaṃsu, cittamattano ujukaṃ akaṃsu {note:ujukamakaṃsu (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Sārathīva nettāni gahetvā, indriyāni rakkhanti paṇḍitā’’ti.
::

Atha {pb:P:1.0027} kho aparā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Chetvā khīlaṃ chetvā palighaṃ, indakhīlaṃ ūhacca manejā;
::

::gathalast
Te caranti suddhā vimalā, cakkhumatā sudantā susunāgā’’ti.
::

Atha kho aparā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Ye keci buddhaṃ saraṇaṃ gatāse, na te gamissanti apāyabhūmiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pahāya mānusaṃ dehaṃ, devakāyaṃ paripūressantī’’ti.
::

#### 8. Sakalikasuttaṃ

{para:38} 38\. Evaṃ me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati maddakucchismiṃ {pb:T:1.0038} migadāye. Tena kho pana samayena bhagavato pādo sakalikāya {note:sakkhalikāya (ka.)} khato hoti. Bhusā sudaṃ bhagavato vedanā vattanti sārīrikā vedanā dukkhā tibbā {note:tippā (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} kharā kaṭukā asātā amanāpā; tā sudaṃ bhagavā sato sampajāno {pb:V:1.0032} adhivāseti avihaññamāno. Atha kho bhagavā catugguṇaṃ saṅghāṭiṃ paññāpetvā dakkhiṇena passena sīhaseyyaṃ kappeti pāde pādaṃ accādhāya sato sampajāno.

Atha {pb:M:1.0026} kho sattasatā satullapakāyikā devatāyo abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇā kevalakappaṃ maddakucchiṃ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhaṃsu. Ekamantaṃ ṭhitā kho ekā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ udānaṃ udānesi – ‘‘nāgo {pb:P:1.0028} vata, bho, samaṇo gotamo; nāgavatā ca samuppannā sārīrikā vedanā dukkhā tibbā kharā kaṭukā asātā amanāpā sato sampajāno adhivāseti avihaññamāno’’ti.

Atha kho aparā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ udānaṃ udānesi – ‘‘sīho vata, bho, samaṇo gotamo; sīhavatā ca samuppannā sārīrikā vedanā dukkhā tibbā kharā kaṭukā asātā amanāpā sato sampajāno adhivāseti avihaññamāno’’ti.

Atha {pb:T:1.0039} kho aparā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ udānaṃ udānesi – ‘‘ājānīyo vata, bho, samaṇo gotamo; ājānīyavatā ca samuppannā sārīrikā vedanā dukkhā tibbā kharā kaṭukā asātā amanāpā sato sampajāno adhivāseti avihaññamāno’’ti.

Atha kho aparā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ udānaṃ udānesi – ‘‘nisabho vata, bho, samaṇo gotamo; nisabhavatā ca samuppannā sārīrikā vedanā dukkhā tibbā kharā kaṭukā asātā amanāpā sato sampajāno adhivāseti avihaññamāno’’ti.

Atha kho aparā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ udānaṃ udānesi – ‘‘dhorayho vata, bho, samaṇo gotamo; dhorayhavatā ca samuppannā sārīrikā vedanā dukkhā tibbā kharā kaṭukā asātā amanāpā sato sampajāno adhivāseti avihaññamāno’’ti.

Atha kho aparā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ udānaṃ udānesi – ‘‘danto vata, bho, samaṇo {pb:V:1.0033} gotamo; dantavatā ca samuppannā sārīrikā vedanā dukkhā tibbā kharā kaṭukā asātā amanāpā sato sampajāno adhivāseti avihaññamāno’’ti.

Atha kho aparā devatā bhagavato santike imaṃ udānaṃ udānesi – ‘‘passa samādhiṃ subhāvitaṃ cittañca suvimuttaṃ, na cābhinataṃ na {pb:T:1.0040} cāpanataṃ na {pb:M:1.0027} ca sasaṅkhāraniggayhavāritagataṃ {note:sasaṅkhāraniggayhavāritavataṃ (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.), sasaṅkhāraniggayhavārivāvataṃ (ka.)}. Yo evarūpaṃ purisanāgaṃ purisasīhaṃ purisaājānīyaṃ {pb:P:1.0029} purisanisabhaṃ purisadhorayhaṃ purisadantaṃ atikkamitabbaṃ maññeyya kimaññatra adassanā’’ti.

::gatha1
‘‘Pañcavedā sataṃ samaṃ, tapassī brāhmaṇā caraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Cittañca nesaṃ na sammā vimuttaṃ, hīnattharūpā na pāraṅgamā te.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṇhādhipannā vatasīlabaddhā, lūkhaṃ tapaṃ vassasataṃ carantā;
::

::gathalast
Cittañca nesaṃ na sammā vimuttaṃ, hīnattharūpā na pāraṅgamā te.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na mānakāmassa damo idhatthi, na monamatthi asamāhitassa;
::

::gathalast
Eko araññe viharaṃ pamatto, na maccudheyyassa tareyya pāra’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mānaṃ pahāya susamāhitatto, sucetaso sabbadhi vippamutto;
::

::gathalast
Eko araññe viharamappamatto, sa maccudheyyassa tareyya pāra’’nti.
::

#### 9. Paṭhamapajjunnadhītusuttaṃ

{para:39} 39\. Evaṃ {pb:T:1.0041} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā vesāliyaṃ viharati mahāvane kūṭāgārasālāyaṃ. Atha kho kokanadā pajjunnassa dhītā abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇā kevalakappaṃ mahāvanaṃ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṃ ṭhitā kho sā devatā kokanadā pajjunnassa dhītā bhagavato santike imā gāthāyo abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Vesāliyaṃ {pb:V:1.0034} vane viharantaṃ, aggaṃ sattassa sambuddhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kokanadāhamasmi {pb:P:1.0030} abhivande, kokanadā pajjunnassa dhītā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sutameva pure āsi, dhammo cakkhumatānubuddho;
::

::gathalast
Sāhaṃ dāni sakkhi jānāmi, munino desayato sugatassa.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye keci ariyaṃ dhammaṃ, vigarahantā caranti dummedhā;
::

::gathalast
Upenti roruvaṃ ghoraṃ, cirarattaṃ dukkhaṃ anubhavanti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye ca kho ariye dhamme, khantiyā upasamena upetā;
::

::gathalast
Pahāya mānusaṃ dehaṃ, devakāya paripūressantī’’ti.
::

#### 10. Dutiyapajjunnadhītusuttaṃ

{para:40} 40\. Evaṃ {pb:M:1.0028} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā vesāliyaṃ viharati mahāvane kūṭāgārasālāyaṃ. Atha kho cūḷakokanadā {note:cullakokanadā (sī. syā. kaṃ.)} pajjunnassa dhītā {pb:T:1.0042} abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇā kevalakappaṃ mahāvanaṃ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṃ ṭhitā kho sā devatā cūḷakokanadā pajjunnassa dhītā bhagavato santike imā gāthāyo abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Idhāgamā vijjupabhāsavaṇṇā, kokanadā pajjunnassa dhītā;
::

::gathalast
Buddhañca dhammañca namassamānā, gāthācimā atthavatī abhāsi.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bahunāpi {pb:P:1.0031} kho taṃ vibhajeyyaṃ, pariyāyena tādiso dhammo;
::

::gathalast
Saṃkhittamatthaṃ {note:saṃkhittamattaṃ (ka.)} lapayissāmi, yāvatā me manasā pariyattaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāpaṃ na kayirā vacasā manasā,
::

::gatha2
Kāyena vā kiñcana sabbaloke;
::

::gatha3
Kāme {pb:V:1.0035} pahāya satimā sampajāno,
::

::gathalast
Dukkhaṃ na sevetha anatthasaṃhita’’nti.
::

::centre
Satullapakāyikavaggo catuttho.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Sabbhimaccharinā sādhu, na santujjhānasaññino;
::

::gathalast
Saddhā samayo sakalikaṃ, ubho pajjunnadhītaroti.
::

#### 5. Ādittavaggo

#### 1. Ādittasuttaṃ

{para:41} 41\. Evaṃ {pb:T:1.0043} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Atha kho aññatarā devatā abhikkantāya {pb:M:1.0029} rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇā kevalakappaṃ jetavanaṃ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṃ ṭhitā kho sā devatā bhagavato santike imā gāthāyo abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Ādittasmiṃ agārasmiṃ, yaṃ nīharati bhājanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ tassa hoti atthāya, no ca yaṃ tattha ḍayhati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ ādittako loko, jarāya maraṇena ca;
::

::gathalast
Nīharetheva dānena, dinnaṃ hoti sunīhataṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dinnaṃ {pb:V:1.0036}{pb:P:1.0032} sukhaphalaṃ hoti, nādinnaṃ hoti taṃ tathā;
::

::gathalast
Corā haranti rājāno, aggi ḍahati nassati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atha {pb:T:1.0044} antena jahati, sarīraṃ sapariggahaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Etadaññāya medhāvī, bhuñjetha ca dadetha ca;
::

::gatha3
Datvā ca bhutvā ca yathānubhāvaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anindito saggamupeti ṭhāna’’nti.
::

#### 2. Kiṃdadasuttaṃ

::hangnum
42\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃdado balado hoti, kiṃdado hoti vaṇṇado;
::

::gatha2
Kiṃdado sukhado hoti, kiṃdado hoti cakkhudo;
::

::gathalast
Ko ca sabbadado hoti, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Annado balado hoti, vatthado hoti vaṇṇado;
::

::gathalast
Yānado sukhado hoti, dīpado hoti cakkhudo.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So ca sabbadado hoti, yo dadāti upassayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Amataṃ dado ca so hoti, yo dhammamanusāsatī’’ti.
::

#### 3. Annasuttaṃ

::hangnum
43\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Annamevābhinandanti, ubhaye devamānusā;
::

::gathalast
Atha ko nāma so yakkho, yaṃ annaṃ nābhinandatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye {pb:M:1.0030} naṃ dadanti saddhāya, vippasannena cetasā;
::

::gathalast
Tameva annaṃ bhajati, asmiṃ loke paramhi ca.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasmā {pb:T:1.0045}{pb:V:1.0037} vineyya maccheraṃ, dajjā dānaṃ malābhibhū;
::

::gathalast
Puññāni paralokasmiṃ, patiṭṭhā honti pāṇina’’nti.
::

#### 4. Ekamūlasuttaṃ

::hangnum
44\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ekamūlaṃ dvirāvaṭṭaṃ, timalaṃ pañcapattharaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Samuddaṃ dvādasāvaṭṭaṃ, pātālaṃ atarī isī’’ti.
::

#### 5. Anomasuttaṃ

::hangnum
45\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anomanāmaṃ {pb:P:1.0033} nipuṇatthadassiṃ, paññādadaṃ kāmālaye asattaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ passatha sabbaviduṃ sumedhaṃ, ariye pathe kamamānaṃ mahesi’’nti.
::

#### 6. Accharāsuttaṃ

::hangnum
46\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Accharāgaṇasaṅghuṭṭhaṃ, pisācagaṇasevitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vanantaṃ mohanaṃ nāma, kathaṃ yātrā bhavissatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ujuko nāma so maggo, abhayā nāma sā disā;
::

::gathalast
Ratho akūjano nāma, dhammacakkehi saṃyuto.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hirī tassa apālambo, satyassa parivāraṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Dhammāhaṃ sārathiṃ brūmi, sammādiṭṭhipurejavaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yassa etādisaṃ yānaṃ, itthiyā purisassa vā;
::

::gathalast
Sa ve etena yānena, nibbānasseva santike’’ti.
::

#### 7. Vanaropasuttaṃ

::hangnum
47\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kesaṃ {pb:T:1.0046}{pb:V:1.0038} divā ca ratto ca, sadā puññaṃ pavaḍḍhati;
::

::gathalast
Dhammaṭṭhā sīlasampannā, ke janā saggagāmino’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ārāmaropā vanaropā, ye janā setukārakā;
::

::gathalast
Papañca udapānañca, ye dadanti upassayaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tesaṃ {pb:M:1.0031} divā ca ratto ca, sadā puññaṃ pavaḍḍhati;
::

::gathalast
Dhammaṭṭhā sīlasampannā, te janā saggagāmino’’ti.
::

#### 8. Jetavanasuttaṃ

::hangnum
48\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idañhi taṃ jetavanaṃ, isisaṅghanisevitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Āvutthaṃ {note:āvuṭṭhaṃ (ka.)} dhammarājena, pītisañjananaṃ mama.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kammaṃ {pb:P:1.0034} vijjā ca dhammo ca, sīlaṃ jīvitamuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Etena maccā sujjhanti, na gottena dhanena vā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasmā hi paṇḍito poso, sampassaṃ atthamattano;
::

::gathalast
Yoniso vicine dhammaṃ, evaṃ tattha visujjhati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāriputtova paññāya, sīlena upasamena ca;
::

::gathalast
Yopi pāraṅgato bhikkhu, etāvaparamo siyā’’ti.
::

#### 9. Maccharisuttaṃ

::hangnum
49\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yedha {pb:V:1.0039} maccharino loke, kadariyā paribhāsakā;
::

::gathalast
Aññesaṃ dadamānānaṃ, antarāyakarā narā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kīdiso {pb:T:1.0047} tesaṃ vipāko, samparāyo ca kīdiso;
::

::gathalast
Bhagavantaṃ puṭṭhumāgamma, kathaṃ jānemu taṃ maya’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yedha maccharino loke, kadariyā paribhāsakā;
::

::gathalast
Aññesaṃ dadamānānaṃ, antarāyakarā narā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nirayaṃ tiracchānayoniṃ, yamalokaṃ upapajjare;
::

::gathalast
Sace enti manussattaṃ, dalidde jāyare kule.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Coḷaṃ piṇḍo ratī khiḍḍā, yattha kicchena labbhati;
::

::gatha2
Parato āsīsare {note:āsiṃsare (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} bālā, tampi tesaṃ na labbhati;
::

::gathalast
Diṭṭhe dhammesa vipāko, samparāye {note:samparāyo (syā. kaṃ. pī.)} ca duggatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Itihetaṃ vijānāma, aññaṃ pucchāma gotama;
::

::gathalast
Yedha laddhā manussattaṃ, vadaññū vītamaccharā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddhe {pb:M:1.0032} pasannā dhamme ca, saṅghe ca tibbagāravā;
::

::gatha2
Kīdiso tesaṃ vipāko, samparāyo ca kīdiso;
::

::gathalast
Bhagavantaṃ puṭṭhumāgamma, kathaṃ jānemu taṃ maya’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yedha laddhā manussattaṃ, vadaññū vītamaccharā;
::

::gatha2
Buddhe pasannā dhamme ca, saṅghe ca tibbagāravā;
::

::gathalast
Ete saggā {note:sagge (sī. syā. kaṃ.)} pakāsanti, yattha te upapajjare.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace {pb:V:1.0040}{pb:P:1.0035} enti manussattaṃ, aḍḍhe ājāyare kule;
::

::gathalast
Coḷaṃ piṇḍo ratī khiḍḍā, yatthākicchena labbhati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Parasambhatesu {pb:T:1.0048} bhogesu, vasavattīva modare;
::

::gathalast
Diṭṭhe dhammesa vipāko, samparāye ca suggatī’’ti.
::

#### 10. Ghaṭīkārasuttaṃ

::hangnum
50\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Avihaṃ upapannāse, vimuttā satta bhikkhavo;
::

::gathalast
Rāgadosaparikkhīṇā, tiṇṇā loke visattika’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ke ca te ataruṃ paṅkaṃ {note:saṅgaṃ (sī. syā.)}, maccudheyyaṃ suduttaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ke hitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, dibbayogaṃ upaccagu’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upako palagaṇḍo ca, pukkusāti ca te tayo;
::

::gatha2
Bhaddiyo khaṇḍadevo ca, bāhuraggi ca siṅgiyo {note:bahudantī ca piṅgayo (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Te hitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, dibbayogaṃ upaccagu’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kusalī bhāsasī tesaṃ, mārapāsappahāyinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kassa te dhammamaññāya, acchiduṃ bhavabandhana’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na aññatra bhagavatā, nāññatra tava sāsanā;
::

::gathalast
Yassa te dhammamaññāya, acchiduṃ bhavabandhanaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yattha nāmañca rūpañca, asesaṃ uparujjhati;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ te dhammaṃ idhaññāya, acchiduṃ bhavabandhana’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gambhīraṃ {pb:V:1.0041} bhāsasī vācaṃ, dubbijānaṃ sudubbudhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kassa tvaṃ {pb:T:1.0049} dhammamaññāya, vācaṃ bhāsasi īdisa’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kumbhakāro {pb:M:1.0033} pure āsiṃ, vekaḷiṅge {note:vehaḷiṅge (sī.), vebhaḷiṅge (syā. kaṃ.)} ghaṭīkaro;
::

::gathalast
Mātāpettibharo āsiṃ, kassapassa upāsako.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Virato {pb:P:1.0036} methunā dhammā, brahmacārī nirāmiso;
::

::gathalast
Ahuvā te sagāmeyyo, ahuvā te pure sakhā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sohamete pajānāmi, vimutte satta bhikkhavo;
::

::gathalast
Rāgadosaparikkhīṇe, tiṇṇe loke visattika’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evametaṃ tadā āsi, yathā bhāsasi bhaggava;
::

::gatha2
Kumbhakāro pure āsi, vekaḷiṅge ghaṭīkaro;
::

::gathalast
Mātāpettibharo āsi, kassapassa upāsako.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Virato methunā dhammā, brahmacārī nirāmiso;
::

::gathalast
Ahuvā me sagāmeyyo, ahuvā me pure sakhā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evametaṃ purāṇānaṃ, sahāyānaṃ ahu saṅgamo;
::

::gathalast
Ubhinnaṃ bhāvitattānaṃ, sarīrantimadhārina’’nti.
::

::centre
Ādittavaggo pañcamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Ādittaṃ kiṃdadaṃ annaṃ, ekamūlaanomiyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Accharāvanaropajetaṃ, maccharena ghaṭīkaroti.
::

#### 6. Jarāvaggo

#### 1. Jarāsuttaṃ

::hangnum
51\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsu {pb:T:1.0050}{pb:V:1.0042} yāva jarā sādhu, kiṃsu sādhu patiṭṭhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃsu narānaṃ ratanaṃ, kiṃsu corehi dūhara’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sīlaṃ yāva jarā sādhu, saddhā sādhu patiṭṭhitā;
::

::gathalast
Paññā narānaṃ ratanaṃ, puññaṃ corehi dūhara’’nti.
::

#### 2. Ajarasāsuttaṃ

::hangnum
52\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsu {pb:M:1.0034} ajarasā sādhu, kiṃsu sādhu adhiṭṭhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃsu narānaṃ ratanaṃ, kiṃsu corehyahāriya’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sīlaṃ {pb:P:1.0037} ajarasā sādhu, saddhā sādhu adhiṭṭhitā;
::

::gathalast
Paññā narānaṃ ratanaṃ, puññaṃ corehyahāriya’’nti.
::

#### 3. Mittasuttaṃ

::hangnum
53\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsu pavasato {note:pathavato (pī. ka.)} mittaṃ, kiṃsu mittaṃ sake ghare;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ mittaṃ atthajātassa, kiṃ mittaṃ samparāyika’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sattho pavasato mittaṃ, mātā mittaṃ sake ghare;
::

::gatha2
Sahāyo {pb:T:1.0051} atthajātassa, hoti mittaṃ punappunaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sayaṃkatāni puññāni, taṃ mittaṃ samparāyika’’nti.
::

#### 4. Vatthusuttaṃ

::hangnum
54\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsu {pb:V:1.0043} vatthu manussānaṃ, kiṃsūdha paramo sakhā;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃsu bhūtā upajīvanti, ye pāṇā pathavissitā’’ti {note:pathaviṃ sitāti (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)}.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Puttā vatthu manussānaṃ, bhariyā ca {note:bhariyāva (sī.), bhariyā (syā. kaṃ.)} paramo sakhā;
::

::gathalast
Vuṭṭhiṃ bhūtā upajīvanti, ye pāṇā pathavissitā’’ti.
::

#### 5. Paṭhamajanasuttaṃ

::hangnum
55\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsu janeti purisaṃ, kiṃsu tassa vidhāvati;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃsu saṃsāramāpādi, kiṃsu tassa mahabbhaya’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṇhā janeti purisaṃ, cittamassa vidhāvati;
::

::gathalast
Satto saṃsāramāpādi, dukkhamassa mahabbhaya’’nti.
::

#### 6. Dutiyajanasuttaṃ

::hangnum
56\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsu {pb:M:1.0035} janeti purisaṃ, kiṃsu tassa vidhāvati;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃsu saṃsāramāpādi, kismā na parimuccatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṇhā janeti purisaṃ, cittamassa vidhāvati;
::

::gathalast
Satto saṃsāramāpādi, dukkhā na parimuccatī’’ti.
::

#### 7. Tatiyajanasuttaṃ

::hangnum
57\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsu {pb:P:1.0038} janeti purisaṃ, kiṃsu tassa vidhāvati;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃsu saṃsāramāpādi, kiṃsu tassa parāyana’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṇhā {pb:T:1.0052}{pb:V:1.0044} janeti purisaṃ, cittamassa vidhāvati;
::

::gathalast
Satto saṃsāramāpādi, kammaṃ tassa parāyana’’nti.
::

#### 8. Uppathasuttaṃ

::hangnum
58\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsu uppatho akkhāto, kiṃsu rattindivakkhayo;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ malaṃ brahmacariyassa, kiṃ sinānamanodaka’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rāgo uppatho akkhāto, vayo rattindivakkhayo;
::

::gatha2
Itthī malaṃ brahmacariyassa, etthāyaṃ sajjate pajā;
::

::gathalast
Tapo ca brahmacariyañca, taṃ sinānamanodaka’’nti.
::

#### 9. Dutiyasuttaṃ

::hangnum
59\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsu dutiyā {note:dutiyaṃ (syā. kaṃ. pī.)} purisassa hoti, kiṃsu cenaṃ pasāsati;
::

::gathalast
Kissa cābhirato macco, sabbadukkhā pamuccatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saddhā dutiyā purisassa hoti, paññā cenaṃ pasāsati;
::

::gathalast
Nibbānābhirato macco, sabbadukkhā pamuccatī’’ti.
::

#### 10. Kavisuttaṃ

::hangnum
60\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsu nidānaṃ gāthānaṃ, kiṃsu tāsaṃ viyañjanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃsu sannissitā gāthā, kiṃsu gāthānamāsayo’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Chando {pb:M:1.0036} nidānaṃ gāthānaṃ, akkharā tāsaṃ viyañjanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nāmasannissitā gāthā, kavi gāthānamāsayo’’ti.
::

::centre
Jarāvaggo chaṭṭho.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Jarā {pb:T:1.0053}{pb:V:1.0045} ajarasā mittaṃ, vatthu tīṇi janāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Uppatho ca dutiyo ca, kavinā pūrito vaggoti.
::

#### 7. Addhavaggo

#### 1. Nāmasuttaṃ

::hangnum
61\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsu {pb:T:1.0054}{pb:P:1.0039} sabbaṃ addhabhavi {note:anvabhavi (sī.)}, kismā bhiyyo na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Kissassu ekadhammassa, sabbeva vasamanvagū’’ti {note:vasamaddhagū (ka.)}.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāmaṃ sabbaṃ addhabhavi, nāmā bhiyyo na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Nāmassa ekadhammassa, sabbeva vasamanvagū’’ti.
::

#### 2. Cittasuttaṃ

::hangnum
62\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kenassu nīyati loko, kenassu parikassati;
::

::gathalast
Kissassu ekadhammassa, sabbeva vasamanvagū’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cittena nīyati loko, cittena parikassati;
::

::gathalast
Cittassa ekadhammassa, sabbeva vasamanvagū’’ti.
::

#### 3. Taṇhāsuttaṃ

::hangnum
63\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kenassu nīyati loko, kenassu parikassati;
::

::gathalast
Kissassu ekadhammassa, sabbeva vasamanvagū’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṇhāya {pb:V:1.0046} nīyati loko, taṇhāya parikassati;
::

::gathalast
Taṇhāya ekadhammassa, sabbeva vasamanvagū’’ti.
::

#### 4. Saṃyojanasuttaṃ

::hangnum
64\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsu {pb:T:1.0055}{pb:M:1.0037} saṃyojano loko, kiṃsu tassa vicāraṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kissassu vippahānena, nibbānaṃ iti vuccatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nandīsaṃyojano {note:nandisaṃyojano (sī. syā. kaṃ.)} loko, vitakkassa vicāraṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṇhāya vippahānena, nibbānaṃ iti vuccatī’’ti.
::

#### 5. Bandhanasuttaṃ

::hangnum
65\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsu sambandhano loko, kiṃsu tassa vicāraṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kissassu vippahānena, sabbaṃ chindati bandhana’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nandīsambandhano {pb:P:1.0040} loko, vitakkassa vicāraṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṇhāya vippahānena, sabbaṃ chindati bandhana’’nti.
::

#### 6. Attahatasuttaṃ

::hangnum
66\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kenassubbhāhato loko, kenassu parivārito;
::

::gathalast
Kena sallena otiṇṇo, kissa dhūpāyito sadā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Maccunābbhāhato loko, jarāya parivārito;
::

::gathalast
Taṇhāsallena otiṇṇo, icchādhūpāyito sadā’’ti.
::

#### 7. Uḍḍitasuttaṃ

::hangnum
67\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kenassu {pb:V:1.0047} uḍḍito loko, kenassu parivārito;
::

::gathalast
Kenassu pihito loko, kismiṃ loko patiṭṭhito’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Taṇhāya uḍḍito loko, jarāya parivārito;
::

::gathalast
Maccunā pihito loko, dukkhe loko patiṭṭhito’’ti.
::

#### 8. Pihitasuttaṃ

::hangnum
68\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kenassu {pb:T:1.0056} pihito loko, kismiṃ loko patiṭṭhito;
::

::gathalast
Kenassu uḍḍito loko, kenassu parivārito’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Maccunā {pb:M:1.0038} pihito loko, dukkhe loko patiṭṭhito;
::

::gathalast
Taṇhāya uḍḍito loko, jarāya parivārito’’ti.
::

#### 9. Icchāsuttaṃ

::hangnum
69\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kenassu bajjhatī loko, kissa vinayāya muccati;
::

::gathalast
Kissassu vippahānena, sabbaṃ chindati bandhana’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Icchāya bajjhatī loko, icchāvinayāya muccati;
::

::gathalast
Icchāya vippahānena, sabbaṃ chindati bandhana’’nti.
::

#### 10. Lokasuttaṃ

::hangnum
70\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kismiṃ {pb:P:1.0041} loko samuppanno, kismiṃ kubbati santhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kissa loko upādāya, kismiṃ loko vihaññatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Chasu {pb:V:1.0048} loko samuppanno, chasu kubbati santhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Channameva upādāya, chasu loko vihaññatī’’ti.
::

::centre
Addhavaggo {note:anvavaggo (sī.)} sattamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Nāmaṃ cittañca taṇhā ca, saṃyojanañca bandhanā;
::

::gathalast
Abbhāhatuḍḍito pihito, icchā lokena te dasāti.
::

#### 8. Chetvāvaggo

#### 1. Chetvāsuttaṃ

{para:71} 71\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Ekamantaṃ {pb:T:1.0057} ṭhitā kho sā devatā bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsu chetvā {note:jhatvā (sī.), ghatvā (syā. kaṃ.) evamuparipi} sukhaṃ seti, kiṃsu chetvā na socati;
::

::gathalast
Kissassu ekadhammassa, vadhaṃ rocesi gotamā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kodhaṃ {pb:M:1.0039} chetvā sukhaṃ seti, kodhaṃ chetvā na socati;
::

::gatha2
Kodhassa visamūlassa, madhuraggassa devate;
::

::gathalast
Vadhaṃ ariyā pasaṃsanti, tañhi chetvā na socatī’’ti.
::

#### 2. Rathasuttaṃ

::hangnum
72\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsu rathassa paññāṇaṃ, kiṃsu paññāṇamaggino;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃsu raṭṭhassa paññāṇaṃ, kiṃsu paññāṇamitthiyā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhajo {pb:V:1.0049}{pb:P:1.0042} rathassa paññāṇaṃ, dhūmo paññāṇamaggino;
::

::gathalast
Rājā raṭṭhassa paññāṇaṃ, bhattā paññāṇamitthiyā’’ti.
::

#### 3. Vittasuttaṃ

::hangnum
73\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsūdha vittaṃ purisassa seṭṭhaṃ, kiṃsu suciṇṇo sukhamāvahati;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃsu {pb:T:1.0058} have sādutaraṃ {note:sādhutaraṃ (ka.)} rasānaṃ, kathaṃjīviṃ {note:kiṃsujīviṃ (ka.)} jīvitamāhu seṭṭha’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saddhīdha vittaṃ purisassa seṭṭhaṃ, dhammo suciṇṇo sukhamāvahati;
::

::gathalast
Saccaṃ have sādutaraṃ rasānaṃ, paññājīviṃ jīvitamāhu seṭṭha’’nti.
::

#### 4. Vuṭṭhisuttaṃ

::hangnum
74\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsu uppatataṃ seṭṭhaṃ, kiṃsu nipatataṃ varaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃsu pavajamānānaṃ, kiṃsu pavadataṃ vara’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bījaṃ uppatataṃ seṭṭhaṃ, vuṭṭhi nipatataṃ varā;
::

::gathalast
Gāvo pavajamānānaṃ, putto pavadataṃ varoti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vijjā uppatataṃ seṭṭhā, avijjā nipatataṃ varā;
::

::gathalast
Saṅgho pavajamānānaṃ, buddho pavadataṃ varo’’ti.
::

#### 5. Bhītāsuttaṃ

::hangnum
75\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsūdha bhītā janatā anekā,
::

::gatha2
Maggo canekāyatanappavutto;
::

::gatha3
Pucchāmi taṃ gotama bhūripañña,
::

::gathalast
Kismiṃ ṭhito paralokaṃ na bhāye’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vācaṃ {pb:V:1.0050}{pb:M:1.0040} manañca paṇidhāya sammā,
::

::gatha2
Kāyena {pb:T:1.0059} pāpāni akubbamāno;
::

::gatha3
Bavhannapānaṃ gharamāvasanto,
::

::gatha2
Saddho {pb:P:1.0043} mudū saṃvibhāgī vadaññū;
::

::gatha3
Etesu dhammesu ṭhito catūsu,
::

::gathalast
Dhamme ṭhito paralokaṃ na bhāye’’ti.
::

#### 6. Najīratisuttaṃ

::hangnum
76\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ jīrati kiṃ na jīrati, kiṃsu uppathoti vuccati;
::

::gatha2
Kiṃsu dhammānaṃ paripantho, kiṃsu rattindivakkhayo;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ malaṃ brahmacariyassa, kiṃ sinānamanodakaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kati lokasmiṃ chiddāni, yattha vittaṃ {note:cittaṃ (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} na tiṭṭhati;
::

::gathalast
Bhagavantaṃ puṭṭhumāgamma, kathaṃ jānemu taṃ maya’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rūpaṃ jīrati maccānaṃ, nāmagottaṃ na jīrati;
::

::gathalast
Rāgo uppathoti vuccati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Lobho dhammānaṃ paripantho, vayo rattindivakkhayo;
::

::gatha2
Itthī malaṃ brahmacariyassa, etthāyaṃ sajjate pajā;
::

::gathalast
Tapo ca brahmacariyañca, taṃ sinānamanodakaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cha lokasmiṃ chiddāni, yattha vittaṃ na tiṭṭhati;
::

::gatha2
Ālasyañca {note:ālassañca (sī. pī.)} pamādo ca, anuṭṭhānaṃ asaṃyamo;
::

::gathalast
Niddā tandī {note:tandi (sī.)} ca te chidde, sabbaso taṃ vivajjaye’’ti.
::

#### 7. Issariyasuttaṃ

::hangnum
77\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsu {pb:T:1.0060}{pb:V:1.0051} issariyaṃ loke, kiṃsu bhaṇḍānamuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃsu satthamalaṃ loke, kiṃsu lokasmimabbudaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsu harantaṃ vārenti, haranto pana ko piyo;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃsu punappunāyantaṃ, abhinandanti paṇḍitā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vaso {pb:M:1.0041} issariyaṃ loke, itthī bhaṇḍānamuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kodho satthamalaṃ loke, corā lokasmimabbudā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Coraṃ harantaṃ vārenti, haranto samaṇo piyo;
::

::gathalast
Samaṇaṃ punappunāyantaṃ, abhinandanti paṇḍitā’’ti.
::

#### 8. Kāmasuttaṃ

::hangnum
78\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kimatthakāmo {pb:P:1.0044} na dade, kiṃ macco na pariccaje;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃsu muñceyya kalyāṇaṃ, pāpikaṃ na ca mocaye’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Attānaṃ na dade poso, attānaṃ na pariccaje;
::

::gathalast
Vācaṃ muñceyya kalyāṇaṃ, pāpikañca na mocaye’’ti.
::

#### 9. Pātheyyasuttaṃ

::hangnum
79\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsu bandhati pātheyyaṃ, kiṃsu bhogānamāsayo;
::

::gatha2
Kiṃsu naraṃ parikassati, kiṃsu lokasmi dujjahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kismiṃ baddhā puthū sattā, pāsena sakuṇī yathā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saddhā {pb:T:1.0061}{pb:V:1.0052} bandhati pātheyyaṃ, sirī bhogānamāsayo;
::

::gatha2
Icchā naraṃ parikassati, icchā lokasmi dujjahā;
::

::gathalast
Icchābaddhā puthū sattā, pāsena sakuṇī yathā’’ti.
::

#### 10. Pajjotasuttaṃ

::hangnum
80\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsu lokasmi pajjoto, kiṃsu lokasmi jāgaro;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃsu kamme sajīvānaṃ, kimassa iriyāpatho.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsu alasaṃ analasañca {note:kiṃ ālasyānālasyañca (ka.)}, mātā puttaṃva posati;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ bhūtā upajīvanti, ye pāṇā pathavissitā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paññā lokasmi pajjoto, sati lokasmi jāgaro;
::

::gathalast
Gāvo kamme sajīvānaṃ, sītassa iriyāpatho.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vuṭṭhi alasaṃ analasañca, mātā puttaṃva posati;
::

::gathalast
Vuṭṭhiṃ bhūtā upajīvanti, ye pāṇā pathavissitā’’ti.
::

#### 11. Araṇasuttaṃ

::hangnum
81\.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kesūdha {pb:M:1.0042} araṇā loke, kesaṃ vusitaṃ na nassati;
::

::gathalast
Kedha icchaṃ parijānanti, kesaṃ bhojissiyaṃ sadā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsu {pb:P:1.0045} mātā pitā bhātā, vandanti naṃ patiṭṭhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃsu idha jātihīnaṃ, abhivādenti khattiyā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samaṇīdha araṇā loke, samaṇānaṃ vusitaṃ na nassati;
::

::gathalast
Samaṇā icchaṃ parijānanti, samaṇānaṃ bhojissiyaṃ sadā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Samaṇaṃ {pb:T:1.0062}{pb:V:1.0053} mātā pitā bhātā, vandanti naṃ patiṭṭhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Samaṇīdha jātihīnaṃ, abhivādenti khattiyā’’ti.
::

::centre
Chetvāvaggo aṭṭhamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Chetvā rathañca cittañca, vuṭṭhi bhītā najīrati;
::

::gathalast
Issaraṃ kāmaṃ pātheyyaṃ, pajjoto araṇena cāti.
::

::centre
Devatāsaṃyuttaṃ samattaṃ.
::

### 2. Devaputtasaṃyuttaṃ

#### 1. Paṭhamavaggo

#### 1. Paṭhamakassapasuttaṃ

{para:82} 82\. Evaṃ {pb:T:1.0063}{pb:V:1.0054}{pb:P:1.0046}{pb:M:1.0043} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Atha kho kassapo devaputto abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇo kevalakappaṃ jetavanaṃ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṃ ṭhito kho kassapo devaputto bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘bhikkhuṃ bhagavā pakāsesi, no ca bhikkhuno anusāsa’’nti. ‘‘Tena hi kassapa, taññevettha paṭibhātū’’ti.

::gatha1
‘‘Subhāsitassa sikkhetha, samaṇūpāsanassa ca;
::

::gathalast
Ekāsanassa ca raho, cittavūpasamassa cā’’ti.
::

Idamavoca kassapo devaputto; samanuñño satthā ahosi. Atha kho kassapo devaputto ‘‘samanuñño me satthā’’ti bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaṃ katvā tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 2. Dutiyakassapasuttaṃ

{para:83} 83\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Ekamantaṃ ṭhito kho kassapo devaputto bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Bhikkhu {pb:T:1.0064}{pb:V:1.0055} siyā jhāyī vimuttacitto,
::

::gatha2
Ākaṅkhe ce hadayassānupattiṃ;
::

::gatha3
Lokassa ñatvā udayabbayañca,
::

::gathalast
Sucetaso anissito tadānisaṃso’’ti.
::

#### 3. Māghasuttaṃ

{para:84} 84\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:P:1.0047}. Atha kho māgho devaputto abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇo kevalakappaṃ jetavanaṃ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi{pb:M:1.0044}. Ekamantaṃ ṭhito kho māgho devaputto bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsu chetvā sukhaṃ seti, kiṃsu chetvā na socati;
::

::gathalast
Kissassu ekadhammassa, vadhaṃ rocesi gotamā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kodhaṃ chetvā sukhaṃ seti, kodhaṃ chetvā na socati;
::

::gatha2
Kodhassa visamūlassa, madhuraggassa vatrabhū;
::

::gathalast
Vadhaṃ ariyā pasaṃsanti, tañhi chetvā na socatī’’ti.
::

#### 4. Māgadhasuttaṃ

{para:85} 85\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Ekamantaṃ ṭhito kho māgadho devaputto bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kati {pb:T:1.0065} lokasmiṃ pajjotā, yehi loko pakāsati;
::

::gathalast
Bhavantaṃ puṭṭhumāgamma, kathaṃ jānemu taṃ maya’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cattāro {pb:V:1.0056} loke pajjotā, pañcamettha na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Divā tapati ādicco, rattimābhāti candimā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atha aggi divārattiṃ, tattha tattha pakāsati;
::

::gathalast
Sambuddho tapataṃ seṭṭho, esā ābhā anuttarā’’ti.
::

#### 5. Dāmalisuttaṃ

{para:86} 86\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Atha kho dāmali devaputto abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇo kevalakappaṃ jetavanaṃ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṃ ṭhito kho dāmali devaputto bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Karaṇīyametaṃ brāhmaṇena, padhānaṃ akilāsunā;
::

::gathalast
Kāmānaṃ vippahānena, na tenāsīsate bhava’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Natthi kiccaṃ brāhmaṇassa (dāmalīti bhagavā),
::

::gathalast
Katakicco hi brāhmaṇo.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yāva {pb:M:1.0045} na gādhaṃ labhati nadīsu,
::

::gatha2
Āyūhati {pb:P:1.0048} sabbagattebhi jantu;
::

::gatha3
Gādhañca laddhāna thale ṭhito yo,
::

::gathalast
Nāyūhatī {pb:T:1.0066} pāragato hi sova {note:soti (sī. pī. ka.), hoti (syā. kaṃ.), so (?)}.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Esūpamā dāmali brāhmaṇassa,
::

::gatha2
Khīṇāsavassa nipakassa jhāyino;
::

::gatha3
Pappuyya jātimaraṇassa antaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Nāyūhatī pāragato hi so’’ti {note:hotīti (syā. kaṃ.)}.
::

#### 6. Kāmadasuttaṃ

{para:87} 87\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:V:1.0057}. Ekamantaṃ ṭhito kho kāmado devaputto bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘dukkaraṃ bhagavā, sudukkaraṃ bhagavā’’ti.

::gatha1
‘‘Dukkaraṃ vāpi karonti (kāmadāti bhagavā),
::

::gatha2
Sekhā sīlasamāhitā;
::

::gatha3
Ṭhitattā anagāriyupetassa,
::

::gathalast
Tuṭṭhi hoti sukhāvahā’’ti.
::

‘‘Dullabhā bhagavā yadidaṃ tuṭṭhī’’ti.

::gatha1
‘‘Dullabhaṃ vāpi labhanti (kāmadāti bhagavā),
::

::gatha2
Cittavūpasame ratā;
::

::gatha3
Yesaṃ divā ca ratto ca,
::

::gathalast
Bhāvanāya rato mano’’ti.
::

‘‘Dussamādahaṃ bhagavā yadidaṃ citta’’nti.

::gatha1
‘‘Dussamādahaṃ vāpi samādahanti (kāmadāti bhagavā),
::

::gatha2
Indriyūpasame ratā;
::

::gatha3
Te chetvā maccuno jālaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Ariyā gacchanti kāmadā’’ti.
::

‘‘Duggamo {pb:M:1.0046} bhagavā visamo maggo’’ti.

::gatha1
‘‘Duggame visame vāpi, ariyā gacchanti kāmada;
::

::gatha2
Anariyā visame magge, papatanti avaṃsirā;
::

::gathalast
Ariyānaṃ samo maggo, ariyā hi visame samā’’ti.
::

#### 7. Pañcālacaṇḍasuttaṃ

{para:88} 88\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:V:1.0058}. Ekamantaṃ {pb:T:1.0067} ṭhito kho pañcālacaṇḍo devaputto bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sambādhe vata okāsaṃ, avindi bhūrimedhaso;
::

::gathalast
Yo jhānamabujjhi {note:jhānamabudhā (ka. sī.), jhānamabuddhi (syā. kaṃ. pī. ka.)} buddho, paṭilīnanisabho munī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sambādhe vāpi vindanti (pañcālacaṇḍāti bhagavā),
::

::gatha2
Dhammaṃ nibbānapattiyā;
::

::gatha3
Ye satiṃ paccalatthaṃsu,
::

::gathalast
Sammā te susamāhitā’’ti.
::

#### 8. Tāyanasuttaṃ

{para:89} 89\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Atha {pb:P:1.0049} kho tāyano devaputto purāṇatitthakaro abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇo kevalakappaṃ jetavanaṃ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṃ ṭhito kho tāyano devaputto bhagavato santike imā gāthāyo abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Chinda sotaṃ parakkamma, kāme panuda brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
Nappahāya munī kāme, nekattamupapajjati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kayirā ce kayirāthenaṃ, daḷhamenaṃ parakkame;
::

::gathalast
Sithilo hi paribbājo, bhiyyo ākirate rajaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akataṃ {pb:T:1.0068} dukkaṭaṃ {note:dukkataṃ (sī. pī.)} seyyo, pacchā tapati dukkaṭaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Katañca sukataṃ seyyo, yaṃ katvā nānutappati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kuso {pb:V:1.0059}{pb:M:1.0047} yathā duggahito, hatthamevānukantati;
::

::gathalast
Sāmaññaṃ dupparāmaṭṭhaṃ, nirayāyūpakaḍḍhati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ kiñci sithilaṃ kammaṃ, saṃkiliṭṭhañca yaṃ vataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saṅkassaraṃ brahmacariyaṃ, na taṃ hoti mahapphala’’nti.
::

Idamavoca tāyano devaputto; idaṃ vatvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaṃ katvā tatthevantaradhāyīti.

Atha kho bhagavā tassā rattiyā accayena bhikkhū āmantesi – ‘‘imaṃ, bhikkhave, rattiṃ tāyano nāma devaputto purāṇatitthakaro abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇo kevalakappaṃ jetavanaṃ obhāsetvā yenāhaṃ tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā maṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṃ ṭhito kho, bhikkhave, tāyano devaputto mama santike imā gāthāyo abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Chinda sotaṃ parakkamma, kāme panuda brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
Nappahāya munī kāme, nekattamupapajjati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kayirā ce kayirāthenaṃ, daḷhamenaṃ parakkame;
::

::gathalast
Sithilo {pb:P:1.0050} hi paribbājo, bhiyyo ākirate rajaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akataṃ dukkaṭaṃ seyyo, pacchā tapati dukkaṭaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Katañca sukataṃ seyyo, yaṃ katvā nānutappati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kuso {pb:T:1.0069} yathā duggahito, hatthamevānukantati;
::

::gathalast
Sāmaññaṃ dupparāmaṭṭhaṃ, nirayāyūpakaḍḍhati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ {pb:V:1.0060} kiñci sithilaṃ kammaṃ, saṃkiliṭṭhañca yaṃ vataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saṅkassaraṃ brahmacariyaṃ, na taṃ hoti mahapphala’’nti.
::

‘‘Idamavoca, bhikkhave, tāyano devaputto, idaṃ vatvā maṃ abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaṃ katvā tatthevantaradhāyi. Uggaṇhātha, bhikkhave, tāyanagāthā; pariyāpuṇātha, bhikkhave, tāyanagāthā; dhāretha, bhikkhave, tāyanagāthā. Atthasaṃhitā, bhikkhave, tāyanagāthā ādibrahmacariyikā’’ti.

#### 9. Candimasuttaṃ

{para:90} 90\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:M:1.0048}. Tena kho pana samayena candimā devaputto rāhunā asurindena gahito hoti. Atha kho candimā devaputto bhagavantaṃ anussaramāno tāyaṃ velāyaṃ imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Namo te buddha vīratthu, vippamuttosi sabbadhi;
::

::gathalast
Sambādhapaṭipannosmi, tassa me saraṇaṃ bhavā’’ti.
::

Atha kho bhagavā candimaṃ devaputtaṃ ārabbha rāhuṃ asurindaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Tathāgataṃ arahantaṃ, candimā saraṇaṃ gato;
::

::gathalast
Rāhu candaṃ pamuñcassu, buddhā lokānukampakā’’ti.
::

Atha kho rāhu asurindo candimaṃ devaputtaṃ muñcitvā taramānarūpo yena vepacitti asurindo tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā saṃviggo {pb:T:1.0070} lomahaṭṭhajāto ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho rāhuṃ asurindaṃ vepacitti asurindo gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ nu santaramānova, rāhu candaṃ pamuñcasi;
::

::gathalast
Saṃviggarūpo āgamma, kiṃ nu bhītova tiṭṭhasī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sattadhā {pb:V:1.0061} me phale muddhā, jīvanto na sukhaṃ labhe;
::

::gathalast
Buddhagāthābhigītomhi, no ce muñceyya candima’’nti.
::

#### 10. Sūriyasuttaṃ

{para:91} 91\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Tena {pb:P:1.0051} kho pana samayena sūriyo devaputto rāhunā asurindena gahito hoti. Atha kho sūriyo devaputto bhagavantaṃ anussaramāno tāyaṃ velāyaṃ imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Namo te buddha vīratthu, vippamuttosi sabbadhi;
::

::gathalast
Sambādhapaṭipannosmi, tassa me saraṇaṃ bhavā’’ti.
::

Atha kho bhagavā sūriyaṃ devaputtaṃ ārabbha rāhuṃ asurindaṃ gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Tathāgataṃ {pb:M:1.0049} arahantaṃ, sūriyo saraṇaṃ gato;
::

::gathalast
Rāhu sūriyaṃ {note:suriyaṃ (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} pamuñcassu, buddhā lokānukampakā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo andhakāre tamasi pabhaṅkaro,
::

::gatha2
Verocano maṇḍalī uggatejo;
::

::gatha3
Mā {pb:T:1.0071} rāhu gilī caramantalikkhe,
::

::gathalast
Pajaṃ mamaṃ rāhu pamuñca sūriya’’nti.
::

Atha kho rāhu asurindo sūriyaṃ devaputtaṃ muñcitvā taramānarūpo yena vepacitti asurindo tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā saṃviggo lomahaṭṭhajāto ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho rāhuṃ asurindaṃ vepacitti asurindo gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ nu santaramānova, rāhu sūriyaṃ pamuñcasi;
::

::gathalast
Saṃviggarūpo āgamma, kiṃ nu bhītova tiṭṭhasī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sattadhā {pb:V:1.0062} me phale muddhā, jīvanto na sukhaṃ labhe;
::

::gathalast
Buddhagāthābhigītomhi, no ce muñceyya sūriya’’nti.
::

::centre
Paṭhamo vaggo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Dve kassapā ca māgho ca, māgadho dāmali kāmado;
::

::gathalast
Pañcālacaṇḍo tāyano, candimasūriyena te dasāti.
::

#### 2. Anāthapiṇḍikavaggo

#### 1. Candimasasuttaṃ

{para:92} 92\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:T:1.0072}. Atha kho candimaso {note:candimāso (ka.)} devaputto abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇo kevalakappaṃ jetavanaṃ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā {pb:P:1.0052} tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi{pb:M:1.0050}. Ekamantaṃ ṭhito kho candimaso devaputto bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Te hi sotthiṃ gamissanti, kacche vāmakase magā;
::

::gathalast
Jhānāni upasampajja, ekodi nipakā satā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te hi pāraṃ gamissanti, chetvā jālaṃva ambujo;
::

::gathalast
Jhānāni upasampajja, appamattā raṇañjahā’’ti.
::

#### 2. Veṇḍusuttaṃ

{para:93} 93\. Ekamantaṃ {pb:V:1.0063} ṭhito kho veṇḍu {note:veṇhu (sī.)} devaputto bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sukhitāva te {note:sukhitā vata te (sī. syā. kaṃ.)} manujā, sugataṃ payirupāsiya;
::

::gathalast
Yuñjaṃ {note:yujja (sī.), yuñja (syā. kaṃ. pī.)} gotamasāsane, appamattā nu sikkhare’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye {pb:T:1.0073} me pavutte siṭṭhipade {note:satthipade (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} (veṇḍūti bhagavā),
::

::gatha2
Anusikkhanti jhāyino;
::

::gatha3
Kāle te appamajjantā,
::

::gathalast
Na maccuvasagā siyu’’nti.
::

#### 3. Dīghalaṭṭhisuttaṃ

{para:94} 94\. Evaṃ me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati veḷuvane kalandakanivāpe. Atha kho dīghalaṭṭhi devaputto abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇo kevalakappaṃ veḷuvanaṃ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṃ ṭhito kho dīghalaṭṭhi devaputto bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Bhikkhu siyā jhāyī vimuttacitto,
::

::gatha2
Ākaṅkhe ce hadayassānupattiṃ;
::

::gatha3
Lokassa ñatvā udayabbayañca,
::

::gathalast
Sucetaso anissito tadānisaṃso’’ti.
::

#### 4. Nandanasuttaṃ

{para:95} 95\. Ekamantaṃ {pb:M:1.0051} ṭhito kho nandano devaputto bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Pucchāmi taṃ gotama bhūripañña,
::

::gatha2
Anāvaṭaṃ bhagavato ñāṇadassanaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Kathaṃvidhaṃ {pb:T:1.0074}{pb:V:1.0064}{pb:P:1.0053} sīlavantaṃ vadanti,
::

::gatha2
Kathaṃvidhaṃ paññavantaṃ vadanti;
::

::gatha3
Kathaṃvidho dukkhamaticca iriyati,
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃvidhaṃ devatā pūjayantī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo sīlavā paññavā bhāvitatto,
::

::gatha2
Samāhito jhānarato satīmā;
::

::gatha3
Sabbassa sokā vigatā pahīnā,
::

::gathalast
Khīṇāsavo antimadehadhārī.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tathāvidhaṃ sīlavantaṃ vadanti,
::

::gatha2
Tathāvidhaṃ paññavantaṃ vadanti;
::

::gatha3
Tathāvidho dukkhamaticca iriyati,
::

::gathalast
Tathāvidhaṃ devatā pūjayantī’’ti.
::

#### 5. Candanasuttaṃ

{para:96} 96\. Ekamantaṃ ṭhito kho candano devaputto bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kathaṃsu {note:kosudha (sī.)} tarati oghaṃ, rattindivamatandito;
::

::gathalast
Appatiṭṭhe anālambe, ko gambhīre na sīdatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbadā sīlasampanno, paññavā susamāhito;
::

::gathalast
Āraddhavīriyo pahitatto, oghaṃ tarati duttaraṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Virato {pb:T:1.0075} kāmasaññāya, rūpasaṃyojanātigo;
::

::gathalast
Nandīrāgaparikkhīṇo, so gambhīre na sīdatī’’ti.
::

#### 6. Vāsudattasuttaṃ

{para:97} 97\. Ekamantaṃ {pb:V:1.0065}{pb:M:1.0052} ṭhito kho vāsudatto devaputto bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sattiyā viya omaṭṭho, ḍayhamānova {note:ḍayhamāneva (sabbattha)} matthake;
::

::gathalast
Kāmarāgappahānāya, sato bhikkhu paribbaje’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sattiyā viya omaṭṭho, ḍayhamānova matthake;
::

::gathalast
Sakkāyadiṭṭhippahānāya, sato bhikkhu paribbaje’’ti.
::

#### 7. Subrahmasuttaṃ

{para:98} 98\. Ekamantaṃ ṭhito kho subrahmā devaputto bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Niccaṃ utrastamidaṃ cittaṃ, niccaṃ ubbiggamidaṃ {note:ubbiggidaṃ (mahāsatipaṭṭhānasuttavaṇṇanāyaṃ)} mano;
::

::gatha2
Anuppannesu {pb:P:1.0054} kicchesu {note:kiccesu (bahūsu)}, atho uppatitesu ca;
::

::gathalast
Sace atthi anutrastaṃ, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāññatra bojjhā tapasā {note:bojjhaṅgatapasā (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)}, nāññatrindriyasaṃvarā;
::

::gathalast
Nāññatra sabbanissaggā, sotthiṃ passāmi pāṇina’’nti.
::

‘‘Idamavoca…pe… tatthevantaradhāyī’’ti.

#### 8. Kakudhasuttaṃ

{para:99} 99\. Evaṃ {pb:T:1.0076} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sākete viharati añjanavane migadāye. Atha kho kakudho devaputto abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇo kevalakappaṃ añjanavanaṃ obhāsetvā {pb:V:1.0066} yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṃ ṭhito kho kakudho devaputto bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘nandasi, samaṇā’’ti? ‘‘Kiṃ laddhā, āvuso’’ti? ‘‘Tena hi, samaṇa, socasī’’ti? ‘‘Kiṃ jīyittha, āvuso’’ti? ‘‘Tena hi, samaṇa, neva nandasi na ca {note:neva (sī. syā. kaṃ.)} socasī’’ti? ‘‘Evamāvuso’’ti.

::gatha1
‘‘Kacci {pb:M:1.0053} tvaṃ anagho {note:anigho (sabbattha)} bhikkhu, kacci nandī {note:nandi (sī. syā. kaṃ.)} na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Kacci taṃ ekamāsīnaṃ, aratī nābhikīratī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anagho ve ahaṃ yakkha, atho nandī na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Atho maṃ ekamāsīnaṃ, aratī nābhikīratī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kathaṃ tvaṃ anagho bhikkhu, kathaṃ nandī na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃ taṃ ekamāsīnaṃ, aratī nābhikīratī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aghajātassa ve nandī, nandījātassa ve aghaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anandī anagho bhikkhu, evaṃ jānāhi āvuso’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cirassaṃ vata passāmi, brāhmaṇaṃ parinibbutaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anandiṃ anaghaṃ bhikkhuṃ, tiṇṇaṃ loke visattika’’nti.
::

#### 9. Uttarasuttaṃ

{para:100} 100\. Rājagahanidānaṃ{pb:T:1.0077}. Ekamantaṃ ṭhito kho uttaro devaputto bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Upanīyati {pb:P:1.0055} jīvitamappamāyu,
::

::gatha2
Jarūpanītassa na santi tāṇā;
::

::gatha3
Etaṃ {pb:V:1.0067} bhayaṃ maraṇe pekkhamāno,
::

::gathalast
Puññāni kayirātha sukhāvahānī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upanīyati jīvitamappamāyu,
::

::gatha2
Jarūpanītassa na santi tāṇā;
::

::gatha3
Etaṃ bhayaṃ maraṇe pekkhamāno,
::

::gathalast
Lokāmisaṃ pajahe santipekkho’’ti.
::

#### 10. Anāthapiṇḍikasuttaṃ

{para:101} 101\. Ekamantaṃ ṭhito kho anāthapiṇḍiko devaputto bhagavato santike imā gāthāyo abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Idañhi taṃ jetavanaṃ, isisaṅghanisevitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Āvutthaṃ dhammarājena, pītisañjananaṃ mama.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kammaṃ {pb:M:1.0054} vijjā ca dhammo ca, sīlaṃ jīvitamuttamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Etena maccā sujjhanti, na gottena dhanena vā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasmā hi paṇḍito poso, sampassaṃ atthamattano;
::

::gathalast
Yoniso {pb:T:1.0078}{pb:P:1.0056} vicine dhammaṃ, evaṃ tattha visujjhati.
::

::gatha1
