Bhareyyāsi taṃ purisaṃ, attho ca te tādisena purisenā’’ti? ‘‘Bhareyyāhaṃ, bhante, taṃ purisaṃ, attho ca me tādisena purisenā’’ti.

‘‘Evameva kho, mahārāja, yasmā kasmā cepi {note:yasmā cepi (sī. syā. kaṃ. ka.)} kulā agārasmā anagāriyaṃ pabbajito hoti, so ca hoti pañcaṅgavippahīno pañcaṅgasamannāgato, tasmiṃ {pb:M:1.0100} dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ hoti. Katamāni pañcaṅgāni pahīnāni honti? Kāmacchando pahīno hoti, byāpādo pahīno hoti, thinamiddhaṃ pahīnaṃ hoti, uddhaccakukkuccaṃ pahīnaṃ hoti, vicikicchā pahīnā hoti. Imāni pañcaṅgāni pahīnāni honti. Katamehi pañcahaṅgehi {pb:T:1.0145} samannāgato hoti? Asekkhena sīlakkhandhena samannāgato hoti, asekkhena samādhikkhandhena samannāgato hoti, asekkhena paññākkhandhena samannāgato {pb:P:1.0100} hoti, asekkhena vimuttikkhandhena samannāgato hoti, asekkhena vimuttiñāṇadassanakkhandhena samannāgato hoti. Imehi pañcahaṅgehi samannāgato hoti. Iti pañcaṅgavippahīne pañcaṅgasamannāgate dinnaṃ mahapphala’’nti. Idamavoca bhagavā…pe… satthā –

::gatha1
‘‘Issattaṃ {note:issatthaṃ (sī. syā. kaṃ.)} balavīriyañca {note:balaviriyañca (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)}, yasmiṃ vijjetha māṇave;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ yuddhattho bhare rājā, nāsūraṃ jātipaccayā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatheva khantisoraccaṃ, dhammā yasmiṃ patiṭṭhitā;
::

::gathalast
Ariyavuttiṃ medhāviṃ, hīnajaccampi pūjaye.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kāraye assame ramme, vāsayettha bahussute;
::

::gathalast
Papañca vivane kayirā, dugge saṅkamanāni ca.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Annaṃ {pb:V:1.0119} pānaṃ khādanīyaṃ, vatthasenāsanāni ca;
::

::gathalast
Dadeyya ujubhūtesu, vippasannena cetasā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathā hi megho thanayaṃ, vijjumālī satakkaku;
::

::gathalast
Thalaṃ ninnañca pūreti, abhivassaṃ vasundharaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tatheva saddho sutavā, abhisaṅkhacca bhojanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vanibbake tappayati, annapānena paṇḍito.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āmodamāno pakireti, detha dethāti bhāsati;
::

::gatha2
Taṃ {pb:T:1.0146} hissa gajjitaṃ hoti, devasseva pavassato;
::

::gathalast
Sā puññadhārā vipulā, dātāraṃ abhivassatī’’ti.
::

#### 5. Pabbatūpamasuttaṃ

{para:136} 136\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:M:1.0101}. Ekamantaṃ nisinnaṃ kho rājānaṃ pasenadiṃ kosalaṃ bhagavā etadavoca – ‘‘handa, kuto nu tvaṃ, mahārāja, āgacchasi divā divassā’’ti? ‘‘Yāni tāni, bhante, raññaṃ khattiyānaṃ muddhāvasittānaṃ issariyamadamattānaṃ kāmagedhapariyuṭṭhitānaṃ janapadatthāvariyappattānaṃ mahantaṃ pathavimaṇḍalaṃ abhivijiya ajjhāvasantānaṃ rājakaraṇīyāni bhavanti, tesu khvāhaṃ, etarahi ussukkamāpanno’’ti.

‘‘Taṃ kiṃ maññasi, mahārāja, idha te puriso āgaccheyya {pb:P:1.0101} puratthimāya disāya saddhāyiko paccayiko. So taṃ upasaṅkamitvā evaṃ vadeyya – ‘yagghe, mahārāja, jāneyyāsi, ahaṃ āgacchāmi puratthimāya disāya. Tatthaddasaṃ mahantaṃ pabbataṃ abbhasamaṃ sabbe pāṇe nippothento āgacchati. Yaṃ te, mahārāja, karaṇīyaṃ, taṃ karohī’ti. Atha dutiyo puriso āgaccheyya pacchimāya disāya…pe… atha tatiyo puriso āgaccheyya uttarāya disāya…pe… atha catuttho puriso āgaccheyya dakkhiṇāya disāya saddhāyiko paccayiko. So taṃ {pb:T:1.0147} upasaṅkamitvā evaṃ vadeyya – ‘yagghe mahārāja, jāneyyāsi, ahaṃ āgacchāmi {pb:V:1.0120} dakkhiṇāya disāya. Tatthaddasaṃ mahantaṃ pabbataṃ abbhasamaṃ sabbe pāṇe nippothento āgacchati. Yaṃ te, mahārāja, karaṇīyaṃ taṃ karohī’ti. Evarūpe te, mahārāja, mahati mahabbhaye samuppanne dāruṇe manussakkhaye {note:manussakāye (ka.)} dullabhe manussatte kimassa karaṇīya’’nti?

‘‘Evarūpe me, bhante, mahati mahabbhaye samuppanne dāruṇe manussakkhaye dullabhe manussatte kimassa karaṇīyaṃ aññatra dhammacariyāya aññatra samacariyāya aññatra kusalakiriyāya aññatra puññakiriyāyā’’ti?

‘‘Ārocemi kho te, mahārāja, paṭivedemi kho te, mahārāja, adhivattati kho taṃ, mahārāja, jarāmaraṇaṃ. Adhivattamāne ce te, mahārāja, jarāmaraṇe kimassa karaṇīya’’nti? ‘‘Adhivattamāne ca me, bhante, jarāmaraṇe kimassa karaṇīyaṃ aññatra dhammacariyāya samacariyāya kusalakiriyāya puññakiriyāya? Yāni tāni, bhante, raññaṃ khattiyānaṃ muddhāvasittānaṃ issariyamadamattānaṃ {pb:M:1.0102} kāmagedhapariyuṭṭhitānaṃ janapadatthāvariyappattānaṃ mahantaṃ pathavimaṇḍalaṃ abhivijiya ajjhāvasantānaṃ hatthiyuddhāni bhavanti; tesampi, bhante, hatthiyuddhānaṃ natthi gati natthi visayo adhivattamāne jarāmaraṇe. Yānipi tāni, bhante, raññaṃ khattiyānaṃ muddhāvasittānaṃ…pe… ajjhāvasantānaṃ assayuddhāni bhavanti…pe… rathayuddhāni bhavanti {pb:T:1.0148} …pe… pattiyuddhāni bhavanti; tesampi{pb:P:1.0102}, bhante, pattiyuddhānaṃ natthi gati natthi visayo adhivattamāne jarāmaraṇe. Santi kho pana, bhante, imasmiṃ rājakule mantino mahāmattā, ye pahonti {note:yesaṃ honti (ka.)} āgate paccatthike mantehi bhedayituṃ. Tesampi, bhante, mantayuddhānaṃ natthi gati natthi visayo adhivattamāne jarāmaraṇe. Saṃvijjati kho pana, bhante, imasmiṃ rājakule pahūtaṃ hiraññasuvaṇṇaṃ bhūmigatañceva vehāsaṭṭhañca, yena mayaṃ pahoma āgate paccatthike dhanena upalāpetuṃ. Tesampi, bhante, dhanayuddhānaṃ natthi gati natthi visayo adhivattamāne jarāmaraṇe. Adhivattamāne ca me, bhante, jarāmaraṇe kimassa karaṇīyaṃ aññatra dhammacariyāya samacariyāya kusalakiriyāya puññakiriyāyā’’ti?

‘‘Evametaṃ, mahārāja, evametaṃ, mahārāja! Adhivattamāne jarāmaraṇe kimassa karaṇīyaṃ aññatra dhammacariyāya samacariyāya kusalakiriyāya puññakiriyāyā’’ti? Idamavoca bhagavā…pe… satthā –

::gatha1
‘‘Yathāpi {pb:V:1.0121} selā vipulā, nabhaṃ āhacca pabbatā;
::

::gathalast
Samantānupariyāyeyyuṃ, nippothento catuddisā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ jarā ca maccu ca, adhivattanti pāṇine {note:pāṇino (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)};
::

::gatha2
Khattiye brāhmaṇe vesse, sudde caṇḍālapukkuse;
::

::gathalast
Na {pb:T:1.0149} kiñci {note:na kañci (?)} parivajjeti, sabbamevābhimaddati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na tattha hatthīnaṃ bhūmi, na rathānaṃ na pattiyā;
::

::gathalast
Na cāpi mantayuddhena, sakkā jetuṃ dhanena vā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasmā hi paṇḍito poso, sampassaṃ atthamattano;
::

::gathalast
Buddhe dhamme ca saṅghe ca, dhīro saddhaṃ nivesaye.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo {pb:M:1.0103} dhammaṃ cari {note:dhammacārī (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} kāyena, vācāya uda cetasā;
::

::gathalast
Idheva naṃ pasaṃsanti, pecca sagge pamodatī’’ti.
::

::centre
Tatiyo vaggo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Puggalo ayyikā loko, issattaṃ {note:issatthaṃ (sī. syā. kaṃ.)} pabbatūpamā;
::

::gathalast
Desitaṃ buddhaseṭṭhena, imaṃ kosalapañcakanti.
::

::centre
Kosalasaṃyuttaṃ samattaṃ.
::

### 4. Mārasaṃyuttaṃ

#### 1. Paṭhamavaggo

#### 1. Tapokammasuttaṃ

{para:137} 137\. Evaṃ {pb:T:1.0150}{pb:V:1.0122}{pb:P:1.0103}{pb:M:1.0104} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā uruvelāyaṃ viharati najjā nerañjarāya tīre ajapālanigrodhamūle paṭhamābhisambuddho. Atha kho bhagavato rahogatassa paṭisallīnassa evaṃ cetaso parivitakko udapādi – ‘‘mutto vatamhi tāya dukkarakārikāya. Sādhu mutto vatamhi tāya anatthasaṃhitāya dukkarakārikāya. Sādhu vatamhi mutto bodhiṃ samajjhaga’’nti {note:sādhu ṭhito sato bodhiṃ samajjheganti (sī. pī.), sādhu vatamhi satto bodhisamajjhagūti (syā. kaṃ.)}.

Atha kho māro pāpimā bhagavato cetasā cetoparivitakkamaññāya yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Tapokammā apakkamma, yena na sujjhanti māṇavā;
::

::gathalast
Asuddho maññasi suddho, suddhimaggā aparaddho’’ {note:suddhimaggamaparaddho (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} ti.
::

Atha kho bhagavā ‘‘māro ayaṃ pāpimā’’ iti viditvā māraṃ pāpimantaṃ gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Anatthasaṃhitaṃ {pb:T:1.0151} ñatvā, yaṃ kiñci amaraṃ tapaṃ {note:aparaṃ tapaṃ (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Sabbaṃ natthāvahaṃ hoti, phiyārittaṃva dhammani {note:vammani (sī.), dhammaniṃ (pī.), jammaniṃ (ka.) etthāyaṃ dhammasaddo sakkate dhanvanaṃ-saddena sadiso maruvācakoti veditabbo, yathā daḷhadhammātipadaṃ}.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sīlaṃ samādhi paññañca, maggaṃ bodhāya bhāvayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pattosmi paramaṃ suddhiṃ, nihato tvamasi antakā’’ti.
::

Atha {pb:V:1.0123} kho māro pāpimā ‘‘jānāti maṃ bhagavā, jānāti maṃ sugato’’ti, dukkhī dummano tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 2. Hatthirājavaṇṇasuttaṃ

{para:138} 138\. Evaṃ {pb:M:1.0105} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā uruvelāyaṃ viharati najjā nerañjarāya tīre ajapālanigrodhamūle paṭhamābhisambuddho{pb:P:1.0104}. Tena kho pana samayena bhagavā rattandhakāratimisāyaṃ abbhokāse nisinno hoti, devo ca ekamekaṃ phusāyati. Atha kho māro pāpimā bhagavato bhayaṃ chambhitattaṃ lomahaṃsaṃ uppādetukāmo mahantaṃ hatthirājavaṇṇaṃ abhinimminitvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami. Seyyathāpi nāma mahāariṭṭhako maṇi, evamassa sīsaṃ hoti. Seyyathāpi nāma suddhaṃ rūpiyaṃ, evamassa dantā honti. Seyyathāpi nāma mahatī naṅgalīsā {note:naṅgalasīsā (pī. ka.)}, evamassa soṇḍo hoti. Atha kho bhagavā ‘‘māro ayaṃ pāpimā’’ iti viditvā māraṃ pāpimantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Saṃsaraṃ dīghamaddhānaṃ, vaṇṇaṃ katvā subhāsubhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Alaṃ te tena pāpima, nihato tvamasi antakā’’ti.
::

Atha {pb:T:1.0152} kho māro pāpimā ‘‘jānāti maṃ bhagavā, jānāti maṃ sugato’’ti dukkhī dummano tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 3. Subhasuttaṃ

{para:139} 139\. Evaṃ me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā uruvelāyaṃ viharati najjā nerañjarāya tīre ajapālanigrodhamūle paṭhamābhisambuddho. Tena kho pana samayena bhagavā rattandhakāratimisāyaṃ abbhokāse nisinno hoti, devo ca ekamekaṃ phusāyati. Atha kho māro pāpimā, bhagavato bhayaṃ chambhitattaṃ lomahaṃsaṃ uppādetukāmo, yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavato avidūre uccāvacā vaṇṇanibhā upadaṃseti, subhā ceva asubhā ca. Atha kho bhagavā ‘‘māro ayaṃ pāpimā’’ iti viditvā māraṃ pāpimantaṃ gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Saṃsaraṃ {pb:V:1.0124} dīghamaddhānaṃ, vaṇṇaṃ katvā subhāsubhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Alaṃ te tena pāpima, nihato tvamasi antaka.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye {pb:M:1.0106} ca kāyena vācāya, manasā ca susaṃvutā;
::

::gathalast
Na te māravasānugā, na te mārassa baddhagū’’ {note:baddhabhū (ka.), paccagū (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} ti.
::

Atha kho māro…pe… tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 4. Paṭhamamārapāsasuttaṃ

{para:140} 140\. Evaṃ {pb:P:1.0105} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā bārāṇasiyaṃ viharati isipatane migadāye. Tatra kho bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi – ‘‘bhikkhavo’’ti. ‘‘Bhadante’’ti {pb:T:1.0153} te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṃ. Bhagavā etadavoca –

‘‘Mayhaṃ kho, bhikkhave, yoniso manasikārā yoniso sammappadhānā anuttarā vimutti anuppattā, anuttarā vimutti sacchikatā. Tumhepi, bhikkhave, yoniso manasikārā yoniso sammappadhānā anuttaraṃ vimuttiṃ anupāpuṇātha, anuttaraṃ vimuttiṃ sacchikarothā’’ti. Atha kho māro pāpimā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Baddhosi mārapāsena, ye dibbā ye ca mānusā;
::

::gathalast
Mārabandhanabaddhosi, na me samaṇa mokkhasī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Muttāhaṃ {note:muttohaṃ (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} mārapāsena, ye dibbā ye ca mānusā;
::

::gathalast
Mārabandhanamuttomhi, nihato tvamasi antakā’’ti.
::

Atha kho māro pāpimā…pe… tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 5. Dutiyamārapāsasuttaṃ

{para:141} 141\. Ekaṃ {pb:V:1.0125} samayaṃ bhagavā bārāṇasiyaṃ viharati isipatane migadāye. Tatra kho bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi – ‘‘bhikkhavo’’ti. ‘‘Bhadante’’ti te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṃ. Bhagavā etadavoca –

‘‘Muttāhaṃ, bhikkhave, sabbapāsehi ye dibbā ye ca mānusā. Tumhepi, bhikkhave, muttā sabbapāsehi ye dibbā ye ca mānusā. Caratha, bhikkhave, cārikaṃ bahujanahitāya bahujanasukhāya lokānukampāya atthāya hitāya {pb:T:1.0154} sukhāya devamanussānaṃ. Mā ekena dve agamittha. Desetha, bhikkhave, dhammaṃ ādikalyāṇaṃ majjhekalyāṇaṃ pariyosānakalyāṇaṃ sātthaṃ sabyañjanaṃ {pb:M:1.0107} kevalaparipuṇṇaṃ parisuddhaṃ brahmacariyaṃ pakāsetha. Santi sattā apparajakkhajātikā, assavanatā dhammassa {pb:P:1.0106} parihāyanti. Bhavissanti dhammassa aññātāro. Ahampi, bhikkhave, yena uruvelā senānigamo tenupasaṅkamissāmi dhammadesanāyā’’ti. Atha kho māro pāpimā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Baddhosi sabbapāsehi, ye dibbā ye ca mānusā;
::

::gathalast
Mahābandhanabaddhosi, na me samaṇa mokkhasī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Muttāhaṃ sabbapāsehi, ye dibbā ye ca mānusā;
::

::gathalast
Mahābandhanamuttomhi, nihato tvamasi antakā’’ti.
::

Atha kho māro pāpimā…pe… tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 6. Sappasuttaṃ

{para:142} 142\. Evaṃ me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati veḷuvane kalandakanivāpe. Tena kho pana samayena bhagavā rattandhakāratimisāyaṃ abbhokāse nisinno hoti, devo ca ekamekaṃ phusāyati.

Atha {pb:T:1.0155}{pb:V:1.0126} kho māro pāpimā bhagavato bhayaṃ chambhitattaṃ lomahaṃsaṃ uppādetukāmo mahantaṃ sapparājavaṇṇaṃ abhinimminitvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami. Seyyathāpi nāma mahatī ekarukkhikā nāvā, evamassa kāyo hoti. Seyyathāpi nāma mahantaṃ soṇḍikākiḷañjaṃ, evamassa phaṇo hoti. Seyyathāpi nāma mahatī kosalikā kaṃsapāti, evamassa akkhīni bhavanti. Seyyathāpi nāma deve gaḷagaḷāyante vijjullatā niccharanti, evamassa mukhato jivhā niccharati. Seyyathāpi nāma kammāragaggariyā dhamamānāya saddo hoti, evamassa assāsapassāsānaṃ saddo hoti.

Atha kho bhagavā ‘‘māro ayaṃ pāpimā’’ iti viditvā māraṃ pāpimantaṃ gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Yo suññagehāni sevati,
::

::gatha2
Seyyo so muni attasaññato;
::

::gatha3
Vossajja careyya tattha so,
::

::gathalast
Patirūpañhi tathāvidhassa taṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Carakā {pb:M:1.0108} bahū bheravā bahū,
::

::gatha2
Atho ḍaṃsasarīsapā {note:ḍaṃsa siriṃsapā (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} bahū;
::

::gatha3
Lomampi {pb:P:1.0107} na tattha iñjaye,
::

::gathalast
Suññāgāragato mahāmuni.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nabhaṃ {pb:T:1.0156} phaleyya pathavī caleyya,
::

::gatha2
Sabbepi pāṇā uda santaseyyuṃ;
::

::gatha3
Sallampi ce urasi pakappayeyyuṃ,
::

::gathalast
Upadhīsu tāṇaṃ na karonti buddhā’’ti.
::

Atha kho māro pāpimā ‘‘jānāti maṃ bhagavā, jānāti maṃ sugato’’ti dukkhī dummano tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 7. Supatisuttaṃ

{para:143} 143\. Ekaṃ {pb:V:1.0127} samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati veḷuvane kalandakanivāpe. Atha kho bhagavā bahudevarattiṃ abbhokāse caṅkamitvā rattiyā paccūsasamayaṃ pāde pakkhāletvā vihāraṃ pavisitvā dakkhiṇena passena sīhaseyyaṃ kappesi pāde pādaṃ accādhāya sato sampajāno uṭṭhānasaññaṃ manasi karitvā. Atha kho māro pāpimā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ soppasi kiṃ nu soppasi,
::

::gatha2
Kimidaṃ soppasi dubbhago {note:dubbhato (syā. kaṃ.), dubbhayo (pī.)} viya;
::

::gatha3
Suññamagāranti soppasi,
::

::gathalast
Kimidaṃ soppasi sūriye uggate’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yassa {pb:T:1.0157} jālinī visattikā,
::

::gatha2
Taṇhā natthi kuhiñci netave;
::

::gatha3
Sabbūpadhiparikkhayā buddho,
::

::gathalast
Soppati kiṃ tavettha mārā’’ti.
::

Atha kho māro pāpimā…pe… tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 8. Nandatisuttaṃ

{para:144} 144\. Evaṃ {pb:M:1.0109} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Atha kho māro pāpimā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Nandati puttehi puttimā, gomā gobhi tatheva nandati;
::

::gathalast
Upadhīhi {pb:P:1.0108} narassa nandanā, na hi so nandati yo nirūpadhī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Socati {pb:V:1.0128} puttehi puttimā, gomā gobhi tatheva socati;
::

::gathalast
Upadhīhi narassa socanā, na hi so socati yo nirūpadhī’’ti.
::

Atha kho māro pāpimā ‘‘jānāti maṃ bhagavā, jānāti maṃ sugato’’ti dukkhī dummano tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 9. Paṭhamaāyusuttaṃ

{para:145} 145\. Evaṃ {pb:T:1.0158} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati veḷuvane kalandakanivāpe. Tatra kho bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi – ‘‘bhikkhavo’’ti. ‘‘Bhadante’’ti te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṃ. Bhagavā etadavoca –

‘‘Appamidaṃ, bhikkhave, manussānaṃ āyu. Gamanīyo samparāyo, kattabbaṃ kusalaṃ, caritabbaṃ brahmacariyaṃ. Natthi jātassa amaraṇaṃ. Yo, bhikkhave, ciraṃ jīvati, so vassasataṃ appaṃ vā bhiyyo’’ti.

Atha kho māro pāpimā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Dīghamāyu manussānaṃ, na naṃ hīḷe suporiso;
::

::gathalast
Careyya khīramattova, natthi maccussa āgamo’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Appamāyu manussānaṃ, hīḷeyya naṃ suporiso;
::

::gathalast
Careyyādittasīsova, natthi maccussa nāgamo’’ti.
::

Atha kho māro…pe… tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 10. Dutiyaāyusuttaṃ

{para:146} 146\. Evaṃ {pb:V:1.0129}{pb:M:1.0110} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati veḷuvane kalandakanivāpe. Tatra kho bhagavā…pe… etadavoca –

‘‘Appamidaṃ, bhikkhave, manussānaṃ āyu. Gamanīyo samparāyo, kattabbaṃ kusalaṃ, caritabbaṃ brahmacariyaṃ. Natthi jātassa amaraṇaṃ. Yo, bhikkhave, ciraṃ jīvati, so vassasataṃ appaṃ vā bhiyyo’’ti.

Atha kho māro pāpimā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā {pb:T:1.0159} bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Nāccayanti {pb:P:1.0109} ahorattā, jīvitaṃ nūparujjhati;
::

::gathalast
Āyu anupariyāyati, maccānaṃ nemīva rathakubbara’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Accayanti ahorattā, jīvitaṃ uparujjhati;
::

::gathalast
Āyu khīyati maccānaṃ, kunnadīnaṃva odaka’’nti.
::

Atha kho māro pāpimā ‘‘jānāti maṃ bhagavā, jānāti maṃ sugato’’ti dukkhī dummano tatthevantaradhāyīti.

::centre
Paṭhamo vaggo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Tapokammañca nāgo ca, subhaṃ pāsena te duve;
::

::gathalast
Sappo supati nandanaṃ, āyunā apare duveti.
::

#### 2. Dutiyavaggo

#### 1. Pāsāṇasuttaṃ

{para:147} 147\. Ekaṃ {pb:T:1.0160}{pb:V:1.0130} samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati gijjhakūṭe pabbate. Tena kho pana samayena bhagavā rattandhakāratimisāyaṃ abbhokāse nisinno hoti, devo ca ekamekaṃ phusāyati. Atha kho māro pāpimā bhagavato bhayaṃ chambhitattaṃ lomahaṃsaṃ uppādetukāmo yena bhagavā {pb:M:1.0111} tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavato avidūre mahante pāsāṇe padālesi.

Atha kho bhagavā ‘‘māro ayaṃ pāpimā’’ iti viditvā māraṃ pāpimantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sacepi kevalaṃ sabbaṃ, gijjhakūṭaṃ calessasi {note:gaḷeyyasi (syā. kaṃ.), caleyyāsi (ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Neva sammāvimuttānaṃ, buddhānaṃ atthi iñjita’’nti.
::

Atha kho māro pāpimā ‘‘jānāti maṃ bhagavā, jānāti maṃ sugato’’ti dukkhī dummano tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 2. Kinnusīhasuttaṃ

{para:148} 148\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa {pb:T:1.0161} ārāme. Tena kho pana samayena bhagavā mahatiyā parisāya parivuto dhammaṃ deseti.

Atha {pb:P:1.0110} kho mārassa pāpimato etadahosi – ‘‘ayaṃ kho samaṇo gotamo mahatiyā parisāya parivuto dhammaṃ deseti. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ yena samaṇo gotamo tenupasaṅkameyyaṃ vicakkhukammāyā’’ti. Atha kho māro pāpimā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kinnu {pb:V:1.0131} sīhova nadasi, parisāyaṃ visārado;
::

::gathalast
Paṭimallo hi te atthi, vijitāvī nu maññasī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nadanti ve mahāvīrā, parisāsu visāradā;
::

::gathalast
Tathāgatā balappattā, tiṇṇā loke visattika’’nti.
::

Atha kho māro pāpimā ‘‘jānāti maṃ bhagavā, jānāti maṃ sugato’’ti dukkhī dummano tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 3. Sakalikasuttaṃ

{para:149} 149\. Evaṃ me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati maddakucchismiṃ migadāye. Tena kho pana samayena bhagavato pādo sakalikāya {pb:M:1.0112} khato hoti, bhusā sudaṃ bhagavato vedanā vattanti sārīrikā dukkhā tibbā kharā kaṭukā asātā amanāpā. Tā sudaṃ bhagavā sato sampajāno adhivāseti avihaññamāno. Atha kho bhagavā catugguṇaṃ saṅghāṭiṃ paññapetvā dakkhiṇena passena sīhaseyyaṃ kappesi {pb:T:1.0162} pāde pādaṃ accādhāya sato sampajāno. Atha kho māro pāpimā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Mandiyā nu kho sesi udāhu kāveyyamatto,
::

::gatha2
Atthā nu te sampacurā na santi;
::

::gatha3
Eko vivitte sayanāsanamhi,
::

::gathalast
Niddāmukho kimidaṃ soppase vā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na mandiyā sayāmi nāpi kāveyyamatto,
::

::gatha2
Atthaṃ sameccāhamapetasoko;
::

::gatha3
Eko vivitte sayanāsanamhi,
::

::gathalast
Sayāmahaṃ sabbabhūtānukampī.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yesampi sallaṃ urasi paviṭṭhaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Muhuṃ muhuṃ hadayaṃ vedhamānaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Tepīdha {pb:V:1.0132} soppaṃ labhare sasallā,
::

::gathalast
Tasmā {pb:P:1.0111} ahaṃ na supe vītasallo.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jaggaṃ na saṅke napi bhemi sottuṃ,
::

::gatha2
Rattindivā nānutapanti māmaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Hāniṃ na passāmi kuhiñci loke,
::

::gathalast
Tasmā supe sabbabhūtānukampī’’ti.
::

Atha {pb:T:1.0163} kho māro pāpimā ‘‘jānāti maṃ bhagavā, jānāti maṃ sugato’’ti dukkhī dummano tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 4. Patirūpasuttaṃ

{para:150} 150\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā kosalesu viharati ekasālāyaṃ brāhmaṇagāme. Tena kho pana samayena bhagavā mahatiyā gihiparisāya parivuto dhammaṃ deseti.

Atha {pb:M:1.0113} kho mārassa pāpimato etadahosi – ‘‘ayaṃ kho samaṇo gotamo mahatiyā gihiparisāya parivuto dhammaṃ deseti. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ yena samaṇo gotamo tenupasaṅkameyyaṃ vicakkhukammāyā’’ti. Atha kho māro pāpimā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Netaṃ tava patirūpaṃ, yadaññamanusāsasi;
::

::gathalast
Anurodhavirodhesu, mā sajjittho tadācara’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hitānukampī sambuddho, yadaññamanusāsati;
::

::gathalast
Anurodhavirodhehi, vippamutto tathāgato’’ti.
::

Atha {pb:V:1.0133} kho māro pāpimā ‘‘jānāti maṃ bhagavā, jānāti maṃ sugato’’ti dukkhī dummano tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 5. Mānasasuttaṃ

{para:151} 151\. Evaṃ me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Atha {pb:T:1.0164} kho māro pāpimā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Antalikkhacaro pāso, yvāyaṃ carati mānaso;
::

::gathalast
Tena taṃ bādhayissāmi, na me samaṇa mokkhasī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rūpā saddā rasā gandhā, phoṭṭhabbā ca manoramā;
::

::gathalast
Ettha me vigato chando, nihato tvamasi antakā’’ti.
::

Atha kho māro pāpimā ‘‘jānāti maṃ bhagavā, jānāti maṃ sugato’’ti dukkhī dummano tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 6. Pattasuttaṃ

{para:152} 152\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:P:1.0112}. Tena kho pana samayena bhagavā pañcannaṃ upādānakkhandhānaṃ upādāya bhikkhūnaṃ dhammiyā kathāya sandasseti samādapeti {note:samādāpeti (?)} samuttejeti sampahaṃseti. Te ca bhikkhū aṭṭhiṃ katvā {note:aṭṭhikatvā (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} manasi {pb:M:1.0114} katvā sabbacetasā {note:sabbacetaso (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.), sabbaṃ cetasā (ka.)} samannāharitvā ohitasotā dhammaṃ suṇanti.

Atha kho mārassa pāpimato etadahosi – ‘‘ayaṃ kho samaṇo gotamo pañcannaṃ upādānakkhandhānaṃ upādāya bhikkhūnaṃ dhammiyā kathāya sandasseti samādapeti samuttejeti sampahaṃseti. Te ca bhikkhū aṭṭhiṃ katvā manasi katvā sabbacetasā samannāharitvā ohitasotā {pb:V:1.0134} dhammaṃ suṇanti. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ yena samaṇo gotamo tenupasaṅkameyyaṃ vicakkhukammāyā’’ti.

Tena kho pana samayena sambahulā pattā abbhokāse nikkhittā honti. Atha {pb:T:1.0165} kho māro pāpimā balībaddavaṇṇaṃ abhinimminitvā yena te pattā tenupasaṅkami. Atha kho aññataro bhikkhu aññataraṃ bhikkhuṃ etadavoca – ‘‘bhikkhu, bhikkhu, eso balībaddo patte bhindeyyā’’ti. Evaṃ vutte bhagavā taṃ bhikkhuṃ etadavoca – ‘‘na so, bhikkhu, balībaddo. Māro eso pāpimā tumhākaṃ vicakkhukammāya āgato’’ti. Atha kho bhagavā ‘‘māro ayaṃ pāpimā’’ iti viditvā māraṃ pāpimantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Rūpaṃ vedayitaṃ saññā, viññāṇaṃ yañca saṅkhataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nesohamasmi netaṃ me, evaṃ tattha virajjati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ virattaṃ khemattaṃ, sabbasaṃyojanātigaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anvesaṃ sabbaṭṭhānesu, mārasenāpi nājjhagā’’ti.
::

Atha kho māro pāpimā…pe… tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 7. Chaphassāyatanasuttaṃ

{para:153} 153\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā vesāliyaṃ viharati mahāvane kūṭāgārasālāyaṃ. Tena {pb:P:1.0113} kho pana samayena bhagavā channaṃ phassāyatanānaṃ upādāya bhikkhūnaṃ dhammiyā kathāya sandasseti samādapeti samuttejeti sampahaṃseti. Te ca bhikkhū aṭṭhiṃ katvā manasi katvā sabbacetasā samannāharitvā ohitasotā dhammaṃ suṇanti.

Atha {pb:M:1.0115} kho mārassa pāpimato etadahosi – ‘‘ayaṃ kho samaṇo gotamo channaṃ phassāyatanānaṃ upādāya bhikkhūnaṃ dhammiyā kathāya sandasseti samādapeti samuttejeti sappahaṃseti{pb:T:1.0166}. Te ca bhikkhū aṭṭhiṃ katvā manasi katvā sabbacetasā samannāharitvā ohitasotā {pb:V:1.0135} dhammaṃ suṇanti. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ yena samaṇo gotamo tenupasaṅkameyyaṃ vicakkhukammāyā’’ti. Atha kho māro pāpimā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavato avidūre mahantaṃ bhayabheravaṃ saddamakāsi, apissudaṃ pathavī maññe undrīyati {note:udrīyati (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī) u + dara + ya + ti = udrīyati}. Atha kho aññataro bhikkhu aññataraṃ bhikkhuṃ etadavoca – ‘‘bhikkhu, bhikkhu, esā pathavī maññe undrīyatī’’ti. Evaṃ vutte, bhagavā taṃ bhikkhuṃ etadavoca – ‘‘nesā bhikkhu pathavī undrīyati. Māro eso pāpimā tumhākaṃ vicakkhukammāya āgato’’ti. Atha kho bhagavā ‘‘māro ayaṃ pāpimā’’ iti viditvā māraṃ pāpimantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Rūpā saddā rasā gandhā, phassā dhammā ca kevalā;
::

::gathalast
Etaṃ lokāmisaṃ ghoraṃ, ettha loko vimucchito.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etañca samatikkamma, sato buddhassa sāvako;
::

::gathalast
Māradheyyaṃ atikkamma, ādiccova virocatī’’ti.
::

Atha kho māro pāpimā…pe… tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 8. Piṇḍasuttaṃ

{para:154} 154\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā magadhesu viharati pañcasālāyaṃ brāhmaṇagāme. Tena {pb:P:1.0114} kho pana samayena pañcasālāyaṃ brāhmaṇagāme kumārikānaṃ {pb:T:1.0167} pāhunakāni bhavanti. Atha kho bhagavā pubbaṇhasamayaṃ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya pañcasālaṃ brāhmaṇagāmaṃ piṇḍāya pāvisi. Tena kho pana samayena pañcasāleyyakā brāhmaṇagahapatikā mārena pāpimatā anvāviṭṭhā bhavanti – mā samaṇo gotamo piṇḍamalatthāti.

Atha kho bhagavā yathādhotena pattena pañcasālaṃ brāhmaṇagāmaṃ piṇḍāya pāvisi tathādhotena {note:yathādhotena (?)} pattena paṭikkami. Atha kho māro pāpimā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘api {pb:M:1.0116} tvaṃ, samaṇa, piṇḍamalatthā’’ti? ‘‘Tathā nu tvaṃ, pāpima, akāsi yathāhaṃ piṇḍaṃ {pb:V:1.0136} na labheyya’’nti. ‘‘Tena hi, bhante, bhagavā dutiyampi pañcasālaṃ brāhmaṇagāmaṃ piṇḍāya pavisatu. Tathāhaṃ karissāmi yathā bhagavā piṇḍaṃ lacchatī’’ti.

::gatha1
‘‘Apuññaṃ pasavi māro, āsajja naṃ tathāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ nu maññasi pāpima, na me pāpaṃ vipaccati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Susukhaṃ vata jīvāma, yesaṃ no natthi kiñcanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pītibhakkhā bhavissāma, devā ābhassarā yathā’’ti.
::

Atha kho māro pāpimā ‘‘jānāti maṃ bhagavā, jānāti maṃ sugato’’ti dukkhī dummano tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 9. Kassakasuttaṃ

{para:155} 155\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Tena kho pana samayena bhagavā bhikkhūnaṃ nibbānapaṭisaṃyuttāya dhammiyā kathāya sandasseti samādapeti samuttejeti sampahaṃseti{pb:T:1.0168}. Te ca bhikkhū aṭṭhiṃ katvā manasi katvā sabbacetasā samannāharitvā ohitasotā dhammaṃ suṇanti.

Atha {pb:P:1.0115} kho mārassa pāpimato etadahosi – ‘‘ayaṃ kho samaṇo gotamo bhikkhūnaṃ nibbānapaṭisaṃyuttāya dhammiyā kathāya…pe… yaṃnūnāhaṃ yena samaṇo gotamo tenupasaṅkameyyaṃ vicakkhukammāyā’’ti. Atha kho māro pāpimā kassakavaṇṇaṃ abhinimminitvā mahantaṃ naṅgalaṃ khandhe karitvā dīghapācanayaṭṭhiṃ gahetvā haṭahaṭakeso sāṇasāṭinivattho kaddamamakkhitehi pādehi yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘api, samaṇa, balībadde addasā’’ti? ‘‘Kiṃ pana, pāpima, te balībaddehī’’ti? ‘‘Mameva, samaṇa, cakkhu, mama rūpā, mama cakkhusamphassaviññāṇāyatanaṃ. Kuhiṃ me, samaṇa, gantvā mokkhasi? Mameva, samaṇa, sotaṃ, mama saddā…pe… mameva, samaṇa, ghānaṃ, mama gandhā; mameva, samaṇa, jivhā, mama rasā; mameva, samaṇa, kāyo, mama phoṭṭhabbā; mameva, samaṇa, mano, mama dhammā, mama manosamphassaviññāṇāyatanaṃ. Kuhiṃ me, samaṇa, gantvā mokkhasī’’ti?

‘‘Taveva{pb:V:1.0137}{pb:M:1.0117}, pāpima, cakkhu, tava rūpā, tava cakkhusamphassaviññāṇāyatanaṃ. Yattha ca kho, pāpima, natthi cakkhu, natthi rūpā, natthi cakkhusamphassaviññāṇāyatanaṃ, agati tava tattha, pāpima. Taveva, pāpima{pb:T:1.0169}, sotaṃ, tava saddā, tava sotasamphassaviññāṇāyatanaṃ. Yattha ca kho, pāpima, natthi sotaṃ, natthi saddā, natthi sotasamphassaviññāṇāyatanaṃ, agati tava tattha, pāpima. Taveva{pb:P:1.0116}, pāpima, ghānaṃ, tava gandhā, tava ghānasamphassaviññāṇāyatanaṃ. Yattha ca kho, pāpima, natthi ghānaṃ, natthi gandhā, natthi ghānasamphassaviññāṇāyatanaṃ, agati tava tattha, pāpima. Taveva, pāpima, jivhā, tava rasā, tava jivhāsamphassaviññāṇāyatanaṃ…pe… taveva, pāpima, kāyo, tava phoṭṭhabbā, tava kāyasamphassaviññāṇāyatanaṃ…pe… taveva, pāpima, mano, tava dhammā, tava manosamphassaviññāṇāyatanaṃ. Yattha ca kho, pāpima, natthi mano, natthi dhammā, natthi manosamphassaviññāṇāyatanaṃ, agati tava tattha, pāpimā’’ti.

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ vadanti mama yidanti, ye vadanti mamanti ca;
::

::gathalast
Ettha ce te mano atthi, na me samaṇa mokkhasī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ vadanti na taṃ mayhaṃ, ye vadanti na te ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ pāpima jānāhi, na me maggampi dakkhasī’’ti.
::

Atha kho māro pāpimā…pe… tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 10. Rajjasuttaṃ

{para:156} 156\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā kosalesu viharati himavantapadese {note:himavantapasse (sī.)} araññakuṭikāyaṃ. Atha kho bhagavato rahogatassa paṭisallīnassa evaṃ cetaso {pb:T:1.0170} parivitakko udapādi – ‘‘sakkā nu kho rajjaṃ kāretuṃ ahanaṃ aghātayaṃ ajinaṃ ajāpayaṃ asocaṃ asocāpayaṃ dhammenā’’ti?

Atha kho māro pāpimā bhagavato cetasā cetoparivitakkamaññāya yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘kāretu, bhante, bhagavā rajjaṃ, kāretu, sugato, rajjaṃ ahanaṃ aghātayaṃ ajinaṃ ajāpayaṃ asocaṃ asocāpayaṃ dhammenā’’ti. ‘‘Kiṃ pana me tvaṃ, pāpima, passasi yaṃ maṃ tvaṃ evaṃ vadesi – ‘kāretu, bhante, bhagavā rajjaṃ, kāretu sugato{pb:V:1.0138}, rajjaṃ ahanaṃ aghātayaṃ ajinaṃ ajāpayaṃ asocaṃ asocāpayaṃ {pb:M:1.0118} dhammenā’’’ti? ‘‘Bhagavatā kho, bhante, cattāro iddhipādā bhāvitā bahulīkatā yānīkatā vatthukatā anuṭṭhitā paricitā susamāraddhā. Ākaṅkhamāno ca, bhante, bhagavā himavantaṃ pabbatarājaṃ suvaṇṇaṃ tveva adhimucceyya suvaṇṇañca panassā’’ti {note:suvaṇṇapabbatassāti (sī. syā. kaṃ.), suvaṇṇañca pabbatassāti (pī.)}.

::gatha1
‘‘Pabbatassa {pb:P:1.0117} suvaṇṇassa, jātarūpassa kevalo;
::

::gathalast
Dvittāva nālamekassa, iti vidvā samañcare.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo dukkhamaddakkhi yatonidānaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Kāmesu so jantu kathaṃ nameyya;
::

::gatha3
Upadhiṃ viditvā saṅgoti loke,
::

::gathalast
Tasseva jantu vinayāya sikkhe’’ti.
::

Atha kho {pb:T:1.0171} māro pāpimā ‘‘jānāti maṃ bhagavā, jānāti maṃ sugato’’ti dukkhī dummano tatthevantaradhāyīti.

::centre
Dutiyo vaggo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Pāsāṇo sīho sakalikaṃ {note:sakkhalikaṃ (ka.)}, patirūpañca mānasaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Pattaṃ āyatanaṃ piṇḍaṃ, kassakaṃ rajjena te dasāti.
::

#### 3. Tatiyavaggo

#### 1. Sambahulasuttaṃ

{para:157} 157\. Evaṃ {pb:T:1.0172}{pb:V:1.0139} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sakkesu viharati silāvatiyaṃ. Tena kho pana samayena sambahulā bhikkhū bhagavato avidūre appamattā ātāpino pahitattā viharanti. Atha kho māro pāpimā brāhmaṇavaṇṇaṃ abhinimminitvā mahantena jaṭaṇḍuvena ajinakkhipanivattho jiṇṇo gopānasivaṅko ghurughurupassāsī udumbaradaṇḍaṃ gahetvā yena te bhikkhū tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā te bhikkhū etadavoca – ‘‘daharā bhavanto {pb:M:1.0119} pabbajitā susū kāḷakesā bhadrena yobbanena samannāgatā paṭhamena vayasā anikkīḷitāvino kāmesu. Bhuñjantu bhavanto mānusake kāme. Mā sandiṭṭhikaṃ hitvā kālikaṃ anudhāvitthā’’ti. ‘‘Na kho mayaṃ, brāhmaṇa, sandiṭṭhikaṃ hitvā kālikaṃ anudhāvāma. Kālikañca kho mayaṃ, brāhmaṇa, hitvā sandiṭṭhikaṃ anudhāvāma. Kālikā hi, brāhmaṇa, kāmā vuttā bhagavatā bahudukkhā bahupāyāsā, ādīnavo ettha bhiyyo. Sandiṭṭhiko ayaṃ dhammo akāliko ehipassiko opaneyyiko paccattaṃ veditabbo viññūhī’’ti. Evaṃ {pb:P:1.0118} vutte, māro pāpimā sīsaṃ okampetvā jivhaṃ nillāletvā tivisākhaṃ nalāṭe nalāṭikaṃ vuṭṭhāpetvā daṇḍamolubbha pakkāmi.

Atha {pb:T:1.0173} kho te bhikkhū yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ nisīdiṃsu. Ekamantaṃ nisinnā kho te bhikkhū bhagavantaṃ etadavocuṃ – ‘‘idha mayaṃ, bhante, bhagavato avidūre appamattā ātāpino pahitattā viharāma. Atha kho, bhante, aññataro brāhmaṇo mahantena jaṭaṇḍuvena ajinakkhipanivattho jiṇṇo gopānasivaṅko ghurughurupassāsī udumbaradaṇḍaṃ gahetvā yena mayaṃ tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā amhe etadavoca – ‘daharā bhavanto pabbajitā susū kāḷakesā bhadrena yobbanena samannāgatā paṭhamena vayasā anikkīḷitāvino kāmesu. Bhuñjantu bhavanto mānusake kāme. Mā sandiṭṭhikaṃ hitvā kālikaṃ anudhāvitthā’ti. Evaṃ vutte, mayaṃ, bhante, taṃ brāhmaṇaṃ etadavocumha – ‘na kho mayaṃ, brāhmaṇa, sandiṭṭhikaṃ hitvā kālikaṃ anudhāvāma. Kālikañca kho mayaṃ, brāhmaṇa, hitvā sandiṭṭhikaṃ anudhāvāma. Kālikā hi, brāhmaṇa, kāmā {pb:V:1.0140} vuttā bhagavatā bahudukkhā bahupāyāsā, ādīnavo ettha bhiyyo. Sandiṭṭhiko ayaṃ dhammo akāliko ehipassiko opaneyyiko paccattaṃ veditabbo viññūhī’ti. Evaṃ vutte, bhante, so brāhmaṇo sīsaṃ okampetvā jivhaṃ nillāletvā tivisākhaṃ nalāṭe nalāṭikaṃ vuṭṭhāpetvā daṇḍamolubbha pakkanto’’ti.

‘‘Neso, bhikkhave, brāhmaṇo. Māro eso pāpimā tumhākaṃ vicakkhukammāya āgato’’ti. Atha kho bhagavā etamatthaṃ viditvā {pb:T:1.0174} tāyaṃ velāyaṃ imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Yo {pb:M:1.0120} dukkhamaddakkhi yatonidānaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Kāmesu so jantu kathaṃ nameyya;
::

::gatha3
Upadhiṃ viditvā saṅgoti loke,
::

::gathalast
Tasseva jantu vinayāya sikkhe’’ti.
::

#### 2. Samiddhisuttaṃ

{para:158} 158\. Ekaṃ {pb:P:1.0119} samayaṃ bhagavā sakkesu viharati silāvatiyaṃ. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā samiddhi bhagavato avidūre appamatto ātāpī pahitatto viharati. Atha kho āyasmato samiddhissa rahogatassa paṭisallīnassa evaṃ cetaso parivitakko udapādi – ‘‘lābhā vata me, suladdhaṃ vata me, yassa me satthā arahaṃ sammāsambuddho. Lābhā vata me, suladdhaṃ vata me, yvāhaṃ evaṃ svākkhāte dhammavinaye pabbajito. Lābhā vata me, suladdhaṃ vata me, yassa me sabrahmacārino sīlavanto kalyāṇadhammā’’ti. Atha kho māro pāpimā āyasmato samiddhissa cetasā cetoparivitakkamaññāya yenāyasmā samiddhi tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmato samiddhissa avidūre mahantaṃ bhayabheravaṃ saddamakāsi, apissudaṃ pathavī maññe undrīyati.

Atha kho āyasmā samiddhi yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi. Ekamantaṃ nisinno {pb:T:1.0175} āyasmā samiddhi bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘idhāhaṃ, bhante, bhagavato avidūre appamatto ātāpī pahitatto viharāmi. Tassa mayhaṃ, bhante, rahogatassa {pb:V:1.0141} paṭisallīnassa evaṃ cetaso parivitakko udapādi – ‘lābhā vata me, suladdhaṃ vata me, yassa me satthā arahaṃ sammāsambuddho. Lābhā vata me, suladdhaṃ vata me, yvāhaṃ evaṃ svākkhāte dhammavinaye pabbajito. Lābhā vata me, suladdhaṃ vata me, yassa me sabrahmacārino sīlavanto kalyāṇadhammā’ti. Tassa mayhaṃ, bhante, avidūre mahābhayabheravasaddo ahosi, apissudaṃ pathavī maññe undrīyatī’’ti.

‘‘Nesā, samiddhi, pathavī undrīyati. Māro eso pāpimā tuyhaṃ vicakkhukammāya āgato. Gaccha tvaṃ, samiddhi, tattheva appamatto ātāpī pahitatto viharāhī’’ti. ‘‘Evaṃ, bhante’’ti kho āyasmā samiddhi bhagavato paṭissutvā {pb:M:1.0121}{pb:P:1.0120} uṭṭhāyāsanā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaṃ katvā pakkāmi. Dutiyampi kho āyasmā samiddhi tattheva appamatto ātāpī pahitatto vihāsi. Dutiyampi kho āyasmato samiddhissa rahogatassa paṭisallīnassa…pe… dutiyampi kho māro pāpimā āyasmato samiddhissa cetasā cetoparivitakkamaññāya…pe… apissudaṃ pathavī maññe undrīyati. Atha kho āyasmā samiddhi māraṃ {pb:T:1.0176} pāpimantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Saddhāyāhaṃ pabbajito, agārasmā anagāriyaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Sati paññā ca me buddhā, cittañca susamāhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kāmaṃ karassu rūpāni, neva maṃ byādhayissasī’’ti.
::

Atha kho māro pāpimā ‘‘jānāti maṃ samiddhi bhikkhū’’ti dukkhī dummano tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 3. Godhikasuttaṃ

{para:159} 159\. Evaṃ me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati veḷuvane kalandakanivāpe. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā godhiko isigilipasse viharati kāḷasilāyaṃ. Atha kho āyasmā godhiko appamatto ātāpī pahitatto viharanto sāmayikaṃ cetovimuttiṃ phusi. Atha kho āyasmā godhiko tamhā sāmayikāya cetovimuttiyā parihāyi{pb:V:1.0142}. Dutiyampi kho āyasmā godhiko appamatto ātāpī pahitatto viharanto sāmayikaṃ cetovimuttiṃ phusi. Dutiyampi kho āyasmā godhiko tamhā sāmayikāya cetovimuttiyā parihāyi. Tatiyampi kho āyasmā godhiko appamatto ātāpī pahitatto viharanto sāmayikaṃ cetovimuttiṃ phusi. Tatiyampi kho āyasmā godhiko tamhā…pe… parihāyi. Catutthampi kho āyasmā godhiko appamatto…pe… vimuttiṃ phusi{pb:T:1.0177}. Catutthampi kho āyasmā godhiko tamhā…pe… parihāyi. Pañcamampi {pb:P:1.0121} kho āyasmā godhiko…pe… cetovimuttiṃ phusi. Pañcamampi kho āyasmā…pe… vimuttiyā parihāyi. Chaṭṭhampi kho āyasmā godhiko appamatto ātāpī pahitatto viharanto sāmayikaṃ cetovimuttiṃ phusi. Chaṭṭhampi kho āyasmā godhiko tamhā sāmayikāya cetovimuttiyā parihāyi. Sattamampi {pb:M:1.0122} kho āyasmā godhiko appamatto ātāpī pahitatto viharanto sāmayikaṃ cetovimuttiṃ phusi.

Atha kho āyasmato godhikassa etadahosi – ‘‘yāva chaṭṭhaṃ khvāhaṃ sāmayikāya cetovimuttiyā parihīno. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ satthaṃ āhareyya’’nti. Atha kho māro pāpimā āyasmato godhikassa cetasā cetoparivitakkamaññāya yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Mahāvīra mahāpañña, iddhiyā yasasā jala;
::

::gathalast
Sabbaverabhayātīta, pāde vandāmi cakkhuma.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sāvako te mahāvīra, maraṇaṃ maraṇābhibhū;
::

::gathalast
Ākaṅkhati cetayati, taṃ nisedha jutindhara.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kathañhi bhagavā tuyhaṃ, sāvako sāsane rato;
::

::gathalast
Appattamānaso sekkho, kālaṃ kayirā janesutā’’ti.
::

Tena kho pana samayena āyasmato godhikena satthaṃ āharitaṃ hoti. Atha kho bhagavā ‘‘māro ayaṃ pāpimā’’ iti viditvā māraṃ {pb:T:1.0178} pāpimantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Evañhi {pb:V:1.0143} dhīrā kubbanti, nāvakaṅkhanti jīvitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Samūlaṃ taṇhamabbuyha, godhiko parinibbuto’’ti.
::

Atha kho bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi – ‘‘āyāma, bhikkhave, yena isigilipassaṃ kāḷasilā tenupasaṅkamissāma yattha godhikena kulaputtena satthaṃ āharita’’nti. ‘‘Evaṃ, bhante’’ti kho te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṃ.

Atha kho bhagavā sambahulehi bhikkhūhi saddhiṃ yena isigilipassaṃ kāḷasilā tenupasaṅkami. Addasā kho bhagavā āyasmantaṃ godhikaṃ dūratova mañcake vivattakkhandhaṃ semānaṃ {note:seyyamānaṃ (syā. kaṃ.), soppamānaṃ (ka.)}. Tena {pb:P:1.0122} kho pana samayena dhūmāyitattaṃ timirāyitattaṃ gacchateva purimaṃ disaṃ, gacchati pacchimaṃ disaṃ, gacchati uttaraṃ disaṃ, gacchati dakkhiṇaṃ disaṃ, gacchati uddhaṃ, gacchati adho, gacchati anudisaṃ.

Atha {pb:M:1.0123} kho bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi – ‘‘passatha no tumhe, bhikkhave, etaṃ dhūmāyitattaṃ timirāyitattaṃ gacchateva purimaṃ disaṃ, gacchati pacchimaṃ disaṃ, gacchati uttaraṃ disaṃ, gacchati dakkhiṇaṃ disaṃ, gacchati uddhaṃ, gacchati adho, gacchati anudisa’’nti? ‘‘Evaṃ, bhante’’. ‘‘Eso kho, bhikkhave, māro pāpimā godhikassa kulaputtassa viññāṇaṃ samanvesati – ‘kattha godhikassa kulaputtassa viññāṇaṃ patiṭṭhita’nti? Appatiṭṭhitena ca, bhikkhave, viññāṇena godhiko kulaputto parinibbuto’’ti. Atha {pb:T:1.0179} kho māro pāpimā beluvapaṇḍuvīṇaṃ ādāya yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Uddhaṃ adho ca tiriyaṃ, disā anudisā svahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anvesaṃ nādhigacchāmi, godhiko so kuhiṃ gato’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo {note:so (sī. pī.)} dhīro dhitisampanno, jhāyī jhānarato sadā;
::

::gathalast
Ahorattaṃ anuyuñjaṃ, jīvitaṃ anikāmayaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jetvāna {pb:V:1.0144} maccuno {note:bhetvā namucino (sī.)} senaṃ, anāgantvā punabbhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Samūlaṃ taṇhamabbuyha, godhiko parinibbuto’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa sokaparetassa, vīṇā kacchā abhassatha;
::

::gathalast
Tato so dummano yakkho, tatthevantaradhāyathā’’ti {note:tatthevantaradhāyithāti (syā. kaṃ.), tattheva antaradhāyīti (ka.)}.
::

#### 4. Sattavassānubandhasuttaṃ

{para:160} 160\. Evaṃ me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā uruvelāyaṃ viharati najjā nerañjarāya tīre ajapālanigrodhe. Tena kho pana samayena māro pāpimā sattavassāni bhagavantaṃ anubandho hoti otārāpekkho otāraṃ alabhamāno. Atha kho māro pāpimā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sokāvatiṇṇo {pb:P:1.0123} nu vanamhi jhāyasi,
::

::gatha2
Vittaṃ nu jīno uda patthayāno;
::

::gatha3
Āguṃ nu gāmasmimakāsi kiñci,
::

::gatha2
Kasmā {pb:T:1.0180} janena na karosi sakkhiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sakkhī na sampajjati kenaci te’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sokassa {pb:M:1.0124} mūlaṃ palikhāya sabbaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Anāgu jhāyāmi asocamāno;
::

::gatha3
Chetvāna sabbaṃ bhavalobhajappaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Anāsavo jhāyāmi pamattabandhū’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ vadanti mama yidanti, ye vadanti mamanti ca;
::

::gathalast
Ettha ce te mano atthi, na me samaṇa mokkhasī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ {pb:V:1.0145} vadanti na taṃ mayhaṃ, ye vadanti na te ahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ pāpima jānāhi, na me maggampi dakkhasī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace maggaṃ anubuddhaṃ, khemaṃ amatagāminaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Apehi gaccha tvameveko, kimaññamanusāsasī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Amaccudheyyaṃ pucchanti, ye janā pāragāmino;
::

::gathalast
Tesāhaṃ puṭṭho akkhāmi, yaṃ saccaṃ taṃ nirūpadhi’’nti.
::

‘‘Seyyathāpi, bhante, gāmassa vā nigamassa vā avidūre pokkharaṇī. Tatrassa kakkaṭako. Atha kho, bhante, sambahulā kumārakā vā kumārikāyo vā tamhā gāmā vā nigamā vā nikkhamitvā yena sā pokkharaṇī tenupasaṅkameyyuṃ; upasaṅkamitvā taṃ kakkaṭakaṃ udakā uddharitvā thale patiṭṭhapeyyuṃ. Yaṃ yadeva hi so, bhante, kakkaṭako aḷaṃ abhininnāmeyya taṃ tadeva te kumārakā vā {pb:T:1.0181} kumārikāyo vā kaṭṭhena vā kathalāya vā sañchindeyyuṃ sambhañjeyyuṃ sampalibhañjeyyuṃ. Evañhi so, bhante, kakkaṭako sabbehi aḷehi sañchinnehi sambhaggehi sampalibhaggehi abhabbo taṃ pokkharaṇiṃ otarituṃ. Evameva kho, bhante, yāni kānici visūkāyikāni {note:yāni visukāyikāni (sī. pī. ka.)} visevitāni vipphanditāni, sabbāni tāni {note:kānici kānici sabbāni (sī. pī. ka.)} bhagavatā sañchinnāni sambhaggāni {pb:P:1.0124} sampalibhaggāni. Abhabbo dānāhaṃ, bhante, puna bhagavantaṃ upasaṅkamituṃ yadidaṃ otārāpekkho’’ti. Atha kho māro pāpimā bhagavato santike imā nibbejanīyā gāthāyo abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Medavaṇṇañca pāsāṇaṃ, vāyaso anupariyagā;
::

::gathalast
Apettha muduṃ vindema, api assādanā siyā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aladdhā {pb:M:1.0125} tattha assādaṃ, vāyasetto apakkame;
::

::gathalast
Kākova selamāsajja, nibbijjāpema gotamā’’ti.
::

#### 5. Māradhītusuttaṃ

{para:161} 161\. Atha {pb:V:1.0146} kho māro pāpimā bhagavato santike imā nibbejanīyā gāthāyo abhāsitvā tamhā ṭhānā apakkamma bhagavato avidūre pathaviyaṃ pallaṅkena nisīdi tuṇhībhūto maṅkubhūto pattakkhandho adhomukho pajjhāyanto appaṭibhāno kaṭṭhena bhūmiṃ vilikhanto. Atha kho taṇhā ca arati ca ragā ca māradhītaro yena māro pāpimā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā māraṃ pāpimantaṃ gāthāya {pb:T:1.0182} ajjhabhāsiṃsu –

::gatha1
‘‘Kenāsi dummano tāta, purisaṃ kaṃ nu socasi;
::

::gatha2
Mayaṃ taṃ rāgapāsena, āraññamiva kuñjaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Bandhitvā ānayissāma, vasago te bhavissatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Arahaṃ sugato loke, na rāgena suvānayo;
::

::gathalast
Māradheyyaṃ atikkanto, tasmā socāmahaṃ bhusa’’nti.
::

Atha kho taṇhā ca arati ca ragā ca māradhītaro yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ etadavocuṃ – ‘‘pāde te, samaṇa, paricāremā’’ti. Atha kho bhagavā na manasākāsi, yathā taṃ anuttare upadhisaṅkhaye vimutto.

Atha kho taṇhā ca arati ca ragā ca māradhītaro ekamantaṃ apakkamma evaṃ samacintesuṃ – ‘‘uccāvacā kho purisānaṃ adhippāyā. Yaṃnūna mayaṃ ekasataṃ ekasataṃ kumārivaṇṇasataṃ abhinimmineyyāmā’’ti. Atha {pb:P:1.0125} kho taṇhā ca arati ca ragā ca māradhītaro ekasataṃ ekasataṃ kumārivaṇṇasataṃ abhinimminitvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ etadavocuṃ – ‘‘pāde te, samaṇa, paricāremā’’ti. Tampi bhagavā na manasākāsi, yathā taṃ anuttare upadhisaṅkhaye vimutto.

Atha kho taṇhā ca arati ca ragā ca māradhītaro ekamantaṃ apakkamma evaṃ samacintesuṃ – ‘‘uccāvacā kho purisānaṃ adhippāyā{pb:T:1.0183}. Yaṃnūna mayaṃ ekasataṃ ekasataṃ avijātavaṇṇasataṃ abhinimmineyyāmā’’ti. Atha kho taṇhā ca arati ca ragā ca māradhītaro ekasataṃ ekasataṃ {pb:M:1.0126} avijātavaṇṇasataṃ {pb:V:1.0147} abhinimminitvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ etadavocuṃ – ‘‘pāde te, samaṇa, paricāremā’’ti. Tampi bhagavā na manasākāsi, yathā taṃ anuttare upadhisaṅkhaye vimutto.

Atha kho taṇhā ca…pe… yaṃnūna mayaṃ ekasataṃ ekasataṃ sakiṃ vijātavaṇṇasataṃ abhinimmineyyāmāti. Atha kho taṇhā ca…pe… sakiṃ vijātavaṇṇasataṃ abhinimminitvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ etadavocuṃ – ‘‘pāde te, samaṇa, paricāremā’’ti. Tampi bhagavā na manasākāsi, yathā taṃ anuttare upadhisaṅkhaye vimutto.

Atha kho taṇhā ca…pe… yaṃnūna mayaṃ ekasataṃ ekasataṃ duvijātavaṇṇasataṃ abhinimmineyyāmāti. Atha kho taṇhā ca…pe… duvijātavaṇṇasataṃ abhinimminitvā yena bhagavā…pe… yathā taṃ anuttare upadhisaṅkhaye vimutto. Atha kho taṇhā ca…pe… majjhimitthivaṇṇasataṃ abhinimmineyyāmāti. Atha kho taṇhā ca…pe… majjhimitthivaṇṇasataṃ abhinimminitvā…pe… anuttare upadhisaṅkhaye vimutto.

Atha kho taṇhā ca…pe… mahitthivaṇṇasataṃ abhinimmineyyāmāti{pb:T:1.0184}. Atha kho taṇhā ca…pe… mahitthivaṇṇasataṃ abhinimminitvā yena bhagavā…pe… anuttare upadhisaṅkhaye vimutto. Atha kho taṇhā ca arati ca ragā ca māradhītaro ekamantaṃ apakkamma etadavocuṃ – saccaṃ kira no pitā avoca –

::gatha1
‘‘Arahaṃ sugato loke, na rāgena suvānayo;
::

::gathalast
Māradheyyaṃ atikkanto, tasmā socāmahaṃ bhusa’’nti.
::

‘‘Yañhi mayaṃ samaṇaṃ vā brāhmaṇaṃ vā avītarāgaṃ iminā upakkamena upakkameyyāma hadayaṃ vāssa phaleyya, uṇhaṃ lohitaṃ vā mukhato uggaccheyya, ummādaṃ {pb:P:1.0126} vā pāpuṇeyya cittakkhepaṃ {pb:V:1.0148} vā. Seyyathā vā pana naḷo harito luto ussussati visussati milāyati; evameva ussusseyya visusseyya milāyeyyā’’ti.

Atha {pb:M:1.0127} kho taṇhā ca arati ca ragā ca māradhītaro yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhaṃsu. Ekamantaṃ ṭhitā kho taṇhā māradhītā bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sokāvatiṇṇo nu vanamhi jhāyasi,
::

::gatha2
Vittaṃ nu jīno uda patthayāno;
::

::gatha3
Āguṃ nu gāmasmimakāsi kiñci,
::

::gatha2
Kasmā janena na karosi sakkhiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sakkhī na sampajjati kenaci te’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atthassa {pb:T:1.0185} pattiṃ hadayassa santiṃ,
::

::gatha2
Jetvāna senaṃ piyasātarūpaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Ekohaṃ {note:ekāhaṃ (syā. kaṃ. pī. ka.)} jhāyaṃ sukhamanubodhiṃ,
::

::gatha2
Tasmā janena na karomi sakkhiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sakkhī na sampajjati kenaci me’’ti.
::

Atha kho arati {note:arati ca (ka.)} māradhītā bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kathaṃ vihārībahulodha bhikkhu,
::

::gatha2
Pañcoghatiṇṇo atarīdha chaṭṭhaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Kathaṃ jhāyiṃ {note:kathaṃ jhāyaṃ (syā. kaṃ. pī.), kathajjhāyaṃ (ka.)} bahulaṃ kāmasaññā,
::

::gathalast
Paribāhirā honti aladdha yo ta’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Passaddhakāyo suvimuttacitto,
::

::gatha2
Asaṅkharāno satimā anoko;
::

::gatha3
Aññāya {pb:V:1.0149} dhammaṃ avitakkajhāyī,
::

::gathalast
Na kuppati na sarati na thino {note:na kuppatī nassaratī na thīno (sī.)}.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃvihārībahulodha bhikkhu,
::

::gatha2
Pañcoghatiṇṇo atarīdha chaṭṭhaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Evaṃ jhāyiṃ bahulaṃ kāmasaññā,
::

::gathalast
Paribāhirā honti aladdha yo ta’’nti.
::

Atha {pb:M:1.0128}{pb:P:1.0127} kho ragā {note:ragāca (ka.)} māradhītā bhagavato santike gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Acchejja {pb:T:1.0186} taṇhaṃ gaṇasaṅghacārī,
::

::gatha2
Addhā carissanti {note:tarissanti (sī.)} bahū ca saddhā;
::

::gatha3
Bahuṃ vatāyaṃ janataṃ anoko,
::

::gathalast
Acchejja nessati maccurājassa pāra’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nayanti ve mahāvīrā, saddhammena tathāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Dhammena nayamānānaṃ, kā usūyā vijānata’’nti.
::

Atha kho taṇhā ca arati ca ragā ca māradhītaro yena māro pāpimā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu. Addasā kho māro pāpimā taṇhañca aratiñca ragañca māradhītaro dūratova āgacchantiyo. Disvāna gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Bālā kumudanāḷehi, pabbataṃ abhimatthatha {note:abhimanthatha (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Giriṃ nakhena khanatha, ayo dantehi khādatha.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Selaṃva sirasūhacca {note:sirasi ūhacca (sī.), sirasi ohacca (syā. kaṃ.)}, pātāle gādhamesatha;
::

::gathalast
Khāṇuṃva urasāsajja, nibbijjāpetha gotamā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Daddallamānā {pb:V:1.0150} āgañchuṃ, taṇhā ca aratī ragā;
::

::gathalast
Tā tattha panudī satthā, tūlaṃ bhaṭṭhaṃva māluto’’ti.
::

::centre
Tatiyo vaggo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Sambahulā {pb:T:1.0187} samiddhi ca, godhikaṃ sattavassāni;
::

::gathalast
Dhītaraṃ desitaṃ buddha, seṭṭhena imaṃ mārapañcakanti.
::

::centre
Mārasaṃyuttaṃ samattaṃ.
::

### 5. Bhikkhunīsaṃyuttaṃ

#### 1. Āḷavikāsuttaṃ

{para:162} 162\. Evaṃ {pb:T:1.0188}{pb:V:1.0151}{pb:P:1.0128}{pb:M:1.0129} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Atha kho āḷavikā bhikkhunī pubbaṇhasamayaṃ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya sāvatthiṃ piṇḍāya pāvisi. Sāvatthiyaṃ piṇḍāya caritvā pacchābhattaṃ piṇḍapātapaṭikkantā yena andhavanaṃ tenupasaṅkami vivekatthinī. Atha kho māro pāpimā āḷavikāya bhikkhuniyā bhayaṃ chambhitattaṃ lomahaṃsaṃ uppādetukāmo vivekamhā cāvetukāmo yena āḷavikā bhikkhunī tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā āḷavikaṃ bhikkhuniṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Natthi nissaraṇaṃ loke, kiṃ vivekena kāhasi;
::

::gathalast
Bhuñjassu kāmaratiyo, māhu pacchānutāpinī’’ti.
::

Atha kho āḷavikāya bhikkhuniyā etadahosi – ‘‘ko nu khvāyaṃ manusso vā amanusso vā gāthaṃ bhāsatī’’ti? Atha kho āḷavikāya bhikkhuniyā etadahosi – ‘‘māro kho ayaṃ pāpimā mama bhayaṃ chambhitattaṃ lomahaṃsaṃ uppādetukāmo vivekamhā cāvetukāmo gāthaṃ bhāsatī’’ti. Atha kho āḷavikā bhikkhunī ‘‘māro ayaṃ pāpimā’’ iti viditvā māraṃ pāpimantaṃ {pb:T:1.0189} gāthāhi paccabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Atthi nissaraṇaṃ loke, paññāya me suphussitaṃ {note:suphassitaṃ (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Pamattabandhu pāpima, na tvaṃ jānāsi taṃ padaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sattisūlūpamā {pb:V:1.0152} kāmā, khandhāsaṃ adhikuṭṭanā;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ tvaṃ kāmaratiṃ brūsi, arati mayha sā ahū’’ti.
::

Atha {pb:P:1.0129} kho māro pāpimā ‘‘jānāti maṃ āḷavikā bhikkhunī’’ti dukkhī dummano tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 2. Somāsuttaṃ

{para:163} 163\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:M:1.0130}. Atha kho somā bhikkhunī pubbaṇhasamayaṃ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya sāvatthiṃ piṇḍāya pāvisi. Sāvatthiyaṃ piṇḍāya caritvā pacchābhattaṃ piṇḍapātapaṭikkantā yena andhavanaṃ tenupasaṅkami divāvihārāya. Andhavanaṃ ajjhogāhetvā aññatarasmiṃ rukkhamūle divāvihāraṃ nisīdi. Atha kho māro pāpimā somāya bhikkhuniyā bhayaṃ chambhitattaṃ lomahaṃsaṃ uppādetukāmo samādhimhā cāvetukāmo yena somā bhikkhunī tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā somaṃ bhikkhuniṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ taṃ isīhi pattabbaṃ, ṭhānaṃ durabhisambhavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Na taṃ dvaṅgulapaññāya, sakkā pappotumitthiyā’’ti.
::

Atha kho somāya bhikkhuniyā etadahosi – ‘‘ko nu khvāyaṃ manusso vā amanusso vā gāthaṃ bhāsatī’’ti? Atha kho somāya bhikkhuniyā {pb:T:1.0190} etadahosi – ‘‘māro kho ayaṃ pāpimā mama bhayaṃ chambhitattaṃ lomahaṃsaṃ uppādetukāmo samādhimhā cāvetukāmo gāthaṃ bhāsatī’’ti. Atha kho somā bhikkhunī ‘‘māro ayaṃ pāpimā’’ iti viditvā māraṃ pāpimantaṃ gāthāhi paccabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Itthibhāvo kiṃ kayirā, cittamhi susamāhite;
::

::gathalast
Ñāṇamhi vattamānamhi, sammā dhammaṃ vipassato.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yassa {pb:V:1.0153} nūna siyā evaṃ, itthāhaṃ purisoti vā;
::

::gathalast
Kiñci vā pana aññasmi {note:asmīti (syā. kaṃ. pī.)}, taṃ māro vattumarahatī’’ti.
::

Atha kho māro pāpimā ‘‘jānāti maṃ somā bhikkhunī’’ti dukkhī dummano tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 3. Kisāgotamīsuttaṃ

{para:164} 164\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Atha kho kisāgotamī bhikkhunī pubbaṇhasamayaṃ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya sāvatthiṃ piṇḍāya pāvisi. Sāvatthiyaṃ piṇḍāya caritvā pacchābhattaṃ piṇḍapātapaṭikkantā {pb:P:1.0130} yena andhavanaṃ tenupasaṅkami{pb:M:1.0131}, divāvihārāya. Andhavanaṃ ajjhogāhetvā aññatarasmiṃ rukkhamūle divāvihāraṃ nisīdi. Atha kho māro pāpimā kisāgotamiyā bhikkhuniyā bhayaṃ chambhitattaṃ lomahaṃsaṃ uppādetukāmo samādhimhā cāvetukāmo yena kisāgotamī bhikkhunī tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā kisāgotamiṃ bhikkhuniṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ {pb:T:1.0191} nu tvaṃ mataputtāva, ekamāsi rudammukhī;
::

::gathalast
Vanamajjhagatā ekā, purisaṃ nu gavesasī’’ti.
::

Atha kho kisāgotamiyā bhikkhuniyā etadahosi – ‘‘ko nu khvāyaṃ manusso vā amanusso vā gāthaṃ bhāsatī’’ti? Atha kho kisāgotamiyā bhikkhuniyā etadahosi – ‘‘māro kho ayaṃ pāpimā mama bhayaṃ chambhitattaṃ lomahaṃsaṃ uppādetukāmo samādhimhā cāvetukāmo gāthaṃ bhāsatī’’ti.

Atha kho kisāgotamī bhikkhunī ‘‘māro ayaṃ pāpimā’’ iti viditvā māraṃ pāpimantaṃ gāthāhi paccabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Accantaṃ {pb:V:1.0154} mataputtāmhi, purisā etadantikā;
::

::gathalast
Na socāmi na rodāmi, na taṃ bhāyāmi āvuso.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbattha vihatā nandī, tamokkhandho padālito;
::

::gathalast
Jetvāna maccuno {note:jetvā namucino (sī.)} senaṃ, viharāmi anāsavā’’ti.
::

Atha kho māro pāpimā ‘‘jānāti maṃ kisāgotamī bhikkhunī’’ti dukkhī dummano tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 4. Vijayāsuttaṃ

{para:165} 165\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Atha kho vijayā bhikkhunī pubbaṇhasamayaṃ nivāsetvā…pe… aññatarasmiṃ rukkhamūle divāvihāraṃ nisīdi. Atha kho māro pāpimā vijayāya bhikkhuniyā bhayaṃ chambhitattaṃ lomahaṃsaṃ uppādetukāmo samādhimhā cāvetukāmo yena vijayā bhikkhunī tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā vijayaṃ bhikkhuniṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Daharā {pb:T:1.0192}{pb:M:1.0132}{pb:P:1.0131} tvaṃ rūpavatī, ahañca daharo susu;
::

::gathalast
Pañcaṅgikena turiyena, ehayyebhiramāmase’’ti {note:ehi ayye ramāmaseti (sī.)}.
::

Atha kho vijayāya bhikkhuniyā etadahosi – ‘‘ko nu khvāyaṃ manusso vā amanusso vā gāthaṃ bhāsatī’’ti? Atha kho vijayāya bhikkhuniyā etadahosi – ‘‘māro kho ayaṃ pāpimā mama bhayaṃ chambhitattaṃ lomahaṃsaṃ uppādetukāmo samādhimhā cāvetukāmo gāthaṃ bhāsatī’’ti. Atha kho vijayā bhikkhunī ‘‘māro ayaṃ pāpimā’’ iti viditvā māraṃ pāpimantaṃ gāthāhi paccabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Rūpā saddā rasā gandhā, phoṭṭhabbā ca manoramā;
::

::gathalast
Niyyātayāmi tuyheva, māra nāhaṃ tenatthikā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iminā {pb:V:1.0155} pūtikāyena, bhindanena pabhaṅgunā;
::

::gathalast
Aṭṭīyāmi harāyāmi, kāmataṇhā samūhatā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye ca rūpūpagā sattā, ye ca arūpaṭṭhāyino {note:āruppaṭṭhāyino (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Yā ca santā samāpatti, sabbattha vihato tamo’’ti.
::

Atha kho māro pāpimā ‘‘jānāti maṃ vijayā bhikkhunī’’ti dukkhī dummano tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 5. Uppalavaṇṇāsuttaṃ

{para:166} 166\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Atha kho uppalavaṇṇā bhikkhunī pubbaṇhasamayaṃ nivāsetvā…pe… aññatarasmiṃ supupphitasālarukkhamūle aṭṭhāsi. Atha {pb:T:1.0193} kho māro pāpimā uppalavaṇṇāya bhikkhuniyā bhayaṃ chambhitattaṃ lomahaṃsaṃ uppādetukāmo samādhimhā cāvetukāmo yena uppalavaṇṇā bhikkhunī tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā uppalavaṇṇaṃ bhikkhuniṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Supupphitaggaṃ upagamma bhikkhuni,
::

::gatha2
Ekā tuvaṃ tiṭṭhasi sālamūle;
::

::gatha3
Na catthi te dutiyā vaṇṇadhātu,
::

::gathalast
Bāle na tvaṃ bhāyasi dhuttakāna’’nti.
::

Atha {pb:M:1.0133} kho uppalavaṇṇāya bhikkhuniyā etadahosi – ‘‘ko {pb:P:1.0132} nu khvāyaṃ manusso vā amanusso vā gāthaṃ bhāsatī’’ti? Atha kho uppalavaṇṇāya bhikkhuniyā etadahosi – ‘‘māro kho ayaṃ pāpimā mama bhayaṃ chambhitattaṃ lomahaṃsaṃ uppādetukāmo samādhimhā cāvetukāmo gāthaṃ bhāsatī’’ti. Atha kho uppalavaṇṇā bhikkhunī ‘‘māro ayaṃ pāpimā’’ iti viditvā māraṃ pāpimantaṃ gāthāhi paccabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sataṃ {pb:V:1.0156} sahassānipi dhuttakānaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Idhāgatā tādisakā bhaveyyuṃ;
::

::gatha3
Lomaṃ na iñjāmi na santasāmi,
::

::gathalast
Na māra bhāyāmi tamekikāpi.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Esā antaradhāyāmi, kucchiṃ vā pavisāmi te;
::

::gathalast
Pakhumantarikāyampi, tiṭṭhantiṃ maṃ na dakkhasi.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cittasmiṃ {pb:T:1.0194} vasībhūtāmhi, iddhipādā subhāvitā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbabandhanamuttāmhi, na taṃ bhāyāmi āvuso’’ti.
::

Atha kho māro pāpimā ‘‘jānāti maṃ uppalavaṇṇā bhikkhunī’’ti dukkhī dummano tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 6. Cālāsuttaṃ

{para:167} 167\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Atha kho cālā bhikkhunī pubbaṇhasamayaṃ nivāsetvā…pe… aññatarasmiṃ rukkhamūle divāvihāraṃ nisīdi. Atha kho māro pāpimā yena cālā bhikkhunī tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā cālaṃ bhikkhuniṃ etadavoca – ‘‘kiṃ nu tvaṃ, bhikkhuni, na rocesī’’ti? ‘‘Jātiṃ khvāhaṃ, āvuso, na rocemī’’ti.

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ nu jātiṃ na rocesi, jāto kāmāni bhuñjati;
::

::gathalast
Ko nu taṃ idamādapayi, jātiṃ mā roca {note:mā rocesi (sī. pī.)} bhikkhunī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Jātassa maraṇaṃ hoti, jāto dukkhāni phussati {note:passati (sī. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Bandhaṃ vadhaṃ pariklesaṃ, tasmā jātiṃ na rocaye.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Buddho {pb:M:1.0134} dhammamadesesi, jātiyā samatikkamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbadukkhappahānāya, so maṃ sacce nivesayi.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye {pb:V:1.0157}{pb:P:1.0133} ca rūpūpagā sattā, ye ca arūpaṭṭhāyino;
::

::gathalast
Nirodhaṃ appajānantā, āgantāro punabbhava’’nti.
::

Atha kho māro pāpimā ‘‘jānāti maṃ cālā bhikkhunī’’ti dukkhī dummano tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 7. Upacālāsuttaṃ

{para:168} 168\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:T:1.0195}. Atha kho upacālā bhikkhunī pubbaṇhasamayaṃ nivāsetvā…pe… aññatarasmiṃ rukkhamūle divāvihāraṃ nisīdi. Atha kho māro pāpimā yena upacālā bhikkhunī tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā upacālaṃ bhikkhuniṃ etadavoca – ‘‘kattha nu tvaṃ, bhikkhuni, uppajjitukāmā’’ti? ‘‘Na khvāhaṃ, āvuso, katthaci uppajjitukāmā’’ti.

::gatha1
‘‘Tāvatiṃsā ca yāmā ca, tusitā cāpi devatā;
::

::gatha2
Nimmānaratino devā, ye devā vasavattino;
::

::gathalast
Tattha cittaṃ paṇidhehi, ratiṃ paccanubhossasī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tāvatiṃsā ca yāmā ca, tusitā cāpi devatā;
::

::gatha2
Nimmānaratino devā, ye devā vasavattino;
::

::gathalast
Kāmabandhanabaddhā te, enti māravasaṃ puna.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbo ādīpito {note:sabbova āditto (syā. kaṃ.)} loko, sabbo loko padhūpito;
::

::gathalast
Sabbo pajjalito {note:pajjalito (sabbattha)} loko, sabbo loko pakampito.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akampitaṃ apajjalitaṃ {note:acalitaṃ (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)}, aputhujjanasevitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Agati yattha mārassa, tattha me nirato mano’’ti.
::

Atha {pb:V:1.0158} kho māro pāpimā ‘‘jānāti maṃ upacālā bhikkhunī’’ti dukkhī dummano tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 8. Sīsupacālāsuttaṃ

{para:169} 169\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:M:1.0135}. Atha kho sīsupacālā {note:sīsūpacālā (sī.)} bhikkhunī pubbaṇhasamayaṃ nivāsetvā {pb:T:1.0196} …pe… aññatarasmiṃ rukkhamūle divāvihāraṃ nisīdi. Atha kho māro pāpimā yena sīsupacālā bhikkhunī tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā sīsupacālaṃ bhikkhuniṃ etadavoca – ‘‘kassa nu tvaṃ, bhikkhuni, pāsaṇḍaṃ rocesī’’ti? ‘‘Na khvāhaṃ, āvuso, kassaci pāsaṇḍaṃ rocemī’’ti.

::gatha1
‘‘Kaṃ nu uddissa muṇḍāsi, samaṇī viya dissasi;
::

::gathalast
Na ca rocesi pāsaṇḍaṃ, kimiva carasi momūhā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ito bahiddhā pāsaṇḍā, diṭṭhīsu pasīdanti te;
::

::gathalast
Na tesaṃ dhammaṃ rocemi, te dhammassa akovidā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atthi {pb:P:1.0134} sakyakule jāto, buddho appaṭipuggalo;
::

::gathalast
Sabbābhibhū māranudo, sabbatthamaparājito.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbattha mutto asito, sabbaṃ passati cakkhumā;
::

::gatha2
Sabbakammakkhayaṃ patto, vimutto upadhisaṅkhaye;
::

::gathalast
So mayhaṃ bhagavā satthā, tassa rocemi sāsana’’nti.
::

Atha kho māro pāpimā ‘‘jānāti maṃ sīsupacālā bhikkhunī’’ti dukkhī dummano tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 9. Selāsuttaṃ

{para:170} 170\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:V:1.0159}. Atha kho selā bhikkhunī pubbaṇhasamayaṃ nivāsetvā…pe… aññatarasmiṃ rukkhamūle divāvihāraṃ nisīdi. Atha kho māro pāpimā selāya bhikkhuniyā bhayaṃ chambhitattaṃ lomahaṃsaṃ uppādetukāmo…pe… selaṃ {pb:T:1.0197} bhikkhuniṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kenidaṃ pakataṃ bimbaṃ, kvanu {note:kvannu (sī. pī.), kvaci (syā. kaṃ. ka.)} bimbassa kārako;
::

::gathalast
Kvanu bimbaṃ samuppannaṃ, kvanu bimbaṃ nirujjhatī’’ti.
::

Atha kho selāya bhikkhuniyā etadahosi – ‘‘ko nu khvāyaṃ manusso vā amanusso vā gāthaṃ bhāsatī’’ti? Atha kho selāya bhikkhuniyā {pb:M:1.0136} etadahosi – ‘‘māro kho ayaṃ pāpimā mama bhayaṃ chambhitattaṃ lomahaṃsaṃ uppādetukāmo samādhimhā cāvetukāmo gāthaṃ bhāsatī’’ti. Atha kho selā bhikkhunī ‘‘māro ayaṃ pāpimā’’ iti viditvā māraṃ pāpimantaṃ gāthāhi paccabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Nayidaṃ attakataṃ {note:nayidaṃ pakataṃ (syā. kaṃ.)} bimbaṃ, nayidaṃ parakataṃ {note:nayidaṃ pakataṃ (syā. kaṃ.)} aghaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Hetuṃ paṭicca sambhūtaṃ, hetubhaṅgā nirujjhati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathā aññataraṃ bījaṃ, khette vuttaṃ virūhati;
::

::gathalast
Pathavīrasañcāgamma, sinehañca tadūbhayaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ khandhā ca dhātuyo, cha ca āyatanā ime;
::

::gathalast
Hetuṃ paṭicca sambhūtā, hetubhaṅgā nirujjhare’’ti.
::

Atha kho māro pāpimā ‘‘jānāti maṃ selā bhikkhunī’’ti dukkhī dummano tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 10. Vajirāsuttaṃ

{para:171} 171\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:V:1.0160}. Atha kho vajirā bhikkhunī pubbaṇhasamayaṃ {pb:T:1.0198} nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya sāvatthiṃ piṇḍāya pāvisi. Sāvatthiyaṃ piṇḍāya caritvā pacchābhattaṃ piṇḍapātapaṭikkantā {pb:P:1.0135} yena andhavanaṃ tenupasaṅkami divāvihārāya. Andhavanaṃ ajjhogāhetvā aññatarasmiṃ rukkhamūle divāvihāraṃ nisīdi. Atha kho māro pāpimā vajirāya bhikkhuniyā bhayaṃ chambhitattaṃ lomahaṃsaṃ uppādetukāmo samādhimhā cāvetukāmo yena vajirā bhikkhunī tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā vajiraṃ bhikkhuniṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kenāyaṃ pakato satto, kuvaṃ sattassa kārako;
::

::gathalast
Kuvaṃ satto samuppanno, kuvaṃ satto nirujjhatī’’ti.
::

Atha kho vajirāya bhikkhuniyā etadahosi – ‘‘ko nu khvāyaṃ manusso vā amanusso vā gāthaṃ bhāsatī’’ti? Atha kho vajirāya bhikkhuniyā etadahosi – ‘‘māro kho ayaṃ pāpimā mama bhayaṃ chambhitattaṃ lomahaṃsaṃ uppādetukāmo samādhimhā cāvetukāmo gāthaṃ bhāsatī’’ti. Atha kho {pb:M:1.0137} vajirā bhikkhunī ‘‘māro ayaṃ pāpimā’’ iti viditvā, māraṃ pāpimantaṃ gāthāhi paccabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ nu sattoti paccesi, māra diṭṭhigataṃ nu te;
::

::gathalast
Suddhasaṅkhārapuñjoyaṃ, nayidha sattupalabbhati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yathā hi aṅgasambhārā, hoti saddo ratho iti;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ khandhesu santesu, hoti sattoti sammuti {note:sammati (syā. kaṃ.)}.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dukkhameva {pb:T:1.0199} hi sambhoti, dukkhaṃ tiṭṭhati veti ca;
::

::gathalast
Nāññatra dukkhā sambhoti, nāññaṃ dukkhā nirujjhatī’’ti.
::

Atha {pb:V:1.0161} kho māro pāpimā ‘‘jānāti maṃ vajirā bhikkhunī’’ti dukkhī dummano tatthevantaradhāyīti.

::centre
Bhikkhunīsaṃyuttaṃ samattaṃ.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Āḷavikā ca somā ca, gotamī vijayā saha;
::

::gatha1
Uppalavaṇṇā ca cālā, upacālā sīsupacālā ca;
::

::gathalast
Selā vajirāya te dasāti.
::

### 6. Brahmasaṃyuttaṃ

#### 1. Paṭhamavaggo

#### 1. Brahmāyācanasuttaṃ

{para:172} 172\. Evaṃ {pb:T:1.0200}{pb:V:1.0162}{pb:P:1.0136}{pb:M:1.0138} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā uruvelāyaṃ viharati najjā nerañjarāya tīre ajapālanigrodhamūle paṭhamābhisambuddho. Atha kho bhagavato rahogatassa paṭisallīnassa evaṃ cetaso parivitakko udapādi – ‘‘adhigato kho myāyaṃ dhammo gambhīro duddaso duranubodho santo paṇīto atakkāvacaro nipuṇo paṇḍitavedanīyo. Ālayarāmā kho panāyaṃ pajā ālayaratā ālayasammuditā. Ālayarāmāya kho pana pajāya ālayaratāya ālayasammuditāya duddasaṃ idaṃ ṭhānaṃ yadidaṃ idappaccayatāpaṭiccasamuppādo. Idampi kho ṭhānaṃ duddasaṃ yadidaṃ sabbasaṅkhārasamatho sabbūpadhipaṭinissaggo taṇhākkhayo virāgo nirodho nibbānaṃ. Ahañceva kho pana dhammaṃ deseyyaṃ; pare ca me na ājāneyyuṃ; so mamassa kilamatho, sā mamassa vihesā’’ti. Apissu bhagavantaṃ imā anacchariyā gāthāyo paṭibhaṃsu pubbe assutapubbā –

::gatha1
‘‘Kicchena me adhigataṃ, halaṃ dāni pakāsituṃ;
::

::gathalast
Rāgadosaparetehi, nāyaṃ dhammo susambudho.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭisotagāmiṃ {pb:T:1.0201} nipuṇaṃ, gambhīraṃ duddasaṃ aṇuṃ;
::

::gathalast
Rāgarattā na dakkhanti, tamokhandhena āvuṭā’’ti {note:tamokkhandhena āvutāti (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)}.
::

Itiha {pb:P:1.0137} bhagavato paṭisañcikkhato appossukkatāya cittaṃ namati, no dhammadesanāya.

Atha {pb:V:1.0163} kho brahmuno sahampatissa bhagavato cetasā cetoparivitakkamaññāya etadahosi – ‘‘nassati vata bho loko, vinassati vata bho loko, yatra hi nāma tathāgatassa arahato sammāsambuddhassa appossukkatāya cittaṃ namati {note:namissati (?)}, no dhammadesanāyā’’ti. Atha {pb:M:1.0139} kho brahmā sahampati – seyyathāpi nāma balavā puriso samiñjitaṃ {note:sammiñjitaṃ (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} vā bāhaṃ pasāreyya, pasāritaṃ vā bāhaṃ samiñjeyya evameva – brahmaloke antarahito bhagavato purato pāturahosi. Atha kho brahmā sahampati ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā dakkhiṇajāṇumaṇḍalaṃ pathaviyaṃ nihantvā yena bhagavā tenañjaliṃ paṇāmetvā bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘desetu, bhante, bhagavā dhammaṃ, desetu sugato dhammaṃ. Santi sattā apparajakkhajātikā, assavanatā dhammassa parihāyanti. Bhavissanti dhammassa aññātāro’’ti. Idamavoca brahmā sahampati, idaṃ vatvā athāparaṃ etadavoca –

::gatha1
‘‘Pāturahosi magadhesu pubbe,
::

::gatha2
Dhammo asuddho samalehi cintito;
::

::gatha3
Apāpuretaṃ {note:avāpuretaṃ (sī.)} amatassa dvāraṃ,
::

::gathalast
Suṇantu {pb:T:1.0202} dhammaṃ vimalenānubuddhaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sele yathā pabbatamuddhaniṭṭhito,
::

::gatha2
Yathāpi passe janataṃ samantato;
::

::gatha3
Tathūpamaṃ dhammamayaṃ sumedha,
::

::gatha2
Pāsādamāruyha samantacakkhu;
::

::gatha3
Sokāvatiṇṇaṃ {note:sokāvakiṇṇaṃ (sī.)} janatamapetasoko,
::

::gathalast
Avekkhassu jātijarābhibhūtaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uṭṭhehi vīra vijitasaṅgāma,
::

::gatha2
Satthavāha anaṇa {note:aṇaṇa (rūpasiddhiṭīkā)} vicara loke;
::

::gatha3
Desassu {note:desetu (syā. kaṃ. pī. ka.)} bhagavā dhammaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Aññātāro bhavissantī’’ti.
::

Atha {pb:P:1.0138} kho bhagavā brahmuno ca ajjhesanaṃ viditvā sattesu ca kāruññataṃ paṭicca buddhacakkhunā {pb:V:1.0164} lokaṃ volokesi. Addasā kho bhagavā buddhacakkhunā lokaṃ volokento satte apparajakkhe mahārajakkhe tikkhindriye mudindriye svākāre dvākāre suviññāpaye duviññāpaye, appekacce paralokavajjabhayadassāvine viharante, appekacce na paralokavajjabhayadassāvine {pb:M:1.0140} {note:dassāvino (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} viharante. Seyyathāpi nāma uppaliniyaṃ vā paduminiyaṃ vā puṇḍarīkiniyaṃ vā appekaccāni uppalāni vā padumāni vā puṇḍarīkāni vā udake jātāni udake saṃvaḍḍhāni udakānuggatāni anto nimuggaposīni, appekaccāni uppalāni vā {pb:T:1.0203} padumāni vā puṇḍarīkāni vā udake jātāni udake saṃvaḍḍhāni samodakaṃ ṭhitāni, appekaccāni uppalāni vā padumāni vā puṇḍarīkāni vā udake jātāni udake saṃvaḍḍhāni udakā accuggamma ṭhitāni {note:tiṭṭhanti (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} anupalittāni udakena; evameva bhagavā buddhacakkhunā lokaṃ volokento addasa satte apparajakkhe mahārajakkhe tikkhindriye mudindriye svākāre dvākāre suviññāpaye duviññāpaye, appekacce paralokavajjabhayadassāvine viharante, appekacce na paralokavajjabhayadassāvine viharante. Disvāna brahmānaṃ sahampatiṃ gāthāya paccabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Apārutā tesaṃ amatassa dvārā,
::

::gatha2
Ye sotavanto pamuñcantu saddhaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Vihiṃsasaññī paguṇaṃ na bhāsiṃ,
::

::gathalast
Dhammaṃ paṇītaṃ manujesu brahme’’ti.
::

Atha kho brahmā sahampati ‘‘katāvakāso khomhi bhagavatā dhammadesanāyā’’ti bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaṃ katvā tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 2. Gāravasuttaṃ

{para:173} 173\. Evaṃ me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā uruvelāyaṃ viharati najjā nerañjarāya tīre ajapālanigrodhamūle paṭhamābhisambuddho. Atha {pb:P:1.0139} kho bhagavato rahogatassa paṭisallīnassa evaṃ cetaso parivitakko udapādi – ‘‘dukkhaṃ kho agāravo viharati appatisso, kaṃ nu khvāhaṃ samaṇaṃ vā brāhmaṇaṃ vā sakkatvā garuṃ katvā {note:garukatvā (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} upanissāya vihareyya’’nti?

Atha {pb:M:1.0141} kho bhagavato etadahosi – ‘‘aparipuṇṇassa kho sīlakkhandhassa pāripūriyā aññaṃ samaṇaṃ vā brāhmaṇaṃ vā sakkatvā garuṃ katvā upanissāya vihareyyaṃ{pb:T:1.0204}{pb:V:1.0165}. Na kho panāhaṃ passāmi sadevake loke samārake sabrahmake sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya attanā sīlasampannataraṃ aññaṃ samaṇaṃ vā brāhmaṇaṃ vā, yamahaṃ sakkatvā garuṃ katvā upanissāya vihareyyaṃ.

‘‘Aparipuṇṇassa kho samādhikkhandhassa pāripūriyā aññaṃ samaṇaṃ vā brāhmaṇaṃ vā sakkatvā garuṃ katvā upanissāya vihareyyaṃ. Na kho panāhaṃ passāmi sadevake loke…pe… attanā samādhisampannataraṃ aññaṃ samaṇaṃ vā brāhmaṇaṃ vā, yamahaṃ sakkatvā garuṃ katvā upanissāya vihareyyaṃ.

‘‘Aparipuṇṇassa paññākkhandhassa pāripūriyā aññaṃ samaṇaṃ vā brāhmaṇaṃ vā sakkatvā garuṃ katvā upanissāya vihareyyaṃ. Na kho panāhaṃ passāmi sadevake…pe… attanā paññāsampannataraṃ aññaṃ samaṇaṃ vā brāhmaṇaṃ vā, yamahaṃ sakkatvā garuṃ katvā upanissāya vihareyyaṃ.

‘‘Aparipuṇṇassa kho vimuttikkhandhassa pāripūriyā aññaṃ samaṇaṃ vā brāhmaṇaṃ vā sakkatvā garuṃ katvā upanissāya vihareyyaṃ. Na kho panāhaṃ passāmi sadevake…pe… attanā vimuttisampannataraṃ aññaṃ samaṇaṃ vā brāhmaṇaṃ vā, yamahaṃ sakkatvā garuṃ katvā upanissāya vihareyyaṃ.

‘‘Aparipuṇṇassa kho vimuttiñāṇadassanakkhandhassa pāripūriyā aññaṃ samaṇaṃ vā brāhmaṇaṃ vā {pb:T:1.0205} sakkatvā garuṃ katvā upanissāya vihareyyaṃ. Na kho panāhaṃ passāmi sadevake loke samārake sabrahmake sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya attanā vimuttiñāṇadassanasampannataraṃ aññaṃ samaṇaṃ vā brāhmaṇaṃ vā, yamahaṃ sakkatvā garuṃ katvā upanissāya vihareyyaṃ. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ yvāyaṃ dhammo mayā abhisambuddho tameva dhammaṃ sakkatvā garuṃ katvā upanissāya vihareyya’’nti.

Atha kho brahmā sahampati bhagavato cetasā cetoparivitakkamaññāya – seyyathāpi nāma balavā puriso samiñjitaṃ vā bāhaṃ pasāreyya pasāritaṃ vā bāhaṃ samiñjeyya evameva – brahmaloke {pb:V:1.0166} antarahito bhagavato purato pāturahosi. Atha kho brahmā sahampati ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā yena bhagavā tenañjaliṃ paṇāmetvā bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘evametaṃ{pb:P:1.0140}, bhagavā, evametaṃ, sugata! Yepi te, bhante, ahesuṃ atītamaddhānaṃ arahanto sammāsambuddhā, tepi {pb:M:1.0142} bhagavanto dhammaññeva sakkatvā garuṃ katvā upanissāya vihariṃsu; yepi te, bhante, bhavissanti anāgatamaddhānaṃ arahanto sammāsambuddhā tepi bhagavanto dhammaññeva sakkatvā garuṃ katvā upanissāya viharissanti. Bhagavāpi, bhante, etarahi arahaṃ sammāsambuddho dhammaññeva sakkatvā garuṃ katvā upanissāya viharatū’’ti. Idamavoca brahmā sahampati, idaṃ vatvā athāparaṃ etadavoca –

::gatha1
‘‘Ye {pb:T:1.0206} ca atītā sambuddhā, ye ca buddhā anāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Yo cetarahi sambuddho, bahūnaṃ {note:bahunnaṃ (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} sokanāsano.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbe saddhammagaruno, vihaṃsu {note:vihariṃsu (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} viharanti ca;
::

::gathalast
Tathāpi viharissanti, esā buddhāna dhammatā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasmā hi attakāmena {note:atthakāmena (sī. pī. ka.)}, mahattamabhikaṅkhatā;
::

::gathalast
Saddhammo garukātabbo, saraṃ buddhāna sāsana’’nti.
::

#### 3. Brahmadevasuttaṃ

{para:174} 174\. Evaṃ me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Tena kho pana samayena aññatarissā brāhmaṇiyā brahmadevo nāma putto bhagavato santike agārasmā anagāriyaṃ pabbajito hoti.

Atha kho āyasmā brahmadevo eko vūpakaṭṭho appamatto ātāpī pahitatto viharanto nacirasseva – yassatthāya kulaputtā sammadeva agārasmā anagāriyaṃ pabbajanti, tadanuttaraṃ brahmacariyapariyosānaṃ diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṃ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja vihāsi. ‘‘Khīṇā jāti{pb:V:1.0167}, vusitaṃ brahmacariyaṃ, kataṃ karaṇīyaṃ, nāparaṃ itthattāyā’’ti abbhaññāsi. Aññataro ca panāyasmā brahmadevo arahataṃ ahosi.

Atha kho āyasmā brahmadevo pubbaṇhasamayaṃ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya sāvatthiṃ piṇḍāya pāvisi. Sāvatthiyaṃ sapadānaṃ piṇḍāya caramāno yena sakamātu nivesanaṃ tenupasaṅkami. Tena {pb:P:1.0141} kho pana {pb:T:1.0207} samayena āyasmato brahmadevassa mātā brāhmaṇī brahmuno āhutiṃ niccaṃ paggaṇhāti{pb:M:1.0143}. Atha kho brahmuno sahampatissa etadahosi – ‘‘ayaṃ kho āyasmato brahmadevassa mātā brāhmaṇī brahmuno āhutiṃ niccaṃ paggaṇhāti. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ taṃ upasaṅkamitvā saṃvejeyya’’nti. Atha kho brahmā sahampati – seyyathāpi nāma balavā puriso samiñjitaṃ vā bāhaṃ pasāreyya, pasāritaṃ vā bāhaṃ samiñjeyya evameva – brahmaloke antarahito āyasmato brahmadevassa mātu nivesane pāturahosi. Atha kho brahmā sahampati vehāsaṃ ṭhito āyasmato brahmadevassa mātaraṃ brāhmaṇiṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Dūre ito brāhmaṇi brahmaloko,
::

::gatha2
Yassāhutiṃ paggaṇhāsi niccaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Netādiso brāhmaṇi brahmabhakkho,
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ jappasi brahmapathaṃ ajānaṃ {note:ajānantī (sī. pī. ka.)}.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Eso hi te brāhmaṇi brahmadevo,
::

::gatha2
Nirūpadhiko atidevapatto;
::

::gatha3
Akiñcano bhikkhu anaññaposī,
::

::gathalast
Yo te so {note:te so (sī. pī.), yo te sa (?)} piṇḍāya gharaṃ paviṭṭho.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āhuneyyo vedagu bhāvitatto,
::

::gatha2
Narānaṃ devānañca dakkhiṇeyyo;
::

::gatha3
Bāhitvā pāpāni anūpalitto,
::

::gathalast
Ghāsesanaṃ {pb:T:1.0208} iriyati sītibhūto.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:V:1.0168} tassa pacchā na puratthamatthi,
::

::gatha2
Santo vidhūmo anigho nirāso;
::

::gatha3
Nikkhittadaṇḍo tasathāvaresu,
::

::gathalast
So tyāhutiṃ bhuñjatu aggapiṇḍaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Visenibhūto upasantacitto,
::

::gatha2
Nāgova danto carati anejo;
::

::gatha3
Bhikkhu susīlo suvimuttacitto,
::

::gathalast
So tyāhutiṃ bhuñjatu aggapiṇḍaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasmiṃ {pb:M:1.0144} pasannā avikampamānā,
::

::gatha2
Patiṭṭhapehi {pb:P:1.0142} dakkhiṇaṃ dakkhiṇeyye;
::

::gatha3
Karohi puññaṃ sukhamāyatikaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Disvā muniṃ brāhmaṇi oghatiṇṇa’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasmiṃ pasannā avikampamānā,
::

::gatha2
Patiṭṭhapesi dakkhiṇaṃ dakkhiṇeyye;
::

::gatha3
Akāsi puññaṃ sukhamāyatikaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Disvā muniṃ brāhmaṇī oghatiṇṇa’’nti.
::

#### 4. Bakabrahmasuttaṃ

{para:175} 175\. Evaṃ me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Tena kho pana samayena bakassa brahmuno evarūpaṃ pāpakaṃ {pb:T:1.0209} diṭṭhigataṃ uppannaṃ hoti – ‘‘idaṃ niccaṃ, idaṃ dhuvaṃ, idaṃ sassataṃ, idaṃ kevalaṃ, idaṃ acavanadhammaṃ, idañhi na jāyati na jīyati na mīyati na cavati na upapajjati, ito ca panaññaṃ uttariṃ {note:uttariṃ (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} nissaraṇaṃ natthī’’ti.

Atha {pb:V:1.0169} kho bhagavā bakassa brahmuno cetasā cetoparivitakkamaññāya – seyyathāpi nāma balavā puriso samiñjitaṃ vā bāhaṃ pasāreyya, pasāritaṃ vā bāhaṃ samiñjeyya evameva – jetavane antarahito tasmiṃ brahmaloke pāturahosi. Addasā kho bako brahmā bhagavantaṃ dūratova āgacchantaṃ. Disvāna bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘ehi kho mārisa, svāgataṃ te, mārisa! Cirassaṃ kho mārisa! Imaṃ pariyāyamakāsi yadidaṃ idhāgamanāya. Idañhi, mārisa, niccaṃ, idaṃ dhuvaṃ, idaṃ sassataṃ, idaṃ kevalaṃ, idaṃ acavanadhammaṃ, idañhi na jāyati na jīyati na mīyati na cavati na upapajjati. Ito ca panaññaṃ uttari nissaraṇaṃ natthī’’ti.

Evaṃ vutte, bhagavā bakaṃ brahmānaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘avijjāgato vata, bho, bako brahmā; avijjāgato vata, bho, bako brahmā. Yatra {pb:M:1.0145} hi nāma aniccaṃyeva samānaṃ niccanti vakkhati, adhuvaṃyeva samānaṃ dhuvanti vakkhati, asassataṃyeva samānaṃ sassatanti vakkhati, akevalaṃyeva {pb:P:1.0143} samānaṃ kevalanti vakkhati, cavanadhammaṃyeva samānaṃ acavanadhammanti vakkhati. Yattha ca pana jāyati ca jīyati ca mīyati ca cavati ca upapajjati ca, tañca tathā vakkhati – ‘idañhi na jāyati na jīyati na mīyati na cavati na {pb:T:1.0210} upapajjati’. Santañca panaññaṃ uttari nissaraṇaṃ, ‘natthaññaṃ uttari nissaraṇa’nti vakkhatī’’ti.

::gatha1
‘‘Dvāsattati gotama puññakammā,
::

::gatha2
Vasavattino jātijaraṃ atītā;
::

::gatha3
Ayamantimā vedagū brahmupapatti,
::

::gathalast
Asmābhijappanti janā anekā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Appañhi etaṃ na hi dīghamāyu,
::

::gatha2
Yaṃ tvaṃ baka maññasi dīghamāyuṃ;
::

::gatha3
Sataṃ sahassānaṃ {note:sahassāna (syā. kaṃ.)} nirabbudānaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Āyuṃ pajānāmi tavāhaṃ brahme’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anantadassī bhagavāhamasmi,
::

::gatha2
Jātijaraṃ sokamupātivatto;
::

::gatha3
Kiṃ {pb:V:1.0170} me purāṇaṃ vatasīlavattaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Ācikkha me taṃ yamahaṃ vijaññā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ tvaṃ apāyesi bahū manusse,
::

::gatha2
Pipāsite ghammani samparete;
::

::gatha3
Taṃ te purāṇaṃ vatasīlavattaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Suttappabuddhova anussarāmi.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ eṇikūlasmiṃ janaṃ gahītaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Amocayī gayhakaṃ nīyamānaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Taṃ {pb:T:1.0211} te purāṇaṃ vatasīlavattaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Suttappabuddhova anussarāmi.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gaṅgāya {pb:M:1.0146} sotasmiṃ gahītanāvaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Luddena nāgena manussakamyā;
::

::gatha3
Pamocayittha balasā pasayha,
::

::gatha2
Taṃ te purāṇaṃ vatasīlavattaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Suttappabuddhova anussarāmi.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kappo {pb:P:1.0144} ca te baddhacaro ahosiṃ,
::

::gatha2
Sambuddhimantaṃ {note:sambuddhivantaṃ (bahūsu)} vatinaṃ amaññi;
::

::gatha3
Taṃ te purāṇaṃ vatasīlavattaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Suttappabuddhova anussarāmī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addhā pajānāsi mametamāyuṃ,
::

::gatha2
Aññepi {note:aññampi (sī. pī.)} jānāsi tathā hi buddho;
::

::gatha3
Tathā hi tyāyaṃ jalitānubhāvo,
::

::gathalast
Obhāsayaṃ tiṭṭhati brahmaloka’’nti.
::

#### 5. Aññatarabrahmasuttaṃ

{para:176} 176\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:V:1.0171}. Tena kho pana samayena aññatarassa brahmuno evarūpaṃ pāpakaṃ diṭṭhigataṃ uppannaṃ hoti – ‘‘natthi so samaṇo vā brāhmaṇo vā yo idha āgaccheyyā’’ti. Atha {pb:T:1.0212} kho bhagavā tassa brahmuno cetasā cetoparivitakkamaññāya – seyyathāpi nāma balavā puriso…pe… tasmiṃ brahmaloke pāturahosi. Atha kho bhagavā tassa brahmuno upari vehāsaṃ pallaṅkena nisīdi tejodhātuṃ samāpajjitvā.

Atha kho āyasmato mahāmoggallānassa etadahosi – ‘‘kahaṃ nu kho bhagavā etarahi viharatī’’ti? Addasā kho āyasmā mahāmoggallāno {note:mahāmoggalāno (ka.)} bhagavantaṃ dibbena cakkhunā visuddhena atikkantamānusakena tassa brahmuno upari vehāsaṃ pallaṅkena nisinnaṃ tejodhātuṃ samāpannaṃ. Disvāna – seyyathāpi nāma balavā puriso samiñjitaṃ vā bāhaṃ pasāreyya, pasāritaṃ vā bāhaṃ samiñjeyya evameva – jetavane antarahito tasmiṃ brahmaloke pāturahosi. Atha kho āyasmā mahāmoggallāno {pb:M:1.0147} puratthimaṃ disaṃ nissāya {note:upanissāya (sī.)} tassa brahmuno upari vehāsaṃ pallaṅkena nisīdi tejodhātuṃ samāpajjitvā nīcataraṃ bhagavato.

Atha kho āyasmato mahākassapassa etadahosi – ‘‘kahaṃ nu kho bhagavā etarahi viharatī’’ti? Addasā kho āyasmā mahākassapo bhagavantaṃ dibbena cakkhunā…pe… disvāna – seyyathāpi nāma balavā puriso…pe… evameva – jetavane {pb:P:1.0145} antarahito tasmiṃ brahmaloke pāturahosi. Atha kho āyasmā mahākassapo dakkhiṇaṃ disaṃ nissāya tassa brahmuno upari vehāsaṃ pallaṅkena nisīdi tejodhātuṃ samāpajjitvā nīcataraṃ bhagavato.

Atha {pb:T:1.0213} kho āyasmato mahākappinassa etadahosi – ‘‘kahaṃ nu kho bhagavā etarahi viharatī’’ti? Addasā kho āyasmā mahākappino bhagavantaṃ dibbena cakkhunā…pe… tejodhātuṃ samāpannaṃ. Disvāna – seyyathāpi nāma balavā puriso…pe… evameva – jetavane antarahito tasmiṃ brahmaloke pāturahosi. Atha kho āyasmā mahākappino pacchimaṃ disaṃ nissāya tassa brahmuno upari vehāsaṃ pallaṅkena nisīdi tejodhātuṃ samāpajjitvā nīcataraṃ bhagavato.

Atha {pb:V:1.0172} kho āyasmato anuruddhassa etadahosi – ‘‘kahaṃ nu kho bhagavā etarahi viharatī’’ti? Addasā kho āyasmā anuruddho…pe… tejodhātuṃ samāpannaṃ. Disvāna – seyyathāpi nāma balavā puriso…pe… tasmiṃ brahmaloke pāturahosi. Atha kho āyasmā anuruddho uttaraṃ disaṃ nissāya tassa brahmuno upari vehāsaṃ pallaṅkena nisīdi tejodhātuṃ samāpajjitvā nīcataraṃ bhagavato.

Atha kho āyasmā mahāmoggallāno taṃ brahmānaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Ajjāpi te āvuso sā diṭṭhi, yā te diṭṭhi pure ahu;
::

::gathalast
Passasi vītivattantaṃ, brahmaloke pabhassara’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na me mārisa sā diṭṭhi, yā me diṭṭhi pure ahu;
::

::gatha2
Passāmi vītivattantaṃ, brahmaloke pabhassaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Svāhaṃ ajja kathaṃ vajjaṃ, ahaṃ niccomhi sassato’’ti.
::

Atha {pb:T:1.0214}{pb:M:1.0148} kho bhagavā taṃ brahmānaṃ saṃvejetvā – seyyathāpi nāma balavā puriso samiñjitaṃ vā bāhaṃ pasāreyya, pasāritaṃ vā bāhaṃ samiñjeyya evameva – tasmiṃ brahmaloke antarahito jetavane pāturahosi. Atha kho so brahmā aññataraṃ brahmapārisajjaṃ āmantesi – ‘‘ehi tvaṃ, mārisa, yenāyasmā mahāmoggallāno tenupasaṅkama; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmantaṃ mahāmoggallānaṃ evaṃ vadehi – ‘atthi nu kho, mārisa moggallāna, aññepi tassa bhagavato sāvakā evaṃmahiddhikā evaṃmahānubhāvā{pb:P:1.0146}; seyyathāpi bhavaṃ moggallāno kassapo kappino anuruddho’’’ti? ‘‘Evaṃ, mārisā’’ti kho so brahmapārisajjo tassa brahmuno paṭissutvā yenāyasmā mahāmoggallāno tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmantaṃ mahāmoggallānaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘atthi nu kho, mārisa moggallāna, aññepi tassa bhagavato sāvakā evaṃmahiddhikā evaṃmahānubhāvā; seyyathāpi bhavaṃ moggallāno kassapo kappino anuruddho’’ti? Atha kho āyasmā mahāmoggallāno taṃ brahmapārisajjaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Tevijjā {pb:V:1.0173} iddhipattā ca, cetopariyāyakovidā;
::

::gathalast
Khīṇāsavā arahanto, bahū buddhassa sāvakā’’ti.
::

Atha {pb:T:1.0215} kho so brahmapārisajjo āyasmato mahāmoggallānassa bhāsitaṃ abhinanditvā anumoditvā yena so brahmā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā taṃ brahmānaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘āyasmā mārisa, mahāmoggallāno evamāha –

::gatha1
‘‘Tevijjā iddhipattā ca, cetopariyāyakovidā;
::

::gathalast
Khīṇāsavā arahanto, bahū buddhassa sāvakā’’ti.
::

Idamavoca so brahmapārisajjo. Attamano ca so brahmā tassa brahmapārisajjassa bhāsitaṃ abhinandīti.
