#### 6. Brahmalokasuttaṃ

{para:177} 177\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Tena kho pana samayena bhagavā divāvihāragato hoti paṭisallīno. Atha kho subrahmā ca paccekabrahmā suddhāvāso {pb:M:1.0149} ca paccekabrahmā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā paccekaṃ dvārabāhaṃ {note:paccekadvārabāhaṃ (pī. ka.)} upanissāya aṭṭhaṃsu. Atha kho subrahmā paccekabrahmā suddhāvāsaṃ paccekabrahmānaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘akālo kho tāva, mārisa, bhagavantaṃ payirupāsituṃ; divāvihāragato bhagavā paṭisallīno ca. Asuko ca brahmaloko iddho ceva phīto ca, brahmā ca tatra pamādavihāraṃ viharati. Āyāma, mārisa, yena so brahmaloko tenupasaṅkamissāma; upasaṅkamitvā taṃ brahmānaṃ saṃvejeyyāmā’’ti. ‘‘Evaṃ{pb:P:1.0147}, mārisā’’ti kho suddhāvāso paccekabrahmā subrahmuno paccekabrahmuno paccassosi.

Atha kho subrahmā ca paccekabrahmā {pb:T:1.0216} suddhāvāso ca paccekabrahmā – seyyathāpi nāma balavā puriso…pe… evameva – bhagavato purato antarahitā tasmiṃ brahmaloke pāturahesuṃ. Addasā kho so brahmā te brahmāno dūratova āgacchante. Disvāna te brahmāno etadavoca – ‘‘handa kuto nu tumhe, mārisā, āgacchathā’’ti? ‘‘Āgatā kho mayaṃ, mārisa, amha tassa bhagavato {pb:V:1.0174} santikā arahato sammāsambuddhassa. Gaccheyyāsi pana tvaṃ, mārisa, tassa bhagavato upaṭṭhānaṃ arahato sammāsambuddhassā’’ti?

Evaṃ vutto {note:evaṃ vutte (sī. syā. kaṃ.)} kho so brahmā taṃ vacanaṃ anadhivāsento sahassakkhattuṃ attānaṃ abhinimminitvā subrahmānaṃ paccekabrahmānaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘passasi me no tvaṃ, mārisa, evarūpaṃ iddhānubhāva’’nti? ‘‘Passāmi kho tyāhaṃ, mārisa, evarūpaṃ iddhānubhāva’’nti. ‘‘So khvāhaṃ, mārisa, evaṃmahiddhiko evaṃmahānubhāvo kassa aññassa samaṇassa vā brāhmaṇassa vā upaṭṭhānaṃ gamissāmī’’ti?

Atha kho subrahmā paccekabrahmā dvisahassakkhattuṃ attānaṃ abhinimminitvā taṃ brahmānaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘passasi me no tvaṃ, mārisa, evarūpaṃ iddhānubhāva’’nti? ‘‘Passāmi kho tyāhaṃ, mārisa, evarūpaṃ iddhānubhāva’’nti. ‘‘Tayā ca kho, mārisa, mayā ca sveva bhagavā mahiddhikataro ceva mahānubhāvataro ca. Gaccheyyāsi tvaṃ, mārisa, tassa bhagavato upaṭṭhānaṃ arahato sammāsambuddhassā’’ti? Atha {pb:T:1.0217} kho so brahmā subrahmānaṃ paccekabrahmānaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Tayo {pb:M:1.0150}{pb:P:1.0148} supaṇṇā caturo ca haṃsā,
::

::gatha2
Byagghīnisā pañcasatā ca jhāyino;
::

::gatha3
Tayidaṃ vimānaṃ jalate ca {note:jalateva (pī. ka.)} brahme,
::

::gathalast
Obhāsayaṃ uttarassaṃ disāya’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiñcāpi te taṃ jalate vimānaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Obhāsayaṃ uttarassaṃ disāyaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Rūpe raṇaṃ disvā sadā pavedhitaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Tasmā na rūpe ramatī sumedho’’ti.
::

Atha kho subrahmā ca paccekabrahmā suddhāvāso ca paccekabrahmā taṃ brahmānaṃ saṃvejetvā tatthevantaradhāyiṃsu{pb:V:1.0175}. Agamāsi ca kho so brahmā aparena samayena bhagavato upaṭṭhānaṃ arahato sammāsambuddhassāti.

#### 7. Kokālikasuttaṃ

{para:178} 178\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Tena kho pana samayena bhagavā divāvihāragato hoti paṭisallīno. Atha kho subrahmā ca paccekabrahmā suddhāvāso ca paccekabrahmā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā paccekaṃ dvārabāhaṃ nissāya aṭṭhaṃsu. Atha kho subrahmā paccekabrahmā kokālikaṃ bhikkhuṃ ārabbha {pb:T:1.0218} bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Appameyyaṃ paminanto, kodha vidvā vikappaye;
::

::gathalast
Appameyyaṃ pamāyinaṃ, nivutaṃ taṃ maññe puthujjana’’nti.
::

#### 8. Katamodakatissasuttaṃ

{para:179} 179\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Tena kho pana samayena bhagavā divāvihāragato hoti paṭisallīno. Atha kho subrahmā ca paccekabrahmā suddhāvāso ca paccekabrahmā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā paccekaṃ dvārabāhaṃ nissāya aṭṭhaṃsu. Atha kho suddhāvāso paccekabrahmā katamodakatissakaṃ {note:katamorakatissakaṃ (sī. syā. kaṃ.)} bhikkhuṃ ārabbha bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Appameyyaṃ {pb:M:1.0151}{pb:P:1.0149} paminanto, kodha vidvā vikappaye;
::

::gathalast
Appameyyaṃ pamāyinaṃ, nivutaṃ taṃ maññe akissava’’nti.
::

#### 9. Turūbrahmasuttaṃ

{para:180} 180\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Tena kho pana samayena kokāliko bhikkhu ābādhiko hoti dukkhito bāḷhagilāno. Atha kho turū {note:tudu (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} paccekabrahmā abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇo kevalakappaṃ jetavanaṃ obhāsetvā yena kokāliko bhikkhu tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā vehāsaṃ {pb:V:1.0176} ṭhito kokālikaṃ bhikkhuṃ etadavoca – ‘‘pasādehi, kokālika, sāriputtamoggallānesu cittaṃ. Pesalā sāriputtamoggallānā’’ti. ‘‘Kosi tvaṃ, āvuso’’ti? ‘‘Ahaṃ turū paccekabrahmā’’ti. ‘‘Nanu tvaṃ, āvuso, bhagavatā {pb:T:1.0219} anāgāmī byākato, atha kiñcarahi idhāgato? Passa, yāvañca te idaṃ aparaddha’’nti.

::gatha1
‘‘Purisassa hi jātassa, kuṭhārī {note:dudhārī (syā. kaṃ. ka.)} jāyate mukhe;
::

::gathalast
Yāya chindati attānaṃ, bālo dubbhāsitaṃ bhaṇaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo nindiyaṃ pasaṃsati,
::

::gatha2
Taṃ vā nindati yo pasaṃsiyo;
::

::gatha3
Vicināti mukhena so kaliṃ,
::

::gathalast
Kalinā tena sukhaṃ na vindati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Appamattako ayaṃ kali,
::

::gatha2
Yo akkhesu dhanaparājayo;
::

::gatha3
Sabbassāpi sahāpi attanā,
::

::gatha2
Ayameva mahantataro kali;
::

::gathalast
Yo sugatesu manaṃ padosaye.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sataṃ sahassānaṃ nirabbudānaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Chattiṃsati pañca ca abbudāni;
::

::gatha3
Yamariyagarahī {note:yamariye garahī (syā. kaṃ.), yamariyaṃ garahaṃ (ka.)} nirayaṃ upeti,
::

::gathalast
Vācaṃ manañca paṇidhāya pāpaka’’nti.
::

#### 10. Kokālikasuttaṃ

{para:181} 181\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:M:1.0152}. Atha kho kokāliko bhikkhu yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami{pb:P:1.0150}; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi. Ekamantaṃ nisinno kho kokāliko bhikkhu {pb:V:1.0177} bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘pāpicchā, bhante, sāriputtamoggallānā pāpikānaṃ icchānaṃ vasaṃ gatā’’ti. Evaṃ {pb:T:1.0220} vutte, bhagavā kokālikaṃ bhikkhuṃ etadavoca – ‘‘mā hevaṃ, kokālika, avaca; mā hevaṃ, kokālika, avaca. Pasādehi, kokālika, sāriputtamoggallānesu cittaṃ. Pesalā sāriputtamoggallānā’’ti. Dutiyampi kho kokāliko bhikkhu bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘kiñcāpi me, bhante, bhagavā saddhāyiko paccayiko; atha kho pāpicchāva bhante, sāriputtamoggallānā pāpikānaṃ icchānaṃ vasaṃ gatā’’ti. Dutiyampi kho bhagavā kokālikaṃ bhikkhuṃ etadavoca – ‘‘mā hevaṃ, kokālika, avaca; mā hevaṃ, kokālika, avaca. Pasādehi, kokālika, sāriputtamoggallānesu cittaṃ. Pesalā sāriputtamoggallānā’’ti. Tatiyampi kho kokāliko bhikkhu bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘kiñcāpi…pe… icchānaṃ vasaṃ gatā’’ti. Tatiyampi kho bhagavā kokālikaṃ bhikkhuṃ etadavoca – ‘‘mā hevaṃ…pe… pesalā sāriputtamoggallānā’’ti.

Atha kho kokāliko bhikkhu uṭṭhāyāsanā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaṃ katvā pakkāmi. Acirapakkantassa ca kokālikassa bhikkhuno sāsapamattīhi pīḷakāhi {note:piḷakāhi (sī. pī.)} sabbo kāyo phuṭo ahosi. Sāsapamattiyo hutvā muggamattiyo ahesuṃ, muggamattiyo hutvā kalāyamattiyo ahesuṃ, kalāyamattiyo hutvā kolaṭṭhimattiyo ahesuṃ, kolaṭṭhimattiyo hutvā kolamattiyo ahesuṃ, kolamattiyo hutvā āmalakamattiyo ahesuṃ, āmalakamattiyo hutvā beluvasalāṭukamattiyo ahesuṃ, beluvasalāṭukamattiyo hutvā billamattiyo ahesuṃ, billamattiyo {pb:T:1.0221} hutvā pabhijjiṃsu. Pubbañca lohitañca pagghariṃsu. Atha kho kokāliko bhikkhu teneva ābādhena kālamakāsi{pb:P:1.0151}. Kālaṅkato ca kokāliko bhikkhu padumaṃ nirayaṃ upapajji sāriputtamoggallānesu cittaṃ āghātetvā.

Atha {pb:M:1.0153} kho brahmā sahampati abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇo kevalakappaṃ jetavanaṃ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṃ ṭhito kho brahmā sahampati bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘kokāliko, bhante, bhikkhu kālaṅkato. Kālaṅkato ca, bhante, kokāliko bhikkhu padumaṃ nirayaṃ upapanno sāriputtamoggallānesu cittaṃ āghātetvā’’ti. Idamavoca brahmā sahampati, idaṃ vatvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaṃ katvā tatthevantaradhāyīti.

Atha {pb:V:1.0178} kho bhagavā tassā rattiyā accayena bhikkhū āmantesi – ‘‘imaṃ, bhikkhave, rattiṃ brahmā sahampati abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇo kevalakappaṃ jetavanaṃ obhāsetvā yenāhaṃ tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā maṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṃ ṭhito kho, bhikkhave, brahmā sahampati maṃ etadavoca – ‘kokāliko, bhante, bhikkhu kālaṅkato. Kālaṅkato ca, bhante, kokāliko bhikkhu padumaṃ nirayaṃ upapanno sāriputtamoggallānesu cittaṃ āghātetvā’ti. Idamavoca, bhikkhave{pb:T:1.0222}, brahmā sahampati, idaṃ vatvā maṃ abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaṃ katvā tatthevantaradhāyī’’ti.

Evaṃ vutte, aññataro bhikkhu bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘kīvadīghaṃ nu kho, bhante, padume niraye āyuppamāṇa’’nti? ‘‘Dīghaṃ kho, bhikkhu, padume niraye āyuppamāṇaṃ. Taṃ na sukaraṃ saṅkhātuṃ – ettakāni vassāni iti vā, ettakāni vassasatāni iti vā, ettakāni vassasahassāni iti vā, ettakāni vassasatasahassāni iti vā’’ti. ‘‘Sakkā pana, bhante, upamaṃ kātu’’nti? ‘‘Sakkā{pb:P:1.0152}, bhikkhū’’ti bhagavā avoca –

‘‘Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu vīsatikhāriko kosalako tilavāho. Tato puriso vassasatassa vassasatassa accayena ekamekaṃ tilaṃ uddhareyya; khippataraṃ kho so, bhikkhu, vīsatikhāriko kosalako tilavāho iminā upakkamena parikkhayaṃ pariyādānaṃ gaccheyya, na tveva eko abbudo nirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati abbudā nirayā, evameko nirabbudanirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati nirabbudā nirayā, evameko ababo nirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati ababā nirayā, evameko {pb:M:1.0154} aṭaṭo nirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati aṭaṭā nirayā, evameko ahaho nirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati ahahā nirayā, evameko kumudo nirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati kumudā nirayā, evameko sogandhiko nirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati sogandhikā nirayā, evameko uppalanirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati uppalā nirayā, evameko puṇḍariko nirayo. Seyyathāpi{pb:T:1.0223}, bhikkhu, vīsati puṇḍarikā nirayā, evameko padumo nirayo. Padume pana, bhikkhu, niraye kokāliko bhikkhu upapanno sāriputtamoggallānesu cittaṃ āghātetvā’’ti. Idamavoca bhagavā, idaṃ vatvāna sugato athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

::gatha1
‘‘Purisassa {pb:V:1.0179} hi jātassa,
::

::gatha2
Kuṭhārī jāyate mukhe;
::

::gatha3
Yāya chindati attānaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Bālo dubbhāsitaṃ bhaṇaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo nindiyaṃ pasaṃsati,
::

::gatha2
Taṃ vā nindati yo pasaṃsiyo;
::

::gatha3
Vicināti mukhena so kaliṃ,
::

::gathalast
Kalinā tena sukhaṃ na vindati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Appamattako ayaṃ kali,
::

::gatha2
Yo akkhesu dhanaparājayo;
::

::gatha3
Sabbassāpi sahāpi attanā,
::

::gatha2
Ayameva mahantaro kali;
::

::gathalast
Yo sugatesu manaṃ padosaye.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sataṃ sahassānaṃ nirabbudānaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Chattiṃsati pañca ca abbudāni;
::

::gatha3
Yamariyagarahī {pb:P:1.0153} nirayaṃ upeti,
::

::gathalast
Vācaṃ manañca paṇidhāya pāpaka’’nti.
::

::centre
Paṭhamo vaggo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Āyācanaṃ {pb:T:1.0224}{pb:M:1.0155} gāravo brahmadevo,
::

::gatha2
Bako ca brahmā aparā ca diṭṭhi;
::

::gatha3
Pamādakokālikatissako ca,
::

::gathalast
Turū ca brahmā aparo ca kokālikoti.
::

#### 2. Dutiyavaggo

#### 1. Sanaṅkumārasuttaṃ

{para:182} 182\. Evaṃ {pb:T:1.0225}{pb:V:1.0180} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati sappinītīre. Atha kho brahmā sanaṅkumāro abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇo kevalakappaṃ sappinītīraṃ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṃ ṭhito kho brahmā sanaṅkumāro bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Khattiyo seṭṭho janetasmiṃ, ye gottapaṭisārino;
::

::gathalast
Vijjācaraṇasampanno, so seṭṭho devamānuse’’ti.
::

Idamavoca brahmā sanaṅkumāro. Samanuñño satthā ahosi. Atha kho brahmā sanaṅkumāro ‘‘samanuñño me satthā’’ti bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaṃ katvā tatthevantaradhāyīti.

#### 2. Devadattasuttaṃ

{para:183} 183\. Evaṃ me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati gijjhakūṭe pabbate acirapakkante devadatte. Atha kho brahmā sahampati abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇo kevalakappaṃ gijjhakūṭaṃ {pb:T:1.0226} pabbataṃ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṃ {pb:P:1.0154} ṭhito kho brahmā sahampati devadattaṃ ārabbha bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Phalaṃ {pb:M:1.0156} ve kadaliṃ hanti, phalaṃ veḷuṃ phalaṃ naḷaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sakkāro kāpurisaṃ hanti, gabbho assatariṃ yathā’’ti.
::

#### 3. Andhakavindasuttaṃ

{para:184} 184\. Ekaṃ {pb:V:1.0181} samayaṃ bhagavā māgadhesu viharati andhakavinde. Tena kho pana samayena bhagavā rattandhakāratimisāyaṃ abbhokāse nisinno hoti, devo ca ekamekaṃ phusāyati. Atha kho brahmā sahampati abhikkantāya rattiyā abhikkantavaṇṇo kevalakappaṃ andhakavindaṃ obhāsetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṃ ṭhito kho brahmā sahampati bhagavato santike imā gāthāyo abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sevetha pantāni senāsanāni,
::

::gatha2
Careyya saṃyojanavippamokkhā;
::

::gatha3
Sace ratiṃ nādhigaccheyya tattha,
::

::gathalast
Saṅghe vase rakkhitatto satīmā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kulākulaṃ piṇḍikāya caranto,
::

::gatha2
Indriyagutto {pb:T:1.0227} nipako satīmā;
::

::gatha3
Sevetha pantāni senāsanāni,
::

::gathalast
Bhayā pamutto abhaye vimutto.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yattha bheravā sarīsapā {note:siriṃ sapā (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)},
::

::gatha2
Vijju sañcarati thanayati devo;
::

::gatha3
Andhakāratimisāya rattiyā,
::

::gathalast
Nisīdi tattha bhikkhu vigatalomahaṃso.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idañhi jātu me diṭṭhaṃ, nayidaṃ itihītihaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ekasmiṃ brahmacariyasmiṃ, sahassaṃ maccuhāyinaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhiyyo {note:bhīyo (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} pañcasatā sekkhā, dasā ca dasadhā dasa;
::

::gathalast
Sabbe sotasamāpannā, atiracchānagāmino.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Athāyaṃ {pb:V:1.0182}{pb:M:1.0157} {note:atthāyaṃ-itipi dī. ni. 2.290} itarā pajā, puññabhāgāti me mano;
::

::gathalast
Saṅkhātuṃ nopi sakkomi, musāvādassa ottapa’’nti {note:ottapeti (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.), ottappeti (ka.)}.
::

#### 4. Aruṇavatīsuttaṃ

{para:185} 185\. Evaṃ {pb:P:1.0155} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati…pe… tatra kho bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi – ‘‘bhikkhavo’’ti. ‘‘Bhadante’’ti te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṃ. Bhagavā etadavoca –

‘‘Bhūtapubbaṃ, bhikkhave, rājā ahosi aruṇavā nāma. Rañño kho pana, bhikkhave, aruṇavato aruṇavatī nāma rājadhānī ahosi. Aruṇavatiṃ kho pana, bhikkhave, rājadhāniṃ {note:aruṇavatiyaṃ kho pana bhikkhave rājadhāniyaṃ (pī. ka.)} sikhī bhagavā {pb:T:1.0228} arahaṃ sammāsambuddho upanissāya vihāsi. Sikhissa kho pana, bhikkhave, bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa abhibhūsambhavaṃ nāma sāvakayugaṃ ahosi aggaṃ bhaddayugaṃ. Atha kho, bhikkhave, sikhī bhagavā arahaṃ sammāsambuddho abhibhuṃ bhikkhuṃ āmantesi – ‘āyāma, brāhmaṇa, yena aññataro brahmaloko tenupasaṅkamissāma, yāva bhattassa kālo bhavissatī’ti. ‘Evaṃ, bhante’ti kho bhikkhave, abhibhū bhikkhu sikhissa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa paccassosi. Atha kho, bhikkhave, sikhī bhagavā arahaṃ sammāsambuddho abhibhū ca bhikkhu – seyyathāpi nāma balavā puriso samiñjitaṃ vā bāhaṃ pasāreyya, pasāritaṃ vā bāhaṃ samiñjeyya evameva – aruṇavatiyā rājadhāniyā antarahitā tasmiṃ brahmaloke pāturahesuṃ.

‘‘Atha kho, bhikkhave, sikhī bhagavā arahaṃ sammāsambuddho abhibhuṃ bhikkhuṃ āmantesi – ‘paṭibhātu, brāhmaṇa, taṃ brahmuno ca brahmaparisāya ca brahmapārisajjānañca dhammī kathā’ti. ‘Evaṃ, bhante’ti kho, bhikkhave, abhibhū bhikkhu sikhissa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa paṭissutvā, brahmānañca brahmaparisañca brahmapārisajje ca dhammiyā kathāya sandassesi samādapesi samuttejesi sampahaṃsesi. Tatra sudaṃ, bhikkhave, brahmā ca brahmaparisā ca brahmapārisajjā {pb:P:1.0156} ca ujjhāyanti khiyyanti {note:khīyanti (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} vipācenti – ‘acchariyaṃ vata{pb:M:1.0158}, bho, abbhutaṃ vata bho, kathañhi nāma satthari sammukhībhūte sāvako dhammaṃ desessatī’’’ti{pb:T:1.0229}!

‘‘Atha {pb:V:1.0183} kho, bhikkhave, sikhī bhagavā arahaṃ sammāsambuddho abhibhuṃ bhikkhuṃ āmantesi – ‘ujjhāyanti kho te, brāhmaṇa, brahmā ca brahmaparisā ca brahmapārisajjā ca – acchariyaṃ vata, bho, abbhutaṃ vata, bho, kathañhi nāma satthari sammukhībhūte sāvako dhammaṃ desessatīti! Tena hi tvaṃ brāhmaṇa, bhiyyosomattāya brahmānañca brahmaparisañca brahmapārisajje ca saṃvejehī’ti. ‘Evaṃ, bhante’ti kho, bhikkhave, abhibhū bhikkhu sikhissa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa paṭissutvā dissamānenapi kāyena dhammaṃ desesi, adissamānenapi kāyena dhammaṃ desesi, dissamānenapi heṭṭhimena upaḍḍhakāyena adissamānena uparimena upaḍḍhakāyena dhammaṃ desesi, dissamānenapi uparimena upaḍḍhakāyena adissamānena heṭṭhimena upaḍḍhakāyena dhammaṃ desesi. Tatra sudaṃ, bhikkhave, brahmā ca brahmaparisā ca brahmapārisajjā ca acchariyabbhutacittajātā ahesuṃ – ‘acchariyaṃ vata, bho, abbhutaṃ vata, bho, samaṇassa mahiddhikatā mahānubhāvatā’’’ti!

‘‘Atha kho abhibhū bhikkhu sikhiṃ bhagavantaṃ arahantaṃ sammāsambuddhaṃ etadavoca – ‘abhijānāmi khvāhaṃ, bhante, bhikkhusaṅghassa majjhe evarūpiṃ vācaṃ bhāsitā – pahomi khvāhaṃ āvuso, brahmaloke ṭhito sahassilokadhātuṃ {pb:T:1.0230} {note:sahassīlokadhātuṃ (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} sarena viññāpetu’nti. ‘Etassa, brāhmaṇa, kālo, etassa, brāhmaṇa, kālo; yaṃ tvaṃ, brāhmaṇa, brahmaloke ṭhito sahassilokadhātuṃ sarena viññāpeyyāsī’ti. ‘Evaṃ, bhante’ti kho, bhikkhave, abhibhū bhikkhu sikhissa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa paṭissutvā brahmaloke ṭhito imā gāthāyo abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Ārambhatha {note:ārabbhatha (sabbattha)} nikkamatha {note:nikkhamatha (sī. pī.)}, yuñjatha buddhasāsane;
::

::gathalast
Dhunātha maccuno senaṃ, naḷāgāraṃva kuñjaro.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo {pb:P:1.0157} imasmiṃ dhammavinaye, appamatto vihassati;
::

::gathalast
Pahāya jātisaṃsāraṃ, dukkhassantaṃ karissatī’’ti.
::

‘‘Atha {pb:M:1.0159} kho, bhikkhave, sikhī ca bhagavā arahaṃ sammāsambuddho abhibhū ca bhikkhu brahmānañca brahmaparisañca brahmapārisajje ca saṃvejetvā – seyyathāpi nāma…pe… tasmiṃ brahmaloke antarahitā aruṇavatiyā rājadhāniyā pāturahesuṃ. Atha kho, bhikkhave, sikhī bhagavā {pb:V:1.0184} arahaṃ sammāsambuddho bhikkhū āmantesi – ‘assuttha no, tumhe, bhikkhave, abhibhussa bhikkhuno brahmaloke ṭhitassa gāthāyo bhāsamānassā’ti? ‘Assumha kho mayaṃ, bhante, abhibhussa bhikkhuno brahmaloke ṭhitassa gāthāyo bhāsamānassā’ti. ‘Yathā kathaṃ pana tumhe, bhikkhave, assuttha abhibhussa bhikkhuno brahmaloke ṭhitassa gāthāyo bhāsamānassā’’’ti? Evaṃ kho mayaṃ, bhante, assumha abhibhussa bhikkhuno brahmaloke ṭhitassa gāthāyo bhāsamānassa –

::gatha1
‘‘Ārambhatha nikkamatha, yuñjatha buddhasāsane;
::

::gathalast
Dhunātha maccuno senaṃ, naḷāgāraṃva kuñjaro.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo {pb:T:1.0231} imasmiṃ dhammavinaye, appamatto vihassati;
::

::gathalast
Pahāya jātisaṃsāraṃ, dukkhassantaṃ karissatī’’ti.
::

‘‘‘Evaṃ kho mayaṃ, bhante, assumha abhibhussa bhikkhuno brahmaloke ṭhitassa gāthāyo bhāsamānassā’ti. ‘Sādhu sādhu, bhikkhave; sādhu kho tumhe, bhikkhave! Assuttha abhibhussa bhikkhuno brahmaloke ṭhitassa gāthāyo bhāsamānassā’’’ti.

Idamavoca bhagavā, attamanā te bhikkhū bhagavato bhāsitaṃ abhinandunti.

#### 5. Parinibbānasuttaṃ

{para:186} 186\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā kusinārāyaṃ viharati upavattane mallānaṃ sālavane antarena yamakasālānaṃ parinibbānasamaye. Atha kho bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi – ‘‘handa dāni, bhikkhave{pb:P:1.0158}, āmantayāmi vo – ‘vayadhammā saṅkhārā, appamādena sampādethā’ti. Ayaṃ tathāgatassa pacchimā vācā’’.

Atha {pb:M:1.0160} kho bhagavā paṭhamaṃ jhānaṃ {note:paṭhamajjhānaṃ (syā. kaṃ.) evaṃ dutiyaṃ jhānaṃ iccādīsupi} samāpajji. Paṭhamā jhānā {note:paṭhamajjhānā (syā. kaṃ.) evaṃ dutiyā jhānā iccādīsupi} vuṭṭhahitvā dutiyaṃ jhānaṃ samāpajji. Dutiyā jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā tatiyaṃ jhānaṃ samāpajji. Tatiyā jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā catutthaṃ {pb:V:1.0185} jhānaṃ samāpajji. Catutthā jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā ākāsānañcāyatanaṃ samāpajji. Ākāsānañcāyatanā vuṭṭhahitvā viññāṇañcāyatanaṃ samāpajji. Viññāṇañcāyatanā vuṭṭhahitvā ākiñcaññāyatanaṃ samāpajji. Ākiñcaññāyatanā vuṭṭhahitvā nevasaññānāsaññāyatanaṃ samāpajji. Nevasaññānāsaññāyatanā {pb:T:1.0232} vuṭṭhahitvā saññāvedayitanirodhaṃ samāpajji.

Saññāvedayitanirodhā vuṭṭhahitvā nevasaññānāsaññāyatanaṃ samāpajji. Nevasaññānāsaññāyatanā vuṭṭhahitvā ākiñcaññāyatanaṃ samāpajji. Ākiñcaññāyatanā vuṭṭhahitvā viññāṇañcāyatanaṃ samāpajji. Viññāṇañcāyatanā vuṭṭhahitvā ākāsānañcāyatanaṃ samāpajji. Ākāsānañcāyatanā vuṭṭhahitvā catutthaṃ jhānaṃ samāpajji. Catutthā jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā tatiyaṃ jhānaṃ samāpajji. Tatiyā jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā dutiyaṃ jhānaṃ samāpajji. Dutiyā jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā paṭhamaṃ jhānaṃ samāpajji. Paṭhamā jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā dutiyaṃ jhānaṃ samāpajji. Dutiyā jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā tatiyaṃ jhānaṃ samāpajji. Tatiyā jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā catutthaṃ jhānaṃ samāpajji. Catutthā jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā samanantaraṃ bhagavā parinibbāyi. Parinibbute bhagavati saha parinibbānā brahmā sahampati imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbeva nikkhipissanti, bhūtā loke samussayaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Yattha etādiso satthā, loke appaṭipuggalo;
::

::gathalast
Tathāgato balappatto, sambuddho parinibbuto’’ti.
::

Parinibbute bhagavati saha parinibbānā sakko devānamindo imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Aniccā vata saṅkhārā, uppādavayadhammino;
::

::gathalast
Uppajjitvā nirujjhanti, tesaṃ vūpasamo sukho’’ti.
::

Parinibbute {pb:T:1.0233}{pb:M:1.0161} bhagavati saha parinibbānā āyasmā ānando imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Tadāsi yaṃ bhiṃsanakaṃ, tadāsi lomahaṃsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sabbākāravarūpete, sambuddhe parinibbute’’ti.
::

Parinibbute {pb:V:1.0186}{pb:P:1.0159} bhagavati saha parinibbānā āyasmā anuruddho imā gāthāyo abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Nāhu assāsapassāso, ṭhitacittassa tādino;
::

::gathalast
Anejo santimārabbha, cakkhumā parinibbuto {note:yaṃ kālamakarī muni (mahāparinibbānasutte)}.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Asallīnena cittena, vedanaṃ ajjhavāsayi;
::

::gathalast
Pajjotasseva nibbānaṃ, vimokkho cetaso ahū’’ti.
::

::centre
Dutiyo vaggo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Brahmāsanaṃ devadatto, andhakavindo aruṇavatī;
::

::gathalast
Parinibbānena ca desitaṃ, idaṃ brahmapañcakanti.
::

::centre
Brahmasaṃyuttaṃ samattaṃ. {note:ito paraṃ marammapotthakesu evampi dissati –§brahmāyācanaṃ agāravañca, brahmadevo bako ca brahmā.§aññataro ca brahmākokālikañca, tissakañca turū ca.§brahmā kokālikabhikkhu, sanaṅkumārena devadattaṃ.§andhakavindaṃ aruṇavati, parinibbānena pannarasāti.}
::

### 7. Brāhmaṇasaṃyuttaṃ

#### 1. Arahantavaggo

#### 1. Dhanañjānīsuttaṃ

{para:187} 187\. Evaṃ {pb:T:1.0235}{pb:V:1.0187}{pb:P:1.0160}{pb:M:1.0162} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati veḷuvane kalandakanivāpe. Tena kho pana samayena aññatarassa bhāradvājagottassa brāhmaṇassa dhanañjānī {note:dhānañjānī (pī. sī. aṭṭha.)} nāma brāhmaṇī abhippasannā hoti buddhe ca dhamme ca saṅghe ca. Atha kho dhanañjānī brāhmaṇī bhāradvājagottassa brāhmaṇassa bhattaṃ upasaṃharantī upakkhalitvā tikkhattuṃ udānaṃ udānesi –

::gatha1
‘‘Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa;
::

::gatha1
Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa;
::

::gathalast
Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassā’’ti.
::

Evaṃ vutte, bhāradvājagotto brāhmaṇo dhanañjāniṃ brāhmaṇiṃ etadavoca – ‘‘evamevaṃ panāyaṃ vasalī yasmiṃ vā tasmiṃ vā tassa muṇḍakassa samaṇassa vaṇṇaṃ bhāsati. Idāni tyāhaṃ, vasali, tassa satthuno vādaṃ āropessāmī’’ti. ‘‘Na khvāhaṃ taṃ, brāhmaṇa, passāmi sadevake loke samārake sabrahmake sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya, yo tassa bhagavato vādaṃ āropeyya arahato sammāsambuddhassa. Api ca tvaṃ, brāhmaṇa, gaccha, gantvā vijānissasī’’ti {note:gantvāpi jānissasīti (syā. kaṃ.)}.

Atha {pb:T:1.0236} kho bhāradvājagotto brāhmaṇo kupito anattamano yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavatā saddhiṃ sammodi. Sammodanīyaṃ kathaṃ sāraṇīyaṃ vītisāretvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi. Ekamantaṃ {pb:P:1.0161} nisinno kho bhāradvājagotto brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsu {pb:V:1.0188} chetvā sukhaṃ seti, kiṃsu chetvā na socati;
::

::gathalast
Kissassu ekadhammassa, vadhaṃ rocesi gotamā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kodhaṃ {pb:M:1.0163} chetvā sukhaṃ seti, kodhaṃ chetvā na socati;
::

::gatha2
Kodhassa visamūlassa, madhuraggassa brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
Vadhaṃ ariyā pasaṃsanti, tañhi chetvā na socatī’’ti.
::

Evaṃ vutte, bhāradvājagotto brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama, abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama! Seyyathāpi, bho gotama, nikkujjitaṃ vā ukkujjeyya, paṭicchannaṃ vā vivareyya, mūḷhassa vā maggaṃ ācikkheyya, andhakāre vā telapajjotaṃ dhāreyya – cakkhumanto rūpāni dakkhantīti; evamevaṃ bhotā gotamena anekapariyāyena dhammo pakāsito. Esāhaṃ, bhante, bhagavantaṃ gotamaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi dhammañca bhikkhusaṅghañca. Labheyyāhaṃ bhoto gotamassa santike pabbajjaṃ, labheyyaṃ upasampada’’nti.

Alattha kho bhāradvājagotto brāhmaṇo bhagavato santike pabbajjaṃ, alattha upasampadaṃ. Acirūpasampanno kho panāyasmā bhāradvājo eko vūpakaṭṭho appamatto {pb:T:1.0237} ātāpī pahitatto viharanto nacirasseva – yassatthāya kulaputtā sammadeva agārasmā anagāriyaṃ pabbajanti tadanuttaraṃ – brahmacariyapariyosānaṃ diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṃ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja vihāsi. ‘‘Khīṇā jāti, vusitaṃ brahmacariyaṃ, kataṃ karaṇīyaṃ, nāparaṃ itthattāyā’’ti abbhaññāsi. Aññataro ca panāyasmā bhāradvājo arahataṃ ahosīti.

#### 2. Akkosasuttaṃ

{para:188} 188\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati veḷuvane kalandakanivāpe. Assosi kho akkosakabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo – ‘‘bhāradvājagotto kira brāhmaṇo samaṇassa gotamassa santike agārasmā anagāriyaṃ pabbajito’’ti kupito anattamano yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā {pb:P:1.0162} bhagavantaṃ asabbhāhi pharusāhi vācāhi akkosati paribhāsati.

Evaṃ {pb:V:1.0189} vutte, bhagavā akkosakabhāradvājaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘taṃ kiṃ maññasi, brāhmaṇa, api nu kho te āgacchanti mittāmaccā ñātisālohitā atithiyo {note:atithayo (?)}’’ti? ‘‘Appekadā me, bho gotama, āgacchanti mittāmaccā {pb:M:1.0164} ñātisālohitā atithiyo’’ti. ‘‘‘Taṃ kiṃ maññasi, brāhmaṇa, api nu tesaṃ anuppadesi khādanīyaṃ vā bhojanīyaṃ vā sāyanīyaṃ vā’’’ti? ‘‘‘Appekadā nesāhaṃ, bho gotama, anuppademi khādanīyaṃ vā bhojanīyaṃ vā sāyanīyaṃ vā’’’ti. ‘‘‘Sace kho pana te, brāhmaṇa, nappaṭiggaṇhanti{pb:T:1.0238}, kassa taṃ hotī’’’ti? ‘‘‘Sace te, bho gotama, nappaṭiggaṇhanti, amhākameva taṃ hotī’’’ti. ‘‘Evameva kho, brāhmaṇa, yaṃ tvaṃ amhe anakkosante akkosasi, arosente rosesi, abhaṇḍante bhaṇḍasi, taṃ te mayaṃ nappaṭiggaṇhāma. Tavevetaṃ, brāhmaṇa, hoti; tavevetaṃ, brāhmaṇa, hoti’’.

‘‘Yo kho, brāhmaṇa, akkosantaṃ paccakkosati, rosentaṃ paṭiroseti, bhaṇḍantaṃ paṭibhaṇḍati, ayaṃ vuccati, brāhmaṇa, sambhuñjati vītiharatīti. Te mayaṃ tayā neva sambhuñjāma na vītiharāma. Tavevetaṃ, brāhmaṇa, hoti; tavevetaṃ, brāhmaṇa, hotī’’ti. ‘‘Bhavantaṃ kho gotamaṃ sarājikā parisā evaṃ jānāti – ‘arahaṃ samaṇo gotamo’ti. Atha ca pana bhavaṃ gotamo kujjhatī’’ti.

::gatha1
‘‘Akkodhassa kuto kodho, dantassa samajīvino;
::

::gathalast
Sammadaññā vimuttassa, upasantassa tādino.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasseva tena pāpiyo, yo kuddhaṃ paṭikujjhati;
::

::gathalast
Kuddhaṃ appaṭikujjhanto, saṅgāmaṃ jeti dujjayaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ubhinnamatthaṃ carati, attano ca parassa ca;
::

::gathalast
Paraṃ saṅkupitaṃ ñatvā, yo sato upasammati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ubhinnaṃ tikicchantānaṃ, attano ca parassa ca;
::

::gathalast
Janā maññanti bāloti, ye dhammassa akovidā’’ti.
::

Evaṃ {pb:V:1.0190}{pb:P:1.0163} vutte, akkosakabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama…pe… esāhaṃ {pb:T:1.0239} bhavantaṃ gotamaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi dhammañca bhikkhusaṅghañca. Labheyyāhaṃ, bhante, bhoto gotamassa santike pabbajjaṃ, labheyyaṃ upasampada’’nti.

Alattha kho akkosakabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavato santike pabbajjaṃ, alattha upasampadaṃ. Acirūpasampanno kho panāyasmā akkosakabhāradvājo eko vūpakaṭṭho appamatto ātāpī pahitatto viharanto {pb:M:1.0165} nacirasseva – yassatthāya kulaputtā sammadeva agārasmā anagāriyaṃ pabbajanti tadanuttaraṃ – brahmacariyapariyosānaṃ diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṃ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja vihāsi. ‘‘Khīṇā jāti, vusitaṃ brahmacariyaṃ, kataṃ karaṇīyaṃ nāparaṃ itthattāyā’’ti abbhaññāsi. Aññataro ca panāyasmā bhāradvājo arahataṃ ahosīti.

#### 3. Asurindakasuttaṃ

{para:189} 189\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati veḷuvane kalandakanivāpe. Assosi kho asurindakabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo – ‘‘bhāradvājagotto brāhmaṇo kira samaṇassa gotamassa santike agārasmā anagāriyaṃ pabbajito’’ti kupito anattamano yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ asabbhāhi pharusāhi vācāhi akkosati paribhāsati. Evaṃ vutte, bhagavā tuṇhī ahosi. Atha kho asurindakabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘jitosi, samaṇa, jitosi, samaṇā’’ti.

::gatha1
‘‘Jayaṃ {pb:T:1.0240} ve maññati bālo, vācāya pharusaṃ bhaṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Jayañcevassa taṃ hoti, yā titikkhā vijānato.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasseva tena pāpiyo, yo kuddhaṃ paṭikujjhati;
::

::gathalast
Kuddhaṃ appaṭikujjhanto, saṅgāmaṃ jeti dujjayaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ubhinnamatthaṃ carati, attano ca parassa ca;
::

::gathalast
Paraṃ saṅkupitaṃ ñatvā, yo sato upasammati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ubhinnaṃ {pb:V:1.0191} tikicchantānaṃ, attano ca parassa ca;
::

::gathalast
Janā maññanti bāloti, ye dhammassa akovidā’’ti.
::

Evaṃ {pb:P:1.0164} vutte, asurindakabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama…pe… abbhaññāsi. Aññataro ca panāyasmā bhāradvājo arahataṃ ahosī’’ti.

#### 4. Bilaṅgikasuttaṃ

{para:190} 190\. Ekaṃ {pb:M:1.0166} samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati veḷuvane kalandakanivāpe. Assosi kho bilaṅgikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo – ‘‘bhāradvājagotto kira brāhmaṇo samaṇassa gotamassa santike agārasmā anagāriyaṃ pabbajito’’ti kupito anattamano yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā tuṇhībhūto ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Atha kho bhagavā bilaṅgikassa bhāradvājassa brāhmaṇassa cetasā cetoparivitakkamaññāya bilaṅgikaṃ bhāradvājaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi {pb:T:1.0241} –

::gatha1
‘‘Yo appaduṭṭhassa narassa dussati,
::

::gatha2
Suddhassa posassa anaṅgaṇassa;
::

::gatha3
Tameva bālaṃ pacceti pāpaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Sukhumo rajo paṭivātaṃva khitto’’ti.
::

Evaṃ vutte, vilaṅgikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama…pe… abbhaññāsi. Aññataro ca panāyasmā bhāradvājo arahataṃ ahosī’’ti.

#### 5. Ahiṃsakasuttaṃ

{para:191} 191\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Atha kho ahiṃsakabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavatā saddhiṃ sammodi. Sammodanīyaṃ kathaṃ sāraṇīyaṃ vītisāretvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi. Ekamantaṃ {pb:P:1.0165} nisinno kho ahiṃsakabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘ahiṃsakāhaṃ, bho gotama, ahiṃsakāhaṃ, bho gotamā’’ti.

::gatha1
‘‘Yathā {pb:T:1.0242}{pb:V:1.0192} nāmaṃ tathā cassa, siyā kho tvaṃ ahiṃsako;
::

::gatha2
Yo ca kāyena vācāya, manasā ca na hiṃsati;
::

::gathalast
Sa ve ahiṃsako hoti, yo paraṃ na vihiṃsatī’’ti.
::

Evaṃ vutte, ahiṃsakabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama…pe… abbhaññāsi. Aññataro ca panāyasmā ahiṃsakabhāradvājo arahataṃ ahosī’’ti.

#### 6. Jaṭāsuttaṃ

{para:192} 192\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:M:1.0167}. Atha kho jaṭābhāradvājo brāhmaṇo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavatā saddhiṃ sammodi. Sammodanīyaṃ kathaṃ sāraṇīyaṃ vītisāretvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi. Ekamantaṃ nisinno kho jaṭābhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Antojaṭā bahijaṭā, jaṭāya jaṭitā pajā;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ taṃ gotama pucchāmi, ko imaṃ vijaṭaye jaṭa’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sīle patiṭṭhāya naro sapañño, cittaṃ paññañca bhāvayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ātāpī nipako bhikkhu, so imaṃ vijaṭaye jaṭaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yesaṃ rāgo ca doso ca, avijjā ca virājitā;
::

::gathalast
Khīṇāsavā arahanto, tesaṃ vijaṭitā jaṭā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yattha nāmañca rūpañca, asesaṃ uparujjhati;
::

::gathalast
Paṭighaṃ rūpasaññā ca, etthesā chijjate jaṭā’’ti.
::

Evaṃ {pb:T:1.0243} vutte, jaṭābhāradvājo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama…pe… aññataro ca panāyasmā bhāradvājo arahataṃ ahosī’’ti.

#### 7. Suddhikasuttaṃ

{para:193} 193\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:V:1.0193}. Atha kho suddhikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavatā saddhiṃ sammodi. Sammodanīyaṃ kathaṃ sāraṇīyaṃ vītisāretvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi. Ekamantaṃ {pb:P:1.0166} nisinno kho suddhikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Na brāhmaṇo {note:nābrāhmaṇo (?)} sujjhati koci, loke sīlavāpi tapokaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vijjācaraṇasampanno, so sujjhati na aññā itarā pajā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bahumpi palapaṃ jappaṃ, na jaccā hoti brāhmaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Antokasambu saṅkiliṭṭho, kuhanaṃ upanissito.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Khattiyo {pb:M:1.0168} brāhmaṇo vesso, suddo caṇḍālapukkuso;
::

::gatha2
Āraddhavīriyo pahitatto, niccaṃ daḷhaparakkamo;
::

::gathalast
Pappoti paramaṃ suddhiṃ, evaṃ jānāhi brāhmaṇā’’ti.
::

Evaṃ vutte, suddhikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama…pe… aññataro ca panāyasmā bhāradvājo arahataṃ ahosī’’ti.

#### 8. Aggikasuttaṃ

{para:194} 194\. Ekaṃ {pb:T:1.0244} samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati veḷuvane kalandakanivāpe. Tena kho pana samayena aggikabhāradvājassa brāhmaṇassa sappinā pāyaso sannihito hoti – ‘‘aggiṃ juhissāmi, aggihuttaṃ paricarissāmī’’ti.

Atha kho bhagavā pubbaṇhasamayaṃ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya rājagahaṃ piṇḍāya pāvisi. Rājagahe sapadānaṃ piṇḍāya caramāno yena aggikabhāradvājassa brāhmaṇassa nivesanaṃ tenupasaṅkami{pb:V:1.0194}; upasaṅkamitvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Addasā kho aggikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ piṇḍāya ṭhitaṃ. Disvāna bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Tīhi vijjāhi sampanno, jātimā sutavā bahū;
::

::gathalast
Vijjācaraṇasampanno, somaṃ bhuñjeyya pāyasa’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bahumpi palapaṃ jappaṃ, na jaccā hoti brāhmaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Antokasambu saṃkiliṭṭho, kuhanāparivārito.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ {pb:P:1.0167} yo vedī, saggāpāyañca passati;
::

::gathalast
Atho jātikkhayaṃ patto, abhiññāvosito muni.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etāhi tīhi vijjāhi, tevijjo hoti brāhmaṇo;
::

::gathalast
Vijjācaraṇasampanno, somaṃ bhuñjeyya pāyasa’’nti.
::

‘‘Bhuñjatu bhavaṃ gotamo. Brāhmaṇo bhava’’nti.

::gatha1
‘‘Gāthābhigītaṃ {pb:T:1.0245}{pb:M:1.0169} me abhojaneyyaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Sampassataṃ brāhmaṇa nesa dhammo;
::

::gatha3
Gāthābhigītaṃ panudanti buddhā,
::

::gathalast
Dhamme sati brāhmaṇa vuttiresā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aññena ca kevalinaṃ mahesiṃ,
::

::gatha2
Khīṇāsavaṃ kukkuccavūpasantaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Annena pānena upaṭṭhahassu,
::

::gathalast
Khettañhi taṃ puññapekkhassa hotī’’ti.
::

Evaṃ {pb:V:1.0195} vutte, aggikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama…pe… aññataro ca panāyasmā aggikabhāradvājo arahataṃ ahosī’’ti.

#### 9. Sundarikasuttaṃ

{para:195} 195\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā kosalesu viharati sundarikāya nadiyā tīre. Tena kho pana samayena sundarikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo sundarikāya nadiyā tīre aggiṃ juhati, aggihuttaṃ paricarati. Atha kho sundarikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo aggiṃ juhitvā aggihuttaṃ paricaritvā uṭṭhāyāsanā samantā catuddisā anuvilokesi – ‘‘ko nu kho imaṃ habyasesaṃ bhuñjeyyā’’ti? Addasā kho sundarikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ aññatarasmiṃ rukkhamūle sasīsaṃ pārutaṃ nisinnaṃ. Disvāna vāmena hatthena {pb:T:1.0246} habyasesaṃ gahetvā dakkhiṇena hatthena kamaṇḍaluṃ gahetvā yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami. Atha kho bhagavā sundarikabhāradvājassa brāhmaṇassa padasaddena sīsaṃ vivari. Atha kho sundarikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo ‘muṇḍo ayaṃ {pb:P:1.0168} bhavaṃ, muṇḍako ayaṃ bhava’nti tatova puna nivattitukāmo ahosi. Atha kho sundarikabhāradvājassa brāhmaṇassa etadahosi – ‘muṇḍāpi hi idhekacce brāhmaṇā bhavanti; yaṃnūnāhaṃ taṃ upasaṅkamitvā jātiṃ puccheyya’nti.

Atha kho sundarikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘kiṃjacco bhava’nti?

::gatha1
‘‘Mā {pb:M:1.0170} jātiṃ puccha caraṇañca puccha,
::

::gatha2
Kaṭṭhā have jāyati jātavedo;
::

::gatha3
Nīcākulīnopi muni dhitimā,
::

::gathalast
Ājānīyo hoti hirīnisedho.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saccena danto damasā upeto,
::

::gatha2
Vedantagū vusitabrahmacariyo;
::

::gatha3
Yaññopanīto {pb:V:1.0196} tamupavhayetha,
::

::gathalast
Kālena so juhati dakkhiṇeyye’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addhā suyiṭṭhaṃ suhutaṃ mama yidaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Yaṃ tādisaṃ vedagumaddasāmi;
::

::gatha3
Tumhādisānañhi {pb:T:1.0247} adassanena,
::

::gathalast
Añño jano bhuñjati habyasesa’’nti.
::

‘‘Bhuñjatu bhavaṃ gotamo. Brāhmaṇo bhava’’nti.

::gatha1
‘‘Gāthābhigītaṃ me abhojaneyyaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Sampassataṃ brāhmaṇa nesa dhammo;
::

::gatha3
Gāthābhigītaṃ panudanti buddhā,
::

::gathalast
Dhamme sati brāhmaṇa vuttiresā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aññena ca kevalinaṃ mahesiṃ,
::

::gatha2
Khīṇāsavaṃ kukkuccavūpasantaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Annena pānena upaṭṭhahassu,
::

::gathalast
Khettañhi taṃ puññapekkhassa hotī’’ti.
::

‘‘Atha kassa cāhaṃ, bho gotama, imaṃ habyasesaṃ dammī’’ti? ‘‘Na khvāhaṃ, brāhmaṇa, passāmi sadevake loke samārake sabrahmake sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya yasseso habyaseso bhutto sammā pariṇāmaṃ gaccheyya {pb:P:1.0169} aññatra, brāhmaṇa, tathāgatassa vā tathāgatasāvakassa vā. Tena hi tvaṃ, brāhmaṇa, taṃ habyasesaṃ appaharite vā chaḍḍehi appāṇake vā udake opilāpehī’’ti.

Atha kho sundarikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo taṃ habyasesaṃ appāṇake udake opilāpesi. Atha kho so habyaseso udake pakkhitto cicciṭāyati {pb:M:1.0171} ciṭiciṭāyati sandhūpāyati sampadhūpāyati{pb:V:1.0197}. Seyyathāpi nāma {pb:T:1.0248} phālo {note:loho (ka.)} divasaṃsantatto {note:divasasantatto (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} udake pakkhitto cicciṭāyati ciṭiciṭāyati sandhūpāyati sampadhūpāyati; evameva so habyaseso udake pakkhitto cicciṭāyati ciṭiciṭāyati sandhūpāyati sampadhūpāyati.

Atha kho sundarikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo saṃviggo lomahaṭṭhajāto yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṃ ṭhitaṃ kho sundarikabhāradvājaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ bhagavā gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Mā brāhmaṇa dāru samādahāno,
::

::gatha2
Suddhiṃ amaññi bahiddhā hi etaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Na hi tena suddhiṃ kusalā vadanti,
::

::gathalast
Yo bāhirena parisuddhimicche.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Hitvā ahaṃ brāhmaṇa dārudāhaṃ
::

::gatha2
Ajjhattamevujjalayāmi {note:ajjhattameva jalayāmi (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} jotiṃ;
::

::gatha1
Niccagginī niccasamāhitatto,
::

::gathalast
Arahaṃ ahaṃ brahmacariyaṃ carāmi.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Māno hi te brāhmaṇa khāribhāro,
::

::gatha2
Kodho dhumo bhasmani mosavajjaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Jivhā sujā hadayaṃ jotiṭhānaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Attā sudanto purisassa joti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammo {pb:T:1.0249} rahado brāhmaṇa sīlatittho,
::

::gatha2
Anāvilo sabbhi sataṃ pasattho;
::

::gatha3
Yattha have vedaguno sinātā,
::

::gathalast
Anallagattāva {note:anallīnagattāva (sī. pī. ka.)} taranti pāraṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saccaṃ dhammo saṃyamo brahmacariyaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Majjhe sitā brāhmaṇa brahmapatti;
::

::gatha3
Sa {pb:V:1.0198}{pb:P:1.0170} tujjubhūtesu namo karohi,
::

::gathalast
Tamahaṃ naraṃ dhammasārīti brūmī’’ti.
::

Evaṃ {pb:M:1.0172} vutte, sundarikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama…pe… aññataro ca panāyasmā bhāradvājo arahataṃ ahosī’’ti.

#### 10. Bahudhītarasuttaṃ

{para:196} 196\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe. Tena kho pana samayena aññatarassa bhāradvājagottassa brāhmaṇassa catuddasa balībaddā naṭṭhā honti. Atha kho bhāradvājagotto brāhmaṇo te balībadde gavesanto yena so vanasaṇḍo tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā addasa bhagavantaṃ tasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe nisinnaṃ pallaṅkaṃ ābhujitvā ujuṃ kāyaṃ paṇidhāya parimukhaṃ satiṃ upaṭṭhapetvā. Disvāna yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavato santike imā gāthāyo abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:T:1.0250} hi nūnimassa {note:nahanūnimassa (sī. syā. kaṃ.)} samaṇassa, balībaddā catuddasa;
::

::gathalast
Ajjasaṭṭhiṃ na dissanti, tenāyaṃ samaṇo sukhī.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na hi nūnimassa samaṇassa, tilākhettasmi pāpakā;
::

::gathalast
Ekapaṇṇā dupaṇṇā {note:dvipaṇṇā (sī. pī.)} ca, tenāyaṃ samaṇo sukhī.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na hi nūnimassa samaṇassa, tucchakoṭṭhasmi mūsikā;
::

::gathalast
Ussoḷhikāya naccanti, tenāyaṃ samaṇo sukhī.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na hi nūnimassa samaṇassa, santhāro sattamāsiko;
::

::gathalast
Uppāṭakehi sañchanno, tenāyaṃ samaṇo sukhī.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:V:1.0199} hi nūnimassa samaṇassa, vidhavā satta dhītaro;
::

::gathalast
Ekaputtā duputtā {note:dviputtā (sī. pī.)} ca, tenāyaṃ samaṇo sukhī.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na hi nūnimassa samaṇassa, piṅgalā tilakāhatā;
::

::gathalast
Sottaṃ pādena bodheti, tenāyaṃ samaṇo sukhī.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na hi nūnimassa samaṇassa, paccūsamhi iṇāyikā;
::

::gathalast
Detha dethāti codenti, tenāyaṃ samaṇo sukhī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:M:1.0173} hi mayhaṃ brāhmaṇa, balībaddā catuddasa;
::

::gathalast
Ajjasaṭṭhiṃ na dissanti, tenāhaṃ brāhmaṇā sukhī.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:P:1.0171} hi mayhaṃ brāhmaṇa, tilākhettasmi pāpakā;
::

::gathalast
Ekapaṇṇā dupaṇṇā ca, tenāhaṃ brāhmaṇā sukhī.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na hi mayhaṃ brāhmaṇa, tucchakoṭṭhasmi mūsikā;
::

::gathalast
Ussoḷhikāya naccanti, tenāhaṃ brāhmaṇā sukhī.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:T:1.0251} hi mayhaṃ brāhmaṇa, santhāro sattamāsiko;
::

::gathalast
Uppāṭakehi sañchanno, tenāhaṃ brāhmaṇā sukhī.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na hi mayhaṃ brāhmaṇa, vidhavā satta dhītaro;
::

::gathalast
Ekaputtā duputtā ca, tenāhaṃ brāhmaṇā sukhī.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na hi mayhaṃ brāhmaṇa, piṅgalā tilakāhatā;
::

::gathalast
Sottaṃ pādena bodheti, tenāhaṃ brāhmaṇā sukhī.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:V:1.0200} hi mayhaṃ brāhmaṇa, paccūsamhi iṇāyikā;
::

::gathalast
Detha dethāti codenti, tenāhaṃ brāhmaṇā sukhī’’ti.
::

Evaṃ vutte, bhāradvājagotto brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama, abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama! Seyyathāpi, bho gotama, nikkujjitaṃ vā ukkujjeyya, paṭicchannaṃ vā vivareyya, mūḷhassa vā maggaṃ ācikkheyya, andhakāre vā telapajjotaṃ dhāreyya – cakkhumanto rūpāni dakkhantīti; evameva bhotā gotamena anekapariyāyena dhammo pakāsito. Esāhaṃ bhavantaṃ gotamaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāmi dhammañca bhikkhusaṅghañca. Labheyyāhaṃ bhoto gotamassa santike pabbajjaṃ, labheyyaṃ upasampada’’nti.

Alattha kho bhāradvājagotto brāhmaṇo bhagavato santike pabbajjaṃ, alattha upasampadaṃ. Acirūpasampanno panāyasmā bhāradvājo eko vūpakaṭṭho appamatto ātāpī pahitatto viharanto nacirasseva – yassatthāya kulaputtā sammadeva agārasmā anagāriyaṃ pabbajanti, tadanuttaraṃ – brahmacariyapariyosānaṃ {pb:T:1.0252} diṭṭheva dhamme sayaṃ abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja vihāsi. ‘‘Khīṇā jāti, vusitaṃ brahmacariyaṃ, kataṃ karaṇīyaṃ, nāparaṃ {pb:M:1.0174} itthattāyā’’ti abbhaññāsi. Aññataro ca panāyasmā bhāradvājo arahataṃ ahosīti.

::centre
Arahantavaggo paṭhamo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Dhanañjānī ca akkosaṃ, asurindaṃ bilaṅgikaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Ahiṃsakaṃ jaṭā ceva, suddhikañceva aggikā;
::

::gathalast
Sundarikaṃ bahudhītarena ca te dasāti.
::

#### 2. Upāsakavaggo

#### 1. Kasibhāradvājasuttaṃ

{para:197} 197\. Evaṃ {pb:T:1.0253}{pb:V:1.0201}{pb:P:1.0172} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā magadhesu viharati dakkhiṇāgirismiṃ ekanāḷāyaṃ brāhmaṇagāme. Tena kho pana samayena kasibhāradvājassa {note:kasikabhāradvājassa (ka.)} brāhmaṇassa pañcamattāni naṅgalasatāni payuttāni honti vappakāle. Atha kho bhagavā pubbaṇhasamayaṃ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya yena kasibhāradvājassa brāhmaṇassa kammanto tenupasaṅkami.

Tena kho pana samayena kasibhāradvājassa brāhmaṇassa parivesanā vattati. Atha kho bhagavā yena parivesanā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Addasā kho kasibhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ piṇḍāya ṭhitaṃ. Disvā bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘ahaṃ kho, samaṇa, kasāmi ca vapāmi ca, kasitvā ca vapitvā ca bhuñjāmi. Tvampi, samaṇa, kasassu ca vapassu ca, kasitvā ca vapitvā ca bhuñjassū’’ti. ‘‘Ahampi kho, brāhmaṇa, kasāmi ca vapāmi ca, kasitvā ca vapitvā ca bhuñjāmī’’ti. Na kho mayaṃ passāma bhoto gotamassa yugaṃ vā naṅgalaṃ vā phālaṃ vā pācanaṃ vā balībadde vā, atha ca pana {pb:T:1.0254} bhavaṃ gotamo evamāha – ‘‘ahampi kho, brāhmaṇa, kasāmi ca vapāmi ca, kasitvā ca vapitvā ca bhuñjāmī’’ti{pb:M:1.0175}. Atha kho kasibhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kassako paṭijānāsi, na ca passāmi te kasiṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kassako pucchito brūhi, kathaṃ jānemu taṃ kasi’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saddhā bījaṃ tapo vuṭṭhi, paññā me yuganaṅgalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Hirī īsā mano yottaṃ, sati me phālapācanaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kāyagutto {pb:V:1.0202} vacīgutto, āhāre udare yato;
::

::gathalast
Saccaṃ karomi niddānaṃ, soraccaṃ me pamocanaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vīriyaṃ {pb:P:1.0173} me dhuradhorayhaṃ, yogakkhemādhivāhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Gacchati anivattantaṃ, yattha gantvā na socati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evamesā kasī kaṭṭhā, sā hoti amatapphalā;
::

::gathalast
Etaṃ kasiṃ kasitvāna, sabbadukkhā pamuccatī’’ti.
::

‘‘Bhuñjatu bhavaṃ gotamo. Kassako bhavaṃ. Yañhi bhavaṃ gotamo amatapphalampi kasiṃ kasatī’’ti {note:bhāsatīti (ka.)}.

::gatha1
‘‘Gāthābhigītaṃ me abhojaneyyaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Sampassataṃ brāhmaṇa nesa dhammo;
::

::gatha3
Gāthābhigītaṃ panudanti buddhā,
::

::gathalast
Dhamme sati brāhmaṇa vuttiresā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aññena {pb:T:1.0255} ca kevalinaṃ mahesiṃ,
::

::gatha2
Khīṇāsavaṃ kukkuccavūpasantaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Annena pānena upaṭṭhahassu,
::

::gathalast
Khettañhi taṃ puññapekkhassa hotī’’ti.
::

Evaṃ vutte, kasibhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama…pe… ajjatagge pāṇupetaṃ saraṇaṃ gata’’nti.

#### 2. Udayasuttaṃ

{para:198} 198\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Atha kho bhagavā pubbaṇhasamayaṃ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya yena {pb:V:1.0203} udayassa brāhmaṇassa nivesanaṃ tenupasaṅkami. Atha {pb:M:1.0176} kho udayo brāhmaṇo bhagavato pattaṃ odanena pūresi. Dutiyampi kho bhagavā pubbaṇhasamayaṃ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya yena udayassa brāhmaṇassa nivesanaṃ tenupasaṅkami…pe… tatiyampi kho udayo brāhmaṇo bhagavato pattaṃ odanena {pb:P:1.0174} pūretvā bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘pakaṭṭhakoyaṃ samaṇo gotamo punappunaṃ āgacchatī’’ti.

::gatha1
‘‘Punappunañceva {pb:T:1.0256} vapanti bījaṃ, punappunaṃ vassati devarājā;
::

::gathalast
Punappunaṃ khettaṃ kasanti kassakā, punappunaṃ dhaññamupeti raṭṭhaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Punappunaṃ yācakā yācayanti, punappunaṃ dānapatī dadanti;
::

::gathalast
Punappunaṃ dānapatī daditvā, punappunaṃ saggamupenti ṭhānaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Punappunaṃ khīranikā duhanti, punappunaṃ vaccho upeti mātaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Punappunaṃ kilamati phandati ca, punappunaṃ gabbhamupeti mando.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Punappunaṃ jāyati mīyati ca, punappunaṃ sivathikaṃ {note:sīvathikaṃ (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} haranti;
::

::gathalast
Maggañca laddhā apunabbhavāya, na punappunaṃ jāyati bhūripañño’’ti {note:punappunaṃ jāyati bhūripaññoti (syā. kaṃ. ka.)}.
::

Evaṃ vutte, udayo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama…pe… upāsakaṃ maṃ bhavaṃ gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupetaṃ saraṇaṃ gata’’nti.

#### 3. Devahitasuttaṃ

{para:199} 199\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:T:1.0257}. Tena kho pana samayena bhagavā vātehābādhiko hoti; āyasmā ca upavāṇo bhagavato upaṭṭhāko hoti. Atha kho bhagavā āyasmantaṃ upavāṇaṃ āmantesi – ‘‘iṅgha me tvaṃ, upavāṇa, uṇhodakaṃ jānāhī’’ti. ‘‘Evaṃ, bhante’’ti kho āyasmā upavāṇo bhagavato paṭissutvā nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya yena devahitassa brāhmaṇassa nivesanaṃ tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā tuṇhībhūto ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Addasā kho devahito brāhmaṇo āyasmantaṃ {pb:V:1.0204} upavāṇaṃ tuṇhībhūtaṃ ekamantaṃ ṭhitaṃ. Disvāna āyasmantaṃ upavāṇaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Tuṇhībhūto {pb:M:1.0177}{pb:P:1.0175} bhavaṃ tiṭṭhaṃ, muṇḍo saṅghāṭipāruto;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃ patthayāno kiṃ esaṃ, kiṃ nu yācitumāgato’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Arahaṃ sugato loke, vātehābādhiko muni;
::

::gathalast
Sace uṇhodakaṃ atthi, munino dehi brāhmaṇa.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pūjito pūjaneyyānaṃ, sakkareyyāna sakkato;
::

::gathalast
Apacito apaceyyānaṃ {note:apacineyyānaṃ (sī. syā. kaṃ.) ṭīkā oloketabbā}, tassa icchāmi hātave’’ti.
::

Atha kho devahito brāhmaṇo uṇhodakassa kājaṃ purisena gāhāpetvā phāṇitassa ca puṭaṃ āyasmato upavāṇassa pādāsi. Atha kho āyasmā upavāṇo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ {pb:T:1.0258} uṇhodakena nhāpetvā {note:nahāpetvā (sī. pī.)} uṇhodakena phāṇitaṃ āloletvā bhagavato pādāsi. Atha kho bhagavato ābādho paṭippassambhi.

Atha kho devahito brāhmaṇo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavatā saddhiṃ sammodi. Sammodanīyaṃ kathaṃ sāraṇīyaṃ vītisāretvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi. Ekamantaṃ nisinno kho devahito brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kattha dajjā deyyadhammaṃ, kattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kathañhi yajamānassa, kathaṃ ijjhati dakkhiṇā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ yo vedī, saggāpāyañca passati;
::

::gathalast
Atho jātikkhayaṃ patto, abhiññāvosito muni.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ettha {pb:V:1.0205} dajjā deyyadhammaṃ, ettha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Evañhi yajamānassa, evaṃ ijjhati dakkhiṇā’’ti.
::

Evaṃ vutte, devahito brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ bho gotama…pe… upāsakaṃ maṃ bhavaṃ gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupetaṃ saraṇaṃ gata’’nti.

#### 4. Mahāsālasuttaṃ

{para:200} 200\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:M:1.0178}. Atha kho aññataro brāhmaṇamahāsālo lūkho lūkhapāvuraṇo {pb:P:1.0176} {note:lūkhapāpuraṇo (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavatā saddhiṃ sammodi. Sammodanīyaṃ kathaṃ sāraṇīyaṃ vītisāretvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi. Ekamantaṃ nisinnaṃ kho taṃ brāhmaṇamahāsālaṃ bhagavā {pb:T:1.0259} etadavoca – ‘‘kinnu tvaṃ, brāhmaṇa, lūkho lūkhapāvuraṇo’’ti? ‘‘Idha me, bho gotama, cattāro puttā. Te maṃ dārehi saṃpuccha gharā nikkhāmentī’’ti. ‘‘Tena hi tvaṃ, brāhmaṇa, imā gāthāyo pariyāpuṇitvā sabhāyaṃ mahājanakāye sannipatite puttesu ca sannisinnesu bhāsassu –

::gatha1
‘‘Yehi jātehi nandissaṃ, yesañca bhavamicchisaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Te maṃ dārehi saṃpuccha, sāva vārenti sūkaraṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Asantā kira maṃ jammā, tāta tātāti bhāsare;
::

::gathalast
Rakkhasā puttarūpena, te jahanti vayogataṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Assova jiṇṇo nibbhogo, khādanā apanīyati;
::

::gathalast
Bālakānaṃ pitā thero, parāgāresu bhikkhati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Daṇḍova kira me seyyo, yañce puttā anassavā;
::

::gathalast
Caṇḍampi goṇaṃ vāreti, atho caṇḍampi kukkuraṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Andhakāre {pb:V:1.0206} pure hoti, gambhīre gādhamedhati;
::

::gathalast
Daṇḍassa ānubhāvena, khalitvā patitiṭṭhatī’’ti.
::

Atha kho so brāhmaṇamahāsālo bhagavato santike imā gāthāyo pariyāpuṇitvā sabhāyaṃ mahājanakāye sannipatite puttesu ca sannisinnesu abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Yehi jātehi nandissaṃ, yesañca bhavamicchisaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Te {pb:T:1.0260} maṃ dārehi saṃpuccha, sāva vārenti sūkaraṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Asantā kira maṃ jammā, tāta tātāti bhāsare;
::

::gathalast
Rakkhasā puttarūpena, te jahanti vayogataṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Assova {pb:M:1.0179} jiṇṇo nibbhogo, khādanā apanīyati;
::

::gathalast
Bālakānaṃ pitā thero, parāgāresu bhikkhati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Daṇḍova kira me seyyo, yañce puttā anassavā;
::

::gathalast
Caṇḍampi goṇaṃ vāreti, atho caṇḍampi kukkuraṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Andhakāre pure hoti, gambhīre gādhamedhati;
::

::gathalast
Daṇḍassa ānubhāvena, khalitvā patitiṭṭhatī’’ti.
::

Atha {pb:P:1.0177} kho naṃ brāhmaṇamahāsālaṃ puttā gharaṃ netvā nhāpetvā paccekaṃ dussayugena acchādesuṃ. Atha kho so brāhmaṇamahāsālo ekaṃ dussayugaṃ ādāya yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavatā saddhiṃ sammodi. Sammodanīyaṃ kathaṃ sāraṇīyaṃ vītisāretvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi. Ekamantaṃ nisinno kho brāhmaṇamahāsālo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘mayaṃ, bho gotama, brāhmaṇā nāma ācariyassa ācariyadhanaṃ pariyesāma. Paṭiggaṇhatu me bhavaṃ gotamo ācariyadhana’’nti. Paṭiggahesi bhagavā anukampaṃ upādāya. Atha kho so brāhmaṇamahāsālo bhagavantaṃ {pb:V:1.0207} etadavoca – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama…pe… upāsakaṃ maṃ bhavaṃ gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupetaṃ saraṇaṃ gata’’nti.

#### 5. Mānatthaddhasuttaṃ

{para:201} 201\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:T:1.0261}. Tena kho pana samayena mānatthaddho nāma brāhmaṇo sāvatthiyaṃ paṭivasati. So neva mātaraṃ abhivādeti, na pitaraṃ abhivādeti, na ācariyaṃ abhivādeti, na jeṭṭhabhātaraṃ abhivādeti. Tena kho pana samayena bhagavā mahatiyā parisāya parivuto dhammaṃ deseti. Atha kho mānatthaddhassa brāhmaṇassa etadahosi – ‘‘ayaṃ kho samaṇo gotamo mahatiyā parisāya parivuto dhammaṃ deseti. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ yena samaṇo gotamo tenupasaṅkameyyaṃ. Sace maṃ samaṇo gotamo ālapissati, ahampi taṃ ālapissāmi. No ce maṃ samaṇo gotamo ālapissati, ahampi nālapissāmī’’ti. Atha kho mānatthaddho brāhmaṇo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā tuṇhībhūto ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Atha kho bhagavā taṃ nālapi. Atha kho mānatthaddho brāhmaṇo – ‘nāyaṃ samaṇo {pb:M:1.0180} gotamo kiñci jānātī’ti tatova puna nivattitukāmo ahosi. Atha {pb:P:1.0178} kho bhagavā mānatthaddhassa brāhmaṇassa cetasā cetoparivitakkamaññāya mānatthaddhaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Na mānaṃ brāhmaṇa sādhu, atthikassīdha brāhmaṇa;
::

::gathalast
Yena atthena āgacchi, tamevamanubrūhaye’’ti.
::

Atha kho mānatthaddho brāhmaṇo – ‘‘cittaṃ me samaṇo gotamo jānātī’’ti tattheva bhagavato pādesu sirasā nipatitvā bhagavato pādāni {pb:T:1.0262} mukhena ca paricumbati pāṇīhi ca parisambāhati, nāmañca sāveti – ‘‘mānatthaddhāhaṃ, bho gotama, mānatthaddhāhaṃ, bho gotamā’’ti. Atha kho sā parisā abbhutacittajātā {note:abbhutacittajātā (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.), acchariyabbhutacittajātā (ka.)} ahosi – ‘acchariyaṃ vata bho, abbhutaṃ vata bho! Ayañhi mānatthaddho brāhmaṇo neva mātaraṃ abhivādeti, na pitaraṃ abhivādeti, na ācariyaṃ abhivādeti, na jeṭṭhabhātaraṃ abhivādeti; atha ca pana samaṇe gotame evarūpaṃ paramanipaccakāraṃ karotī’ti. Atha kho bhagavā mānatthaddhaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘alaṃ, brāhmaṇa{pb:V:1.0208}, uṭṭhehi, sake āsane nisīda. Yato te mayi cittaṃ pasanna’’nti. Atha kho mānatthaddho brāhmaṇo sake āsane nisīditvā bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kesu na mānaṃ kayirātha, kesu cassa sagāravo;
::

::gathalast
Kyassa apacitā assu, kyassu sādhu supūjitā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mātari pitari cāpi, atho jeṭṭhamhi bhātari;
::

::gatha2
Ācariye catutthamhi,
::

::gatha3
Tesu na mānaṃ kayirātha;
::

::gatha2
Tesu assa sagāravo,
::

::gatha3
Tyassa apacitā assu;
::

::gathalast
Tyassu sādhu supūjitā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Arahante sītībhūte, katakicce anāsave;
::

::gathalast
Nihacca mānaṃ athaddho, te namasse anuttare’’ti.
::

Evaṃ {pb:M:1.0181} vutte, mānatthaddho brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama…pe… upāsakaṃ maṃ bhavaṃ gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupetaṃ saraṇaṃ gata’’nti.

#### 6. Paccanīkasuttaṃ

{para:202} 202\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ{pb:T:1.0263}{pb:P:1.0179}. Tena kho pana samayena paccanīkasāto nāma brāhmaṇo sāvatthiyaṃ paṭivasati. Atha kho paccanīkasātassa brāhmaṇassa etadahosi – ‘‘yaṃnūnāhaṃ yena samaṇo gotamo tenupasaṅkameyyaṃ. Yaṃ yadeva samaṇo gotamo bhāsissati taṃ tadevassāhaṃ {note:tadeva sāhaṃ (ka.)} paccanīkāssa’’nti {note:paccanīkassanti (pī.), paccanīkasātanti (ka.)}. Tena kho pana samayena bhagavā abbhokāse caṅkamati. Atha kho paccanīkasāto brāhmaṇo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ caṅkamantaṃ etadavoca – ‘bhaṇa samaṇadhamma’nti.

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:V:1.0209} paccanīkasātena, suvijānaṃ subhāsitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Upakkiliṭṭhacittena, sārambhabahulena ca.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo ca vineyya sārambhaṃ, appasādañca cetaso;
::

::gathalast
Āghātaṃ paṭinissajja, sa ve {note:sace (syā. kaṃ. ka.)} jaññā subhāsita’’nti.
::

Evaṃ vutte, paccanīkasāto brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama, abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama…pe… upāsakaṃ maṃ bhavaṃ gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupetaṃ saraṇaṃ gata’’nti.

#### 7. Navakammikasuttaṃ

{para:203} 203\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe{pb:T:1.0264}. Tena kho pana samayena navakammikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo tasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe kammantaṃ kārāpeti. Addasā kho navakammikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ aññatarasmiṃ sālarukkhamūle nisinnaṃ pallaṅkaṃ ābhujitvā ujuṃ kāyaṃ paṇidhāya parimukhaṃ satiṃ upaṭṭhapetvā. Disvānassa etadahosi – ‘‘ahaṃ kho imasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe kammantaṃ kārāpento ramāmi. Ayaṃ samaṇo gotamo kiṃ kārāpento ramatī’’ti? Atha {pb:M:1.0182} kho navakammikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo yena bhagavā {pb:P:1.0180} tenupasaṅkami. Upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Ke nu kammantā karīyanti, bhikkhu sālavane tava;
::

::gathalast
Yadekako araññasmiṃ, ratiṃ vindati gotamo’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na me vanasmiṃ karaṇīyamatthi,
::

::gatha2
Ucchinnamūlaṃ me vanaṃ visūkaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Svāhaṃ vane nibbanatho visallo,
::

::gathalast
Eko rame aratiṃ vippahāyā’’ti.
::

Evaṃ {pb:V:1.0210} vutte, navakammikabhāradvājo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama…pe… upāsakaṃ maṃ bhavaṃ gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupetaṃ saraṇaṃ gata’’nti.

#### 8. Kaṭṭhahārasuttaṃ

{para:204} 204\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe. Tena kho pana samayena aññatarassa bhāradvājagottassa brāhmaṇassa {pb:T:1.0265} sambahulā antevāsikā kaṭṭhahārakā māṇavakā yena vanasaṇḍo tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā addasaṃsu bhagavantaṃ tasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe nisinnaṃ pallaṅkaṃ ābhujitvā ujuṃ kāyaṃ paṇidhāya parimukhaṃ satiṃ upaṭṭhapetvā. Disvāna yena bhāradvājagotto brāhmaṇo tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā bhāradvājagottaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ etadavocuṃ – ‘‘yagghe, bhavaṃ jāneyyāsi! Asukasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe samaṇo nisinno pallaṅkaṃ ābhujitvā ujuṃ kāyaṃ paṇidhāya parimukhaṃ satiṃ upaṭṭhapetvā’’. Atha kho bhāradvājagotto brāhmaṇo tehi māṇavakehi saddhiṃ yena so vanasaṇḍo tenupasaṅkami. Addasā kho bhagavantaṃ tasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe nisinnaṃ pallaṅkaṃ ābhujitvā ujuṃ kāyaṃ paṇidhāya parimukhaṃ satiṃ upaṭṭhapetvā. Disvāna yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Gambhīrarūpe bahubherave vane,
::

::gatha2
Suññaṃ araññaṃ vijanaṃ vigāhiya;
::

::gatha3
Aniñjamānena {pb:P:1.0181} ṭhitena vaggunā,
::

::gathalast
Sucārurūpaṃ vata bhikkhu jhāyasi.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:M:1.0183} yattha gītaṃ napi yattha vāditaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Eko araññe vanavassito muni;
::

::gatha3
Accherarūpaṃ paṭibhāti maṃ idaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Yadekako pītimano vane vase.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Maññāmahaṃ {pb:T:1.0266} lokādhipatisahabyataṃ,
::

::gatha2
Ākaṅkhamāno tidivaṃ anuttaraṃ;
::

::gatha3
Kasmā {pb:V:1.0211} bhavaṃ vijanamaraññamassito,
::

::gathalast
Tapo idha kubbasi brahmapattiyā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yā kāci kaṅkhā abhinandanā vā,
::

::gatha2
Anekadhātūsu puthū sadāsitā;
::

::gatha3
Aññāṇamūlappabhavā pajappitā,
::

::gathalast
Sabbā mayā byantikatā samūlikā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāhaṃ akaṅkho asito anūpayo,
::

::gatha2
Sabbesu dhammesu visuddhadassano;
::

::gatha3
Pappuyya sambodhimanuttaraṃ sivaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Jhāyāmahaṃ brahma raho visārado’’ti.
::

Evaṃ vutte, bhāradvājagotto brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama…pe… ajjatagge pāṇupetaṃ saraṇaṃ gata’’nti.

#### 9. Mātuposakasuttaṃ

{para:205} 205\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Atha kho mātuposako brāhmaṇo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavatā saddhiṃ sammodi. Sammodanīyaṃ kathaṃ sāraṇīyaṃ vītisāretvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi. Ekamantaṃ nisinno kho mātuposako brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘ahañhi, bho {pb:T:1.0267} gotama, dhammena bhikkhaṃ pariyesāmi, dhammena bhikkhaṃ pariyesitvā mātāpitaro posemi. Kaccāhaṃ, bho gotama, evaṃkārī kiccakārī homī’’ti? ‘‘Taggha tvaṃ, brāhmaṇa, evaṃkārī kiccakārī hosi. Yo kho, brāhmaṇa, dhammena bhikkhaṃ pariyesati, dhammena bhikkhaṃ {pb:P:1.0182} pariyesitvā mātāpitaro poseti, bahuṃ so puññaṃ pasavatī’’ti.

::gatha1
‘‘Yo {pb:V:1.0212}{pb:M:1.0184} mātaraṃ pitaraṃ vā, macco dhammena posati;
::

::gatha2
Tāya naṃ pāricariyāya, mātāpitūsu paṇḍitā;
::

::gathalast
Idheva naṃ pasaṃsanti, pecca sagge pamodatī’’ti.
::

Evaṃ vutte, mātuposako brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ bho gotama, abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama…pe… upāsakaṃ maṃ bhavaṃ gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupetaṃ saraṇaṃ gata’’nti.

#### 10. Bhikkhakasuttaṃ

{para:206} 206\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Atha kho bhikkhako brāhmaṇo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavatā saddhiṃ sammodi. Sammodanīyaṃ kathaṃ sāraṇīyaṃ vītisāretvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi. Ekamantaṃ nisinno kho bhikkhako brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘ahampi kho, bho gotama, bhikkhako, bhavampi bhikkhako, idha no kiṃ nānākaraṇa’’nti?

::gatha1
‘‘Na tena bhikkhako hoti, yāvatā bhikkhate pare;
::

::gathalast
Vissaṃ dhammaṃ samādāya, bhikkhu hoti na tāvatā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yodha {pb:T:1.0268} puññañca pāpañca, bāhitvā brahmacariyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saṅkhāya loke carati, sa ve bhikkhūti vuccatī’’ti.
::

Evaṃ vutte, bhikkhako brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama, abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama…pe… upāsakaṃ maṃ bhavaṃ gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupetaṃ saraṇaṃ gata’’nti.

#### 11. Saṅgāravasuttaṃ

{para:207} 207\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Tena kho pana samayena saṅgāravo nāma brāhmaṇo sāvatthiyaṃ paṭivasati udakasuddhiko, udakena parisuddhiṃ pacceti, sāyaṃ pātaṃ udakorohanānuyogamanuyutto viharati. Atha kho āyasmā ānando pubbaṇhasamayaṃ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya sāvatthiṃ piṇḍāya {pb:V:1.0213} pāvisi. Sāvatthiyaṃ piṇḍāya caritvā pacchābhattaṃ piṇḍapātapaṭikkanto yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi. Ekamantaṃ {pb:P:1.0183} nisinno kho āyasmā ānando bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘idha, bhante, saṅgāravo nāma brāhmaṇo sāvatthiyaṃ paṭivasati udakasuddhiko{pb:M:1.0185}, udakena suddhiṃ pacceti, sāyaṃ pātaṃ udakorohanānuyogamanuyutto viharati. Sādhu, bhante, bhagavā yena saṅgāravassa brāhmaṇassa nivesanaṃ tenupasaṅkamatu anukampaṃ upādāyā’’ti. Adhivāsesi bhagavā tuṇhībhāvena.

Atha kho bhagavā pubbaṇhasamayaṃ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya yena saṅgāravassa brāhmaṇassa nivesanaṃ tenupasaṅkami{pb:T:1.0269}; upasaṅkamitvā paññatte āsane nisīdi. Atha kho saṅgāravo brāhmaṇo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavatā saddhiṃ sammodi. Sammodanīyaṃ kathaṃ sāraṇīyaṃ vītisāretvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi. Ekamantaṃ nisinnaṃ kho saṅgāravaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ bhagavā etadavoca – ‘‘saccaṃ kira tvaṃ, brāhmaṇa, udakasuddhiko, udakena suddhiṃ paccesi, sāyaṃ pātaṃ udakorohanānuyogamanuyutto viharasī’’ti? ‘‘Evaṃ, bho gotama’’. ‘‘Kiṃ pana tvaṃ, brāhmaṇa, atthavasaṃ sampassamāno udakasuddhiko, udakasuddhiṃ paccesi, sāyaṃ pātaṃ udakorohanānuyogamanuyutto viharasī’’ti? ‘‘Idha me, bho gotama {note:idha me bho gotama ahaṃ (pī. ka.)}, yaṃ divā pāpakammaṃ kataṃ hoti, taṃ sāyaṃ nhānena {note:nahānena (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} pavāhemi, yaṃ rattiṃ pāpakammaṃ kataṃ hoti taṃ pātaṃ nhānena pavāhemi. Imaṃ khvāhaṃ, bho gotama, atthavasaṃ sampassamāno udakasuddhiko, udakena suddhiṃ paccemi, sāyaṃ pātaṃ udakorohanānuyogamanuyutto viharāmī’’ti.

::gatha1
‘‘Dhammo rahado brāhmaṇa sīlatittho,
::

::gatha2
Anāvilo sabbhi sataṃ pasattho;
::

::gatha3
Yattha have vedaguno sinātā,
::

::gathalast
Anallagattāva {note:anallīnagattāva (ka.)} taranti pāra’’nti.
::

Evaṃ vutte, saṅgāravo brāhmaṇo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama, abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama…pe… upāsakaṃ maṃ bhavaṃ gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupetaṃ saraṇaṃ gata’’nti.

#### 12. Khomadussasuttaṃ

{para:208} 208\. Evaṃ {pb:T:1.0270}{pb:V:1.0214}{pb:P:1.0184} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sakkesu viharati khomadussaṃ nāmaṃ sakyānaṃ nigamo. Atha kho bhagavā pubbaṇhasamayaṃ nivāsetvā {pb:M:1.0186} pattacīvaramādāya khomadussaṃ nigamaṃ piṇḍāya pāvisi. Tena kho pana samayena khomadussakā brāhmaṇagahapatikā sabhāyaṃ sannipatitā honti kenacideva karaṇīyena, devo ca ekamekaṃ phusāyati. Atha kho bhagavā yena sā sabhā tenupasaṅkami. Addasaṃsu khomadussakā brāhmaṇagahapatikā bhagavantaṃ dūratova āgacchantaṃ. Disvāna etadavocuṃ – ‘‘ke ca muṇḍakā samaṇakā, ke ca sabhādhammaṃ jānissantī’’ti? Atha kho bhagavā khomadussake brāhmaṇagahapatike gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Nesā sabhā yattha na santi santo,
::

::gatha2
Santo na te ye na vadanti dhammaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Rāgañca dosañca pahāya mohaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Dhammaṃ vadantā ca bhavanti santo’’ti.
::

Evaṃ vutte, khomadussakā brāhmaṇagahapatikā bhagavantaṃ etadavocuṃ – ‘‘abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama, abhikkantaṃ, bho gotama; seyyathāpi, bho gotama, nikkujjitaṃ vā ukkujjeyya, paṭicchannaṃ vā vivareyya, mūḷhassa vā maggaṃ ācikkheyya, andhakāre vā telapajjotaṃ dhāreyya – cakkhumanto rūpāni dakkhantīti, evamevaṃ bhotā gotamena anekapariyāyena {pb:T:1.0271} dhammo pakāsito. Ete mayaṃ bhavantaṃ gotamaṃ saraṇaṃ gacchāma dhammañca bhikkhusaṅghañca. Upāsake no bhavaṃ gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupete saraṇaṃ gate’’ti.

::centre
Upāsakavaggo dutiyo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Kasi udayo devahito, aññataramahāsālaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Mānathaddhaṃ paccanīkaṃ, navakammikakaṭṭhahāraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mātuposakaṃ bhikkhako, saṅgāravo ca khomadussena dvādasāti.
::

::centre
Brāhmaṇasaṃyuttaṃ samattaṃ.
::

### 8. Vaṅgīsasaṃyuttaṃ

#### 1. Nikkhantasuttaṃ

{para:209} 209\. Evaṃ {pb:T:1.0272}{pb:V:1.0215}{pb:M:1.0187}{pb:P:1.0185} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ āyasmā vaṅgīso āḷaviyaṃ viharati aggāḷave cetiye āyasmatā nigrodhakappena upajjhāyena saddhiṃ. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā vaṅgīso navako hoti acirapabbajito ohiyyako vihārapālo. Atha kho sambahulā itthiyo samalaṅkaritvā yena aggāḷavako ārāmo tenupasaṅkamiṃsu vihārapekkhikāyo. Atha kho āyasmato vaṅgīsassa tā itthiyo disvā anabhirati uppajjati, rāgo cittaṃ anuddhaṃseti. Atha kho āyasmato vaṅgīsassa etadahosi – ‘‘alābhā vata me, na vata me lābhā; dulladdhaṃ vata me, na vata me suladdhaṃ; yassa me anabhirati uppannā, rāgo cittaṃ anuddhaṃseti, taṃ kutettha labbhā, yaṃ me paro anabhiratiṃ vinodetvā abhiratiṃ uppādeyya. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ attanāva attano anabhiratiṃ vinodetvā abhiratiṃ uppādeyya’’nti. Atha kho āyasmā vaṅgīso attanāva attano anabhiratiṃ vinodetvā abhiratiṃ uppādetvā tāyaṃ velāyaṃ imā gāthāyo abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Nikkhantaṃ vata maṃ santaṃ, agārasmānagāriyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vitakkā upadhāvanti, pagabbhā kaṇhato ime.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uggaputtā {pb:T:1.0273} mahissāsā, sikkhitā daḷhadhammino;
::

::gathalast
Samantā parikireyyuṃ, sahassaṃ apalāyinaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sacepi etato {note:ettato (sī. pī. ka.), ettakā (syā. kaṃ.)} bhiyyo, āgamissanti itthiyo;
::

::gathalast
Neva maṃ byādhayissanti {note:byāthayissanti (?)}, dhamme samhi patiṭṭhitaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sakkhī {pb:V:1.0216}{pb:P:1.0186} hi me sutaṃ etaṃ, buddhassādiccabandhuno;
::

::gathalast
Nibbānagamanaṃ maggaṃ, tattha me nirato mano.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evañce maṃ viharantaṃ, pāpima upagacchasi;
::

::gathalast
Tathā maccu karissāmi, na me maggampi dakkhasī’’ti.
::

#### 2. Aratisuttaṃ

{para:210} 210\. Ekaṃ {pb:M:1.0188} samayaṃ…pe… āyasmā vaṅgīso āḷaviyaṃ viharati aggāḷave cetiye āyasmatā nigrodhakappena upajjhāyena saddhiṃ. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā nigrodhakappo pacchābhattaṃ piṇḍapātapaṭikkanto vihāraṃ pavisati, sāyaṃ vā nikkhamati aparajju vā kāle. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmato vaṅgīsassa anabhirati uppannā hoti, rāgo cittaṃ anuddhaṃseti. Atha kho āyasmato vaṅgīsassa etadahosi – ‘‘alābhā vata me, na vata me lābhā; dulladdhaṃ vata me, na vata me suladdhaṃ; yassa me anabhirati uppannā, rāgo cittaṃ anuddhaṃseti; taṃ kutettha labbhā, yaṃ me paro anabhiratiṃ vinodetvā abhiratiṃ uppādeyya. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ attanāva attano anabhiratiṃ vinodetvā abhiratiṃ uppādeyya’’nti. Atha {pb:T:1.0274} kho āyasmā vaṅgīso attanāva attano anabhiratiṃ vinodetvā abhiratiṃ uppādetvā tāyaṃ velāyaṃ imā gāthāyo abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Aratiñca ratiñca pahāya, sabbaso gehasitañca vitakkaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vanathaṃ na kareyya kuhiñci, nibbanatho arato sa hi bhikkhu {note:sa bhikkhu (ka.)}.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yamidha pathaviñca vehāsaṃ, rūpagatañca jagatogadhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kiñci parijīyati sabbamaniccaṃ, evaṃ samecca caranti mutattā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Upadhīsu janā gadhitāse {note:gathitāse (sī.)}, diṭṭhasute paṭighe ca mute ca;
::

::gathalast
Ettha vinodaya chandamanejo, yo ettha na limpati taṃ munimāhu.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atha {pb:V:1.0217}{pb:P:1.0187} saṭṭhinissitā savitakkā, puthū janatāya adhammā niviṭṭhā;
::

::gathalast
Na ca vaggagatassa kuhiñci, no pana duṭṭhullabhāṇī sa bhikkhu.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dabbo cirarattasamāhito, akuhako nipako apihālu;
::

::gathalast
Santaṃ {pb:T:1.0275} padaṃ ajjhagamā muni paṭicca, parinibbuto kaṅkhati kāla’’nti.
::

#### 3. Pesalasuttaṃ

{para:211} 211\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ āyasmā vaṅgīso āḷaviyaṃ viharati aggāḷave cetiye āyasmatā nigrodhakappena upajjhāyena saddhiṃ. Tena kho pana samayena {pb:M:1.0189} āyasmā vaṅgīso attano paṭibhānena aññe pesale bhikkhū atimaññati. Atha kho āyasmato vaṅgīsassa etadahosi – ‘‘alābhā vata me, na vata me lābhā; dulladdhaṃ vata me, na vata me suladdhaṃ; yvāhaṃ attano paṭibhānena aññe pesale bhikkhū atimaññāmī’’ti. Atha kho āyasmā vaṅgīso attanāva attano vippaṭisāraṃ uppādetvā tāyaṃ velāyaṃ imā gāthāyo abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Mānaṃ pajahassu gotama, mānapathañca pajahassu;
::

::gathalast
Asesaṃ mānapathasmiṃ, samucchito vippaṭisārīhuvā cirarattaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Makkhena makkhitā pajā, mānahatā nirayaṃ papatanti;
::

::gathalast
Socanti janā cirarattaṃ, mānahatā nirayaṃ upapannā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:T:1.0276} hi socati bhikkhu kadāci, maggajino sammāpaṭipanno;
::

::gathalast
Kittiñca sukhañca anubhoti, dhammadasoti tamāhu pahitattaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasmā {pb:P:1.0188} akhilodha padhānavā, nīvaraṇāni pahāya visuddho;
::

::gathalast
Mānañca pahāya asesaṃ, vijjāyantakaro samitāvī’’ti.
::

#### 4. Ānandasuttaṃ

{para:212} 212\. Ekaṃ {pb:V:1.0218} samayaṃ āyasmā ānando sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Atha kho āyasmā ānando pubbaṇhasamayaṃ nivāsetvā pattacīvaramādāya sāvatthiṃ piṇḍāya pāvisi āyasmatā vaṅgīsena pacchāsamaṇena. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmato vaṅgīsassa anabhirati uppannā hoti, rāgo cittaṃ anuddhaṃseti. Atha kho āyasmā vaṅgīso āyasmantaṃ ānandaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kāmarāgena ḍayhāmi, cittaṃ me pariḍayhati;
::

::gathalast
Sādhu nibbāpanaṃ brūhi, anukampāya gotamā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saññāya {pb:T:1.0277} vipariyesā, cittaṃ te pariḍayhati;
::

::gathalast
Nimittaṃ parivajjehi, subhaṃ rāgūpasaṃhitaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṅkhāre parato passa, dukkhato mā ca attato;
::

::gathalast
Nibbāpehi mahārāgaṃ, mā ḍayhittho punappunaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Asubhāya {pb:M:1.0190} cittaṃ bhāvehi, ekaggaṃ susamāhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sati kāyagatā tyatthu, nibbidābahulo bhava.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Animittañca bhāvehi, mānānusayamujjaha;
::

::gathalast
Tato mānābhisamayā, upasanto carissasī’’ti.
::

#### 5. Subhāsitasuttaṃ

{para:213} 213\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. Tatra kho bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi – ‘‘bhikkhavo’’ti. ‘‘Bhadante’’ti te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṃ. Bhagavā etadavoca –

‘‘Catūhi, bhikkhave, aṅgehi samannāgatā vācā subhāsitā hoti, no dubbhāsitā; anavajjā ca ananuvajjā ca viññūnaṃ. Katamehi catūhi? Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu {pb:V:1.0219} subhāsitaṃyeva bhāsati no dubbhāsitaṃ, dhammaṃyeva bhāsati no adhammaṃ, piyaṃyeva {pb:P:1.0189} bhāsati no appiyaṃ, saccaṃyeva bhāsati no alikaṃ. Imehi kho, bhikkhave, catūhi aṅgehi samannāgatā vācā subhāsitā hoti, no dubbhāsitā, anavajjā ca ananuvajjā ca viññūna’’nti. Idamavoca bhagavā, idaṃ vatvāna sugato athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

::gatha1
‘‘Subhāsitaṃ {pb:T:1.0278} uttamamāhu santo,
::

::gatha2
Dhammaṃ bhaṇe nādhammaṃ taṃ dutiyaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Piyaṃ bhaṇe nāppiyaṃ taṃ tatiyaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Saccaṃ bhaṇe nālikaṃ taṃ catuttha’’nti.
::

Atha kho āyasmā vaṅgīso uṭṭhāyāsanā ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā yena bhagavā tenañjaliṃ paṇāmetvā bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘paṭibhāti maṃ bhagavā, paṭibhāti maṃ sugatā’’ti. ‘‘Paṭibhātu taṃ vaṅgīsā’’ti bhagavā avoca. Atha kho āyasmā vaṅgīso bhagavantaṃ sammukhā sāruppāhi gāthāhi abhitthavi –

::gatha1
‘‘Tameva vācaṃ bhāseyya, yāyattānaṃ na tāpaye;
::

::gathalast
Pare ca na vihiṃseyya, sā ve vācā subhāsitā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Piyavācaṃva bhāseyya, yā vācā paṭinanditā;
::

::gathalast
Yaṃ anādāya pāpāni, paresaṃ bhāsate piyaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saccaṃ {pb:M:1.0191} ve amatā vācā, esa dhammo sanantano;
::

::gathalast
Sacce atthe ca dhamme ca, āhu santo patiṭṭhitā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ buddho bhāsate vācaṃ, khemaṃ nibbānapattiyā;
::

::gathalast
Dukkhassantakiriyāya, sā ve vācānamuttamā’’ti.
::

#### 6. Sāriputtasuttaṃ

{para:214} 214\. Ekaṃ {pb:T:1.0279}{pb:V:1.0220} samayaṃ āyasmā sāriputto sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā sāriputto bhikkhū dhammiyā kathāya sandasseti samādapeti samuttejeti sampahaṃseti poriyā vācāya vissaṭṭhāya anelagalāya {note:aneḷagalāya (sī. ka.), anelagaḷāya (syā. kaṃ. pī.)} atthassa viññāpaniyā. Te ca bhikkhū aṭṭhiṃ katvā manasi katvā sabbacetasā samannāharitvā ohitasotā dhammaṃ suṇanti. Atha kho āyasmato vaṅgīsassa etadahosi – ‘‘ayaṃ kho āyasmā {pb:P:1.0190} sāriputto bhikkhū dhammiyā kathāya sandasseti samādapeti samuttejeti sampahaṃseti poriyā vācāya vissaṭṭhāya anelagalāya atthassa viññāpaniyā. Te ca bhikkhū aṭṭhiṃ katvā manasi katvā sabbacetasā samannāharitvā ohitasotā dhammaṃ suṇanti. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ āyasmantaṃ sāriputtaṃ sammukhā sāruppāhi gāthāhi abhitthaveyya’’nti.

Atha kho āyasmā vaṅgīso uṭṭhāyāsanā ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā yenāyasmā sāriputto tenañjaliṃ paṇāmetvā āyasmantaṃ sāriputtaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘paṭibhāti maṃ, āvuso sāriputta, paṭibhāti maṃ, āvuso sāriputtā’’ti. ‘‘Paṭibhātu taṃ, āvuso vaṅgīsā’’ti. Atha kho āyasmā vaṅgīso āyasmantaṃ sāriputtaṃ sammukhā sāruppāhi gāthāhi abhitthavi –

::gatha1
‘‘Gambhīrapañño medhāvī, maggāmaggassa kovido;
::

::gathalast
Sāriputto mahāpañño, dhammaṃ deseti bhikkhunaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṃkhittenapi deseti, vitthārenapi bhāsati;
::

::gathalast
Sāḷikāyiva nigghoso, paṭibhānaṃ udīrayi {note:udīriyi (syā. kaṃ.) udīriyati (sāmaññaphalasuttaṭīkānurūpaṃ)}.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tassa {pb:M:1.0192} taṃ desayantassa, suṇanti madhuraṃ giraṃ;
::

::gatha2
Sarena {pb:T:1.0280} rajanīyena, savanīyena vaggunā;
::

::gathalast
Udaggacittā muditā, sotaṃ odhenti bhikkhavo’’ti.
::

#### 7. Pavāraṇāsuttaṃ

{para:215} 215\. Ekaṃ {pb:V:1.0221} samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati pubbārāme migāramātupāsāde mahatā bhikkhusaṅghena saddhiṃ pañcamattehi bhikkhusatehi sabbeheva arahantehi. Tena kho pana samayena bhagavā tadahuposathe pannarase pavāraṇāya bhikkhusaṅghaparivuto abbhokāse nisinno hoti. Atha kho bhagavā tuṇhībhūtaṃ bhikkhusaṅghaṃ anuviloketvā bhikkhū āmantesi – ‘‘handa dāni, bhikkhave, pavāremi vo. Na ca me kiñci garahatha kāyikaṃ vā vācasikaṃ vā’’ti.

Evaṃ vutte, āyasmā sāriputto uṭṭhāyāsanā ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā yena bhagavā tenañjaliṃ paṇāmetvā bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘na kho mayaṃ, bhante, bhagavato kiñci garahāma kāyikaṃ vā vācasikaṃ vā. Bhagavā hi{pb:P:1.0191}, bhante, anuppannassa maggassa uppādetā, asañjātassa maggassa sañjanetā, anakkhātassa maggassa akkhātā, maggaññū maggavidū maggakovido. Maggānugā ca, bhante, etarahi sāvakā viharanti pacchā samannāgatā; ahañca kho, bhante, bhagavantaṃ pavāremi. Na ca me bhagavā kiñci garahati kāyikaṃ vā vācasikaṃ vā’’ti.

‘‘Na khvāhaṃ te, sāriputta, kiñci garahāmi kāyikaṃ vā vācasikaṃ vā. Paṇḍito tvaṃ, sāriputta, mahāpañño tvaṃ, sāriputta{pb:T:1.0281}, puthupañño tvaṃ, sāriputta, hāsapañño tvaṃ, sāriputta, javanapañño tvaṃ, sāriputta, tikkhapañño tvaṃ, sāriputta, nibbedhikapañño tvaṃ, sāriputta. Seyyathāpi, sāriputta, rañño cakkavattissa jeṭṭhaputto pitarā pavattitaṃ cakkaṃ sammadeva anuppavatteti; evameva kho tvaṃ, sāriputta, mayā anuttaraṃ dhammacakkaṃ pavattitaṃ sammadeva anuppavattesī’’ti.

‘‘No ce kira me, bhante, bhagavā kiñci garahati kāyikaṃ vā vācasikaṃ vā. Imesaṃ pana, bhante, bhagavā pañcannaṃ bhikkhusatānaṃ na kiñci garahati kāyikaṃ vā vācasikaṃ vā’’ti. ‘‘Imesampi khvāhaṃ, sāriputta, pañcannaṃ bhikkhusatānaṃ na {pb:M:1.0193} kiñci garahāmi kāyikaṃ vā vācasikaṃ vā. Imesañhi, sāriputta, pañcannaṃ bhikkhusatānaṃ saṭṭhi bhikkhū tevijjā, saṭṭhi bhikkhū chaḷabhiññā, saṭṭhi bhikkhū ubhatobhāgavimuttā, atha itare paññāvimuttā’’ti.

Atha {pb:V:1.0222} kho āyasmā vaṅgīso uṭṭhāyāsanā ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā yena bhagavā tenañjaliṃ paṇāmetvā bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘paṭibhāti maṃ bhagavā, paṭibhāti maṃ sugatā’’ti. ‘‘Paṭibhātu taṃ, vaṅgīsā’’ti bhagavā avoca. Atha kho āyasmā vaṅgīso bhagavantaṃ sammukhā sāruppāhi gāthāhi abhitthavi –

::gatha1
‘‘Ajja pannarase visuddhiyā, bhikkhū pañcasatā samāgatā;
::

::gathalast
Saṃyojanabandhanacchidā{pb:T:1.0282}, anīghā khīṇapunabbhavā isī.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cakkavattī {pb:P:1.0192} yathā rājā, amaccaparivārito;
::

::gathalast
Samantā anupariyeti, sāgarantaṃ mahiṃ imaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ vijitasaṅgāmaṃ, satthavāhaṃ anuttaraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sāvakā payirupāsanti, tevijjā maccuhāyino.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbe bhagavato puttā, palāpettha na vijjati;
::

::gathalast
Taṇhāsallassa hantāraṃ, vande ādiccabandhuna’’nti.
::

#### 8. Parosahassasuttaṃ

{para:216} 216\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme mahatā bhikkhusaṅghena saddhiṃ aḍḍhatelasehi bhikkhusatehi. Tena kho pana samayena bhagavā bhikkhū nibbānapaṭisaṃyuttāya dhammiyā kathāya sandasseti samādapeti samuttejeti sampahaṃseti. Te ca bhikkhū aṭṭhiṃ katvā manasi katvā sabbacetasā samannāharitvā ohitasotā dhammaṃ suṇanti. Atha kho āyasmato vaṅgīsassa etadahosi – ‘‘ayaṃ kho bhagavā bhikkhū nibbānapaṭisaṃyuttāya dhammiyā kathāya sandasseti samādapeti samuttejeti sampahaṃseti. Te ca bhikkhū aṭṭhiṃ katvā manasi katvā sabbacetasā samannāharitvā ohitasotā dhammaṃ suṇanti. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ bhagavantaṃ sammukhā sāruppāhi gāthāhi abhitthaveyya’’nti.

Atha {pb:T:1.0283}{pb:V:1.0223}{pb:M:1.0194} kho āyasmā vaṅgīso uṭṭhāyāsanā ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā yena bhagavā tenañjaliṃ paṇāmetvā bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘paṭibhāti maṃ bhagavā, paṭibhāti maṃ sugatā’’ti. ‘‘Paṭibhātu taṃ, vaṅgīsā’’ti bhagavā avoca. Atha kho āyasmā vaṅgīso bhagavantaṃ sammukhā sāruppāhi gāthāhi abhitthavi –

::gatha1
‘‘Parosahassaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ, sugataṃ payirupāsati;
::

::gathalast
Desentaṃ virajaṃ dhammaṃ, nibbānaṃ akutobhayaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suṇanti dhammaṃ vimalaṃ, sammāsambuddhadesitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sobhati vata sambuddho, bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhato.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāganāmosi bhagavā, isīnaṃ isisattamo;
::

::gathalast
Mahāmeghova hutvāna, sāvake abhivassati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Divāvihārā {pb:P:1.0193} nikkhamma, satthudassanakamyatā {note:satthudassanakāmatā (sī. syā. kaṃ.)};
::

::gathalast
Sāvako te mahāvīra, pāde vandati vaṅgīso’’ti.
::

‘‘Kiṃ nu te, vaṅgīsa, imā gāthāyo pubbe parivitakkitā, udāhu ṭhānasova taṃ paṭibhantī’’ti? ‘Na kho me, bhante, imā gāthāyo pubbe parivitakkitā, atha kho ṭhānasova maṃ paṭibhantī’ti. ‘Tena hi taṃ, vaṅgīsa, bhiyyosomattāya pubbe aparivitakkitā gāthāyo paṭibhantū’ti. ‘Evaṃ, bhante’ti kho āyasmā vaṅgīso bhagavato paṭissutvā bhiyyosomattāya {pb:T:1.0284} bhagavantaṃ pubbe aparivitakkitāhi gāthāhi abhitthavi –

::gatha1
‘‘Ummaggapathaṃ {note:ummaggasataṃ (syā. kaṃ. ka.)} mārassa abhibhuyya, carati pabhijja khilāni;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ passatha bandhapamuñcakaraṃ, asitaṃ bhāgaso pavibhajaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Oghassa nittharaṇatthaṃ, anekavihitaṃ maggaṃ akkhāsi;
::

::gathalast
Tasmiñce amate akkhāte, dhammaddasā ṭhitā asaṃhīrā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pajjotakaro {pb:V:1.0224} ativijjha {note:ativijjha dhammaṃ (sī. syā. kaṃ.)}, sabbaṭṭhitīnaṃ atikkamamaddasa;
::

::gathalast
Ñatvā ca sacchikatvā ca, aggaṃ so desayi dasaddhānaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ {pb:M:1.0195} sudesite dhamme,
::

::gatha2
Ko pamādo vijānataṃ dhammaṃ {note:ko pamādo vijānataṃ (sī. syā. kaṃ.)};
::

::gatha3
Tasmā hi tassa bhagavato sāsane;
::

::gathalast
Appamatto sadā namassamanusikkhe’’ti.
::

#### 9. Koṇḍaññasuttaṃ

{para:217} 217\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati veḷuvane kalandakanivāpe. Atha kho āyasmā aññāsikoṇḍañño {note:aññākoṇḍañño (sī. syā. kaṃ.)} sucirasseva yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavato pādesu sirasā nipatitvā {pb:T:1.0285} bhagavato pādāni mukhena ca paricumbati, pāṇīhi {pb:P:1.0194} ca parisambāhati, nāmañca sāveti – ‘‘koṇḍaññohaṃ, bhagavā, koṇḍaññohaṃ, sugatā’’ti. Atha kho āyasmato vaṅgīsassa etadahosi – ‘‘ayaṃ kho āyasmā aññāsikoṇḍañño sucirasseva yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavato pādesu sirasā nipatitvā bhagavato pādāni mukhena ca paricumbati, pāṇīhi ca parisambāhati, nāmañca sāveti – ‘koṇḍaññohaṃ, bhagavā, koṇḍaññohaṃ, sugatā’ti. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ āyasmantaṃ aññāsikoṇḍaññaṃ bhagavato sammukhā sāruppāhi gāthāhi abhitthaveyya’’nti.

Atha kho āyasmā vaṅgīso uṭṭhāyāsanā ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā yena bhagavā tenañjaliṃ paṇāmetvā bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘paṭibhāti maṃ, bhagavā, paṭibhāti maṃ, sugatā’’ti. ‘‘Paṭibhātu taṃ, vaṅgīsā’’ti bhagavā avoca. Atha kho āyasmā vaṅgīso āyasmantaṃ aññāsikoṇḍaññaṃ bhagavato sammukhā sāruppāhi gāthāhi abhitthavi –

::gatha1
‘‘Buddhānubuddho so thero, koṇḍañño tibbanikkamo;
::

::gathalast
Lābhī sukhavihārānaṃ, vivekānaṃ abhiṇhaso.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ {pb:V:1.0225} sāvakena pattabbaṃ, satthusāsanakārinā;
::

::gathalast
Sabbassa taṃ anuppattaṃ, appamattassa sikkhato.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mahānubhāvo {pb:T:1.0286} tevijjo, cetopariyāyakovido;
::

::gathalast
Koṇḍañño buddhadāyādo {note:buddhasāvako (pī.)}, pāde vandati satthuno’’ti.
::

#### 10. Moggallānasuttaṃ

{para:218} 218\. Ekaṃ {pb:M:1.0196} samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati isigilipasse kāḷasilāyaṃ mahatā bhikkhusaṅghena saddhiṃ pañcamattehi bhikkhusatehi sabbeheva arahantehi.
