Tesaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mahāmoggallāno cetasā cittaṃ samannesati {note:samanvesati (syā. aṭṭha.)} vippamuttaṃ nirupadhiṃ. Atha kho āyasmato vaṅgīsassa etadahosi – ‘‘ayaṃ kho bhagavā rājagahe viharati isigilipasse kāḷasilāyaṃ mahatā bhikkhusaṅghena saddhiṃ pañcamattehi bhikkhusatehi sabbeheva arahantehi. Tesaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mahāmoggallāno cetasā cittaṃ samannesati vippamuttaṃ nirupadhiṃ. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ āyasmantaṃ mahāmoggallānaṃ bhagavato sammukhā sāruppāhi gāthāhi abhitthaveyya’’nti.

Atha {pb:P:1.0195} kho āyasmā vaṅgīso uṭṭhāyāsanā ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā yena bhagavā tenañjaliṃ paṇāmetvā bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘paṭibhāti maṃ, bhagavā, paṭibhāti maṃ, sugatā’’ti. ‘‘Paṭibhātu taṃ, vaṅgīsā’’ti bhagavā avoca. Atha kho āyasmā vaṅgīso āyasmantaṃ mahāmoggallānaṃ bhagavato sammukhā sāruppāhi gāthāhi abhitthavi –

::gatha1
‘‘Nagassa passe āsīnaṃ, muniṃ dukkhassa pāraguṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sāvakā payirupāsanti, tevijjā maccuhāyino.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Te {pb:T:1.0287} cetasā anupariyeti {note:anupariyesati (sī. syā. kaṃ.)}, moggallāno mahiddhiko;
::

::gathalast
Cittaṃ nesaṃ samannesaṃ {note:samanvesaṃ (syā. aṭṭha.)}, vippamuttaṃ nirūpadhiṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ {pb:V:1.0226} sabbaṅgasampannaṃ, muniṃ dukkhassa pāraguṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anekākārasampannaṃ, payirupāsanti gotama’’nti.
::

#### 11. Gaggarāsuttaṃ

{para:219} 219\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā campāyaṃ viharati gaggarāya pokkharaṇiyā tīre mahatā bhikkhusaṅghena saddhiṃ pañcamattehi bhikkhusatehi sattahi ca upāsakasatehi sattahi ca upāsikāsatehi anekehi ca devatāsahassehi. Tyāssudaṃ bhagavā atirocati {note:ativirocati (ka.)} vaṇṇena ceva yasasā ca. Atha kho āyasmato vaṅgīsassa etadahosi – ‘‘ayaṃ kho {pb:M:1.0197} bhagavā campāyaṃ viharati gaggarāya pokkharaṇiyā tīre mahatā bhikkhusaṅghena saddhiṃ pañcamattehi bhikkhusatehi sattahi ca upāsakasatehi sattahi ca upāsikāsatehi anekehi ca devatāsahassehi. Tyāssudaṃ bhagavā atirocati vaṇṇena ceva yasasā ca. Yaṃnūnāhaṃ bhagavantaṃ sammukhā sāruppāya gāthāya abhitthaveyya’’nti.

Atha kho āyasmā vaṅgīso uṭṭhāyāsanā ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā yena bhagavā tenañjaliṃ paṇāmetvā bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘paṭibhāti maṃ, bhagavā, paṭibhāti maṃ, sugatā’’ti. ‘‘Paṭibhātu taṃ, vaṅgīsā’’ti bhagavā avoca. Atha kho āyasmā vaṅgīso bhagavantaṃ sammukhā sāruppāya gāthāya abhitthavi –

::gatha1
‘‘Cando {pb:T:1.0288}{pb:P:1.0196} yathā vigatavalāhake nabhe,
::

::gatha2
Virocati vigatamalova bhāṇumā;
::

::gatha3
Evampi aṅgīrasa tvaṃ mahāmuni,
::

::gathalast
Atirocasi yasasā sabbaloka’’nti.
::

#### 12. Vaṅgīsasuttaṃ

{para:220} 220\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ āyasmā vaṅgīso sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme{pb:V:1.0227}. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā vaṅgīso aciraarahattappatto hutvā {note:hoti (sī. syā. kaṃ.)} vimuttisukhaṃ paṭisaṃvedī {note:vimuttisukhapaṭisaṃvedī (sī. pī.)} tāyaṃ velāyaṃ imā gāthāyo abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kāveyyamattā vicarimha pubbe, gāmā gāmaṃ purā puraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Athaddasāma sambuddhaṃ, saddhā no upapajjatha.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So me dhammamadesesi, khandhāyatanadhātuyo {note:khandhe āyatanāni dhātuyo (syā. kaṃ. pī. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Tassāhaṃ dhammaṃ sutvāna, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bahunnaṃ vata atthāya, bodhiṃ ajjhagamā muni;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhūnaṃ bhikkhunīnañca, ye niyāmagataddasā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Svāgataṃ {pb:M:1.0198} vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
::

::gathalast
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi, dibbacakkhuṃ visodhitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tevijjo iddhipattomhi, cetopariyāyakovido’’ti.
::

::centre
Vaṅgīsasaṃyuttaṃ samattaṃ.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Nikkhantaṃ {pb:T:1.0289} arati ceva, pesalā atimaññanā;
::

::gatha2
Ānandena subhāsitā, sāriputtapavāraṇā;
::

::gatha3
Parosahassaṃ koṇḍañño, moggallānena gaggarā;
::

::gathalast
Vaṅgīsena dvādasāti.
::

### 9. Vanasaṃyuttaṃ

#### 1. Vivekasuttaṃ

{para:221} 221\. Evaṃ {pb:T:1.0290}{pb:V:1.0228}{pb:P:1.0197}{pb:M:1.0199} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ aññataro bhikkhu kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe. Tena kho pana samayena so bhikkhu divāvihāragato pāpake akusale vitakke vitakketi gehanissite. Atha kho yā tasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā tassa bhikkhuno anukampikā atthakāmā taṃ bhikkhuṃ saṃvejetukāmā yena so bhikkhu tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā taṃ bhikkhuṃ gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Vivekakāmosi vanaṃ paviṭṭho,
::

::gatha2
Atha te mano niccharatī bahiddhā;
::

::gatha3
Jano janasmiṃ vinayassu chandaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Tato sukhī hohisi vītarāgo.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aratiṃ pajahāsi sato, bhavāsi sataṃ taṃ sārayāmase;
::

::gathalast
Pātālarajo hi duttaro, mā taṃ kāmarajo avāhari.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sakuṇo yathā paṃsukunthito {note:paṃsukuṇṭhito (ka.), paṃsukuṇḍito (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)}, vidhunaṃ pātayati sitaṃ rajaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ {pb:T:1.0291} bhikkhu padhānavā satimā, vidhunaṃ pātayati sitaṃ raja’’nti.
::

Atha kho so bhikkhu tāya devatāya saṃvejito saṃvegamāpādīti.

#### 2. Upaṭṭhānasuttaṃ

{para:222} 222\. Ekaṃ {pb:V:1.0229} samayaṃ aññataro bhikkhu kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe. Tena {pb:P:1.0198} kho pana samayena so bhikkhu divāvihāragato supati. Atha kho yā tasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā tassa bhikkhuno anukampikā atthakāmā taṃ bhikkhuṃ saṃvejetukāmā yena so bhikkhu tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā taṃ bhikkhuṃ gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Uṭṭhehi bhikkhu kiṃ sesi, ko attho supitena {note:supinena (sī.)} te;
::

::gathalast
Āturassa hi kā niddā, sallaviddhassa ruppato.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yāya {pb:M:1.0200} saddhāya pabbajito {note:yāya saddhāpabbajito (sī. syā. kaṃ.)}, agārasmānagāriyaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tameva saddhaṃ brūhehi, mā niddāya vasaṃ gamī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aniccā addhuvā kāmā, yesu mandova mucchito;
::

::gathalast
Baddhesu {note:khandhesu (sī.)} muttaṃ asitaṃ, kasmā pabbajitaṃ tape.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Chandarāgassa vinayā, avijjāsamatikkamā;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ ñāṇaṃ paramodānaṃ {note:pariyodātaṃ (sī. pī.), paramodātaṃ (syā. kaṃ.), paramavodānaṃ (sī. aṭṭha.)}, kasmā pabbajitaṃ tape.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Chetvā {pb:T:1.0292} {note:bhetvā (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} avijjaṃ vijjāya, āsavānaṃ parikkhayā;
::

::gathalast
Asokaṃ anupāyāsaṃ, kasmā pabbajitaṃ tape.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Āraddhavīriyaṃ pahitattaṃ, niccaṃ daḷhaparakkamaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nibbānaṃ abhikaṅkhantaṃ, kasmā pabbajitaṃ tape’’ti.
::

#### 3. Kassapagottasuttaṃ

{para:223} 223\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ āyasmā kassapagotto kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe. Tena {pb:V:1.0230} kho pana samayena āyasmā kassapagotto divāvihāragato aññataraṃ chetaṃ ovadati. Atha kho yā tasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā āyasmantaṃ kassapagottaṃ saṃvejetukāmā yenāyasmā kassapagotto tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmantaṃ kassapagottaṃ gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Giriduggacaraṃ chetaṃ, appapaññaṃ acetasaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Akāle ovadaṃ bhikkhu, mandova paṭibhāti maṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Suṇāti na vijānāti, āloketi na passati;
::

::gathalast
Dhammasmiṃ bhaññamānasmiṃ, atthaṃ bālo na bujjhati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sacepi {pb:P:1.0199} dasa pajjote, dhārayissasi kassapa;
::

::gathalast
Neva dakkhati rūpāni, cakkhu hissa na vijjatī’’ti.
::

Atha kho āyasmā kassapagotto tāya devatāya saṃvejito saṃvegamāpādīti.

#### 4. Sambahulasuttaṃ

{para:224} 224\. Ekaṃ {pb:T:1.0293}{pb:M:1.0201} samayaṃ sambahulā bhikkhū kosalesu viharanti aññatarasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe. Atha kho te bhikkhū vassaṃvuṭṭhā {note:vassaṃvutthā (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} temāsaccayena cārikaṃ pakkamiṃsu. Atha kho yā tasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā te bhikkhū apassantī paridevamānā tāyaṃ velāyaṃ imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Arati viya mejja khāyati,
::

::gatha2
Bahuke disvāna vivitte āsane;
::

::gatha3
Te cittakathā bahussutā,
::

::gathalast
Kome gotamasāvakā gatā’’ti.
::

Evaṃ vutte, aññatarā devatā taṃ devataṃ gāthāya paccabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Māgadhaṃ {pb:V:1.0231} gatā kosalaṃ gatā, ekacciyā pana vajjibhūmiyā;
::

::gathalast
Magā viya asaṅgacārino, aniketā viharanti bhikkhavo’’ti.
::

#### 5. Ānandasuttaṃ

{para:225} 225\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ āyasmā ānando kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā ānando ativelaṃ gihisaññattibahulo viharati. Atha kho yā tasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā āyasmato ānandassa {pb:T:1.0294} anukampikā atthakāmā āyasmantaṃ ānandaṃ saṃvejetukāmā yenāyasmā ānando tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmantaṃ ānandaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Rukkhamūlagahanaṃ pasakkiya, nibbānaṃ hadayasmiṃ opiya;
::

::gathalast
Jhā {pb:P:1.0200} gotama mā pamādo {note:mā ca pamādo (sī. pī.)}, kiṃ te biḷibiḷikā karissatī’’ti.
::

Atha kho āyasmā ānando tāya devatāya saṃvejito saṃvegamāpādīti.

#### 6. Anuruddhasuttaṃ

{para:226} 226\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ āyasmā anuruddho kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe. Atha kho aññatarā tāvatiṃsakāyikā devatā jālinī {pb:M:1.0202} nāma āyasmato anuruddhassa purāṇadutiyikā yenāyasmā anuruddho tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā āyasmantaṃ anuruddhaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Tattha cittaṃ paṇidhehi, yattha te vusitaṃ pure;
::

::gatha2
Tāvatiṃsesu devesu, sabbakāmasamiddhisu;
::

::gathalast
Purakkhato parivuto, devakaññāhi sobhasī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Duggatā {pb:V:1.0232} devakaññāyo, sakkāyasmiṃ patiṭṭhitā;
::

::gathalast
Te cāpi duggatā sattā, devakaññāhi patthitā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:T:1.0295} te sukhaṃ pajānanti, ye na passanti nandanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Āvāsaṃ naradevānaṃ, tidasānaṃ yasassina’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na tvaṃ bāle vijānāsi, yathā arahataṃ vaco;
::

::gatha2
Aniccā sabbasaṅkhārā, uppādavayadhammino;
::

::gathalast
Uppajjitvā nirujjhanti, tesaṃ vūpasamo sukho.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Natthi dāni punāvāso, devakāyasmi jālini;
::

::gathalast
Vikkhīṇo jātisaṃsāro, natthi dāni punabbhavo’’ti.
::

#### 7. Nāgadattasuttaṃ

{para:227} 227\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ āyasmā nāgadatto kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā nāgadatto atikālena gāmaṃ pavisati, atidivā paṭikkamati. Atha kho yā tasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā āyasmato nāgadattassa anukampikā atthakāmā āyasmantaṃ nāgadattaṃ saṃvejetukāmā yenāyasmā nāgadatto tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā {pb:P:1.0201} āyasmantaṃ nāgadattaṃ gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kāle pavisa nāgadatta, divā ca āgantvā ativelacārī;
::

::gathalast
Saṃsaṭṭho gahaṭṭhehi, samānasukhadukkho.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhāyāmi nāgadattaṃ suppagabbhaṃ, kulesu vinibaddhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mā heva maccurañño balavato, antakassa vasaṃ upesī’’ti {note:vasameyyāti (sī. pī.), vasamesīti (syā. kaṃ.)}.
::

Atha {pb:M:1.0203} kho āyasmā nāgadatto tāya devatāya saṃvejito saṃvegamāpādīti.

#### 8. Kulagharaṇīsuttaṃ

{para:228} 228\. Ekaṃ {pb:T:1.0296}{pb:V:1.0233} samayaṃ aññataro bhikkhu kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe. Tena kho pana samayena so bhikkhu aññatarasmiṃ kule ativelaṃ ajjhogāḷhappatto viharati. Atha kho yā tasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā tassa bhikkhuno anukampikā atthakāmā taṃ bhikkhuṃ saṃvejetukāmā yā tasmiṃ kule kulagharaṇī, tassā vaṇṇaṃ abhinimminitvā yena so bhikkhu tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā taṃ bhikkhuṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Nadītīresu saṇṭhāne, sabhāsu rathiyāsu ca;
::

::gathalast
Janā saṅgamma mantenti, mañca tañca {note:tvañca (ka.)} kimantara’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bahūhi saddā paccūhā, khamitabbā tapassinā;
::

::gathalast
Na tena maṅku hotabbaṃ, na hi tena kilissati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo ca saddaparittāsī, vane vātamigo yathā;
::

::gathalast
Lahucittoti taṃ āhu, nāssa sampajjate vata’’nti.
::

#### 9. Vajjiputtasuttaṃ

{para:229} 229\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ aññataro vajjiputtako bhikkhu vesāliyaṃ viharati aññatarasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe. Tena kho pana samayena vesāliyaṃ vajjiputtako sabbaratticāro hoti. Atha {pb:P:1.0202} kho so bhikkhu vesāliyā tūriya-tāḷita-vādita-nigghosasaddaṃ {pb:T:1.0297} sutvā paridevamāno tāyaṃ velāyaṃ imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Ekakā mayaṃ araññe viharāma,
::

::gatha2
Apaviddhaṃva {note:apaviṭṭhaṃva (syā. kaṃ.)} vanasmiṃ dārukaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Etādisikāya rattiyā,
::

::gathalast
Ko su nāmamhehi {note:nāma amhehi (sī. pī.)} pāpiyo’’ti.
::

Atha {pb:V:1.0234} kho yā tasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā tassa bhikkhuno anukampikā atthakāmā taṃ bhikkhuṃ saṃvejetukāmā yena so bhikkhu tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā taṃ bhikkhuṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Ekakova {pb:M:1.0204} tvaṃ araññe viharasi, apaviddhaṃva vanasmiṃ dārukaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tassa te bahukā pihayanti, nerayikā viya saggagāmina’’nti.
::

Atha kho so bhikkhu tāya devatāya saṃvejito saṃvegamāpādīti.

#### 10. Sajjhāyasuttaṃ

{para:230} 230\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ aññataro bhikkhu kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe. Tena kho pana samayena so bhikkhu yaṃ sudaṃ pubbe ativelaṃ sajjhāyabahulo viharati so aparena samayena appossukko tuṇhībhūto saṅkasāyati. Atha kho yā tasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā tassa bhikkhuno dhammaṃ asuṇantī yena so bhikkhu tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā taṃ {pb:T:1.0298} bhikkhuṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kasmā tuvaṃ dhammapadāni bhikkhu, nādhīyasi bhikkhūhi saṃvasanto;
::

::gathalast
Sutvāna dhammaṃ labhatippasādaṃ, diṭṭheva dhamme labhatippasaṃsa’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahu pure dhammapadesu chando, yāva virāgena samāgamimha;
::

::gatha2
Yato {pb:P:1.0203} virāgena samāgamimha, yaṃ kiñci diṭṭhaṃva sutaṃ mutaṃ vā;
::

::gathalast
Aññāya nikkhepanamāhu santo’’ti.
::

#### 11. Akusalavitakkasuttaṃ

{para:231} 231\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ aññataro bhikkhu kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe. Tena kho pana samayena so bhikkhu divāvihāragato pāpake akusale vitakke vitakketi, seyyathidaṃ {pb:V:1.0235} – kāmavitakkaṃ, byāpādavitakkaṃ, vihiṃsāvitakkaṃ. Atha kho yā tasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā tassa bhikkhuno anukampikā atthakāmā taṃ bhikkhuṃ saṃvejetukāmā yena so bhikkhu tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā taṃ bhikkhuṃ gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Ayoniso {pb:T:1.0299} manasikārā, so vitakkehi khajjasi;
::

::gathalast
Ayoniso {note:ayoniṃ (pī. ka.)} paṭinissajja, yoniso anucintaya.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satthāraṃ {pb:M:1.0205} dhammamārabbha, saṅghaṃ sīlāni attano;
::

::gatha2
Adhigacchasi pāmojjaṃ, pītisukhamasaṃsayaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tato pāmojjabahulo, dukkhassantaṃ karissasī’’ti.
::

Atha kho so bhikkhu tāya devatāya saṃvejito saṃvegamāpādīti.

#### 12. Majjhanhikasuttaṃ

{para:232} 232\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ aññataro bhikkhu kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe. Atha kho tasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā yena so bhikkhu tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā tassa bhikkhuno santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Ṭhite majjhanhike kāle, sannisīvesu {note:sannisinnesu (syā. kaṃ. pī.)} pakkhisu;
::

::gathalast
Saṇateva brahāraññaṃ, taṃ bhayaṃ paṭibhāti maṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ṭhite majjhanhike kāle, sannisīvesu pakkhisu;
::

::gathalast
Saṇateva brahāraññaṃ, sā rati paṭibhāti ma’’nti.
::

#### 13. Pākatindriyasuttaṃ

{para:233} 233\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ sambahulā bhikkhū kosalesu viharanti aññatarasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe uddhatā unnaḷā capalā mukharā vikiṇṇavācā {pb:P:1.0204} muṭṭhassatino asampajānā asamāhitā vibbhantacittā {pb:V:1.0236} pākatindriyā. Atha {pb:T:1.0300} kho yā tasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā tesaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ anukampikā atthakāmā te bhikkhū saṃvejetukāmā yena te bhikkhū tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā te bhikkhū gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sukhajīvino pure āsuṃ, bhikkhū gotamasāvakā;
::

::gatha2
Anicchā piṇḍamesanā, anicchā sayanāsanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Loke aniccataṃ ñatvā, dukkhassantaṃ akaṃsu te.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Dupposaṃ katvā attānaṃ, gāme gāmaṇikā viya;
::

::gathalast
Bhutvā bhutvā nipajjanti, parāgāresu mucchitā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṅghassa {pb:M:1.0206} añjaliṃ katvā, idhekacce vadāmahaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Apaviddhā {note:apaviṭṭhā (syā. kaṃ.)} anāthā te, yathā petā tatheva te.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye kho pamattā viharanti, te me sandhāya bhāsitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ye appamattā viharanti, namo tesaṃ karomaha’’nti.
::

Atha kho te bhikkhū tāya devatāya saṃvejitā saṃvegamāpādunti.

#### 14. Gandhatthenasuttaṃ

{para:234} 234\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ aññataro bhikkhu kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe. Tena kho pana samayena so bhikkhu pacchābhattaṃ piṇḍapātapaṭikkanto pokkharaṇiṃ ogāhetvā padumaṃ upasiṅghati. Atha kho yā tasmiṃ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā tassa bhikkhuno anukampikā atthakāmā taṃ bhikkhuṃ saṃvejetukāmā yena {pb:T:1.0301} so bhikkhu tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā taṃ bhikkhuṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Yametaṃ vārijaṃ pupphaṃ, adinnaṃ upasiṅghasi;
::

::gathalast
Ekaṅgametaṃ theyyānaṃ, gandhatthenosi mārisā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:V:1.0237} harāmi na bhañjāmi, ārā siṅghāmi vārijaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Atha kena nu vaṇṇena, gandhatthenoti vuccati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yvāyaṃ bhisāni khanati, puṇḍarīkāni bhañjati;
::

::gathalast
Evaṃ ākiṇṇakammanto, kasmā eso na vuccatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ākiṇṇaluddo {pb:P:1.0205} puriso, dhāticelaṃva makkhito;
::

::gathalast
Tasmiṃ me vacanaṃ natthi, tvañcārahāmi vattave.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Anaṅgaṇassa posassa, niccaṃ sucigavesino;
::

::gathalast
Vālaggamattaṃ pāpassa, abbhāmattaṃva khāyatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Addhā maṃ yakkha jānāsi, atho me anukampasi;
::

::gathalast
Punapi yakkha vajjāsi, yadā passasi edisa’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Neva {pb:M:1.0207} taṃ upajīvāma, napi te bhatakāmhase;
::

::gathalast
Tvameva bhikkhu jāneyya, yena gaccheyya suggati’’nti.
::

Atha kho so bhikkhu tāya devatāya saṃvejito saṃvegamāpādīti.

::centre
Vanasaṃyuttaṃ samattaṃ.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Vivekaṃ {pb:T:1.0302} upaṭṭhānañca, kassapagottena sambahulā;
::

::gathalast
Ānando anuruddho ca, nāgadattañca kulagharaṇī.
::

::gatha1
Vajjiputto ca vesālī, sajjhāyena ayoniso;
::

::gathalast
Majjhanhikālamhi pākatindriya, padumapupphena cuddasa bhaveti.
::

### 10. Yakkhasaṃyuttaṃ

#### 1. Indakasuttaṃ

{para:235} 235\. Evaṃ {pb:T:1.0303}{pb:V:1.0238}{pb:M:1.0208} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ {pb:P:1.0206} samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati indakūṭe pabbate, indakassa yakkhassa bhavane. Atha kho indako yakkho yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Rūpaṃ na jīvanti vadanti buddhā, kathaṃ nvayaṃ vindatimaṃ sarīraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kutassa aṭṭhīyakapiṇḍameti, kathaṃ nvayaṃ sajjati gabbharasmi’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Paṭhamaṃ kalalaṃ hoti, kalalā hoti abbudaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Abbudā jāyate pesi, pesi nibbattatī ghano;
::

::gathalast
Ghanā pasākhā jāyanti, kesā lomā nakhāpi ca.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yañcassa bhuñjatī mātā, annaṃ pānañca bhojanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Tena so tattha yāpeti, mātukucchigato naro’’ti.
::

#### 2. Sakkanāmasuttaṃ

{para:236} 236\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati gijjhakūṭe pabbate. Atha kho sakkanāmako yakkho yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā {pb:T:1.0304} bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbaganthappahīnassa{pb:V:1.0239}, vippamuttassa te sato;
::

::gathalast
Samaṇassa na taṃ sādhu, yadaññamanusāsasī’’ti {note:yadaññamanusāsatīti (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)}.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yena kenaci vaṇṇena, saṃvāso sakka jāyati;
::

::gathalast
Na taṃ arahati sappañño, manasā anukampituṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Manasā ce pasannena, yadaññamanusāsati;
::

::gathalast
Na tena hoti saṃyutto, yānukampā {note:sānukampā (sī. pī.)} anuddayā’’ti.
::

#### 3. Sūcilomasuttaṃ

{para:237} 237\. Ekaṃ {pb:P:1.0207} samayaṃ bhagavā gayāyaṃ viharati ṭaṅkitamañce sūcilomassa yakkhassa bhavane. Tena kho pana samayena kharo ca yakkho sūcilomo {pb:M:1.0209} ca yakkho bhagavato avidūre atikkamanti. Atha kho kharo yakkho sūcilomaṃ yakkhaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘eso samaṇo’’ti! ‘‘Neso samaṇo, samaṇako eso’’. ‘‘Yāva jānāmi yadi vā so samaṇo yadi vā pana so samaṇako’’ti.

Atha kho sūcilomo yakkho yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavato kāyaṃ upanāmesi. Atha kho bhagavā kāyaṃ apanāmesi. Atha kho sūcilomo yakkho bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘bhāyasi maṃ samaṇā’’ti? ‘‘Na khvāhaṃ taṃ, āvuso, bhāyāmi; api ca te samphasso pāpako’’ti. ‘‘Pañhaṃ taṃ, samaṇa pucchissāmi. Sace me na byākarissasi, cittaṃ vā te khipissāmi, hadayaṃ vā te phālessāmi, pādesu {pb:T:1.0305} vā gahetvā pāragaṅgāya {note:pāraṃ gaṅgāya (ka.)} khipissāmī’’ti. ‘‘Na khvāhaṃ taṃ, āvuso, passāmi sadevake loke samārake sabrahmake sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya, yo me cittaṃ vā khipeyya hadayaṃ vā phāleyya pādesu vā gahetvā pāragaṅgāya khipeyya; api ca tvaṃ, āvuso, puccha yadā kaṅkhasī’’ti. Atha kho sūcilomo yakkho bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi – ( ) {note:(atha kho sūcilomo yakkho bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi.) (sī.)}

::gatha1
‘‘Rāgo {pb:V:1.0240} ca doso ca kutonidānā,
::

::gatha2
Aratī ratī lomahaṃso kutojā;
::

::gatha3
Kuto samuṭṭhāya manovitakkā,
::

::gathalast
Kumārakā dhaṅkamivossajantī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Rāgo ca doso ca itonidānā,
::

::gatha2
Aratī ratī lomahaṃso itojā;
::

::gatha3
Ito samuṭṭhāya manovitakkā,
::

::gathalast
Kumārakā dhaṅkamivossajanti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Snehajā attasambhūtā, nigrodhasseva khandhajā;
::

::gathalast
Puthū visattā kāmesu, māluvāva vitatā {note:vitthatā (syā. kaṃ.)} vane.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye {pb:M:1.0210}{pb:P:1.0208} naṃ pajānanti yatonidānaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Te naṃ vinodenti suṇohi yakkha;
::

::gatha3
Te duttaraṃ oghamimaṃ taranti,
::

::gathalast
Atiṇṇapubbaṃ apunabbhavāyā’’ti.
::

#### 4. Maṇibhaddasuttaṃ

{para:238} 238\. Ekaṃ {pb:T:1.0306} samayaṃ bhagavā magadhesu viharati maṇimālike cetiye maṇibhaddassa yakkhassa bhavane. Atha kho maṇibhaddo yakkho yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Satīmato {pb:V:1.0241} sadā bhaddaṃ, satimā sukhamedhati;
::

::gathalast
Satīmato suve seyyo, verā ca parimuccatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Satīmato sadā bhaddaṃ, satimā sukhamedhati;
::

::gathalast
Satīmato suve seyyo, verā na parimuccati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yassa sabbamahorattaṃ {note:rattiṃ (syā. kaṃ. ka.)}, ahiṃsāya rato mano;
::

::gathalast
Mettaṃ so sabbabhūtesu, veraṃ tassa na kenacī’’ti.
::

#### 5. Sānusuttaṃ

{para:239} 239\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Tena kho pana samayena aññatarissā upāsikāya sānu nāma putto yakkhena gahito hoti. Atha kho sā upāsikā paridevamānā tāyaṃ velāyaṃ imā gāthāyo abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Cātuddasiṃ {pb:T:1.0307} pañcadasiṃ, yā ca pakkhassa aṭṭhamī;
::

::gathalast
Pāṭihāriyapakkhañca, aṭṭhaṅgasusamāgataṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Uposathaṃ upavasanti, brahmacariyaṃ caranti ye;
::

::gatha2
Na tehi yakkhā kīḷanti, iti me arahataṃ sutaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Sā dāni ajja passāmi, yakkhā kīḷanti sānunā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cātuddasiṃ {pb:M:1.0211} pañcadasiṃ, yā ca pakkhassa aṭṭhamī;
::

::gatha2
Pāṭihāriyapakkhañca, aṭṭhaṅgasusamāgataṃ;
::

::gathalast
Uposathaṃ {pb:P:1.0209} upavasanti, brahmacariyaṃ caranti ye.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na tehi yakkhā kīḷanti, sāhu te arahataṃ sutaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Sānuṃ pabuddhaṃ vajjāsi, yakkhānaṃ vacanaṃ idaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Mākāsi pāpakaṃ kammaṃ, āvi vā yadi vā raho.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace {pb:V:1.0242} ca {note:saceva (syā. kaṃ. pī. ka.), yañceva (sī.)} pāpakaṃ kammaṃ, karissasi karosi vā;
::

::gathalast
Na te dukkhā pamutyatthi, uppaccāpi palāyato’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mataṃ vā amma rodanti, yo vā jīvaṃ na dissati;
::

::gathalast
Jīvantaṃ amma passantī, kasmā maṃ amma rodasī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Mataṃ vā putta rodanti, yo vā jīvaṃ na dissati;
::

::gatha2
Yo ca kāme cajitvāna, punarāgacchate idha;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ vāpi putta rodanti, puna jīvaṃ mato hi so.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kukkuḷā ubbhato tāta, kukkuḷaṃ {note:kukkuḷe (sī.)} patitumicchasi;
::

::gathalast
Narakā ubbhato tāta, narakaṃ patitumicchasi.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abhidhāvatha {pb:T:1.0308} bhaddante, kassa ujjhāpayāmase;
::

::gathalast
Ādittā nīhataṃ {note:nibbhataṃ (syā. kaṃ. ka.), nibhataṃ (pī. ka.)} bhaṇḍaṃ, puna ḍayhitumicchasī’’ti.
::

#### 6. Piyaṅkarasuttaṃ

{para:240} 240\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ āyasmā anuruddho sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā anuruddho rattiyā paccūsasamayaṃ paccuṭṭhāya dhammapadāni bhāsati. Atha kho piyaṅkaramātā yakkhinī puttakaṃ evaṃ tosesi –

::gatha1
‘‘Mā saddaṃ kari piyaṅkara, bhikkhu dhammapadāni bhāsati;
::

::gathalast
Api {note:api (sī.)} ca dhammapadaṃ vijāniya, paṭipajjema hitāya no siyā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Pāṇesu ca saṃyamāmase, sampajānamusā na bhaṇāmase;
::

::gathalast
Sikkhema susīlyamattano {note:susīlamattano (sī. ka.)}, api muccema pisācayoniyā’’ti.
::

#### 7. Punabbasusuttaṃ

{para:241} 241\. Ekaṃ {pb:V:1.0243}{pb:M:1.0212} samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Tena {pb:P:1.0210} kho pana samayena bhagavā bhikkhū nibbānapaṭisaṃyuttāya dhammiyā kathāya sandasseti samādapeti samuttejeti sampahaṃseti. Te ca bhikkhū aṭṭhiṃ katvā manasi katvā sabbacetasā {pb:T:1.0309} samannāharitvā ohitasotā dhammaṃ suṇanti. Atha kho punabbasumātā yakkhinī puttake evaṃ tosesi –

::gatha1
‘‘Tuṇhī uttarike hohi, tuṇhī hohi punabbasu;
::

::gathalast
Yāvāhaṃ buddhaseṭṭhassa, dhammaṃ sossāmi satthuno.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nibbānaṃ bhagavā āha, sabbaganthappamocanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Ativelā ca me hoti, asmiṃ dhamme piyāyanā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Piyo loke sako putto, piyo loke sako pati;
::

::gathalast
Tato piyatarā mayhaṃ, assa dhammassa magganā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na hi putto pati vāpi, piyo dukkhā pamocaye;
::

::gathalast
Yathā saddhammassavanaṃ, dukkhā moceti pāṇinaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Loke dukkhaparetasmiṃ, jarāmaraṇasaṃyute;
::

::gatha2
Jarāmaraṇamokkhāya, yaṃ dhammaṃ abhisambudhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ dhammaṃ sotumicchāmi, tuṇhī hohi punabbasū’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ammā na byāharissāmi, tuṇhībhūtāyamuttarā;
::

::gatha2
Dhammameva nisāmehi, saddhammassavanaṃ sukhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saddhammassa anaññāya, ammā dukkhaṃ carāmase.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Esa {pb:V:1.0244} devamanussānaṃ, sammūḷhānaṃ pabhaṅkaro;
::

::gathalast
Buddho antimasārīro, dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sādhu kho paṇḍito nāma, putto jāto uresayo;
::

::gathalast
Putto me buddhaseṭṭhassa, dhammaṃ suddhaṃ piyāyati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Punabbasu {pb:T:1.0310} sukhī hohi, ajjāhamhi samuggatā;
::

::gathalast
Diṭṭhāni ariyasaccāni, uttarāpi suṇātu me’’ti.
::

#### 8. Sudattasuttaṃ

{para:242} 242\. Ekaṃ {pb:M:1.0213} samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati sītavane. Tena kho pana samayena anāthapiṇḍiko gahapati rājagahaṃ anuppatto hoti kenacideva karaṇīyena. Assosi kho anāthapiṇḍiko gahapati – ‘‘buddho kira loke uppanno’’ti. Tāvadeva ca pana bhagavantaṃ dassanāya upasaṅkamitukāmo hoti. Athassa {pb:P:1.0211} anāthapiṇḍikassa gahapatissa etadahosi – ‘‘akālo kho ajja bhagavantaṃ dassanāya upasaṅkamituṃ. Sve dānāhaṃ kālena bhagavantaṃ dassanāya gamissāmī’’ti buddhagatāya satiyā nipajji. Rattiyā sudaṃ tikkhattuṃ vuṭṭhāsi pabhātanti maññamāno. Atha kho anāthapiṇḍiko gahapati yena sivathikadvāraṃ {note:sīvathikadvāraṃ (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)} tenupasaṅkami. Amanussā dvāraṃ vivariṃsu. Atha kho anāthapiṇḍikassa gahapatissa nagaramhā nikkhamantassa āloko antaradhāyi, andhakāro pāturahosi, bhayaṃ chambhitattaṃ lomahaṃso udapādi, tatova puna nivattitukāmo ahosi. Atha kho sivako {note:sīvako (sī. pī.)} yakkho antarahito saddamanussāvesi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sataṃ hatthī sataṃ assā, sataṃ assatarīrathā;
::

::gatha2
Sataṃ kaññāsahassāni, āmukkamaṇikuṇḍalā;
::

::gathalast
Ekassa padavītihārassa, kalaṃ nāgghanti soḷasiṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abhikkama {pb:T:1.0311} gahapati, abhikkama gahapati;
::

::gathalast
Abhikkamanaṃ te seyyo, no paṭikkamana’’nti.
::

Atha {pb:V:1.0245} kho anāthapiṇḍikassa gahapatissa andhakāro antaradhāyi, āloko pāturahosi, yaṃ ahosi bhayaṃ chambhitattaṃ lomahaṃso, so paṭippassambhi. Dutiyampi kho anāthapiṇḍikassa gahapatissa āloko antaradhāyi, andhakāro pāturahosi, bhayaṃ chambhitattaṃ lomahaṃso udapādi, tatova puna nivattitukāmo ahosi. Dutiyampi kho sivako yakkho antarahito saddamanussāvesi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sataṃ {pb:M:1.0214} hatthī sataṃ assā…pe…
::

::gathalast
Kalaṃ nāgghanti soḷasiṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abhikkama gahapati, abhikkama gahapati;
::

::gathalast
Abhikkamanaṃ te seyyo, no paṭikkamana’’nti.
::

Atha {pb:T:1.0312} kho anāthapiṇḍikassa gahapatissa andhakāro antaradhāyi{pb:P:1.0212}, āloko pāturahosi, yaṃ ahosi bhayaṃ chambhitattaṃ lomahaṃso, so paṭippassambhi. Tatiyampi kho anāthapiṇḍikassa gahapatissa āloko antaradhāyi, andhakāro pāturahosi, bhayaṃ chambhitattaṃ lomahaṃso udapādi, tatova puna nivattitukāmo ahosi. Tatiyampi kho sivako yakkho antarahito saddamanussāvesi –

::gatha1
‘‘Sataṃ hatthī sataṃ assā…pe…
::

::gathalast
Kalaṃ nāgghanti soḷasiṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abhikkama gahapati, abhikkama gahapati;
::

::gathalast
Abhikkamanaṃ te seyyo, no paṭikkamana’’nti.
::

Atha kho anāthapiṇḍikassa gahapatissa andhakāro antaradhāyi, āloko pāturahosi, yaṃ {pb:V:1.0246} ahosi bhayaṃ chambhitattaṃ lomahaṃso, so paṭippassambhi. Atha kho anāthapiṇḍiko gahapati yena sītavanaṃ yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami.

Tena kho pana samayena bhagavā rattiyā paccūsasamayaṃ paccuṭṭhāya abbhokāse caṅkamati. Addasā kho bhagavā anāthapiṇḍikaṃ gahapatiṃ dūratova āgacchantaṃ. Disvāna caṅkamā orohitvā paññatte āsane nisīdi. Nisajja kho bhagavā anāthapiṇḍikaṃ gahapatiṃ etadavoca – ‘‘ehi sudattā’’ti. Atha kho anāthapiṇḍiko gahapati, nāmena maṃ bhagavā ālapatīti, haṭṭho udaggo tattheva bhagavato pādesu sirasā nipatitvā bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘kacci, bhante, bhagavā sukhamasayitthā’’ti?

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbadā ve sukhaṃ seti, brāhmaṇo parinibbuto;
::

::gathalast
Yo na limpati kāmesu, sītibhūto nirūpadhi.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbā āsattiyo chetvā, vineyya hadaye daraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Upasanto sukhaṃ seti, santiṃ pappuyya cetasā’’ti {note:cetasoti (sī.)}.
::

#### 9. Paṭhamasukkāsuttaṃ

{para:243} 243\. Ekaṃ {pb:M:1.0215} samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati veḷuvane kalandakanivāpe. Tena kho pana samayena sukkā bhikkhunī mahatiyā parisāya parivutā dhammaṃ deseti. Atha kho sukkāya bhikkhuniyā abhippasanno yakkho rājagahe rathikāya {pb:T:1.0313} rathikaṃ siṅghāṭakena siṅghāṭakaṃ upasaṅkamitvā tāyaṃ velāyaṃ imā gāthāyo abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ me katā rājagahe manussā, madhupītāva seyare;
::

::gathalast
Ye sukkaṃ na payirupāsanti, desentiṃ amataṃ padaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tañca pana appaṭivānīyaṃ, asecanakamojavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pivanti maññe sappaññā, valāhakamiva panthagū’’ti {note:valāhakamivaddhagūti (sī.)}.
::

#### 10. Dutiyasukkāsuttaṃ

{para:244} 244\. Ekaṃ {pb:V:1.0247} samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati veḷuvane kalandakanivāpe. Tena {pb:P:1.0213} kho pana samayena aññataro upāsako sukkāya bhikkhuniyā bhojanaṃ adāsi. Atha kho sukkāya bhikkhuniyā abhippasanno yakkho rājagahe rathikāya rathikaṃ siṅghāṭakena siṅghāṭakaṃ upasaṅkamitvā tāyaṃ velāyaṃ imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Puññaṃ vata pasavi bahuṃ, sappañño vatāyaṃ upāsako;
::

::gathalast
Yo sukkāya adāsi bhojanaṃ, sabbaganthehi vippamuttiyā’’ti {note:vippamuttāyāti (syā. kaṃ.)}.
::

#### 11. Cīrāsuttaṃ

{para:245} 245\. Evaṃ me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati veḷuvane kalandakanivāpe. Tena kho pana samayena aññataro upāsako cīrāya {note:cirāya (ka.)} bhikkhuniyā cīvaraṃ adāsi. Atha {pb:T:1.0314} kho cīrāya bhikkhuniyā abhippasanno yakkho rājagahe rathikāya rathikaṃ siṅghāṭakena siṅghāṭakaṃ upasaṅkamitvā tāyaṃ velāyaṃ imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Puññaṃ {pb:M:1.0216} vata pasavi bahuṃ, sappañño vatāyaṃ upāsako;
::

::gathalast
Yo cīrāya adāsi cīvaraṃ, sabbayogehi vippamuttiyā’’ti {note:vippamuttāyāti (syā. kaṃ.)}.
::

#### 12. Āḷavakasuttaṃ

{para:246} 246\. Evaṃ me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā āḷaviyaṃ viharati āḷavakassa yakkhassa bhavane. Atha kho āḷavako yakkho yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘nikkhama, samaṇā’’ti. ‘‘Sādhāvuso’’ti bhagavā nikkhami. ‘‘Pavisa, samaṇā’’ti. ‘‘Sādhāvuso’’ti bhagavā pāvisi. Dutiyampi kho āḷavako yakkho bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘nikkhama, samaṇā’’ti. ‘‘Sādhāvuso’’ti bhagavā nikkhami. ‘‘Pavisa, samaṇā’’ti. ‘‘Sādhāvuso’’ti bhagavā pāvisi. Tatiyampi {pb:P:1.0214} kho āḷavako yakkho bhagavantaṃ etadavoca {pb:V:1.0248} – ‘‘nikkhama, samaṇā’’ti. ‘‘Sādhāvuso’’ti bhagavā nikkhami. ‘‘Pavisa, samaṇā’’ti. ‘‘Sādhāvuso’’ti bhagavā pāvisi. Catutthampi kho āḷavako yakkho bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘nikkhama, samaṇā’’ti. ‘‘Na khvāhaṃ taṃ, āvuso, nikkhamissāmi. Yaṃ te karaṇīyaṃ taṃ karohī’’ti. ‘‘Pañhaṃ taṃ, samaṇa, pucchissāmi. Sace me na byākarissasi, cittaṃ vā te khipissāmi, hadayaṃ vā te phālessāmi, pādesu vā gahetvā pāragaṅgāya khipissāmī’’ti. ‘‘Na khvāhaṃ taṃ, āvuso, passāmi sadevake loke samārake {pb:T:1.0315} sabrahmake sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya, ye me cittaṃ vā khipeyya hadayaṃ vā phāleyya, pādesu vā gahetvā pāragaṅgāya khipeyya. Api ca tvaṃ, āvuso, puccha yadā kaṅkhasī’’ti {note:(atha kho āḷavako yakkho bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi.) (sī.)}.

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsūdha vittaṃ purisassa seṭṭhaṃ, kiṃsu suciṇṇaṃ sukhamāvahāti;
::

::gathalast
Kiṃsu have sādutaraṃ rasānaṃ, kathaṃjīviṃ jīvitamāhu seṭṭha’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saddhīdha vittaṃ purissa seṭṭhaṃ, dhammo suciṇṇo sukhamāvahāti;
::

::gathalast
Saccaṃ have sādutaraṃ rasānaṃ, paññājīviṃ jīvitamāhu seṭṭha’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kathaṃsu tarati oghaṃ, kathaṃsu tarati aṇṇavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kathaṃsu dukkhamacceti, kathaṃsu parisujjhatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saddhāya {pb:M:1.0217} tarati oghaṃ, appamādena aṇṇavaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Vīriyena dukkhamacceti, paññāya parisujjhatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kathaṃsu labhate paññaṃ, kathaṃsu vindate dhanaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Kathaṃsu kittiṃ pappoti, kathaṃ mittāni ganthati;
::

::gathalast
Asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ, kathaṃ pecca na socatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saddahāno arahataṃ, dhammaṃ nibbānapattiyā;
::

::gathalast
Sussūsaṃ {pb:T:1.0316} {note:sussūsā (sī. pī.)} labhate paññaṃ, appamatto vicakkhaṇo.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Patirūpakārī {pb:V:1.0249} dhuravā, uṭṭhātā vindate dhanaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Saccena {pb:P:1.0215} kittiṃ pappoti, dadaṃ mittāni ganthati;
::

::gathalast
Asmā lokā paraṃ lokaṃ, evaṃ pecca na socati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yassete caturo dhammā, saddhassa gharamesino;
::

::gathalast
Saccaṃ dammo dhiti cāgo, sa ve pecca na socati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Iṅgha aññepi pucchassu, puthū samaṇabrāhmaṇe;
::

::gathalast
Yadi saccā dammā cāgā, khantyā bhiyyodha vijjatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kathaṃ nu dāni puccheyyaṃ, puthū samaṇabrāhmaṇe;
::

::gathalast
Yohaṃ {note:sohaṃ (sī.), svāhaṃ (ka.)} ajja pajānāmi, yo attho samparāyiko.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Atthāya vata me buddho, vāsāyāḷavimāgamā {note:māgato (pī. ka.)};
::

::gathalast
Yohaṃ {note:sohaṃ (sī.)} ajja pajānāmi, yattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘So ahaṃ vicarissāmi, gāmā gāmaṃ purā puraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Namassamāno sambuddhaṃ, dhammassa ca sudhammata’’nti.
::

::centre
Yakkhasaṃyuttaṃ samattaṃ.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Indako sakka sūci ca, maṇibhaddo ca sānu ca;
::

::gathalast
Piyaṅkara punabbasu sudatto ca, dve sukkā cīraāḷavīti dvādasa.
::

### 11. Sakkasaṃyuttaṃ

#### 1. Paṭhamavaggo

#### 1. Suvīrasuttaṃ

{para:247} 247\. Evaṃ {pb:T:1.0317}{pb:V:1.0250}{pb:P:1.0216}{pb:M:1.0218} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Tatra kho bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi – ‘‘bhikkhavo’’ti. ‘‘Bhadante’’ti te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṃ. Bhagavā etadavoca –

‘‘Bhūtapubbaṃ, bhikkhave, asurā deve abhiyaṃsu. Atha kho, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo suvīraṃ devaputtaṃ āmantesi – ‘ete, tāta suvīra, asurā deve abhiyanti. Gaccha, tāta suvīra, asure paccuyyāhī’ti. ‘Evaṃ bhaddantavā’ti kho, bhikkhave, suvīro devaputto sakkassa devānamindassa paṭissutvā pamādaṃ āpādesi {note:āharesi (katthaci) navaṅguttare sīhanādasuttepi}. Dutiyampi kho, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo suvīraṃ devaputtaṃ āmantesi – ‘ete, tāta suvīra, asurā deve abhiyanti. Gaccha, tāta suvīra, asure paccuyyāhī’ti. ‘Evaṃ bhaddantavā’ti kho, bhikkhave, suvīro devaputto sakkassa devānamindassa paṭissutvā dutiyampi pamādaṃ āpādesi. Tatiyampi kho, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo suvīraṃ devaputtaṃ āmantesi – ‘ete, tāta suvīra, asurā deve abhiyanti. Gaccha, tāta suvīra, asure paccuyyāhī’ti{pb:T:1.0318}. ‘Evaṃ bhaddantavā’ti kho, bhikkhave, suvīro devaputto sakkassa devānamindassa paṭissutvā tatiyampi pamādaṃ āpādesi. Atha {pb:P:1.0217} kho, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo suvīraṃ devaputtaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Anuṭṭhahaṃ avāyāmaṃ, sukhaṃ yatrādhigacchati;
::

::gathalast
Suvīra tattha gacchāhi, mañca tattheva pāpayā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Alasvassa {pb:V:1.0251} {note:alasa’ssa (sī. pī.), alasvāyaṃ (syā. kaṃ.)} anuṭṭhātā, na ca kiccāni kāraye;
::

::gathalast
Sabbakāmasamiddhassa, taṃ me sakka varaṃ disā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yatthālaso {pb:M:1.0219} anuṭṭhātā, accantaṃ sukhamedhati;
::

::gathalast
Suvīra tattha gacchāhi, mañca tattheva pāpayā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akammunā {note:akammanā (sī. pī.)} devaseṭṭha, sakka vindemu yaṃ sukhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Asokaṃ anupāyāsaṃ, taṃ me sakka varaṃ disā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace atthi akammena, koci kvaci na jīvati;
::

::gatha2
Nibbānassa hi so maggo, suvīra tattha gacchāhi;
::

::gathalast
Mañca tattheva pāpayā’’ti.
::

‘‘So hi nāma, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo sakaṃ puññaphalaṃ upajīvamāno devānaṃ tāvatiṃsānaṃ issariyādhipaccaṃ rajjaṃ kārento uṭṭhānavīriyassa vaṇṇavādī bhavissati. Idha kho taṃ, bhikkhave, sobhetha, yaṃ tumhe evaṃ svākkhāte dhammavinaye pabbajitā samānā uṭṭhaheyyātha {pb:T:1.0319} ghaṭeyyātha vāyameyyātha appattassa pattiyā anadhigatassa adhigamāya, asacchikatassa sacchikiriyāyā’’ti.

#### 2. Susīmasuttaṃ

{para:248} 248\. Sāvatthiyaṃ. Tatra kho bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi – ‘‘bhikkhavo’’ti. ‘‘Bhadante’’ti te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṃ. Bhagavā etadavoca –

‘‘Bhūtapubbaṃ, bhikkhave, asurā deve abhiyaṃsu. Atha kho, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo susīmaṃ {note:susimaṃ (syā. kaṃ. ka.)} devaputtaṃ āmantesi – ‘ete, tāta susīma, asurā deve abhiyanti. Gaccha, tāta susīma, asure paccuyyāhī’ti. ‘Evaṃ bhaddantavā’ti kho, bhikkhave, susīmo devaputto sakkassa devānamindassa paṭissutvā pamādaṃ āpādesi. Dutiyampi {pb:P:1.0218} kho, bhikkhave, sakko {pb:V:1.0252} devānamindo susīmaṃ devaputtaṃ āmantesi…pe… dutiyampi pamādaṃ āpādesi. Tatiyampi kho, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo susīmaṃ devaputtaṃ āmantesi…pe… tatiyampi pamādaṃ āpādesi. Atha kho, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo susīmaṃ devaputtaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Anuṭṭhahaṃ {pb:T:1.0320} avāyāmaṃ, sukhaṃ yatrādhigacchati;
::

::gathalast
Susīma tattha gacchāhi, mañca tattheva pāpayā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Alasvassa {pb:M:1.0220} anuṭṭhātā, na ca kiccāni kāraye;
::

::gathalast
Sabbakāmasamiddhassa, taṃ me sakka varaṃ disā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yatthālaso anuṭṭhātā, accantaṃ sukhamedhati;
::

::gathalast
Susīma tattha gacchāhi, mañca tattheva pāpayā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Akammunā devaseṭṭha, sakka vindemu yaṃ sukhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Asokaṃ anupāyāsaṃ, taṃ me sakka varaṃ disā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sace atthi akammena, koci kvaci na jīvati;
::

::gatha2
Nibbānassa hi so maggo, susīma tattha gacchāhi;
::

::gathalast
Mañca tattheva pāpayā’’ti.
::

‘‘So hi nāma, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo sakaṃ puññaphalaṃ upajīvamāno devānaṃ tāvatiṃsānaṃ issariyādhipaccaṃ rajjaṃ kārento uṭṭhānavīriyassa vaṇṇavādī bhavissati. Idha kho taṃ, bhikkhave, sobhetha, yaṃ tumhe evaṃ svākkhāte dhammavinaye pabbajitā samānā uṭṭhaheyyātha ghaṭeyyātha vāyameyyātha appattassa pattiyā, anadhigatassa adhigamāya, asacchikatassa sacchikiriyāyā’’ti.

#### 3. Dhajaggasuttaṃ

{para:249} 249\. Sāvatthiyaṃ{pb:V:1.0253}. Tatra kho bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi – ‘‘bhikkhavo’’ti{pb:T:1.0321}. ‘‘Bhadante’’ti te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṃ. Bhagavā etadavoca –

‘‘Bhūtapubbaṃ, bhikkhave, devāsurasaṅgāmo samupabyūḷho ahosi. Atha kho, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo deve tāvatiṃse āmantesi –

‘Sace, mārisā, devānaṃ saṅgāmagatānaṃ uppajjeyya {pb:P:1.0219} bhayaṃ vā chambhitattaṃ vā lomahaṃso vā, mameva tasmiṃ samaye dhajaggaṃ ullokeyyātha. Mamañhi vo dhajaggaṃ ullokayataṃ yaṃ bhavissati bhayaṃ vā chambhitattaṃ vā lomahaṃso vā, so pahīyissati’.

‘No ce me dhajaggaṃ ullokeyyātha, atha pajāpatissa devarājassa dhajaggaṃ ullokeyyātha. Pajāpatissa hi vo devarājassa dhajaggaṃ ullokayataṃ yaṃ bhavissati bhayaṃ vā chambhitattaṃ vā lomahaṃso vā, so pahīyissati’.

‘No {pb:M:1.0221} ce pajāpatissa devarājassa dhajaggaṃ ullokeyyātha, atha varuṇassa devarājassa dhajaggaṃ ullokeyyātha. Varuṇassa hi vo devarājassa dhajaggaṃ ullokayataṃ yaṃ bhavissati bhayaṃ vā chambhitattaṃ vā lomahaṃso vā, so pahīyissati’.

‘No ce varuṇassa devarājassa dhajaggaṃ ullokeyyātha, atha īsānassa devarājassa dhajaggaṃ ullokeyyātha. Īsānassa hi vo devarājassa dhajaggaṃ ullokayataṃ yaṃ bhavissati bhayaṃ vā chambhitattaṃ vā lomahaṃso vā, so pahīyissatī’’’ti.

‘‘Taṃ kho pana, bhikkhave, sakkassa vā devānamindassa dhajaggaṃ ullokayataṃ, pajāpatissa vā devarājassa dhajaggaṃ ullokayataṃ, varuṇassa vā devarājassa dhajaggaṃ ullokayataṃ, īsānassa vā devarājassa dhajaggaṃ ullokayataṃ yaṃ {pb:T:1.0322} bhavissati bhayaṃ vā chambhitattaṃ vā lomahaṃso vā, so pahīyethāpi nopi pahīyetha {note:no pahīyetha (ka.)}.

‘‘Taṃ {pb:V:1.0254} kissa hetu? Sakko hi, bhikkhave, devānamindo avītarāgo avītadoso avītamoho bhīru chambhī utrāsī palāyīti.

‘‘Ahañca kho, bhikkhave, evaṃ vadāmi – ‘sace tumhākaṃ, bhikkhave, araññagatānaṃ vā rukkhamūlagatānaṃ vā suññāgāragatānaṃ vā uppajjeyya bhayaṃ vā chambhitattaṃ vā lomahaṃso vā, mameva tasmiṃ samaye anussareyyātha – itipi so bhagavā arahaṃ sammāsambuddho vijjācaraṇasampanno sugato lokavidū anuttaro purisadammasārathi satthā devamanussānaṃ buddho bhagavā’ti. Mamañhi vo, bhikkhave, anussarataṃ yaṃ bhavissati bhayaṃ vā chambhitattaṃ vā lomahaṃso vā, so pahīyissati.

‘‘No {pb:P:1.0220} ce maṃ anussareyyātha, atha dhammaṃ anussareyyātha – ‘svākkhāto bhagavatā dhammo sandiṭṭhiko akāliko ehipassiko opaneyyiko paccattaṃ veditabbo viññūhī’ti. Dhammañhi vo, bhikkhave, anussarataṃ yaṃ bhavissati bhayaṃ vā chambhitattaṃ vā lomahaṃso vā, so pahīyissati.

‘‘No ce dhammaṃ anussareyyātha, atha saṅghaṃ anussareyyātha – ‘suppaṭipanno bhagavato sāvakasaṅgho ujuppaṭipanno bhagavato sāvakasaṅgho {pb:M:1.0222} ñāyappaṭipanno bhagavato sāvakasaṅgho sāmīcippaṭipanno bhagavato sāvakasaṅgho, yadidaṃ cattāri purisayugāni aṭṭha purisapuggalā esa bhagavato sāvakasaṅgho, āhuneyyo pāhuneyyo dakkhiṇeyyo añjalikaraṇīyo anuttaraṃ puññakkhettaṃ lokassā’ti. Saṅghañhi vo, bhikkhave, anussarataṃ {pb:T:1.0323} yaṃ bhavissati bhayaṃ vā chambhitattaṃ vā lomahaṃso vā, so pahīyissati.

‘‘Taṃ kissa hetu? Tathāgato hi, bhikkhave, arahaṃ sammāsambuddho vītarāgo vītadoso vītamoho abhīru acchambhī anutrāsī apalāyī’’ti. Idamavoca bhagavā. Idaṃ vatvāna sugato athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

::gatha1
‘‘Araññe rukkhamūle vā, suññāgāreva bhikkhavo;
::

::gathalast
Anussaretha {note:anussareyyātha (ka.) padasiddhi pana cintetabbā} sambuddhaṃ, bhayaṃ tumhāka no siyā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘No {pb:V:1.0255} ce buddhaṃ sareyyātha, lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Atha dhammaṃ sareyyātha, niyyānikaṃ sudesitaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘No ce dhammaṃ sareyyātha, niyyānikaṃ sudesitaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Atha saṅghaṃ sareyyātha, puññakkhettaṃ anuttaraṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Evaṃ buddhaṃ sarantānaṃ, dhammaṃ saṅghañca bhikkhavo;
::

::gathalast
Bhayaṃ vā chambhitattaṃ vā, lomahaṃso na hessatī’’ti.
::

#### 4. Vepacittisuttaṃ

{para:250} 250\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. ‘‘Bhūtapubbaṃ{pb:P:1.0221}, bhikkhave, devāsurasaṅgāmo samupabyūḷho ahosi. Atha kho, bhikkhave, vepacitti asurindo asure āmantesi – ‘sace, mārisā, devānaṃ asurasaṅgāme samupabyūḷhe asurā {pb:T:1.0324} jineyyuṃ devā parājineyyuṃ {note:parājeyyuṃ (sī. pī.)}, yena naṃ sakkaṃ devānamindaṃ kaṇṭhapañcamehi bandhanehi bandhitvā mama santike āneyyātha asurapura’nti. Sakkopi kho, bhikkhave, devānamindo deve tāvatiṃse āmantesi – ‘sace, mārisā, devānaṃ asurasaṅgāme samupabyūḷhe devā jineyyuṃ asurā parājineyyuṃ, yena naṃ vepacittiṃ asurindaṃ kaṇṭhapañcamehi bandhanehi bandhitvā mama santike āneyyātha sudhammasabha’’’nti. Tasmiṃ kho pana, bhikkhave, saṅgāme devā jiniṃsu{pb:M:1.0223}, asurā parājiniṃsu {note:parājiṃsu (sī. pī.)}. Atha kho, bhikkhave, devā tāvatiṃsā vepacittiṃ asurindaṃ kaṇṭhapañcamehi bandhanehi bandhitvā sakkassa devānamindassa santike ānesuṃ sudhammasabhaṃ. Tatra sudaṃ, bhikkhave, vepacitti asurindo kaṇṭhapañcamehi bandhanehi baddho sakkaṃ devānamindaṃ sudhammasabhaṃ pavisantañca nikkhamantañca asabbhāhi pharusāhi vācāhi akkosati paribhāsati. Atha kho, bhikkhave, mātali saṅgāhako sakkaṃ devānamindaṃ gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Bhayā nu maghavā sakka, dubbalyā no titikkhasi;
::

::gathalast
Suṇanto pharusaṃ vācaṃ, sammukhā vepacittino’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Nāhaṃ {pb:V:1.0256} bhayā na dubbalyā, khamāmi vepacittino;
::

::gathalast
Kathañhi mādiso viññū, bālena paṭisaṃyuje’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Bhiyyo bālā pabhijjeyyuṃ, no cassa paṭisedhako;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā bhusena daṇḍena, dhīro bālaṃ nisedhaye’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etadeva {pb:T:1.0325} ahaṃ maññe, bālassa paṭisedhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Paraṃ saṅkupitaṃ ñatvā, yo sato upasammatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etadeva titikkhāya, vajjaṃ passāmi vāsava;
::

::gatha2
Yadā naṃ maññati bālo, bhayā myāyaṃ titikkhati;
::

::gathalast
Ajjhāruhati dummedho, gova bhiyyo palāyina’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kāmaṃ {pb:P:1.0222} maññatu vā mā vā, bhayā myāyaṃ titikkhati;
::

::gathalast
Sadatthaparamā atthā, khantyā bhiyyo na vijjati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo have balavā santo, dubbalassa titikkhati;
::

::gathalast
Tamāhu paramaṃ khantiṃ, niccaṃ khamati dubbalo.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abalaṃ taṃ balaṃ āhu, yassa bālabalaṃ balaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Balassa dhammaguttassa, paṭivattā na vijjati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasseva tena pāpiyo, yo kuddhaṃ paṭikujjhati;
::

::gathalast
Kuddhaṃ appaṭikujjhanto, saṅgāmaṃ jeti dujjayaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ubhinnamatthaṃ {pb:M:1.0224} carati, attano ca parassa ca;
::

::gathalast
Paraṃ saṅkupitaṃ ñatvā, yo sato upasammati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ubhinnaṃ {pb:V:1.0257} tikicchantānaṃ, attano ca parassa ca;
::

::gathalast
Janā maññanti bāloti, ye dhammassa akovidā’’ti.
::

‘‘So hi nāma, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo sakaṃ puññaphalaṃ upajīvamāno devānaṃ tāvatiṃsānaṃ issariyādhipaccaṃ rajjaṃ kārento khantisoraccassa vaṇṇavādī bhavissati. Idha kho taṃ, bhikkhave, sobhetha yaṃ {pb:T:1.0326} tumhe evaṃ svākkhāte dhammavinaye pabbajitā samānā khamā ca bhaveyyātha soratā cā’’ti.

#### 5. Subhāsitajayasuttaṃ

{para:251} 251\. Sāvatthinidānaṃ. ‘‘Bhūtapubbaṃ, bhikkhave, devāsurasaṅgāmo samupabyūḷho ahosi. Atha kho, bhikkhave, vepacitti asurindo sakkaṃ devānamindaṃ etadavoca – ‘hotu, devānaminda, subhāsitena jayo’ti. ‘Hotu, vepacitti, subhāsitena jayo’ti. Atha kho, bhikkhave, devā ca asurā ca pārisajje ṭhapesuṃ – ‘ime no subhāsitadubbhāsitaṃ ājānissantī’ti. Atha kho, bhikkhave, vepacittiṃ asurindo sakkaṃ devānamindaṃ etadavoca – ‘bhaṇa, devānaminda, gātha’nti. Evaṃ vutte, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo vepacitti asurindaṃ etadavoca – ‘tumhe khvettha, vepacitti, pubbadevā. Bhaṇa, vepacitti, gātha’nti. Evaṃ {pb:P:1.0223} vutte, bhikkhave, vepacitti asurindo imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Bhiyyo bālā pabhijjeyyuṃ, no cassa paṭisedhako;
::

::gathalast
Tasmā bhusena daṇḍena, dhīro bālaṃ nisedhaye’’ti.
::

‘‘Bhāsitāya kho pana, bhikkhave, vepacittinā asurindena gāthāya asurā anumodiṃsu, devā tuṇhī ahesuṃ. Atha kho, bhikkhave, vepacitti asurindo sakkaṃ devānamindaṃ etadavoca – ‘bhaṇa, devānaminda, gātha’nti. Evaṃ {pb:T:1.0327} vutte, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Etadeva {pb:V:1.0258} ahaṃ maññe, bālassa paṭisedhanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Paraṃ saṅkupitaṃ ñatvā, yo sato upasammatī’’ti.
::

‘‘Bhāsitāya {pb:M:1.0225} kho pana, bhikkhave, sakkena devānamindena gāthāya, devā anumodiṃsu, asurā tuṇhī ahesuṃ. Atha kho, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo vepacittiṃ asurindaṃ etadavoca – ‘bhaṇa, vepacitti, gātha’nti. Evaṃ vutte, bhikkhave, vepacitti asurindo imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Etadeva titikkhāya, vajjaṃ passāmi vāsava;
::

::gatha2
Yadā naṃ maññati bālo, bhayā myāyaṃ titikkhati;
::

::gathalast
Ajjhāruhati dummedho, gova bhiyyo palāyina’’nti.
::

‘‘Bhāsitāya kho pana, bhikkhave, vepacittinā asurindena gāthāya asurā anumodiṃsu, devā tuṇhī ahesuṃ. Atha kho, bhikkhave, vepacitti asurindo sakkaṃ devānamindaṃ etadavoca – ‘bhaṇa, devānaminda, gātha’nti. Evaṃ vutte, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo imā gāthāyo abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kāmaṃ maññatu vā mā vā, bhayā myāyaṃ titikkhati;
::

::gathalast
Sadatthaparamā atthā, khantyā bhiyyo na vijjati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo have balavā santo, dubbalassa titikkhati;
::

::gathalast
Tamāhu paramaṃ khantiṃ, niccaṃ khamati dubbalo.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abalaṃ {pb:T:1.0328} taṃ balaṃ āhu, yassa bālabalaṃ balaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Balassa dhammaguttassa, paṭivattā na vijjati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasseva tena pāpiyo, yo kuddhaṃ paṭikujjhati;
::

::gathalast
Kuddhaṃ appaṭikujjhanto, saṅgāmaṃ jeti dujjayaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ubhinnamatthaṃ {pb:V:1.0259} carati, attano ca parassa ca;
::

::gathalast
Paraṃ saṅkupitaṃ ñatvā, yo sato upasammati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ubhinnaṃ {pb:P:1.0224} tikicchantānaṃ, attano ca parassa ca;
::

::gathalast
Janā maññanti bāloti, ye dhammassa akovidā’’ti.
::

‘‘Bhāsitāsu kho pana, bhikkhave, sakkena devānamindena gāthāsu, devā anumodiṃsu, asurā tuṇhī ahesuṃ. Atha kho, bhikkhave, devānañca asurānañca pārisajjā etadavocuṃ – ‘bhāsitā kho vepacittinā asurindena gāthāyo. Tā ca kho sadaṇḍāvacarā sasatthāvacarā, iti bhaṇḍanaṃ iti {pb:M:1.0226} viggaho iti kalaho. Bhāsitā kho {note:bhāsitā kho pana (sī.)} sakkena devānamindena gāthāyo. Tā ca kho adaṇḍāvacarā asatthāvacarā, iti abhaṇḍanaṃ iti aviggaho iti akalaho. Sakkassa devānamindassa subhāsitena jayo’ti. Iti kho, bhikkhave sakkassa devānamindassa subhāsitena jayo ahosī’’ti.

#### 6. Kulāvakasuttaṃ

{para:252} 252\. Sāvatthiyaṃ. ‘‘Bhūtapubbaṃ, bhikkhave, devāsurasaṅgāmo samupabyūḷho ahosi. Tasmiṃ kho pana, bhikkhave, saṅgāme asurā jiniṃsu{pb:T:1.0329}, devā parājiniṃsu. Parājitā ca kho, bhikkhave, devā apāyaṃsveva uttarenamukhā, abhiyaṃsveva ne asurā. Atha kho, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo mātali saṅgāhakaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kulāvakā mātali simbalismiṃ,
::

::gatha2
Īsāmukhena parivajjayassu;
::

::gatha3
Kāmaṃ cajāma asuresu pāṇaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Māyime dijā vikulāvakā {note:vikulāvā (syā. kaṃ. ka.)} ahesu’’nti.
::

‘‘‘Evaṃ bhaddantavā’ti kho, bhikkhave, mātali saṅgāhako sakkassa devānamindassa paṭissutvā sahassayuttaṃ ājaññarathaṃ paccudāvattesi. Atha kho, bhikkhave, asurānaṃ etadahosi {pb:V:1.0260} – ‘paccudāvatto kho dāni sakkassa devānamindassa sahassayutto ājaññaratho{pb:P:1.0225}. Dutiyampi kho devā asurehi saṅgāmessantīti bhītā asurapurameva pāvisiṃsu. Iti kho, bhikkhave, sakkassa devānamindassa dhammena jayo ahosī’’’ti.

#### 7. Nadubbhiyasuttaṃ

{para:253} 253\. Sāvatthiyaṃ. ‘‘Bhūtapubbaṃ, bhikkhave, sakkassa devānamindassa rahogatassa paṭisallīnassa evaṃ cetaso parivitakko udapādi – ‘yopi me assa supaccatthiko tassapāhaṃ na dubbheyya’nti. Atha kho, bhikkhave, vepacitti asurindo sakkassa devānamindassa cetasā cetoparivitakkamaññāya {pb:T:1.0330} yena sakko devānamindo tenupasaṅkami. Addasā {pb:M:1.0227} kho, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo vepacittiṃ asurindaṃ dūratova āgacchantaṃ. Disvāna vepacittiṃ asurindaṃ etadavoca – ‘tiṭṭha, vepacitti, gahitosī’’’ti.

‘‘Yadeva te, mārisa, pubbe cittaṃ, tadeva tvaṃ mā pajahāsī’’ti {note:tadeva tvaṃ mārisa pahāsīti (sī. syā. kaṃ.)}.

‘‘Sapassu ca me, vepacitti, adubbhāyā’’ti {note:adrubbhāya (ka.)}.

::gatha1
‘‘Yaṃ musā bhaṇato pāpaṃ, yaṃ pāpaṃ ariyūpavādino;
::

::gatha2
Mittadduno ca yaṃ pāpaṃ, yaṃ pāpaṃ akataññuno;
::

::gathalast
Tameva pāpaṃ phusatu {note:phusati (sī. pī.)}, yo te dubbhe sujampatī’’ti.
::

#### 8. Verocanaasurindasuttaṃ

{para:254} 254\. Sāvatthiyaṃ jetavane. Tena kho pana samayena bhagavā divāvihāragato hoti paṭisallīno. Atha kho sakko ca devānamindo verocano ca asurindo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā paccekaṃ dvārabāhaṃ nissāya aṭṭhaṃsu. Atha kho verocano asurindo bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Vāyametheva {pb:V:1.0261} puriso, yāva atthassa nipphadā;
::

::gathalast
Nipphannasobhano {note:sobhino (sī.), sobhaṇo (pī. ka.)} attho {note:atthā (sī.)}, verocanavaco ida’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Vāyametheva {pb:P:1.0226} puriso, yāva atthassa nipphadā;
::

::gathalast
Nipphannasobhano attho {note:nipphannasobhino atthā (sī. syā. kaṃ.)}, khantyā bhiyyo na vijjatī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbe {pb:T:1.0331} sattā atthajātā, tattha tattha yathārahaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Saṃyogaparamā tveva, sambhogā sabbapāṇinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nipphannasobhano attho, verocanavaco ida’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sabbe sattā atthajātā, tattha tattha yathārahaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Saṃyogaparamā tveva, sambhogā sabbapāṇinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Nipphannasobhano attho, khantyā bhiyyo na vijjatī’’ti.
::

#### 9. Araññāyatanaisisuttaṃ

{para:255} 255\. Sāvatthiyaṃ{pb:M:1.0228}. ‘‘Bhūtapubbaṃ, bhikkhave, sambahulā isayo sīlavanto kalyāṇadhammā araññāyatane paṇṇakuṭīsu sammanti. Atha kho, bhikkhave, sakko ca devānamindo vepacitti ca asurindo yena te isayo sīlavanto kalyāṇadhammā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu. Atha kho, bhikkhave, vepacitti asurindo paṭaliyo {note:aṭaliyo (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.), āṭaliyo (ka.) ma. ni. 2.410} upāhanā ārohitvā khaggaṃ olaggetvā chattena dhāriyamānena aggadvārena assamaṃ pavisitvā te isayo sīlavante kalyāṇadhamme apabyāmato karitvā atikkami. Atha kho, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo paṭaliyo upāhanā orohitvā khaggaṃ aññesaṃ datvā chattaṃ apanāmetvā dvāreneva assamaṃ pavisitvā te isayo sīlavante kalyāṇadhamme anuvātaṃ pañjaliko namassamāno aṭṭhāsi’’. Atha kho, bhikkhave, te isayo sīlavanto kalyāṇadhammā sakkaṃ devānamindaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsiṃsu –

::gatha1
‘‘Gandho {pb:T:1.0332} isīnaṃ ciradikkhitānaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Kāyā cuto gacchati mālutena;
::

::gatha3
Ito {pb:V:1.0262} paṭikkamma sahassanetta,
::

::gathalast
Gandho isīnaṃ asuci devarājā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gandho isīnaṃ ciradikkhitānaṃ,
::

::gatha2
Kāyā cuto gacchatu {note:gacchati (sī. syā. kaṃ.)} mālutena,
::

::gatha3
Sucitrapupphaṃ sirasmiṃva mālaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Gandhaṃ {pb:P:1.0227} etaṃ paṭikaṅkhāma bhante,
::

::gathalast
Na hettha devā paṭikūlasaññino’’ti.
::

#### 10. Samuddakasuttaṃ

{para:256} 256\. Sāvatthiyaṃ. ‘‘Bhūtapubbaṃ, bhikkhave, sambahulā isayo sīlavanto kalyāṇadhammā samuddatīre paṇṇakuṭīsu sammanti. Tena kho pana samayena devāsurasaṅgāmo samupabyūḷho ahosi. Atha kho, bhikkhave, tesaṃ isīnaṃ sīlavantānaṃ kalyāṇadhammānaṃ etadahosi – ‘dhammikā kho devā, adhammikā asurā. Siyāpi no asurato bhayaṃ. Yaṃnūna mayaṃ sambaraṃ asurindaṃ upasaṅkamitvā {pb:M:1.0229} abhayadakkhiṇaṃ yāceyyāmā’’’ti. ‘‘Atha kho, bhikkhave, te isayo sīlavanto kalyāṇadhammā – seyyathāpi {pb:T:1.0333} nāma balavā puriso samiñjitaṃ vā bāhaṃ pasāreyya, pasāritaṃ vā bāhaṃ samiñjeyya evameva – samuddatīre paṇṇakuṭīsu antarahitā sambarassa asurindassa sammukhe pāturahesuṃ. Atha kho, bhikkhave, te isayo sīlavanto kalyāṇadhammā sambaraṃ asurindaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsiṃsu –

::gatha1
‘‘Isayo sambaraṃ pattā, yācanti abhayadakkhiṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Kāmaṃkaro hi te dātuṃ, bhayassa abhayassa vā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Isīnaṃ abhayaṃ natthi, duṭṭhānaṃ sakkasevinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Abhayaṃ yācamānānaṃ, bhayameva dadāmi vo’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Abhayaṃ {pb:V:1.0263} yācamānānaṃ, bhayameva dadāsi no;
::

::gathalast
Paṭiggaṇhāma te etaṃ, akkhayaṃ hotu te bhayaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yādisaṃ vapate bījaṃ, tādisaṃ harate phalaṃ;
::

::gatha2
Kalyāṇakārī kalyāṇaṃ, pāpakārī ca pāpakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Pavuttaṃ tāta te bījaṃ, phalaṃ paccanubhossasī’’ti.
::

‘‘Atha kho, bhikkhave, te isayo sīlavanto kalyāṇadhammā sambaraṃ asurindaṃ abhisapitvā – seyyathāpi nāma balavā puriso samiñjitaṃ vā bāhaṃ pasāreyya, pasāritaṃ vā bāhaṃ samiñjeyya evameva – sambarassa asurindassa sammukhe antarahitā samuddatīre paṇṇakuṭīsu pāturahesuṃ. Atha {pb:T:1.0334}{pb:P:1.0228} kho, bhikkhave, sambaro asurindo tehi isīhi sīlavantehi kalyāṇadhammehi abhisapito rattiyā sudaṃ tikkhattuṃ ubbijjī’’ti.

::centre
Paṭhamo vaggo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Suvīraṃ susīmañceva, dhajaggaṃ vepacittino;
::

::gatha2
Subhāsitaṃ jayañceva, kulāvakaṃ nadubbhiyaṃ;
::

::gatha3
Verocana asurindo, isayo araññakañceva;
::

::gathalast
Isayo ca samuddakāti.
::

#### 2. Dutiyavaggo

#### 1. Vatapadasuttaṃ

{para:257} 257\. Sāvatthiyaṃ{pb:T:1.0335}{pb:M:1.0230}. ‘‘Sakkassa, bhikkhave, devānamindassa pubbe manussabhūtassa satta vatapadāni {pb:V:1.0264} {note:vattapadāni (ka.)} samattāni samādinnāni ahesuṃ, yesaṃ samādinnattā sakko sakkattaṃ ajjhagā. Katamāni satta vatapadāni? Yāvajīvaṃ mātāpettibharo assaṃ, yāvajīvaṃ kule jeṭṭhāpacāyī assaṃ, yāvajīvaṃ saṇhavāco assaṃ, yāvajīvaṃ apisuṇavāco assaṃ, yāvajīvaṃ vigatamalamaccherena cetasā agāraṃ ajjhāvaseyyaṃ muttacāgo payatapāṇi vossaggarato yācayogo dānasaṃvibhāgarato, yāvajīvaṃ saccavāco assaṃ, yāvajīvaṃ akkodhano assaṃ – sacepi me kodho uppajjeyya, khippameva naṃ paṭivineyya’’nti. ‘‘Sakkassa, bhikkhave, devānamindassa pubbe manussabhūtassa imāni satta vatapadāni samattāni samādinnāni ahesuṃ, yesaṃ samādinnattā sakko sakkattaṃ ajjhagā’’ti.

::gatha1
‘‘Mātāpettibharaṃ {pb:T:1.0336} jantuṃ, kule jeṭṭhāpacāyinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saṇhaṃ sakhilasambhāsaṃ, pesuṇeyyappahāyinaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Maccheravinaye yuttaṃ, saccaṃ kodhābhibhuṃ naraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ ve devā tāvatiṃsā, āhu sappuriso itī’’ti.
::

#### 2. Sakkanāmasuttaṃ

{para:258} 258\. Sāvatthiyaṃ {pb:P:1.0229} jetavane. Tatra kho bhagavā bhikkhū etadavoca – ‘‘sakko, bhikkhave, devānamindo pubbe manussabhūto samāno magho nāma māṇavo ahosi, tasmā maghavāti vuccati.

‘‘Sakko, bhikkhave, devānamindo pubbe manussabhūto samāno pure {note:pure pure (sī. pī.)} dānaṃ adāsi, tasmā purindadoti vuccati.

‘‘Sakko, bhikkhave, devānamindo pubbe manussabhūto samāno sakkaccaṃ dānaṃ adāsi, tasmā sakkoti vuccati.

‘‘Sakko{pb:V:1.0265}{pb:M:1.0231}, bhikkhave, devānamindo pubbe manussabhūto samāno āvasathaṃ adāsi, tasmā vāsavoti vuccati.

‘‘Sakko, bhikkhave, devānamindo sahassampi atthānaṃ muhuttena cinteti, tasmā sahassakkhoti vuccati.

‘‘Sakkassa, bhikkhave, devānamindassa sujā nāma asurakaññā pajāpati, tasmā sujampatīti vuccati.

‘‘Sakko, bhikkhave, devānamindo devānaṃ tāvatiṃsānaṃ issariyādhipaccaṃ rajjaṃ kāreti, tasmā devānamindoti vuccati.

‘‘Sakkassa{pb:T:1.0337}, bhikkhave devānamindassa pubbe manussabhūtassa satta vatapadāni samattāni samādinnāni ahesuṃ, yesaṃ samādinnattā sakko sakkattaṃ ajjhagā. Katamāni satta vatapadāni? Yāvajīvaṃ mātāpettibharo assaṃ, yāvajīvaṃ kule jeṭṭhāpacāyī assaṃ, yāvajīvaṃ saṇhavāco assaṃ, yāvajīvaṃ apisuṇavāco assaṃ, yāvajīvaṃ vigatamalamaccherena cetasā agāraṃ ajjhāvaseyyaṃ muttacāgo payatapāṇi vossaggarato yācayogo dānasaṃvibhāgarato, yāvajīvaṃ saccavāco assaṃ, yāvajīvaṃ akkodhano assaṃ – sacepi me kodho uppajjeyya, khippameva naṃ paṭivineyya’’nti. ‘‘Sakkassa, bhikkhave, devānamindassa pubbe manussabhūtassa imāni satta vatapadāni samattāni samādinnāni ahesuṃ, yesaṃ samādinnattā sakko sakkattaṃ ajjhagā’’ti.

::gatha1
‘‘Mātāpettibharaṃ {pb:P:1.0230} jantuṃ, kule jeṭṭhāpacāyinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saṇhaṃ sakhilasambhāsaṃ, pesuṇeyyappahāyinaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Maccheravinaye yuttaṃ, saccaṃ kodhābhibhuṃ naraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ ve devā tāvatiṃsā, āhu sappuriso itī’’ti.
::

#### 3. Mahālisuttaṃ

{para:259} 259\. Evaṃ {pb:V:1.0266} me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā vesāliyaṃ viharati mahāvane kūṭāgārasālāyaṃ. Atha kho mahāli licchavī yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ nisīdi. Ekamantaṃ {pb:T:1.0338} nisinno kho mahāli licchavī bhagavantaṃ etadavoca –

‘‘Diṭṭho kho{pb:M:1.0232}, bhante, bhagavatā sakko devānamindo’’ti?

‘‘Diṭṭho kho me, mahāli, sakko devānamindo’’ti.

‘‘So hi nūna, bhante, sakkapatirūpako bhavissati. Duddaso hi, bhante, sakko devānamindo’’ti.

‘‘Sakkañca khvāhaṃ, mahāli, pajānāmi sakkakaraṇe ca dhamme, yesaṃ dhammānaṃ samādinnattā sakko sakkattaṃ ajjhagā, tañca pajānāmi.

‘‘Sakko, mahāli, devānamindo pubbe manussabhūto samāno magho nāma māṇavo ahosi, tasmā maghavāti vuccati.

‘‘Sakko, mahāli, devānamindo pubbe manussabhūto samāno sakkaccaṃ dānaṃ adāsi, tasmā sakkoti vuccati.

‘‘Sakko, mahāli, devānamindo pubbe manussabhūto samāno pure dānaṃ adāsi, tasmā purindadoti vuccati.

‘‘Sakko, mahāli, devānamindo pubbe manussabhūto samāno āvasathaṃ adāsi, tasmā vāsavoti vuccati.

‘‘Sakko, mahāli, devānamindo sahassampi atthānaṃ muhuttena cinteti, tasmā sahassakkhoti vuccati.

‘‘Sakkassa{pb:V:1.0267}, mahāli, devānamindassa sujā nāma asurakaññā pajāpati, tasmā sujampatīti vuccati.

‘‘Sakko, mahāli, devānamindo devānaṃ tāvatiṃsānaṃ issariyādhipaccaṃ {pb:P:1.0231} rajjaṃ kāreti, tasmā devānamindoti vuccati.

‘‘Sakkassa, mahāli, devānamindassa pubbe manussabhūtassa satta {pb:T:1.0339} vatapadāni samattāni samādinnāni ahesuṃ, yesaṃ samādinnattā sakko sakkattaṃ ajjhagā. Katamāni satta vatapadāni? Yāvajīvaṃ mātāpettibharo assaṃ, yāvajīvaṃ kule jeṭṭhāpacāyī assaṃ, yāvajīvaṃ saṇhavāco assaṃ, yāvajīvaṃ apisuṇavāco assaṃ, yāvajīvaṃ vigatamalamaccherena cetasā agāraṃ ajjhāvaseyyaṃ muttacāgo payatapāṇi vossaggarato yācayogo dānasaṃvibhāgarato, yāvajīvaṃ saccavāco assaṃ, yāvajīvaṃ akkodhano assaṃ – sacepi me kodho uppajeyya, khippameva naṃ paṭivineyya’’nti. ‘‘Sakkassa, mahāli, devānamindassa pubbe manussabhūtassa imāni {pb:M:1.0233} satta vatapadāni samattāni samādinnāni ahesuṃ, yesaṃ samādinnattā sakko sakkattaṃ ajjhagā’’ti.

::gatha1
‘‘Mātāpettibharaṃ jantuṃ, kule jeṭṭhāpacāyinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Saṇhaṃ sakhilasambhāsaṃ, pesuṇeyyappahāyinaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Maccheravinaye yuttaṃ, saccaṃ kodhābhibhuṃ naraṃ;
::

::gathalast
Taṃ ve devā tāvatiṃsā, āhu sappuriso itī’’ti.
::

#### 4. Daliddasuttaṃ

{para:260} 260\. Ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati veḷuvane kalandakanivāpe. Tatra kho bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi – ‘‘bhikkhavo’’ti. ‘‘Bhadante’’ti te bhikkhū bhagavato paccassosuṃ. Bhagavā etadavoca –

‘‘Bhūtapubbaṃ, bhikkhave, aññataro puriso imasmiṃyeva {pb:T:1.0340} rājagahe manussadaliddo {note:manussadaḷiddo (sī. syā. kaṃ.)} ahosi manussakapaṇo {pb:V:1.0268} manussavarāko. So tathāgatappavedite dhammavinaye saddhaṃ samādiyi, sīlaṃ samādiyi, sutaṃ samādiyi, cāgaṃ samādiyi, paññaṃ samādiyi. So tathāgatappavedite dhammavinaye saddhaṃ samādiyitvā sīlaṃ samādiyitvā sutaṃ samādiyitvā cāgaṃ samādiyitvā paññaṃ samādiyitvā kāyassa bhedā paraṃ maraṇā sugatiṃ {pb:P:1.0232} saggaṃ lokaṃ upapajji devānaṃ tāvatiṃsānaṃ sahabyataṃ. So aññe deve atirocati vaṇṇena ceva yasasā ca. Tatra sudaṃ, bhikkhave, devā tāvatiṃsā ujjhāyanti khiyyanti vipācenti – ‘acchariyaṃ vata bho, abbhutaṃ vata bho! Ayañhi devaputto pubbe manussabhūto samāno manussadaliddo ahosi manussakapaṇo manussavarāko; so kāyassa bhedā paraṃ maraṇā sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapanno devānaṃ tāvatiṃsānaṃ sahabyataṃ. So aññe deve atirocati vaṇṇena ceva yasasā cā’’’ti.

‘‘Atha kho, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo deve tāvatiṃse āmantesi – ‘mā kho tumhe, mārisā, etassa devaputtassa ujjhāyittha. Eso kho, mārisā, devaputto pubbe manussabhūto samāno tathāgatappavedite {pb:M:1.0234} dhammavinaye saddhaṃ samādiyi, sīlaṃ samādiyi, sutaṃ samādiyi, cāgaṃ samādiyi, paññaṃ samādiyi. So tathāgatappavedite dhammavinaye saddhaṃ samādiyitvā sīlaṃ samādiyitvā sutaṃ samādiyitvā cāgaṃ samādiyitvā paññaṃ samādiyitvā kāyassa bhedā paraṃ maraṇā sugatiṃ saggaṃ lokaṃ upapanno devānaṃ tāvatiṃsānaṃ sahabyataṃ{pb:T:1.0341}. So aññe deve atirocati vaṇṇena ceva yasasā cā’’’ti. Atha kho, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo deve tāvatiṃse anunayamāno tāyaṃ velāyaṃ imā gāthāyo abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Yassa saddhā tathāgate, acalā suppatiṭṭhitā;
::

::gathalast
Sīlañca yassa kalyāṇaṃ, ariyakantaṃ pasaṃsitaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Saṅghe pasādo yassatthi, ujubhūtañca dassanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Adaliddoti taṃ āhu, amoghaṃ tassa jīvitaṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Tasmā saddhañca sīlañca, pasādaṃ dhammadassanaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Anuyuñjetha medhāvī, saraṃ buddhāna sāsana’’nti.
::

#### 5. Rāmaṇeyyakasuttaṃ

{para:261} 261\. Sāvatthiyaṃ {pb:V:1.0269} jetavane. Atha kho sakko devānamindo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṃ ṭhito kho sakko devānamindo bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘kiṃ nu kho, bhante, bhūmirāmaṇeyyaka’’nti?

::gatha1
‘‘Ārāmacetyā {pb:P:1.0233} vanacetyā, pokkharañño sunimmitā;
::

::gathalast
Manussarāmaṇeyyassa, kalaṃ nāgghanti soḷasiṃ.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Gāme vā yadi vāraññe, ninne vā yadi vā thale;
::

::gathalast
Yattha arahanto viharanti, taṃ bhūmirāmaṇeyyaka’’nti.
::

#### 6. Yajamānasuttaṃ

{para:262} 262\. Ekaṃ {pb:T:1.0342} samayaṃ bhagavā rājagahe viharati gijjhakūṭe pabbate. Atha kho sakko devānamindo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ {pb:M:1.0235} abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṃ ṭhito kho sakko devānamindo bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Yajamānānaṃ manussānaṃ, puññapekkhāna pāṇinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Karotaṃ opadhikaṃ puññaṃ, kattha dinnaṃ mahapphala’’nti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Cattāro ca paṭipannā, cattāro ca phale ṭhitā;
::

::gathalast
Esa saṅgho ujubhūto, paññāsīlasamāhito.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yajamānānaṃ manussānaṃ, puññapekkhāna pāṇinaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Karotaṃ opadhikaṃ puññaṃ, saṅghe dinnaṃ mahapphala’’nti.
::

#### 7. Buddhavandanāsuttaṃ

{para:263} 263\. Sāvatthiyaṃ {pb:V:1.0270} jetavane. Tena kho pana samayena bhagavā divāvihāragato hoti paṭisallīno. Atha kho sakko ca devānamindo brahmā ca sahampati yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā paccekaṃ dvārabāhaṃ nissāya aṭṭhaṃsu. Atha kho sakko devānamindo bhagavato santike imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Uṭṭhehi {pb:T:1.0343} vīra vijitasaṅgāma,
::

::gatha2
Pannabhāra anaṇa vicara loke;
::

::gatha3
Cittañca te suvimuttaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Cando yathā pannarasāya ratti’’nti.
::

‘‘Na {pb:P:1.0234} kho, devānaminda, tathāgatā evaṃ vanditabbā. Evañca kho, devānaminda, tathāgatā vanditabbā –

::gatha1
‘‘Uṭṭhehi vīra vijitasaṅgāma,
::

::gatha2
Satthavāha anaṇa vicara loke;
::

::gatha3
Desassu bhagavā dhammaṃ,
::

::gathalast
Aññātāro bhavissantī’’ti.
::

#### 8. Gahaṭṭhavandanāsuttaṃ

{para:264} 264\. Sāvatthiyaṃ. Tatra…pe… etadavoca – ‘‘bhūtapubbaṃ, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo mātaliṃ saṅgāhakaṃ āmantesi – ‘yojehi, samma mātali, sahassayuttaṃ {pb:M:1.0236} ājaññarathaṃ. Uyyānabhūmiṃ gacchāma subhūmiṃ dassanāyā’ti. ‘Evaṃ bhaddantavā’ti kho, bhikkhave, mātali saṅgāhako sakkassa devānamindassa paṭissutvā sahassayuttaṃ ājaññarathaṃ yojetvā sakkassa devānamindassa paṭivedesi – ‘yutto kho te, mārisa, sahassayutto ājaññaratho. Yassa dāni kālaṃ maññasī’’’ti. Atha kho, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo vejayantapāsādā orohanto {pb:V:1.0271} añjaliṃ katvā {note:pañjaliko (pī.), pañjaliṃ katvā (ka.)} sudaṃ puthuddisā namassati. Atha {pb:T:1.0344} kho, bhikkhave, mātali saṅgāhako sakkaṃ devānamindaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Taṃ namassanti tevijjā, sabbe bhummā ca khattiyā;
::

::gatha2
Cattāro ca mahārājā, tidasā ca yasassino;
::

::gathalast
Atha ko nāma so yakkho, yaṃ tvaṃ sakka namassasī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Maṃ namassanti tevijjā, sabbe bhummā ca khattiyā;
::

::gathalast
Cattāro ca mahārājā, tidasā ca yasassino.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ahañca sīlasampanne, cirarattasamāhite;
::

::gathalast
Sammāpabbajite vande, brahmacariyaparāyane.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye gahaṭṭhā puññakarā, sīlavanto upāsakā;
::

::gathalast
Dhammena dāraṃ posenti, te namassāmi mātalī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Seṭṭhā hi kira lokasmiṃ, ye tvaṃ sakka namassasi;
::

::gathalast
Ahampi te namassāmi, ye namassasi vāsavā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ vatvāna maghavā, devarājā sujampati;
::

::gathalast
Puthuddisā namassitvā, pamukho rathamāruhī’’ti.
::

#### 9. Satthāravandanāsuttaṃ

{para:265} 265\. Sāvatthiyaṃ {pb:P:1.0235} jetavane. ‘‘Bhūtapubbaṃ, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo mātaliṃ saṅgāhakaṃ āmantesi – ‘yojehi, samma mātali, sahassayuttaṃ ājaññarathaṃ, uyyānabhūmiṃ gacchāma subhūmiṃ dassanāyā’ti. ‘Evaṃ bhaddantavā’ti kho, bhikkhave, mātali saṅgāhako sakkassa devānamindassa paṭissutvā {pb:M:1.0237} sahassayuttaṃ ājaññarathaṃ yojetvā sakkassa devānamindassa {pb:T:1.0345} paṭivedesi {pb:V:1.0272} – ‘yutto kho te, mārisa, sahassayutto ājaññaratho. Yassa dāni kālaṃ maññasī’’’ti. Atha kho, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo vejayantapāsādā orohanto añjaliṃ katvā sudaṃ bhagavantaṃ namassati. Atha kho, bhikkhave, mātali saṅgāhako sakkaṃ devānamindaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Yañhi devā manussā ca, taṃ namassanti vāsava;
::

::gathalast
Atha ko nāma so yakkho, yaṃ tvaṃ sakka namassasī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yo idha sammāsambuddho, asmiṃ loke sadevake;
::

::gathalast
Anomanāmaṃ satthāraṃ, taṃ namassāmi mātali.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Yesaṃ rāgo ca doso ca, avijjā ca virājitā;
::

::gathalast
Khīṇāsavā arahanto, te namassāmi mātali.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Ye rāgadosavinayā, avijjāsamatikkamā;
::

::gatha2
Sekkhā apacayārāmā, appamattānusikkhare;
::

::gathalast
Te namassāmi mātalī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Seṭṭhā hi kira lokasmiṃ, ye tvaṃ sakka namassasi;
::

::gathalast
Ahampi te namassāmi, ye namassasi vāsavā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ vatvāna maghavā, devarājā sujampati;
::

::gathalast
Bhagavantaṃ namassitvā, pamukho rathamāruhī’’ti.
::

#### 10. Saṅghavandanāsuttaṃ

{para:266} 266\. Sāvatthiyaṃ {pb:T:1.0346} jetavane. Tatra kho…pe… etadavoca – ‘‘bhūtapubbaṃ, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo mātaliṃ saṅgāhakaṃ āmantesi – ‘yojehi, samma mātali, sahassayuttaṃ ājaññarathaṃ{pb:V:1.0273}, uyyānabhūmiṃ gacchāma subhūmiṃ dassanāyā’ti. ‘Evaṃ {pb:P:1.0236} bhaddantavā’ti kho, bhikkhave, mātali saṅgāhako sakkassa devānamindassa paṭissutvā, sahassayuttaṃ ājaññarathaṃ yojetvā sakkassa devānamindassa paṭivedesi – ‘yutto kho te, mārisa, sahassayutto ājaññaratho, yassa dāni kālaṃ maññasī’’’ti. Atha kho, bhikkhave{pb:M:1.0238}, sakko devānamindo vejayantapāsādā orohanto añjaliṃ katvā sudaṃ bhikkhusaṅghaṃ namassati. Atha kho, bhikkhave, mātali saṅgāhako sakkaṃ devānamindaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Tañhi ete namasseyyuṃ, pūtidehasayā narā;
::

::gathalast
Nimuggā kuṇapamhete, khuppipāsasamappitā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃ nu tesaṃ pihayasi, anāgārāna vāsava;
::

::gathalast
Ācāraṃ isinaṃ brūhi, taṃ suṇoma vaco tavā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Etaṃ tesaṃ pihayāmi, anāgārāna mātali;
::

::gathalast
Yamhā gāmā pakkamanti, anapekkhā vajanti te.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Na tesaṃ koṭṭhe openti, na kumbhi {note:na kumbhā (syā. kaṃ. pī. ka.)} na kaḷopiyaṃ {note:khaḷopiyaṃ (sī.)};
::

::gathalast
Paraniṭṭhitamesānā {note:paraniṭṭhitamesanā (syā. kaṃ. ka.)}, tena yāpenti subbatā.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Sumantamantino {pb:T:1.0347} dhīrā, tuṇhībhūtā samañcarā;
::

::gathalast
Devā viruddhā asurehi, puthu maccā ca mātali.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Aviruddhā viruddhesu, attadaṇḍesu nibbutā;
::

::gathalast
Sādānesu anādānā, te namassāmi mātalī’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Seṭṭhā hi kira lokasmiṃ, ye tvaṃ sakka namassasi;
::

::gathalast
Ahampi te namassāmi, ye namassasi vāsavā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Idaṃ {pb:V:1.0274} vatvāna maghavā, devarājā sujampati;
::

::gathalast
Bhikkhusaṅghaṃ namassitvā, pamukho rathamāruhī’’ti.
::

::centre
Dutiyo vaggo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Devā pana {note:va tapadena (sī. syā. kaṃ.)} tayo vuttā, daliddañca rāmaṇeyyakaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Yajamānañca vandanā, tayo sakkanamassanāti.
::

#### 3. Tatiyavaggo

#### 1. Chetvāsuttaṃ

{para:267} 267\. Sāvatthiyaṃ {pb:T:1.0348}{pb:M:1.0239}{pb:P:1.0237} jetavane. Atha kho sakko devānamindo yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ aṭṭhāsi. Ekamantaṃ ṭhito kho sakko devānamindo bhagavantaṃ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kiṃsu chetvā sukhaṃ seti, kiṃsu chetvā na socati;
::

::gathalast
Kissassu ekadhammassa, vadhaṃ rocesi gotamā’’ti.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kodhaṃ chetvā sukhaṃ seti, kodhaṃ chetvā na socati;
::

::gatha2
Kodhassa visamūlassa, madhuraggassa vāsava;
::

::gathalast
Vadhaṃ ariyā pasaṃsanti, tañhi chetvā na socatī’’ti.
::

#### 2. Dubbaṇṇiyasuttaṃ

{para:268} 268\. Sāvatthiyaṃ {pb:V:1.0275} jetavane. Tatra kho…pe… etadavoca – ‘‘bhūtapubbaṃ, bhikkhave, aññataro yakkho dubbaṇṇo okoṭimako sakkassa devānamindassa āsane nisinno ahosi. Tatra sudaṃ, bhikkhave, devā tāvatiṃsā ujjhāyanti khiyyanti vipācenti – ‘acchariyaṃ vata bho, abbhutaṃ vata, bho! Ayaṃ yakkho dubbaṇṇo okoṭimako sakkassa devānamindassa āsane nisinno’’’ti! Yathā {pb:T:1.0349} yathā kho, bhikkhave, devā tāvatiṃsā ujjhāyanti khiyyanti vipācenti, tathā tathā so yakkho abhirūpataro ceva hoti dassanīyataro ca pāsādikataro ca.

‘‘Atha kho, bhikkhave, devā tāvatiṃsā yena sakko devānamindo tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā sakkaṃ devānamindaṃ etadavocuṃ – ‘idha te, mārisa, aññataro yakkho dubbaṇṇo okoṭimako sakkassa devānamindassa āsane nisinno. Tatra sudaṃ, mārisa, devā tāvatiṃsā ujjhāyanti khiyyanti vipācenti – acchariyaṃ vata, bho, abbhutaṃ vata, bho! Ayaṃ yakkho dubbaṇṇo okoṭimako {pb:P:1.0238} sakkassa devānamindassa āsane nisinnoti. Yathā yathā kho, mārisa, devā ujjhāyanti khiyyanti vipācenti, tathā tathā so yakkho abhirūpataro ceva hoti dassanīyataro {pb:M:1.0240} ca pāsādikataro cāti. So hi nūna, mārisa, kodhabhakkho yakkho bhavissatī’’’ti.

‘‘Atha kho, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo yena so kodhabhakkho yakkho tenupasaṅkami; upasaṅkamitvā ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā dakkhiṇajāṇumaṇḍalaṃ pathaviyaṃ nihantvā yena so kodhabhakkho yakkho tenañjaliṃ paṇāmetvā tikkhattuṃ nāmaṃ sāveti – ‘sakkohaṃ mārisa, devānamindo, sakkohaṃ, mārisa, devānamindo’ti. Yathā yathā kho, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo nāmaṃ sāvesi, tathā tathā so yakkho dubbaṇṇataro ceva ahosi okoṭimakataro ca. Dubbaṇṇataro ceva {pb:T:1.0350} hutvā okoṭimakataro ca tatthevantaradhāyī’’ti. Atha kho, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo sake āsane nisīditvā deve tāvatiṃse anunayamāno tāyaṃ velāyaṃ imā gāthāyo abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Na {pb:V:1.0276} sūpahatacittomhi, nāvattena suvānayo;
::

::gathalast
Na vo cirāhaṃ kujjhāmi, kodho mayi nāvatiṭṭhati.
::

::gatha1
‘‘Kuddhāhaṃ na pharusaṃ brūmi, na ca dhammāni kittaye;
::

::gathalast
Sanniggaṇhāmi attānaṃ, sampassaṃ atthamattano’’ti.
::

#### 3. Sambarimāyāsuttaṃ

{para:269} 269\. Sāvatthiyaṃ…pe… bhagavā etadavoca – ‘‘bhūtapubbaṃ, bhikkhave, vepacitti asurindo ābādhiko ahosi dukkhito bāḷhagilāno. Atha kho bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo yena vepacitti asurindo tenupasaṅkami gilānapucchako. Addasā kho, bhikkhave, vepacitti asurindo sakkaṃ devānamindaṃ dūratova āgacchantaṃ. Disvāna sakkaṃ devānamindaṃ etadavoca – ‘tikiccha maṃ devānamindā’ti. ‘Vācehi {pb:P:1.0239} maṃ, vepacitti, sambarimāya’nti. ‘Na tāvāhaṃ vācemi, yāvāhaṃ, mārisa, asure paṭipucchāmī’’’ti. ‘‘Atha kho, bhikkhave, vepacitti asurindo asure paṭipucchi – ‘vācemahaṃ, mārisā, sakkaṃ devānamindaṃ sambarimāya’nti? ‘Mā kho tvaṃ, mārisa, vācesi sakkaṃ devānamindaṃ sambarimāya’’’nti. Atha kho, bhikkhave, vepacitti asurindo sakkaṃ devānamindaṃ gāthāya {pb:T:1.0351} ajjhabhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Māyāvī {pb:M:1.0241} maghavā sakka, devarāja sujampati;
::

::gathalast
Upeti nirayaṃ ghoraṃ, sambarova sataṃ sama’’nti.
::

#### 4. Accayasuttaṃ

{para:270} 270\. Sāvatthiyaṃ…pe… ārāme. Tena kho pana samayena dve bhikkhū sampayojesuṃ. Tatreko bhikkhu accasarā. Atha kho so bhikkhu tassa bhikkhuno santike accayaṃ accayato deseti; so bhikkhu nappaṭiggaṇhāti. Atha kho sambahulā bhikkhū yena bhagavā tenupasaṅkamiṃsu; upasaṅkamitvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā ekamantaṃ nisīdiṃsu. Ekamantaṃ nisinnā kho te bhikkhū bhagavantaṃ etadavocuṃ – ‘‘idha, bhante, dve bhikkhū sampayojesuṃ, tatreko bhikkhu accasarā{pb:V:1.0277}. Atha kho so, bhante, bhikkhu tassa bhikkhuno santike accayaṃ accayato deseti, so bhikkhu nappaṭiggaṇhātī’’ti.

‘‘Dveme, bhikkhave, bālā. Yo ca accayaṃ accayato na passati, yo ca accayaṃ desentassa yathādhammaṃ nappaṭiggaṇhā’’ti – ime kho, bhikkhave, dve bālā. ‘‘Dveme, bhikkhave, paṇḍitā. Yo ca accayaṃ accayato passati, yo ca accayaṃ desentassa yathādhammaṃ paṭiggaṇhā’’ti – ime kho, bhikkhave, dve paṇḍitā.

‘‘Bhūtapubbaṃ{pb:T:1.0352}, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo sudhammāyaṃ sabhāyaṃ deve tāvatiṃse anunayamāno tāyaṃ velāyaṃ imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Kodho {pb:P:1.0240} vo vasamāyātu, mā ca mittehi vo jarā;
::

::gatha1
Agarahiyaṃ mā garahittha, mā ca bhāsittha pesuṇaṃ;
::

::gathalast
Atha pāpajanaṃ kodho, pabbatovābhimaddatī’’ti.
::

#### 5. Akkodhasuttaṃ

{para:271} 271\. Evaṃ me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. Tatra kho bhagavā bhikkhū…pe… bhagavā etadavoca – ‘‘bhūtapubbaṃ, bhikkhave, sakko devānamindo sudhammāyaṃ sabhāyaṃ deve tāvatiṃse anunayamāno tāyaṃ velāyaṃ imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsi –

::gatha1
‘‘Mā {pb:M:1.0242} vo kodho ajjhabhavi, mā ca kujjhittha kujjhataṃ;
::

::gatha2
Akkodho avihiṃsā ca, ariyesu ca paṭipadā {note:vasatī sadā (sī. syā. kaṃ. pī.)};
::

::gathalast
Atha pāpajanaṃ kodho, pabbatovābhimaddatī’’ti.
::

::centre
Tatiyo vaggo.
::

Tassuddānaṃ {pb:V:1.0278} –

::gatha1
Chetvā dubbaṇṇiyamāyā, accayena akodhano;
::

::gatha2
Desitaṃ buddhaseṭṭhena, idañhi sakkapañcakanti.
::

::centre
Sakkasaṃyuttaṃ samattaṃ.
::

#### Sagāthāvaggo paṭhamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

::gatha1
Devatā {pb:T:1.0353} devaputto ca, rājā māro ca bhikkhunī;
::

::gathalast
Brahmā brāhmaṇa vaṅgīso, vanayakkhena vāsavoti.
::

::centre
Sagāthāvaggasaṃyuttapāḷi niṭṭhitā.
::
